<pb n="r001"/>
<head>ṛjuvimalāpatrcikā</head>
<head>śālikanāthamiśrakṛtā</head>
<head>prathamādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ ।।</head>
<p><q>uktaṃ kāryamarthaṃ pratipādayato vedasya prāmāṇyam</q> । asyārthaḥ-kāryamarthaṃ pradhānatayā
pratipādayato vedasya prāmāṇyamuktam । tatraiva śabdasya prāmāṇyavyutpatteḥ vyatpattyāyattatvācca
tasyeti । sahetukaṃ prāmāṇyamanubhāṣya pūrvapakṣamidānīmāha-<q>yasya punaḥ kārye'rthe'nvayo nāva-
gamyate akāryatayā tasya yaḥ pratipādakaḥ śabdaḥ tasya kathaṃ prāmāṇyaṃ</q> yathā <q>sorodīdityeva-
mādeḥ ।</q> yo hyanuṣṭheyarūpo'rthaḥ tasya kāryātmake vidhyarthe'nvayo bhavati nānyasyeti-yathā karaṇasyeti-
kartavyatāyāśca, adhikāriṇo'pi sādhyataiva, aiśvaryasya sādhyatvāt । tena tasyāpi kāryarūpasyaiva﻿<pb n="r002"/>
kāryānvayaḥ । rudrarodanādikastvartho'kāryātmakaḥ । ataḥ tasya kāryānvayitā nāvagamyate tena
kāryānanvitārthapratipādakatayā so'rodīdityevamādeḥ prāmāṇyaṃ na yuktamityarthaḥ ।</p>
<p>tadevaṃ bhinnavākyāśrayaṇena ekadeśimatena pūrvapakṣitam । tatra rāddhāntaikadeśyāha—
<q>mābhūttasya prāmāṇyaṃ</q> tasya kevalasyārthavādabhāgasya bhavatvapramāṇatā, na kācit kṣatiḥ । nanu
tadaprāmāṇye vidhyuddeśasyāpi jñātaprāmāṇyasya <note n="1">A reads <dn>aprāmāṇyavyutpattiḥ ।</dn></note>aprāmāṇyāpattirmahatī kṣatiḥ ityatrāha—<q>na
tadapramāṇatayā pramāṇamapramāṇaṃ bhavitumarhati ।</q> kāryapratipādakatvābhāvāt yadyarthavādānāma-
prāmāṇyaṃ tadā kāryapratipādakasyānapekṣasya kimityaprāmāṇyam । <q>pramāṇasya hyanapekṣatvamuktam ।</q>
tenāprāmāṇyasyāvakāśo nāsti । na cārthavādāprāmāṇyāt vidhyuddeśasyānapekṣatvamuktamapaiti, kāraṇā-
bhāvāt tadāha—<q>na cānyasyāprāmāṇyāt pramāṇe tadapaitīti ।</q> ākṣeptā samādhāturā-
śaṅkāmāha—<q>atha manyase sakalasya vedasya prāmāṇyaṃ na prāpnotīti</q> kṣatiḥ asti । dūpayati
—<q>kena vedaṃ</q> sakalasya vedasya prāmāṇyaṃ pratijñātaṃ yena tadasiddhau kṣatiḥ syāt । neda
pratijñātaṃ ataḥ tadasiddhāvapi na kācit kṣatiḥ ।</p>﻿<pb n="r003"/>
<p>nanu codanālakṣaṇasūtre pratijñātametadityāha<note n="1">B reads <dn>dityata āha ।</dn></note>—<q>yato'rthāvagatiḥ tasya tallakṣaṇataiveti
pratijñā ।</q> yasmāt kāryarūpo vedārtho'vagamyate tasya tatra prāmāṇyameveti pratijñā, na punarvedaḥ
pramāṇamiti । arthāddhi pramāṇapratijñā । vedārthasvarūpapratijñā tu śrautī—codanālakṣaṇa eva kāryarūpa
eva vedārtha iti । yallakṣaṇaśvāsau saiva codanā tatra pramāṇamityarthāllabhyate । tena kārye'rthe tatprati-
pādakasyaiva prāmāṇyaṃ pratijñāta nārthavādabhāgasya । na cārthavādaprāmāṇyaṃ <note n="2">C <dn>siddhāvapyupayogi ।</dn></note>pratijñāsiddhāvupayogi ।
anapekṣatvamātrasādhyatvāttasyāḥ sādhitañcānapekṣatvaṃ, tatsiddhau siddhaiva pratijñā । tadāha—<q>sā cāna-
pekṣatayā sādhitā । yatastvarthāvagatireva nāsti</q> yajamānaḥ prastara ityevamādeḥ <q>tadapramāṇameva ।</q>
vidhyarthaikavākyatayā hi gauṇyā vṛttyā sāmānādhikaraṇyopapateḥ yajamānaḥ prastara ityevamādeḥ
arthāvagamakatvaṃ anyathā tvanavagamakatvameva । <q>yato vā pramāṇāntarapramitaviṣayaivāvagatiḥ
tasyāpi tata eva pramāṇāntarātprāmāṇyamityuktaṃ</q> <note n="3"><dn>yattu laukikaṃ vacanaṃ taccet pratyayitāt puruṣādindriyaviṣayaṃ vā'vitathameva tat1-1-2</dn></note>pratyayitabhāṣye । pramāṇāntaramālocya
tasya satyārthatetyarthaḥ yathā <quote>āpo vai śāntā</quote> iti । viparyaye cāprāmāṇyameva yathā <quote>uttā-
nā vai devagavā vahanti</quote> iti । atrāpi guṇavādāśrayaṇaṃ vidhyekavākyatāṃ vinā nāstīti yathā-
śrutārthatve pramāṇāntaraviparyayaḥ ।</p>


﻿<pb n="r004"/>
ākṣeptā upasaṃharati—<q>tasmādasaṃbaddhaiveyaṃ cintā-akriyārthānāṃ kathaṃ prāmāṇyamiti ।</q>
samādhāturāśaṅkāntaramāha—<q>tadviparyayāt svādhyāyādhyayanavidheḥ ānarthakyamiti cet</q>
asyārthaḥ-yadā pramāṇāntaraviparyayādarthavādapadānāmarthaśūnyatā tadā <quote>svādhyāyo'dhyetavya</quote>
<note n="1">B <dn>ityasya vidheḥ</dn></note>ityadhyayanavidheḥ ānarthakyaṃ prāpnoti । arthavādabhāge'vivakṣitasvārthe arthāvabodhalakṣaṇaprayojanā-
bhāvāt svādhyāyavidherānarthakyaṃ prāpnoti । tenāvyāpakatayā'rthāvabodhaṃ prayojanaṃ parityajyānyatpra-
yojanaṃ <note n="2">A <dn>kartavyaṃ</dn></note>kalpyam । tataśca yatrāpyarthaḥ pratīyate tavāpyanyaparatvādadhyayanasyā'rthāvivakṣā ।
<note n="3">B <dn>vivakṣāyāṃ</dn></note>avivakṣāyāmaprāmāṇyaṃ prāpnotīti ।</p>
<p>dūṣayati—<q>nānarthakyam</q> । kuta ityāha-<q>svādhyāyaśabdavācyasyārthasyādhyayanaṃ vidhī-
yate nārthavato'narthakasya</q> veti hetoḥ, <q>humityevamādīnāmiva</q> । yathā humityevamādīnāma-
narthakānāmapyadhyayanaṃ vidhīyate, tathā'rthavādānāmapi vidhīyatām । tadvidhāne ca vākyārthasya
nāstyānarthakyam । <q>tasmātko'yamupālambhaḥ</q> ko'yaṃ doṣa ityarthaḥ ।</p>
<p>āśaṅkāntaramāha—<q>svādhyāyavidheḥ prayojanaśūnyatā prāpnotīti cet</q> ।﻿<pb n="r005"/>
dūṣayati—<q>niyogārthanirvṛtteḥ kimanyat prayojanaṃ sarvavidhīnām,</q> yadabhāvāt prayojana-
śūnyatā <note n="1">B <dn>syāt ।</dn></note>prāpnoti । yo'pi hi kāmyo'dhikāraḥ tatrāpi niyogasiddhireva pradhānaṃ prayojanam ।
svargādisiddhistu nāntarīyakī । sa ca niyogārtho'kṣaragrahaṇenaiva nirvṛttaḥ vināpyarthāvabodhanaṃ;
tena nāsti prayojanaśūnyatā । yadi niyogārthanirvṛttireva prayojanaṃ kathaṃ tarhārthāvabodhaḥ
prayojanamityatrāha-<q>arthajñānantvarthājjātaṃ na niyogataḥ pratipannamiti</q> । adhyāpanavidhinaiva
adhyayane'nuṣṭhāpite'pi pratīyamāno'rthaḥ svīkṛtaḥ । na punaḥ vidhinaiva tasya siddhiḥ jñāpitā ।
kuta ityāha—<q>na hyarthajñānakāmasyāyaṃ niyogaḥ</q> । yadi hyarthajñānakāmasya svādhyāyādhyaya-
ne'dhikāraḥ syāt tadā niyoga evārthāvabodhasiddhiṃ jñāpayet । na cāsāvasti । <q>kutaḥ ? na hi
paśvādīnāmiva vedārthasyānyataḥ prasiddhirasti, yena tatkāmasyādhyayanaṃ vidhīyeta</q> । upalabdha-
pūrvake hi priye bhavatīcchā nānupalabdhe । na cānavadhītavedena vedādanyato vedārtho'vagataḥ yena
taṃ kāmayeta yathā paśvādīn ।।</p>
<p><q>nanu ca vedavadvedārthasyāpi svādhyāyādanyataḥ prasiddhirasti । na hyaprasiddhasya
kāraṇatāpi śakyate vaktum</q> । asyārthaḥ—yathā adhyetrantaragato vedaḥ prasiddhaḥ tathā'rthopi
prasiddhaḥ । yadi hyadhyetrantaragato vedaḥ svārthaṃ nāvabodhayet, tato'prasiddho vedārtha. kāraṇamapi
na bhavet prayojakopi na bhavet । adhyāpanavidhyartho'pyapratipannaḥ kathamadhyayanaṃ prayuñjīta
tenādhyāpayitā svaprasiddhaṃ vedārthaṃ svavākyenānadhītavedamapi <note n="2">C <dn>svavākyena pratipādayiṣyati ।</dn></note>pratipādayiṣyati ।</p>﻿<pb n="r006"/>
<p>pariharati—<q>prasiddhaścet sutarāṃ evaṅkāmasya vidhānaṃ nopapadyate</q> । arthāvabodha-
kāmasya sutarāmeva vidhānaṃ nopapadyate, yadi hi prasiddho vedārthaḥ । aprasiddhe hi kāmanāyā
anupapattervidhānāsaṃbhavaḥ । prasiddhe tu kāmanābhāvāt prāpte ca phale pravṛttyabhāvāt vidhānāsaṃbhava
iti <q>sutarāmi</q>tyuktam । kasmāt prasiddhe vedārthe vidhānānupapattirityatrāha—<q>jñeyatayaiva hi tat
kāmyate । jñātasya hi jñeyatayā kāmanā nopapadyate ।।</p>
<p>nanu sāmānyena vedārtho jñātaḥ kaścidartho'bhyudayakārī vedasyāstīti, punarviśeṣeṇa
kāmayiṣyate । naitadevam । nahi vedārthaḥ sarvo'bhyudayakārī naimittikaniṣedhādhikāra-
yostadabhāvāt । na ca kaścidasyārtho'stītyetāvanmātramavagamya kāmanopapattiḥ ।
āśaṅkāntaramāha<q>—niyamārtho vidhiriti cet ।</q> asyārthaḥ—svādhyāyenaiva vedārtho
'vaboddhavya iti niyamārtho vidhiḥ tena jñāte'pi puruṣāntaravacanena vedārthe vedādavagantuṃ
kāmanāstīti । dūṣayati<q>—na niyamārtho vidhiḥ</q> । svādhyāyā<q>danyato</q> vedārthasya
<q>parijñānā'saṃbhavāt</q> । puruṣavacanebhyopi dharmaśāstrakalpasūtrasadasyopadeśādibhyo vedamevānumāya
tata eva vedārthapratyayaḥ । anumito'pi ca vedo'rthamavagamayati iti smṛtivicāre nipuṇatara-
mupapādayiṣyāmaḥ । tadevamupāyāntaraprayuktyabhāvānna niyamārtho vidhiḥ ।</p>
<p>nanu ca svādhyāyaśabdena gṛhīto veda ucyate tena saṃbhavati niyamārtho vidhiḥ । agṛhī-
tāvasthasya <note n="1">C <dn>vedasya vyā ।</dn></note>vedasyaiva vyāvartyasya saṃbhavāt, itīmāmāśaṅkāmāha<q>—grahaṇāntataiva svādhyāya-
śabdenocyata iti cet</q> । dūṣayati—<q>kena voktaṃ grahaṇāntaṃ svādhyā</q>yaśabdenocyata iti
niyamavādyāha—<q>agṛhītāttarhyarthajñānamasti</q> tannivṛttyarthaṃ bhavatviti bhāvaḥ । dūṣayati﻿<pb n="r007"/>
<q>nāgṛhītādarthajñānamasti । agrahaṇe varṇamātragrahaṇāt</q>—na ca varṇamātragrahaṇe vākyārtha-
pratītiḥ api tu vākyagrahaṇe, gṛhīteṣu hi sarvapadeṣu<note n="(1)">B <dn>gṛhītvā hi sarvapadāni ।</dn></note> nyāyabalena vacanavyaktiviśeṣamavadhārya
vākyārthapratipattiriti darśitaṃ <q>vākyārthamātṛkāyām ।</q> niyamavādina āśaṅkāmāha—
<q>vākyāvagamāt iti cet,</q> agṛhīte'pi vedevākyārtho'vagamyata iti cet । dūṣayati
—<q>gṛhītaṃ tarhi vākyaṃ</q> vākvārthamavagamayati <q>nāgṛhītaṃ vākyatvenāvagantuṃ śakyate ।</q>
asyārthaḥ-yadyapi kṛtsnā śākhā na gṛhītā tathāpi vākyaṃ tāvadgṛhītam । na hyagṛhītaṃ
vākyatvenāvagamyate । ekaikameva vākyaṃ vākyārthamavagamayati, tena śākhayaiva gṛhītayā
vākyārthoṃ'vagamayitavya iti niyamo na saṃbhavati । śākhāyā anavagamakatvāt vākyamātrasyāva-
bodhakatvāt । tasya ca <note n="(2)">A <dn>gṛhītatvenaiva ।</dn></note>gṛhītasyaiva vācakatvāt agṛhītasyāvācakatvāditi । <q>tasmānna
niyamasyāyaṃ gocaraḥ । nāpyarthajñānakāmasyāyaṃ vidhiḥ,</q> ataḥ pramāṇaṃ vidhyuddeśaḥ
<q>pramāṇaṃ,</q> apramāṇaṃ cārthavādo'<q>pramāṇamastu ।</q></p>
<p>saṃprati paramapūrvapakṣyāha—<q>satyamevaṃ yathoktaṃ pitṛmatā</q> pitṛmāneva hi pituranuśāsane-
nāvagatasamīcīnanyāyamārgaḥ evaṃ vaktuṃ śaknoti iti pitṛmatetyuktam । yattāvadvidhyuddeśasya
prāmāṇya tadeva tu prāmāṇyaṃ <q>akāryārthasaṃbaddhaṃ</q> akāryabhūtena rudrarodanādinā saṃbaddha-
<q>mavagamyate । tataḥ kim</q> ? uttaram । <q>idaṃ tataḥ । akāryārthatā vedasya prāpnoti</q>
arthavādānāmarthamakāryātmakaṃ vedaḥ pratipādayatīti ।</p>
﻿<pb n="r008"/>
<p><q>nanu ca kāryārthatāpyasti</q> vidhyuddeśasya kāryārthatāpratipādakatvāt । tena sidhyatyeva
kārye'rtheṃ vedasya prāmāṇyam । pariharati—<q>na</q> kāryārthatāsti—<q>akāryapūrvakatvāt</q> kāryasya । kathaṃ
tatpūrvakatvamityatrāha—<q>akāryo'rtho hi hetutāṃ pratipadyate kāryārthasya<note n="(1)">B <dn>kāyasyārthasya ।</dn></note> ।</q></p>
<p>asyārthaḥ—arthavādānāmakāryātmako'rtho vidhyuddeśārthasya kāryarūpasya hetutāṃ
pratipadyate; anyena prakāreṇa sambandhānavagamāt । akāryasya pramāṇāntarāpekṣayā siddhiḥ
na śabdataḥ । śabdasya kāryamātre prāmāṇyavyutpatteḥ । na ca tatpramāṇāntaraṃ rudrarodanādiṣvastīti
hetvasiddhyā hetumadasiddheḥ kāryārtho vedo na bhavet । akāryasya kāryaṃ prati hetutayānvaya iti
<q>pradarśitam—rudraḥ kila ruroda । ato'nyenāpi kila roditavyam iti । tasmāt
tatprabhavaṃ</q> hetubhūtasiddhārthaprabhavaṃ hetumati kārye'rthe vedasya <q>prāmāṇyam । tacca pramāṇāntarāpekṣa-
mityanapekṣatvamevākṣipyate ।</q> anapekṣatayā ca kārye'rthe vedasya prāmāṇyamityāyātaṃ kārye'rthe
vedasyā<note n="(2)">A & B <dn>vedasya prāmāṇyaṃ</dn></note>prāmāṇyamiti codanālakṣaṇapratijñākṣepaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>nanu caitat rudraḥ</q> kila ruroda ato'nyenāpi roditavyamiti <q>prāmāṇyasiddhyarmamupanyastaṃ
bhāṣyakāreṇa । kimityanyatraiva</q> hetvapekṣatvenāprāmāṇasiddhābupanīyate । pariharati
﻿<pb n="r009"/>
satyaṃ prāmāṇyasiddhyartha evāyaṃ prakāra upanyastaḥ tathāpi hetubhāvena <q>siddhasya sādhyenaikavākyatā
pradarśyate । tadekavākyatve ca sati kāryatā nāstītyetadeva</q> aprāmāṇyameva <q>pradarśyate</q> ।
yadyarthavādānāṃ vidhyuddeśenaikavākyatāmevāśrityākṣepo'yaṃ <q>kathaṃ tarhyayaṃ granthaḥ</q> ? athocyeta
<q>adhyāhāreṇa vā</q> vipariṇāmena<note n="(1)">C <dn>adhyāhāreṇa veti</dn></note> veti । <q>kiṃ vā asya granthasya</q> ? uttaram—<q>idamasya</q> granthasya
<q>kartavyatānekavākyatvādaprāmāṇyam । na punarakartavyataikavākyatvāditi ।</q> asyārthaḥ—
<note n="(2)">C <dn>granthādevamaba</dn></note>asmādgranthādidamavagamyate-arthavādabhāgasya kevalasya kartavyataikavākyatā nāstītyaprāmāṇyaṃ na
punarvidhyuddeśasyāpi akartavyataikavākyatvenāprāmāṇyamiti । yadi siddhārthānvayena sādhyārthasyāpramāṇya-
mityeṣa pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ tadā kena viśeṣeṇa adhyāhārādinā <note n="(3)">C <dn>kāryānvayau</dn></note> kāryānvayitocyate । yadi tāvatkāryā-
nvayaśūnyatvenāprāmāṇyamāśaṅkyate tadā adhyāhārādinā kāryānvayāśaṅkā yujyate । tasmādbhinna-
﻿<pb n="r010"/>
vākyāśrayaṇenaivātra pūrvapakṣitamiti pariharati—<q>uktamanekavākyatve'cintanīyo'yamarthaḥ</q> <note n="(1)">A <dn>prāmāṇyamiti</dn></note> aprā-
māṇyamiti । <q>atrāpi ca granthe anarthajño bhavān । atredameva</q> kārye'rthe prāmāṇyamevā-
<q>kṣipyate ।</q> kutaḥ prāmāṇyākṣepa ityatrāha—<q>na hi siddhārthānugamāt kartavyatāvasātuṃ
śakyate ।</q></p>
<p>sāmānyenābhidhāya viśeṣaṃ darśayati—<q>yathā asminneva</q> so'rodīdityādau । ekagranthenāha
-kiṃ śakyante rodanādayaḥ kartum</q> ? na śakyanta eveti yāvat । siddhārthahetukāḥ santo rodanādayaḥ
na śakyante kartuṃm । <q>nanvaśakyatayā na śakyante na punaḥ</q> siddhārthahetukatvena । pariharati—
<q>siddhatayaiva hyaśakyatā uktā;</q> na punaḥ svabhāvato'śakyatā । iṣṭaviyogādisampādanenāpi
śakyatvāt । kathaṃ punaḥ siddhārthānugamanāt aśakyatetrāha—<q>siddhasya pramāṇāntarāpekṣa-
tvāt,</q> kāryaikaviṣayatvena śabdasya prāmāṇyavyutpatteḥ <q>tasya</q> ca pramāṇāntarasyātra rudre iṣṭaviyo-
﻿<pb n="r011"/>
viyogādeḥ । tathā ca pramāṇāntarābhāvaṃ darśayati&mdash;<q>na hyātmano vapāmu-
tkhidya tadutthitena tūpareṇa</q> śakyate yāgaḥ kartumiti । tarhyavāntaravākyoṃ-
panyāsaḥ na punarmahāvākya evaitatpradarśitam । <q>avāntara</q>kalpanāyāmapyeta-
smāt siddhānugamānna mucyata iti bhāvaḥ ।</p>
<p>tadidamucyate&mdash;<q>āmnāyasya kriyārthatvādānarthakyamatadarthānā-
miti</q> । kimidamatadarthānāmiti viśeṣābhidhānam । nanu ca sarva evedānī-
matadartho vedaḥ । vasantāya kapiñjalānālabhetiti nāsti siddhānugama iti﻿<pb n="r012"/>
cet, tadevedamāpatitam acintanīyo'yamartha iti । na kapiñjalādivākyā-
nāmapi kāryārthatvam । teṣāmapi siddhārthenaikavākyatvāt, ato'tadarthānā-
miti na nivartyaṃ kiṃcidavasīyate । idamavasīyate । siddhasādhyārthatvādvākyānāṃ
siddhārthamukhenāyamākṣepaḥ ataḥ idamuktaṃ&mdash;ānarthakyamatadarthānāmiti । yathā
ca siddhārthāpekṣitayā''kṣepaḥ tathoditam । vivṛtaṃ ca bhāṣyakāreṇa&mdash;
<quote>“tānyekadeśākṣepeṇākṣipyante”</quote> iti ।</p>﻿<pb n="r013"/>
<p>kathaṃ tarhi rāddhānta ekavākyatāṃ prati praśnottare ? ko'bhiprāyaḥ ।
ayamabhiprāyaḥ । naikavākyatānibandhano'yamākṣepaḥ । bhinnānāṃ hi vākyānāṃ
kā pratipattiriti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।</p>
<p>ānarthakyamabhidhāyaikavākyatayā rāddhānte stutyarthatvenārthavattoktā ।</p>﻿<pb n="r014"/>
<p>aho ajñānakātaryamāyuṣmataḥ pradarśitaṃ tava&mdash;tānyekadeśākṣepeṇākṣi-
pyanta iti । rāddhānte tu praśnottare tatraiva codanīye parihartavye ca ।﻿<pb n="r015"/>
yatpunaridānīṃ ānarthakyamudāharaṇabhedenopanyastaṃ tat <note n="1"><dn>hetupracayārthaṃ-mā</dn></note>hetuprapañcārtham ।
hetuprapañcasya prayojanamuktam । asmiṃstu pracaye ayamaparo viśeṣaḥ pari-
hārāntarapariharaṇīyatvaṃ ca । tasmādanityamucyata iti&mdash;siddhārthāpekṣitayā
pramāṇāntarasavyapekṣatvamanityatvaṃ śabdārthayornityatvāt loke'pi ।﻿<pb n="16"/>
<p>asyārthaḥ-nānityaśabdena sūtroktena kāraṇavattvamucyate, śabdārthayorlokavedayoḥ
sadasatkāraṇatvāt ; kintu pramāṇāntarasavyapekṣatvādanityatvamatrābhipretam । <q>ata eva ca
bhāṣyakāreṇāyamevārtho'nityaśabdasya vivṛtaḥ</q> <quote>yadyapi nityāni tathāpi na nityakāryaṃ
kurvanti</quote> iti granthena । etadeva vivarītumāha—<q>kiṃ punarnityasya kāryaṃ</q> yadakaraṇāda-
nityamucyate । uttaram—<q>pramāṇāntarānapekṣaṃ svārthasya pratipādanaṃ;</q> yat kila nityaṃ tat
pramāṇāntaramanapekṣyaiva svārthaṃ pratipādayet; na hi <note n="(1)">C <dn>nityasyāpekṣāsti ।</dn></note>nityasyāpekṣyo'rtho'sti । ataḥ <q>pramāṇa-
ntarānapekṣataiva nityatocyate । tenāsyā evāyamākṣepaḥ tasmādanityamucyata iti ।</p>﻿<pb n="17"/>
<p><q>vidhinā tvekavākyatvātstutyarthena vidhīnāṃ syuḥ ।</q> vidhyuddeśenaikavākyatvāditi bhā-
ṣyam; tadākṣipatti <q>vidhyuddeśenaikavākyatvāditi kasyedaṃ vyākhyānam ?</q> uttaram—﻿<pb n="18"/>'?;
<q>vidhinetyasya ।</q> nanu vidhinetyasyedaṃ vyākhyānaṃ <q>nopapadyate</q>, yasmāt vidhirvidhyuddeśo na
bhavati; vidhyuddeśo hi <quote>vāyavyaṃ śvetamālabheta bhūtikāmaḥ</quote> ityevamātmakaḥ; vidhistu
liṅgādipratyayamātram । pariharati—<q>satyaṃ''</q> na vidhirvidhyuddeśaḥ; kintu lakṣaṇayā vidhiśabdena
vidhyuddeśa ucyate avayavena samudāyasya lakṣaṇā । <q>kimiti lakṣaṇā ?</q> uttaram—
<q>ekavākyatvāditi vacanāt ।</q> kime<q>vākyatvaṃ vidhinā saha nopapadyate</q>'rthavādānām,
yenānupapattyā lakṣaṇayā pratīyate । <q>vidhinaiva</q> hi <q>sarvasyaikavākyatvam</q> ataḥ śrauta eva
sambandha upapadyate । uttaram—<q>satyaṃ vidhinaiva sarvasyaikavākyatvam</q> ataḥ śrauta eva
yasya kāryārthatvaṃ tasya vidhinaikavākyatvaṃ yathā viṣayaniyojyādipadānām । <q>na ca stuteḥ
kartavyatā'vasīyate ।</q> na ca stutipadāni kāryamarthaṃ pratipādayanti । kiṃ<note n="1.">C <dn>kathaṃ tarhi ।</dn></note> tarhi ? stutipadānāṃ
<q>stutyena</q> vāyvādinā <q>saha sambandho</q> na vidhinā । <q>kiṃ vidhyartho na stutyarhaḥ ?</q> yena
stutyena saha ekavākyatvepi vidhinaikavākyatā nāsti । uttaram—<q>na brūmo</q> vidhyartho
na stutya iti । <q>kṣepiṣṭhādayastu guṇāḥ vidheye stutimutpādayanti । <note n="2.">B <dn>mata eva ।</dn></note>ta evātadarthā-
nāmityākṣiptāḥ ।</q> yeṣāmevārthavādā vidheye stutimutpādayanti vidhyuddeśānāṃ ta evātrākṣiptāḥ ।
<q>ākṣepasamādhānārthaṃ caitatsūtram । tasmāt</q> ākṣiptavidhyuddeśasambandhyarthavādaikavākyatāpradarśana-﻿<pb n="19"/>
paratvāt sūtrasya <q>yuktā lakṣaṇā ।</q> yata eva sākṣādvidhinaikavākyatvaṃ nāsti, <q>ata eva kathameka-
vākyatvamiti praśnaḥ । kimidaṃ pṛṣṭaṃ</q> kathamekavākyatvamityanena ? uttaram—<q>idamidam-</q>
vidhyuddeśenaikavākyatvaṃ na vidhinaikavākyatvam । <q>vidhyuddeśasyaiva</q>, yathā vidhyuddeśasya vidhinaika-
vākyatvaṃ tathā stuternāsti <q>tadanekavākyatvācca na kartavyatāvagamaḥ; akartavyatāvagame ca
nāsti prāmāṇyam</q>, akartavyasyārthasya hetubhāvena sambandhāt । <q>ato'yaṃ praśnaḥ kathameka-

vākyatvamiti । <q>nanu caivaṃ</q> vidhyuddeśenaikavākyatve sati <q>siddhārthatā prāpnoti na kāryārthatā ।
kimidaṃ siddhārthatā na kāryārthateti ?</q> uttaram—<q>uktam na kāryārthatayā pratīyata iti ।</q>

svīkarturupālambhaḥ ubhayasambhave hi laghūpāyaparityāgena gurūpāyaparigrahe svīkartā upālabhyate ।

dupapāditam । vedādevedamavagamyate, vedamavalokya<note n="2.">C <dn>vedamevālocya</dn></note> sārthavādapadasyaiva vidhyuddeśasya upāyatvamava-

na vidhyuddeśamātranimittā, tadāha—<q>nāvāntarānvayanimittā bhavitumarhatīti ।</q> nanu nirapekṣā-

ākṣeptā''ha—<q>nanvayaṃ doṣaḥ, atrāpi</q> sārthavādakavidhyuddeśaprayogepi kevalasya nimittatvaṃ
pratīyamānaṃ <q>na śakyate'pahnotum ।</q> 'bhavatu naivaṃ sati' ityādirāddhāntabhāṣyaṃ vyācaṣṭe—<q>satyaṃ
pratīyamānaṃ na śakyate'pahnotum; na punarapratīyamānamapi । na cātrāvagatidvayamasti
vākyabhedaprasaṅgādityuktam ।</q> asyārthaḥ—yāvanti padāni prayujyante tāvatāṃ sambhūyakāritvaṃ
sthite ca sambhūyakāritve'vāntarāvagatiritthaṃ bhavet । yadi dve vākye syātāṃ ekaṃ kevalaṃ
vidhyuddeśātmakaṃ, aparañca sārthavādakamiti । <quote>atha yaduktaṃ na kriyā'vagamyate, kriyāsambandhaṃ
vā kiñcit iti</quote> bhāṣyam-tat punaruktamiva manvāno vyācaṣṭe—<q>nanu ca kartavyatā stuti-
padāt nāvagamyate; kartavyatāṃ ca vedaḥ pratipādayatītyavedikatvam ।</q> asyārthaḥ yaḥ
<note n="(1)">Page <dn>23.</dn></note>﻿<pb n="26"/>
kāryamarthaṃ pratipādayati sa vedaḥ । stutipadāni tu na kāryamarthaṃ pratipādayanti, ato na
teṣāṃ vaidikatvam । rāddhāntamāha—<q>kena voktaṃ vaidikatvam ? vedasaṃbandhīti vaidikamucyate,—
arthavādapadāni ca svata eva vedarūpatvānna vedasaṃbandhīni । tadāha—<q>veda evāyaṃ na vaidika

kādeva vākyāt kāryāvagatiḥ ityuktam । parihārāntaramāha—<q>prāmāṇyasya</q> cārthavādapadaika-
vākyatvāt <q>ākṣepaḥ kṛtaḥ; sa cāyaṃ pratisamāhitaḥ । kimatra vaidikatvena ?</q> bhavatu vā
vaidikatvaṃ, mā<note n="(2)">B <dn>māvābhūt</dn></note>bhūdvā, sarvathā arthavādapadaikavākyatvenāprāmāṇyaṃ nāstītyetāvannaḥ sādhyam ।
etacca sādhitam । <q>nanvevaṃ sati</q> yasmātkartavyatāvagamyate sa vedaḥ, na tasya vaidikatvamiti,
<q>vidhyuddeśasyāpi tarhi</q> avaidikatvam । <q>tadapi hi pratipattau nimittam ।</q> tena asā-
vapi hi veda eva । pariharati-bāḍhaṃ, kāryapratipattinimittatayā vedatvaṃ na naimittikatayā ।
vidhyuddeśasyāpi sākṣātkāryarūpo'rthaḥ, stutipadānāñca siddharūpaḥ । tena vidhyuddeśasyārtho
naimittikaḥ nimittaprayojanatvāt । tenārthadvāreṇa vidhyuddeśapadāni naimittikāni । tena
ca rūpeṇa vaidikāni, tasyārthasya vedaprameyatvāt । <q>stutipadāni tu stutinimittameṣa
<note n="(1)"> <dn>coktaṃ mū. pā.</dn></note>﻿<pb n="27"/>
<note n="(1)">A <dn>svayameva prameyatvāt</dn></note>svayamaprameyatvāditi viśeṣaḥ । tena stutipadānāṃ vedatvameva । tulyaṃ tu ।। tulyaṃ tu sāṃ-
pradāyikaṃ' iti vyākhyeyānubhāṣaṇaṃ vyākhyātum । nirākāryamāśaṅkate—<q>kadācit kasyācidā-
śaṅkā syāt । vidhyuddeśastutyarthaṃ bālānāṃ pravṛttaye<note n="(2)"> <dn>pratipattaye-ṭī. pā.</dn></note> prakṣiptānyarthavādapadānīti ।</q> saṃprati
sūtrārthaṃ vyācaṣṭe—<q>tadayuktam । 'tulyaṃ ca sāṃpradāyika'miti naiva kaścitprakṣepamarthavāda-
padānāṃ smarati</q> vidhyuddeśapadānāmiva । yathā vidhyuddeśapadānāṃ pauruṣeyatvaṃ na smaryate﻿<pb n="28"/>
tathā'rthavādapadānāmapi । yadi hi smaryeta vidhyuddeśādhyayana ivādhyetṝṇāmādaro na syāt ।
kiñcārthavādapadāni <note n="(1)"> <dn>vidhyuddeśayajñaiḥ saha</dn></note>vidhyuddeśapadaiḥ saha pratipattyanvitābhidhāyīnyapi na bhaveyuḥ tadā'nanvitatvācca
bālonmattādipraṇītāni bhaveyuḥ । na caitadasti, tadāha—<q>avagatyantaraṃ ca nāstītyuktam ।</q>
sārthavādakāt vākyāt sastutikātkāryāvagatiḥ । <q>evaṃ cet rodanānupaprattiḥ parihṛtā ।</q>

doṣāya । <q>pratyuta kāryāvagatāvayaṃ doṣaḥ । na punaḥ siddhārthāvagatau ।</q> kāryatve hi yathā-
śrutārthaparigrahe pramāṇāntaravirodhādiko doṣa., na siddhārthāvaga<note n="(2)">C <dn>siddhāvagatau</dn></note>tau, atatparatvāt ।</p>
<p><q>nanu caivamapi pramāṇamātraparyavasāyiṣu arthavādapadeṣu mṛgyaṃ pramāṇāntaraṃ stutyavagatau ।</q>
asyārthaḥ—stutāvarthavādapadānāmanvaya ityatrāpi pramāṇāntaraṃ mṛgyam । <q>na ca tadasti; yathā
avakā vidhīyante āpaśca stūyante ।</q> tataśca vyādhikaraṇatayā stuteḥ stāvakatayā'nvaya iti
na śakyate vaditum । evañca yadā stutyā'nvayo'vagamyate stutipadānāṃ tadā arudatyarodīditi
śabdaḥ rodanavādī hi gauṇaḥ yadā stutyā'ntayo nāsti tadā mukhya eva rodanavādaḥ । tadā﻿<pb n="29"/>
arudati 'arodīdi'ti pramāṇāntaravirodhādanupapattireva । <q>evaṃ sarvatra stenādiṣu । tasmāt
punarapyanupapattireva । neyamanupapattiḥ vidhyarthenaikavākyatve sati yathā pramāṇāntareṇa
sambandho'vagamyate tathaiva vyāravyeyam ।</q> asyārthaḥ-yābatkiñcitpadajātaṃ śrūyate tasya sarvasya
vidhyanvitārthapratipādakatvam । sārthavādake ca vākye arthavādapadānāmapi vidhiparatvāt
<q>vidhyarthenaikavākyatve siddhe</q> yathaikavākyatvamupapadyate stutyā nindayā gauṇyā lākṣaṇikyā vā
vṛttyā <q>tathā vyākhyeyam । taduktaṃ guṇavādastviti । hetupracayaparihārastu hetuvadevā-
vagantavyaḥ ।</q> yathā hetavo bhāṣyato'vagatāḥ tathā hetupracayaparihāro'pi bhāṣyata evā-
vagantavyaḥ ।</p>﻿<pb n="30"/>﻿<pb n="31"/>﻿<pb n="32"/>﻿<pb n="33"/>﻿<pb n="34"/>
<p><q>vidhirvā syāt ।। uktaṃ bhūtārthānāmarthavādānāṃ kāryārthapratipādakatayā prāmāṇyam । yatra
punaḥ kāryārthataivāvagamyate kāryāntareṇa caikavākyatvaṃ tatra kathaṃ prāmāṇyaṃ ? yathā <quote>audumbaro
yūpo bhavati urgvā udumbara ūrkpaśava ūrjaivāsmā ūrjaṃpaśūnāpnotyūrjo'varuddhyai</quote> iti
yūpaudumbarayorapi sādhyasādhanatā'vagamyate paśū dumbarayorapi</q> 'audumbaro yūpaḥ kartavya
iti ekā kāryāvagatiḥ 'udumbareṇa paśavaḥ kartavyā' ityaparā । <q>gamyate caikavākyatā'
yasmādaudumbareṇa paśavaḥ sādhyante tasmādaudumbaro yūpaḥ kartavya iti ।</q> rāddhāntī pṛcchati
<note n="(1)">C <dn>yapāvyāsyātam</dn></note>﻿<pb n="35"/>
—kimatra yuktam ?</q> pṛcchataścāyamāśayaḥ-ekavākyatvādekaiva kāryāvagatiyukteti । <q>pūrva-
pakṣyāha—sādhyāvagame saṃbhavati na siddhāvagatiryuktā । kasmāt ? vidhyarthatvādvākyasya
vidheśca sādhyā<note n="(1)">C <dn>sādhyatayākāṅkṣitatvā</dn></note>kāṅkṣitvāt । na ca mukhye'rthe saṃbhavati lakṣaṇā yuktā ।</q> asyārthaḥ-yadā
ekavākyatvenaikakāryāvagatiḥ tadā ūrjaivāsmā ūrjaṃ paśūnāpnotīti siddho'rtho'ṅgīkaraṇīyaḥ ।
na ca sādhyārthatve saṃbhavati siddhārthatva yuktam, vidhyarthatvāt sarvasya । vidhinā ca niyojyasiddhyarthaṃ
sādhyatvenaivāsyārthasyāpekṣitatvāt । yattu sādhyaṃ sat niyojyārthaviśeṣaṇaṃ tadvidhereva sādhyam ।
<note n="(2)">B & C <dn>sādhyatvenocyate</dn></note>tenocyate vidhisaṃbandhitayā<note n="(3)">B omits <dn>sādhyatayā</dn></note> sādhyatayā cākāṅkṣitatvāditi । nanu vidhiḥ prāśastyamapi pravṛttyarthama-
pekṣata eva-atrocyate । na mukhye'rtheṃ saṃbhavati lakṣaṇā yuktā । prāśastyaṃ hi na śrutyocyate,
kintu lakṣaṇayā'vagamyate । sādhyasādhanabhāvastu śrutyaiva paśūdumbarayoravagamyate । tasmāt
sādhyatvenaiva paśūdumbarasaṃbandho'bhyupagantuṃ yuktaḥ । rāddhāntī codayati—<q>nanu ca sādhyadvaya-
mekasmin vākye na sambhavati ।</q> pūrvapakṣī pariharati—<q>vayamapyetadeva brūmaḥ</q> sādhyadvaya-
mekasmin vākye kathaṃ saṃbhavatīti । etacca bruvato'vamāśayaḥ-ekavākyatvaṃ cātrāvagamyate
sādhyadvayañca । etacca parasparaviruddham <note n="(4)">B adds <dn>sādhyadvaye</dn></note>sādhyabhede vākyadvayāpatteḥ । na cātra vākya-
bhedo'pyavagantuṃ <note n="(5)">A & B <dn>gamyate</dn></note>śakyate । tasmānnirbījamevārthadvayaṃ pratīyate ।</q> rāddhāntābhāsī codayati﻿<pb n="36"/>﻿<pb n="37"/>
—nanu vānekasminnapi pratipādye'rthe sambhavati sati ekārthatā dṛṣṭā-yathā iyaṃ gauḥ
krayyetyevamādiṣu</q> laukikeṣu vākyeṣu । tena yadyapi yūpodumbarasaṃbandhaḥ paśūdumbarasabandhaśca
dvāvarthau, tathāpyekārthatā atrāpi bhaviṣyati । pūrvapakṣī pariharati—<q>viṣamo'yamupanyāsaḥ tatra hi
loke pramāṇāntarābagatārthavaśāt vākyanirṇayaḥ</q> vākyasya ekatvānekatvābhyāṃ nirṇayaḥ ।
<q>iha tu śabdādevāvagantavyaṃ</q> vākyam । <note n="(1)">A & B <dn>śabdāccāneka</dn></note>śabdārthānekārthatve sati ekavākyatvaṃ na
śakyate'vagantum । ekavākyatve ca nārthadvayam । <q>ataḥ saṃbhavadvidheyānāṃ stutyarthatvena<note n="(2)"> <dn>stutyarthena prāmāṇyaṃ durghaṭaṃ</dn></note>
prāmāṇyaṃ durlabham ।</p>
<p>atrocyate—<q>uktantu vākyaśeṣatvam,</q> uktaṃ tāvadvākyaśeṣatvamarthavādapadānām । pūrvapakṣī
āha—<q>satyamuktaṃ tattu nopapadyate, dvayoḥ sādhyatvenāvagamādityetadapyuktam ।</q>
rāddhāntī vadati—kimidaṃ pūvāparaviruddhaṃ <q>pralapyate—</q> 'ekavākyatvaṃ sādhyadvayaṃ ceti﻿<pb n="38"/>
na hi dvayoḥ <q>sādhyayoḥ guṇayoriva samatvāt saṃbandhaḥ</q> yathā guṇayordvayoḥ parasparaṃ
sambandho na bhavati tathā sādhyayorapi dvayoḥ । yadi sādhyayordvayorapi paraspara-
sambandho na bhavati <q>kathaṃ tarhyekārthāvagatiḥ ?</q> parasparasambandhe hi sati ekārthatvaṃ
sambhavati । asati tu saṃbandhe kathamekārthāvagatiḥ । rāddhāntyāha—<q>yadyekārthāvagatiḥ
tadanurūpaṃ nimittaṃ parikalpya eko'rthaḥ siddharūpo'bhyupagamyatām । aparaśca sādhyarūpaḥ
yena parasparasambandhe sati ekārthāvagatirupapadyate । pūrvapakṣyāha—<q>nanu ca sādhyadvayaṃ
pratīyate;</q> tena na śakyate ekaḥ <note n="(1)">B <dn>siddho'rtho</dn></note>siddharūpo'vagantum । rāddhāntī pariharati-
yadi sādhyadvayaṃ pratīyena <q>na tarhyekārthāvagatiḥ parasparāsambandhāt । pūrvapakṣyāha﻿<pb n="39"/>
—<q>asti ceyaṃ</q> kāryāvagatiḥ <q>yasmādanenedaṃ bhavati tasmādidaṃ kuryā<note n="(1)">C <dn>kurviti</dn></note>diti ।</q>
yasmādaudumbareṇa yūpena paśavo bhavanti tasmādaudumbaraṃ yūpaṃ kuryāditi । rāddhāntī
vadati - yadyanena prakāreṇaikārthāvagatiḥ <q>siddhaṃ tarhi bhavatītyasyārthasya siddhārthatvam ।</q>
[<note n="(2)">C <dn>omits this</dn></note>yasmādanenedaṃ bhavatītyasya siddhārthatvaṃ siddhaṃ anyathā hyekavākyatāpratīti-
virodhāditi । ] atra codayati—<q>kathaṃ tarhi siddhasya bhavatīti vyapadeśaḥ ?</q> siddhaṃ hi
bhūtamucyate । yacca bhūtaṃ na tan bhavatīti vyapadeṣṭuṃ śakyate<note n="(3)">C <dn>yuktam</dn></note> । pariharati
—<q>pramāṇasiddhiratropayujyate nārthasiddhiḥ</q> siddhiśabdena avagatiḥ niṣpattiścocyate ।
tatrāvagatirūpā siddhiḥ pramāṇasiddhiḥ । <q>pramāṇasiddhiratropayujyate</q> na niṣpattirūpā
siddhiḥ । <q>siddhamasiddhaṃ vā niṣpannamaniṣpannaṃ vā pramāṇāntarapratītaṃ arthāntarāvagatau
nimittatāṃ pratipadyate ।</q> yatkhalu pramāṇāntarapratītaṃ na tat śabdena pratipādyam । kiṃ
tarhi anyārthapratipattyarthaṃ sattasya pratītasyaivānuvādaḥ । tasminnapratipanne tadviśiṣṭasyaitasya
pratyetumaśakteḥ । tasmādekārthatvāt siddhaṃ prāmāṇyamatrāpi ।</p>﻿<pb n="40"/>
<head>vidhiścānarthakaḥ kvacit ।।</head>
<p><q>nanu ca vidhyasaṃbhavādevādhastye'dhikaraṇe pramāṇaparyavasāyitvamuktaṃ arthavāda-
padānāṃ, iha tu prameyatāpyastītyāśaṅkitam, nirastaṃ ca । kimidamucyate vidhiścānarthaka
iti ?</q> iha vidhivannigadā arthavādā udāharaṇam । teṣu ca vidherarthavattvaṃ saṃbhavatyeva
tena vidhyānarthakyena teṣu stutyarthatvaṃ na śakyate vaktum । ākṣepāntaramāha—<q>kva vā vidhe-
rarthavattve saṃbhavati kevalapramāṇataivoktā yenedamucyate vidhiścānarthakaḥ kvaciditi ?</q>
yadi hi vidherarthavattve saṃbhavatyāpi kevalapramāṇataivoktā syāt kvacit tadaivaṃ yujyate vaktuṃ
vidhiścānarthakaḥ kvaciditi । na caitadasti tasmāt kvacicchabdo na yuktaḥ । aparamapyākṣepa-
māha—<q>tatsāmānyāditi ca kimidaṃ tatsāmānyaṃ ? vidhisaṃbhava evātra darśitaḥ
nāsaṃbhavaḥ ।</q> yadi hi vidhyasaṃbhavo'tra bhavet tadāpi vidhyasaṃbhava eva sāmānyaṃ syāt ।
atra ca vidhisaṃbhava eva darśitaḥ । samarthayamāna āha—<q>ayathārthagrāhiṇa idaṃ codyam ।﻿<pb n="41"/>
atra hi sādhyadvayamupanyasyatā vidheyasya stutyarthatā nāvagamyata ityuktam ।</q> paśūduṃbara
saṃbandho hi sādhyaḥ, sa ca vidheyasya yūpoduṃbarasaṃbandhasya stutyarthatvena nāvagamyata ityuktam ।
<q>yatra ca vidheyāsaṃbandhā stutiravagamyate ।</q> yathā vetase vidheye 'āpaśśāntā' iti,
<q>na tatra stutyartheneti śakyate vaktuṃ tadidamucyate vidhiścānarthakaḥ kvaciditi । na hi
vetase vidheye āpaśśāntā iti stutirupapadyate । na cāpsu jāyanta iti vidhissaṃ-
bhavati, tathāpyekārthāvagaternimittatvaṃ parikalpyate evamatrāpi bhavitumarhatīti । idaṃ
tatsāmānyam ।</q> asyārthaḥ-yathā vetase vidheye 'āpaśśāntā' iti yadyapi 1vispaṣṭā stutirnāva-
gamyate tathāpi vidhāvasaṃbhavati ekavākyatvena stutyanvayarūpaṃ nimittamāśritya stutitvaṃ parikalpyate
<note n="(1)">B. <dn>viśiṣṭā</dn></note>﻿<pb n="42"/>
tathā'trāpyāpātamātreṇa sādhyadvayāvagamanena yadyapi vidhemastutirnāvagamyate, tathāpi ekavākyatvena
vidhyantarāsaṃbhavādekavākyatvānurūpaṃ nimittaṃ parikalpayituṃ yuktamiti । prakaraṇe ca saṃbhavanniti
sūtram । tadākṣipati—<q>kimidamanenopanyastam ?</q> samādhatte—<q>idamanenopanyastam । eka-
vidhyarthatve saṃbhavati nānekabidhyarthatā yuktā kalpayituṃ viniyojakavirodhāt ।</q> asyārthaḥ
darśapūrṇamāsaprakaraṇe hi yāvatkiñcitsamāmnāyate tattadadhikāraniyogaparigṛhītam । parigṛhya ca
svātmani viniyuktam । tatra yadi 'yo vidagdhaḥ sa nairṛta' iti vidhiḥ syāt tadā<note n="(1)">C. <dn>tataḥ</dn></note> darśapūrṇamāsa-
prakaraṇādutkṛṣyeta । tadutkarṣe cādhikāravidherniyojakasya virodhaḥ । nanu ca viniyogānu-﻿<pb n="43"/>
sāritvādgrāhakasya viniyogasya ca bhinnavidhipratipattisamarthatvāt <quote>yo vidagdhaḥ sa nairṛta</quote>
ityevamādīnāṃ darśapūrṇamāsādhikāragṛhītatvameva nāsti kathaṃ viniyojakavirodhaḥ ityatrāha<q>—
viniyogamātrāpekṣī viniyojakaḥ, sa na śakyate viniyogabhedādanyathākartuṃ, tadanyathātve
pauruṣeyī kalpanā prāpnoti ।</q> asyārthaḥ—viniyogamātramapekṣya viniyojakaḥ svaviniyojyaṃ
viniyuṅkte, na punarniyogaviśeṣamapekṣate । tatra yadi prakṛtaniyogaṃsambandhe anvayavirodha eva
syāt tadā viniyogāntaragṛhītatvameva bhavet dvādaśopasattāvat । iha tu prakṛtaniyoga-
saṃbandhepi naivānvayavirodhaḥ, stutyarthatvenāpyanvayopapatteḥ । <q>kiñca vidhyantaratvepi vākyabhedaḥ
prāpnoti ।</q> pūrvapakṣī pṛcchati—<q>kiṃ jātaṃ ?</q> yadi vākyabhedo bhavati । uttaraṃ—<q>ekārthā-
vagaterbādho</q> jātaḥ । pūrvapakṣyāha—<q>bādhyatām ।</q> ekārthāvagatiḥ । rāddhāntyāha—<q>na niyogo
viniyogaṃ bādhitumarhati । kāryato hi bādhaṃ bādhavido manyante ।</q> yadi hi sarvasya
sākṣānniyogārthatvaṃ bhavatītyanayā yuktyā vidhibhedo'ṅgīkriyate tadā niyogena viniyogo bādhitavyaḥ ।
viniyogata<note n="(1)">A. <dn>niyoga</dn></note> eva vidhyavagamāt । na ca niyogo viniyogaṃ bādhitumarhati । yathāviniyogaṃ
niyoga iti pratipadādhikaraṇe <note n="(2)">C. <dn>sthitatvāt</dn></note>pratipāditatvāt । nanu ca viniyogo'pi tatra <note n="(3)">A. <dn>bādhitavyaḥ</dn></note>tatra
bādhyata eva avaghātādīnāmiva kṛṣṇaleṣviti । ucyate—<q>tatra kāryato bādhaṃ bādhavido
manyante ।</q> ye hi aupacārikaṃ bādhaṃ vadanti na te kāryato biniyogasya bādhaṃ varṇayanti ।﻿<pb n="44"/>
bādhakāryamananuṣṭhānamastīti bādha iti vyapadeśaḥ । etacca daśamādye prakaṭayipyāmaḥ । <q>tasmādvastutaḥ
sādhyadvayāvagamepi</q> ca yadyapyarthasiddhayā bhavatītyartho na siddhaḥ tena sādhyadvayamavagamyate,
tathāpi <q>pramāṇataḥ siddhasādhyatayaiva hi ekārthāvagatiriti hetoḥ siddhamevaṃbidheṣvapi
prāmāṇyam ।</p>
<p><q>heturvā syāt । kā punaratrāprāmāṇyaśaṅkā ?</q> yannirākaraṇāya <note n="(1)">C. <dn>pramāṇe'rthelakṣaṇamidaṃ</dn></note>pramāṇalakṣaṇe idamadhikaraṇamāra-
bhyate । ekagranthenāha—<q>yadi hetvarthaḥ karaṇaṃ</q> hetvartho'nnasādhanatvaṃ,<note n="(2)">B. & C. <dn>sādhanaṃ</dn></note> yadi tatkaraṇaṃ yena yenānnaṃ
kriyate tena tena homaḥ kartavya iti । tathā <q>yadi śūrpārthaḥ karaṇaṃ,</q> śūrpeṇa homaḥ kartavya iti
<q>ubhayathāpi anvitapadārthako vākyārthaḥ ।</q> tathāpi kimityaprāmāṇyaṃ na bhavatītyatrāha—﻿<pb n="45"/>
<q>ananvayini hi padārthe nimittatayā naimittikatayā vā pratibhāmātraṃ tataścāprāmāṇyaṃ na 
tvanvayini ।</q> dvividho hi padārthānāmanvayaḥ yathā <quote>vāyurvau kṣepiṣṭhā devatā</quote> ityevamādīnāṃ
kevalaṃ nimittatvenaiva, tathā naimittikatvenaiva vidhyuddeśapadārthānāmiva । tatra nimittatayā
naimittikatayā vā ekasmin padārthe ananvīyamāne itarapadārthānvayapratītirapi na śābdī kintu
pratibhāmātrameva padānāṃ saṃbhūyakāritvasya sthitatvāt sakalapadārthānvaye tu prāmāṇyameva tatra । <quote>tena
hyannaṃ kriyate</quote> ityetasminnanvīyamāne ubhayathāpi prāmāṇyameva । <q>tasmāt pramāṇalakṣaṇāntaḥ
pātitā kathamaptyādhikaraṇasya ? na cārthāntaraṃ cintayituṃ yuktam prasaṅgābhāvāt
anaupoddhātikatvācca । nanu cāyamasti prasaṅgaḥ kimarthavādo neti ।</q> pūrvaṃ hi prāmāṇya-
siddhyarthaṃ arthavādatoditā tatprasaṅgenedaṃ cintyate । ākṣeptā''ha<q>—satyamasti prasaṅgaḥ
niṣprayojanastu saḥ । nanu cedamasti prayojanaṃ arthavādatve śūrpeṇaiva homaḥ</q> kartavyaḥ﻿<pb n="46"/>
<q>itarathā'niyama iti ।</q> ākṣeptā''ha—<q>satyamastīdaṃ prayojanaṃ, tārtīyantvetat</q> viniyoga-
viśeṣarūpatvāt । <q>na ca lakṣaṇāntaraprayuktaṃ prāsaṅgikaṃ bhavitumarhati</q> sākṣātsaṅgatisaṃbhave
prasaṅgataścintānupapatteḥ । <q>cintitaṃ caitat</q> viniyogaviśeṣāpādakaṃ arthavādatvaṃ nivītaṃ manuṣyāṇā-
<q>mityevamādiṣu</q> tṛtīya eva । tadvadidamapi tatraiva cintayituṃ yuktam । <q>tasmātpramāṇalakṣaṇāntaḥ
pātitaivāsya vaktavyā;</q> na punaḥ prāsaṅgikatvam । samarthayate—<q>seyaṃ</q> pramāṇalakṣaṇāntaḥ pātitā
<q>ucyate । hetupakṣe hi tannimittaṃ karaṇatvaṃ</q> annasādhanatvanimittaṃ homaṃ prati karaṇatvaṃ vijñāyate
tu vedāt । tenānnasādhanatvasya homakaraṇatvaṃ prati hetubhāve pramāṇāntaramapekṣaṇīyam । na
ca tadasti yadyadannakaraṇaṃ tena tena homaḥ kartavya ityatrāṃśe pramāṇābhāvāt । rāddhāntyāha—
<q>yadi vedādvijñāyate siddhaṃ tarhi vaidikatvam ।</q> vedādevāvagateḥ । pūrvapakṣyāha—<q>satyaṃ vaidikatvaṃ
siddhaṃ sāpekṣatā <note n="(1)">C. <dn>sāpekṣaṃ tu</dn></note>tu । sāpekṣatve ca pramāṇāntaraṃ mṛgyaṃ na ca tadasti iti prati-
bhāmātram ।</q> granthakāra āha—<q>tasmāddhetutvamidānīṃ</q> pūrvapakṣāvasthāyāmaprāmāṇyasiddhyarthaṃ
<q>pratipādyate heturayaṃ</q> annakaraṇatvarūpaḥ śūrpasya homakaraṇatve <q>kāryatvenānvayasaṃbhavāt na
pramāṇamātraparyavasāyitā</q> arthavādamātratā <q>śakyate vaktuṃ kāryārthatvādanvayasya ।</q> nanu ca﻿<pb n="47"/>
śūrpasyānnakaraṇatā na saṃbhavati <q>asādhakatamatvāt ।</q> annaniṣpattau vyavahitavyāpāratvāt
<q>vyāpṛtasya cānyatrākāraṇatvāt ।</q> 'tena hyannaṃ kriyate' iti annaniṣpattau vartamānavyāpāraṃ
karaṇaṃ pratīyate । na ca tathāvidhasya homaṃ prati karaṇatā saṃbhavati ।</p>
<p>pariharati—<q>upapadyate hi karaṇatvamāpekṣikatayā ।</q> sādhakatamaṃ hi karaṇaṃ । tacca
sādhakatamaṃ yatprakṛṣṭaṃ kāryasādhakaṃ, prakarṣaścāpekṣikaḥ । kathamāpekṣika ityāha—<q>āpekṣikī hi
vivakṣā vivakṣātaśca kārakāṇi saṃbhavantīti kārakajñāḥ ।</q> yadā bāhyamaparamapekṣya śūrpasya
prakarṣo vivakṣyate tadā yujyate eva karaṇatvanirdeśaḥ । <note n="(1)">C. <dn>vartamānakālatāpyāpekṣikyeveti</dn></note><q>vartamānakālo'pyāpekṣika evetyuktaṃ
kālajñaiḥ</q> । paramārthato hi bhūtabhaviṣyantāveva kālau pratyāsannatayā vartamānavyavahāraḥ pratyā
sattiścāpekṣikī । <q>tasmādupapanno'yamathoṃ'rthavattvopapattibhyāmiti । avaśyaṃ cāpekṣikaḥ
karaṇabhāvo grahītavyaḥ । stutāvapi tulyatvāt ।</q> siddhāntepi hi annakaraṇatvenaiva
stutiḥ ।</p>
<p><q>stutistu । atrocyate; nāyaṃ hetuḥ । kasmāt ?</q> uttaraṃ—<q>śūrpahome hi hetuḥ
pratīyate</q> śūrpeṇa homaḥ kartavya ityetasminnarthe annakaraṇatvaṃ hetuḥ pratīyate । <q>siddhaśca﻿<pb n="48"/>
hetuḥ na sādhyatayā'vagantuṃ śakyate ।</q> na ca yena yenānnaṃ kriyate tena tena homaḥ kartavya
iti siddho'yamarthaḥ tasmādasiddhatvānnāyaṃ hetuḥ । yuktyantaraṃ cāha—<q>homasya ca sādhyā-
vagatirvedāt ।</q> śūrpeṇa homaḥ kartavyaḥ sādhya iti vedādayamartho'vagamyate । <q>na ca
vedāt sādhyatvenāvagamyamāno'rthaḥ</q> hetuṃ prati <q>sāpekṣo bhavati ।</q> veda eva hi tatra pramāṇa-
miti na pramāṇabhūtaṃ hetvantaramapekṣate । <q>tasmāddhetuvadevāyaṃ na hetuḥ ।</q> evañca kṛtvā
<note n="(1)">B. <dn>vartamānopyavartamānatayā</dn></note>avartamāno'pi <q>vartamānatayā śakyate pratipattuṃ</q>—tena hyannaṃ kriyate iti । yo'yamannakaraṇe
śūrpasya vartamāna iva vyāpāraḥ pratīyate so'vartamāno'pi vartamānatayā śakyate'vagantuṃ pramāṇānta-
rānusāritvāt stutyarthasya । home ca karaṇasya sataḥ śūrpasyānnakaraṇe pramāṇāntareṇa vartamānavyā-﻿<pb n="49"/>
pārānupalabdheḥ । <q>nanu vartamāna eva nāstītyuktaṃ tena</q> kimityavartamānepi vartamānavya-
padeśo'yamucyate, yāvatā sarvatraivameva vartamānavyapadeśaḥ । pariharati—<q>kena voktaṃ sarvatra</q><note n="(1)">B. reads <dn>sarvajñaḥ</dn></note>
pāramārthikaṃ vartamānaṃ ca nāstīti । yāvatā <q>phalaparyanta ārambho vartamānavyapadeśaṃ</q>
labhata iti <q>sthitam ।</q> upakramaprabhṛti samīhitaphalaniṣpattiparyanto vyāpārakṣaṇasantānaḥ eka-
phalavaśīkṛtaḥ<note n="(2)">B. omits <dn>eka eva</dn></note> eka eva san ākhyātaśabdābhidheyaḥ yadārabhyāparisamāpya[pta]tayāvagamyate
tadā mukhyavartamānavyapadeśaṃ labhata iti sthitam । tasmādasti pāramārthikaṃ vartamānavyapadeśatvaṃ
anyatra । iha tu gauṇaṃ tadāśrīyate । <q>na punarvidhipakṣa etadupapadyate</q> gauṇavartamānatvā-
śrayaṇam । <q>na hyarthāntare prayogaśśakyate nirūpayituṃ</q> avartamāne vartamānavyapadeśo'yamiti
vidhipakṣe na śakyate nirūpayitum । vidheyaṃ hi śabdato yathābhūtamavagamyate tathābhūtameva
tadāśrayituṃ śakyate । <q>āpekṣikatvañca karaṇasya madīya eva pakṣe</q> stutyarthamannakaraṇatva-
saṅkīrtanaṃ ityetasminneva <q>śakyate nirūpayitum ।</q> hetuvidhipakṣe punarannakriyāntaratā <q>kena
vāryate ।</q> annakriyāyāṃ yadeva vyavahitaṃ tadeva karaṇatvena gṛhyata ityarthaḥ ।</p>﻿<pb n="50"/>
<p><q>śūrpaśabdāditi cet ।</q> asyārthaḥ—śūrpeṇa homaḥ kartavya iti vidhīyate tena hyannaṃ
kriyate iti nirdeśāt yādṛśaṃ śūrpasya karaṇatvaṃ tādṛśamāśrīyata iti kriyā(na)ntaratā nivāryata
iti cet <q>nivṛttāstarhi darvīpiṭharādayaḥ</q> yadi śūrpanirdeśaḥ tvayā'ṅgīkṛtaḥ tadā darvīpiṭharādīnāṃ
nivṛttaṃ homaṃ prati karaṇatvaṃ, <q>vyāhataśca hetvartho bhavati</q> hetunirdeśārthatvena hi hetvartho
gṛhītaḥ yadi darvīpiṭharādibhirapi homaḥ kriyeta tadā arthavattā hetunirdeśasya । nivṛtteṣu tu
darvīpiṭharādiṣu kiṃ hetvarthena yata eva yathokto'yamarthaḥ prāmāṇikaḥ <q>ata eva cedamuktam ।
yadi heturavatiṣṭheta nirdeśācchūrpa eveti । hetvavyāghāta iti cet ।</q> asyārthaḥ—sākṣātparaṃ-
parayā vā yasya sādhakatvaṃ tasyāpi karaṇatvam । tena darvīpiṭharādīnāmapi annakaraṇatvātteṣvapi
hetvavyāghāta iti cet । <q>avyavasthā tarhi ।</q> sarveṇaiva hi sākṣātparamparayā vā annaṃ kartuṃ
śakyate । tataścānnakaraṇena homaḥ kartavya ityucyamāne yena kenaciddhomaḥ kartavyaḥ ityuktaṃ
bhaveta ityavyavasthā । avyavasthāyāmapi sa eva hetutvavyāghāto nivartyasyābhāvāt anna-﻿<pb n="r051"/>
karaṇena homaḥ kartavyo nānyeneti । yadi vyavasthitaṃ kiñcidan‍nakaraṇaṃ bhavettadā viśeṣavidhānāt
niyamārthatayā vidhānamarthavat bhavet । na ca vyavasthitaṃ kiñcidan‍nakaraṇaṃ; tena nivartyābhāvāda-
narthako'yamupadeśaḥ arthavattvena ca hetupakṣāśrayaṇam । anarthakatve ca hetutvavyāghātaḥ । <q>nanu an‍na-</q>
kriyāyāṃ kathaṃ sarvasya karaṇatvaṃ, na hi kṛtasya karaṇatvamupapadyate yenaikenāpi kṛte'nyadapi
karaṇaṃ bhavetū । <note n="(1)"> A. & B. <dn>ajñāpye</dn></note>jñāpye hi yāvadanekamapi jñāpakaṃ bhaveta ekenāpi jñāpite aparasyāpi
jñāpakatvāghātādityāśaṅkayāha-kārakasya ca hetornivartyābhāvepi ātmalābho jñāpakasyeva ।
asyārthaḥ&mdash;yathā jñāpakahetornivartyābhāvepi ātmalābho bhavati jñāpitasyāpi jñāpanopapatteḥ
tathā kārakasyāpi yadyapyekena kṛte'parasya kārakatvaṃ nopapadyate tathāpyekasmin kārye sākṣātparaṃ-
parayā vā vahūnāmapi kārakatvaṃ ghaṭata eveti tena kārakāntaramanivartyāpi kārakatvamupapadyate
ityannakriyāyāṃ sarvasya <note n="3"> B. <dn>karaṇatvaṃ</dn></note>kārakatvam ।</p>
<p>kecit‍tu nivartyābhāvepyātmalābho bhavati jñāpitasyāpi jñāpanopapattita iti paṭhanti tatra
pūrvok‍to vyāghātaśabdo vipariṇāmena yojanīyaḥ kārakasya ca hetornivartyābhāvepi ātmalābho na
vyāhanyeta jñāpakasyevetyarthaḥ । <q>tasmāddhetuvannigadānāmapi pramāṇatayaivāvasthānam ।</q></p>
<note n="2"> B. & C. <dn>matirekatyaṃ</dn></note>
﻿<pb n="r052"/>
<p><q>tadarthaśāstrāt । yaduk‍taṃ dṛṣṭo hi tasyārthaḥ karmāvavodhanaṃ nāmeti tadayuk‍tam । aviva
kṣitārthatvaṃ svādhyāyasya mantreṣu dṛśyate ।</q> yat svādhyāyasya vivakṣitārthatvamuvataṃ tadayuk‍taṃ
mantrāṇāmavivakṣitārthatvasya darśanāt । <q>kathamavivakṣitārthatvam ?</q> uttaram&mdash;<q>tadartha-
śāstrādibhiḥ ।</q> vivakṣitārthatve mantrāṇāṃ tadarthaśāstramanarthakaṃ liṅgādeva viniyogasiddheḥ । tathā
agnīdagnīn vihareti buddhe'rthe'rthāvabodhanārthaṃ vivakṣitārthatve mantraviniyogo nopapadyate । arthavi-
pratiṣedhaśca vivakṣitārthatve sati bhavati aditirdyauraditirantarikṣamiti । pūrvapakṣamākṣipati&mdash;<q>nanu
cāvivakṣitārthatve tadarthaśāstrādayo'pi avivakṣitārthā eva ।</q> tadarthaśāstrādīnāṃ vivakṣi-
tārthatvena yathā mantrāṇāmavivakṣitārthatvaṃ tathā mantrāṇāṃ vivakṣitārthatvena tadarthaśāstrādīnāmapi﻿<pb n="r053"/>
avivakṣitārthatvaṃ kimiti na syāt tulyatvāt । pūrvapakṣī samarthayate&mdash;<q>omityucyate</q> aṅgīkriyata
eva tadarthaśāstrādīnāmapyavivakṣitārthatvam । yadi tadarthaśāstrādayo'pyavivakṣitārthāḥ <q>kathaṃ tarhi
tairavivakṣitārthatvaṃ mantrāṇām ।</q> uttaramāha&mdash;<q>parasparavyādhātādasaṃbandhārthataivāvivakṣāhetuḥ ।
yadi mantrā aghivakṣitārthāḥ tadarthaśāstrādayopyavivakṣitārthāḥ</q> vivakṣitārtheṣu mantreṣu
tadarthaśāsnāṇāmavivakṣitārthatvaṃ tadarthaśās‍treṣu vivakṣitārtheṣu mantrāṇāmavivakṣitārthatvamiti
<q>parasparavyāghātaḥ ।</q> parasparavyāghātāccāsambaddhārthataiva । asambaddhārthatvena ca avivakṣitārthatvaṃ
seyamasaṃbaddhārthatā tadarthaśāstrādibhirdarśitā । etadeva vivṛṇoti&mdash;<q>raśanābhidhānavivakṣāyāṃ</q>﻿<pb n="r054"/>
mantreṇa raśanābhidhāne vivakṣite <q><quote>‘aśvābhidhānīmādatte’</quote> ityasya tadarthaśāstrasya vyāghātaḥ ।</q>
asya vivakṣitārthatve mantrārthasya vyāghātaḥ । <q>na ca parisaṅkhayādibhiḥ śakyate vyāghātaḥ
parihartumiti pradarśitam ।</q> tadevamavivakṣitārthatve mantratadarthaśāsnāṇāṃ tadekavākyatāpannaṃ﻿<pb n="r055"/>﻿<pb n="r056"/>﻿<pb n="r057"/>
sarvameva prayogaśāstramapramāṇamāpatitamityavivakṣitārthaḥ svādhyāyaḥ । aviśipṭaśtu ।। <q>atrā-
bhidhīyate । nāvivakṣitārthaḥ svādhyāyaḥ niyogasaṃbandhitayā svādhyāyasyārthavattā uktā,
kārye prāmāṇyābhidhānāt ।</q> kārye'rthe vedaḥ pramāṇamityabhidadhatā sutrakāreṇa niyogaprati-
pādakatayā svādhyāyasyārthavattok‍tā । tathā prayoge ca kāryābhidhānatayā yenāpi prayogāvasthāyāṃ﻿<pb n="r058"/>
kāryamamidhīyate tasyāpyarthavattā । <q>kimidaṃ prayoga iti ? uttaraṃ&mdash;anuṣṭhānaṃ ityarthaḥ ।</q> nanu
anuṣṭhīyamānārthapratipādakatayāpi vivakṣitārthatvaṃ tadarthaśāstrādibhirvihataṃ ityatrāha&mdash;<q>anuṣṭhīyamā-
mānārthaupayikatayā vivakṣitārthatvamavagamyamānaṃ tadarthaśāstrādibhirvihantuṃ na śakyate
prāptārthānuvādakānyapi hi vākyāni dṛśyante <quote>‘ya evaṃ vidvān paurṇamāsīṃ yajate﻿<pb n="r059"/>﻿<pb n="r060"/>﻿<pb n="r061"/>﻿<pb n="r062"/>
ityevamādīni ।</q> nanu yāvadeva laukiko mantrasya viniyogo na bhavati tāvadeva kimiti śīghratayā
tadarśaśāstrameva viniyojakaṃ na bhavati yena tasyānuvādatvamucyate । atra brūmaḥ । mantraśak‍ti-
nirūpaṇenaiva tadarthaśāstrādimirapi viniyogaḥ kāryaḥ nānyathā tataśca laiṅgika evātra prathamaṃ
viniyogaḥ । tenānuvādakatvenāpi parihāro nyāyyaḥ । etacca tadarthaśāstrādīnāmarthāntarābhāva-
mabhyupagamyok‍tam । <q>na caitānyanarthakānīti darśitaṃ guṇavidhānādibhirviśeṣaiḥ । evaṃ
pratisūtraṃ draṣṭavyam ।</q></p>
﻿<pb n="r063"/>
<p><q>asya cārthasya vivakṣitārthā mantrā ityasya nyāyyatvaṃ vaidikānyeva liṅgadarśanānyupo-
dvalayanti’</quote> āgreyyā āgnodhramupatiṣṭhate’</quote> ityevamādīni ।</q></p>

dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>
﻿<pb n="r064"/>
<head>tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ ।।</head>
<p><q>dharmasya śabdamūlatvāt&mdash;kimidamaprastutaṃ cintyate ।</q> samādhātā pṛcchati&mdash;<q>kima-
prastutam ?</q> uttaram&mdash;<note n="(1)"> C. <dn>codanārthaḥ</dn></note><q>acodanārthavicāraḥ ।</q> aṣṭakādismṛtivicāro hi vispaṣṭa
evācodanārthavicāraḥ । <q>vravīti ca sūtrakāraḥ dharmasya śabdamūlatvādaśabdamanapekṣaṃ
syāditi ।</q> nanu bravītyeva<note n="(2)"> B. & C. read <dn>bravītyevaṃ</dn></note> sūtrakāraḥ tathāpi kimityatrāha&mdash;aśabda<note n="(3)"> B. & C. <dn>aśabdaṃ</dn></note><q>ścenna pratijñātam ।</q>
aṣṭakā kartavyetyevamādikaṃ yadyaśabdaṃ na tarhi tadvicāryatvena<note n="(4)"> B. & C. <dn>viṣayatvena</dn></note> pratijñātam । <q>apratijñātārtha-
cintā ca pratijñāṃ vihanti ।</q> yadyaśabdamapyatra cintanīyaṃ tadā śabdaikagamyacintā-
pratijñā nopapadyate<note n="(5)"> A <dn>notpadyate</dn></note> । atha śabdaikagamyacintaiva pratijñātā na tarhi aśabdaṃ cintanīyam ।
so'yaṃ pūrvāparavyāghātaḥ sūtrakārasyābuddhipūrvakāritayā prāpnoti । tadāha&mdash;<q>pūrvāparavirodhaścā-</q><note n="(6)"> B. <dn>vighātaśca</dn></note>
﻿<pb n="r065"/>
buddhipūrvakāritayā prāpnoti iti । athāyamabhiprāyaḥ&mdash;idamapi vedavidbhiḥ pramāṇatayā
parigṛhītaṃ, tasmādidamapi vicāraṇīyamiti; tadidamayuk‍taṃ pratyakṣādyapi taiḥ pramāṇatayā
parigṛhītameva tadapi vicāraṇīyaṃ prāpnoti</q> na ca tadvicāritam । tenātiprasaṅgadoṣāt
smṛtivicāro'pi na yuk‍taḥ । <q>nanu vicāritaṃ tat</q> pratyakṣādi । ākṣeptā pṛcchati&mdash;
<q>kva vicāritam ?</q> samādhātaikadeśyuttaramāha&mdash;<q>satsaṃprayoge puruṣasyendriyāṇāmityatra ।</q>
ākṣeptā pṛcchati&mdash;kiṃ <q>pratyakṣaṃ pramāṇamapramāṇamityasya saṃśayasya nirṇayāyaitatsūtram ?</q>
yadi hi pratyakṣaṃ pramāṇamāhosvidapramāṇamityetatsaṃśayanirākaraṇārtha sūtraṃ syāt tadā pratyakṣādi
tatra vicāritaṃ bhavet nānyatheti bhāvaḥ । ṛjvāśayaḥ<note n="(1)"> B. & C. <dn>śuddhāśayaḥ</dn></note> samādhātaikadeśyāha-nāsya saṃśayasya
nirṇayāya tatsūtraṃ; kiṃ tarhi <q>dharma prati</q> pratyakṣādi <q>pramāṇaṃ na bhavatītyevaṃparaṃ
﻿<pb n="r066"/>
tatsūtram ।</q> akṣeprā''ha-yadi dharma prati prāmāṇyanirākaraṇāya tatsūtraṃ <q>na tarhi pramāṇāntaraṃ asmin
śās‍tre pramāṇatayā cintitam ।</q> kiṃ tarhi siddhapramāṇasyaiva pratyakṣādeḥ dharmaṃ prati prāmāṇyaṃ
nirākartum<note n="(1)"> B. & C. <dn>nirākṛtaṃ</dn></note> । na punaḥ pratyakṣādi sarvatra pramāṇameva na bhavatītyāśaṅkaya prāmāṇyaṃ vyutpāditam ।
vṛttikāragranthepi pratyakṣādīnāṃ svarūpaṃ parīkṣitaṃ na prāmāṇyaṃ vyutpāditam । tasmādatiprasaṅgā-
didoṣāt yadeva <q>pratijñātaṃ</q> tadeva <q>cintanīyaṃ</q> nābhyupagataṃ <note n="(2)"> B. <dn>pratijñātaṃ</dn></note>apratijñātaṃ ca smṛtiśāstram ।
<q>ato'saṃbaddhaiveyaṃ cintā । atrābhidhīyate । pratijñātasyaivārthasya cinteyam । nanu ca svatantra-
śabdaghiṣayā sā pratijñā na cātra svātantryamasti ।</q> samādhātā āha&mdash;<q>satyam</q> svatantra-
śabdaviṣayā pratijñā । <q>svatantraśabdaviṣayaiveyaṃ cintā ।</q> ākṣeptā pṛcchati&mdash;<q>kimaṣṭakā-
kartavyeti svatantraśabdaḥ ?</q> yena tadviṣayacintābhavatā svatantraśabdaviṣayocyate । samādhā-
﻿<pb n="r067"/>
tottaramāha&mdash;<q>noyaṃ svatantraśabdaḥ</q> aṣṭakā kartavyeti <q>svatantraśabdasaṃbaddhastu ।</q>
punarākṣeptā pṛcchati&mdash;<q>kena svatantreṇa śabdena asya saṃbandha iti ?</q> samādhātottaramāha&mdash;yāṃ
<q>janāḥ pratinandantītyanena</q> svatantreṇa mantraśavdena । ayaṃ hi mantro rārtri prakāśayan
karsmiścinniyoge <note n="(1)"> A. <dn>tatprakāśakatayā</dn></note>prakāśakatayā saṃbaddhayate । smārte cāṣṭakākarmaṇi rātrirdevateti tenaivāsya
saṃbandhaḥ । ākṣeptā pṛcchati&mdash;<q>tataḥ kiṃ ?</q> yadi svatantreṇa śabdenāsya saṃbandhaḥ ।
uttaraṃ samādhātuḥ&mdash;<q>sāpekṣaparatantratvāt । asyāpi</q> sāpekṣatā <q>prāpnoti ।</q> asyārthaḥ
aṣṭakā kartavyeti pauruṣeyaṃ vacanaṃ pramāṇāntarasāpekṣameva kārya pratipādayati । mantreṇāpi ca
devatābhūtarātriprakāśanadvāreṇa tadeva kāryaṃ smaraṇīyaṃ tataśca sāpekṣapauruṣeyavākyaparatantraṃ vaidikamapi
mantravākyaṃ sāpekṣameva prāpnoti । tatsāmānyāditareṣāmapi sāpekṣatā prāpnoti । <note n="(2)"> B. add <dn>tadāha yadā sva</dn></note>yadā'smaryamāṇa-
puruṣamapi vaidikaṃ mantravākyaṃ pramāṇāntarasāpekṣaṃ sañjātaṃ tadā svābhāvikameva śabdasya sāpekṣārthā-
bhidhāyakatvamiti sarva eva vedaḥ kāryābhidhāyī na syāt । kārye pramāṇāntarasyāpekṣaṇīyasyā-
bhāvāt । <q>tadidamāha&mdash;dharmasya śabdamūlatvādaśabdamanapekṣaṃ syāditi । apekṣitaṃ
caitat yāṃ janāḥ pratinandantītyevamādibhiḥ ata eteṣāma<note n="(3)"> B. <dn>mapyaśa</dn></note>śavdataiveti</q> pūrayitvā sūtraṃ
paṭhitam । yasmāt yāṃ janāḥ pratinandantītyevamādīni aśabdamarthamapekṣante ata eṣāmapya-
śabdataiva ।</p>
﻿<pb n="r068"/>
<p><q>yadyapi svarūpataḥ śabdataivaiṣāṃ</q> tathāpi śabdakāryākaraṇāt aśabdatocyate । kiṃ punaḥ
śabdakāryaṃ ? pramāṇāntarānapekṣaṃ kāryārthapratipādakatvam । tadabhāvādaśabdataiveti । <q>sa eva tu
pratijñātārthaśco</q>danālakṣaṇo'rtho dharma iti <q>punarākṣipyate ।</q> kathamākṣipyata ityatrāha&mdash;
<q>na sāpekṣānapekṣayorekārthatvaṃ saṃbhavatītyuk‍tam viṣayabhedādityanena</q> prakāreṇākṣipyate ।
sāpekṣaṃ vākyaṃ aṣṭakā kartavyetya <note n="(1)"> A. <dn>tyekārthaviṣayaṃ</dn></note>kāryaviṣayam । tatra yadi yāṃ janāḥ pratinandantītyanapekṣaṃ
syāt tadā kāryārthaṃ bhavet । tataśca viṣayabhede sati ekārthatvaṃ na bhavati । gamyate caikārthatvaṃ,
tasmāt yāṃjanāḥ pratinandantītyapi sāpekṣaṃ akāryārthapratipādakamiti kārye'rthe prāmāṇyaṃ pratijñātaṃ
punarākṣipyate । <q>nanu cātrāpi<note n="(2)"> omits <dn>api</dn></note> viṣayabheda eva nāsti dvayoḥ kāryārthatvāt ।</q> smṛtāvapi hi
kāryārthatvameva pratīyate । pūrvapakṣyāha&mdash;<q>tadeva hi</q> smṛteḥ kāryārthatvaṃ <q>na saṃbhavatītyucyate</q>
atra hi tā eva smṛtaya udāharaṇaṃ yāsāmeva hi mūlabhūtaṃ śrutivāvayaṃ kṛts‍ne'pi vede no-
palabhyate । tatra ca smṛteḥ pauruṣeyavākyasya svātantryeṇa kāryapratipādakatvaṃ nāsti । na
cānupalabdhaṃ vedavākyamapi kāryaṃ pratipādayitumalaṃ yena tanmūlatāṃ yāyāt । rāddhāntaikadeśyāha-
<q>nanu ca kāryārthasyaivānumānaṃ bhaviṣyati ।</q> atyārthaḥ&mdash;yadyapi saṃprati pratyakṣaṃ vedavākyaṃ
kāryārthapratipādakaṃ nopalabhyate tathāpyāsīt sa tādṛśo vedaḥ ityanumānaṃ bhaviṣyati । yata<note n="(3)"> C. <dn>tata</dn></note>
upalabhya smṛtikārāḥ kāryārthaṃ svavacanairupabadhnantīti । so'yamutsannavedamūlasmṛtipakṣaḥ । pūrvapakṣa-
vādī dūṣavati&mdash;<q>tatparityāge kāraṇaṃ vak‍tavyam ।</q> yo'sāvāsīdvedaḥ tasyādhyetṛbhiḥ parityāge
﻿<pb n="r069"/>
kāraṇaṃ vak‍tavyam । kena kāraṇenāsāvadhyetṛbhiḥ parityak‍ta iti kāraṇaṃ vak‍tavyam । na ca
tacchakyate vak‍tum । yathānantacaraṇādhyetṛbhiḥ aharaharabhyāsakṛtasaṃskārapaṭavātiśayavaśena
itareṣāṃ vedavākyānāṃ <note n="(1)"> C. <dn>smasṇaṃ</dn></note>dhāraṇaṃ tathā'syāpi<note n="(2)"> C. <dn>tasyāpi</dn></note> syāt । tathā so'pi keṣāṃ cicchākhināṃ
svaśākhāntaḥ patita eva । svaśākhādhāriṇo<note n="(3)"> B. & C. <dn>dhāraṇe</dn></note>'nantamedhābalaśālinaḥ satatābhiyogāt dvijātayo
dṛśyante । tatra ko'vakāśaḥ parityāgasya । parityāgaścāyamavakāśaṃ labhamānaḥ sakalavedavya-
vahāramevāpākuryāt । sakalāṅgopasaṃhāra evādhikārasiddheḥ । tatsiddhayarthatvāccānuṣṭhānasyā-
śaṅkayate eva hi kasyacidaṅgavidheḥ parityāgo'pi । evaṃ padaparityāgaśaṅkayā kasyacidvākya-
syārthoṃ nāvasīyeta padānāṃ saṃbhūyakāritvāt ।</p>
<p>yadapyāpastaṃbenok‍taṃ&mdash;atha brāhmaṇok‍tā vidhayaḥ teṣāmutsannāḥ pāṭhāḥ prayogādanumīyante-iti
tada[pi]nyāyamūlamiti nyāyābhāvādanādartavyam । pūrvapakṣamākṣipati&mdash;<q>nanu ca kāryāvagati-
rapi naiva tyak‍tuṃ śakyate tadānupūrvyesiddhamanumānaṃ kena vāryate ।</q> asyārthaḥ&mdash;aṣṭakā
kartavyeti tāvat kāryāvagatirasti । sā ca kāryabhūtā kādācitkatvāt, kāryaṃ ca kāraṇā-
vinābhāvi । kāraṇabhāva eva bhāvo'bhāve cābhāva eveti<note n="(4)"> C <dn>anādṛtyaṃ</dn></note> kāryāvagatiśceyamaṣṭakā kartavyetyetadvākya
eva bhavati । tena tasyaiva vākyasya kāraṇatvamanumātuṃ yuktam । ataḥ kāryāvagatyānumānānu-
pūrvyeṇa krameṇa siddhamanumānaṃ kena vāryate, avagateḥ kādācitkatvāt । kāryaṃ cānumānaṃ,
kāryatvācca kāraṇavattvānumānaṃ, kāraṇavattvācca smṛtau kāraṇavattvānumānamiti । tadidamātupūrvyaṃ
pūrvapakṣī samādhatte&mdash;<q>satyaṃ na vāryate'numānaṃ yadyatra smaraṇābhimāno na syāt ।</q> asyārthaḥ
&mdash;aṣṭakā kartavyetyevamādivākyaṃ smaraṇatvenābhimataṃ yena smaryate tatsmaraṇam । pramāṇāntara-
pratīto'rtho yena vākyena pratipādyate aṣṭakāḥ kartavyā ityādinā tadityarthaḥ । bhavatvaṣṭakādi-
<note n="(5)"> A. adds <dn>taccakāraṇaṃ yadabhāve'bhāva eva bhāveca bhāva</dn></note>
<note n="(6)"> B. adds <dn>pūrvaṃ</dn></note>﻿<pb n="r070"/>
vākyeṣu smaraṇasaṃmatiḥ tathāpi <q>smaraṇābhimāne ko doṣaḥ ।</q> uttaramāha pūrvapakṣī&mdash;ayaṃ doṣaḥ
<q>smaraṇādanumāne prāp‍noti na kāryataḥ ।</q> smaraṇāt pauruṣeyādvākyādanumānena bhavitavyaṃ na
kāryataḥ । yadi kāryato'vagatirūpādanumānaṃ syāt tataḥ smṛtivākyasyaiva kāraṇatvamanumīyate ।
na caitadarita । bhavatu smaraṇādanumānaṃ tataḥ kiṃ ? uttaramāha pūrvapakṣī&mdash;<q>smaraṇaṃ hi
pramāṇaviṣayaṃ nārthaviṣayaṃ;</q> yadidaṃ smaraṇaṃ vākyarūpaṃ tat pramāṇasyānumāpakamiti pramāṇameva
tasya viṣayaḥ nārthaḥ, arthasyānanumeyatvāt । <q>kimiti । uttaraṃ&mdash;tatpurassaratvādartha-
saṃvidaḥ</q>, yākyaṃ hi pauruṣeyaṃ kāryabhūtaṃ pramāṇamevānumāpayati nārthamiti <quote>‘api ca pauruṣeyā-
dvacanāt’</quote> ityatrok‍tam । asmābhiśca <q>nītipathe ।</q></p>
<p>punaḥ pūrvapakṣamākṣipati&mdash;yadi smaraṇātpramāṇamanumīyate <q>siṃddha tarhi prāmāṇyaṃ vedasya</q>

yadi hi sarva pauruṣeyaṃ vākyaṃ pramāṇapūrvakameva<note n="(1)"> B. <dn>pramāṇameva</dn></note> syāt tadā siddhayatyeva<note n="(2)"> A. <dn>sidhyet</dn></note> prāmāṇyaṃ bhrāntyādi-

smaraṇavyavadhāne tu tannopapadyate । kasmādityāha&mdash;<q>na kāryaṃ smaraṇasaṃbandhi kāraṇasaṃbandhiṃ tat ।</q>
yatkāryāvagatilakṣaṇaṃ kāryaṃ na tat pauruṣeyavākyasaṃbandhi । api tu smaraṇakāraṇabhūtavedavākya-
saṃbandhi tat । <q>na ca vyavahitasya kāryasya nirapekṣaṃ tadeva</q> mūlabhūtaṃ vedavākyama<q>stītyanapekṣaṃ</q>
kāryāvagatilakṣaṇaṃ kāryaṃ; <q>tasmāt vandhyāsutasmaraṇatulyamidaṃ</q> kāryāvagatilakṣaṇaṃ <q>kāryama ।</q>
yathā bandhyāsutasmaraṇamasiddhaṃ tathā kāryāvagatirapyasiddheti hetvasiddhayā nānumānodayaḥ ।

asyārthaḥ&mdash;yadā vedaśabdavācyo'yaṃ granthaḥ brāhmaṇaśabdavācyo'yaṃ puruṣa iti śabdārthasaṃbandhāvagatau

﻿<pb n="r072"/>
pratipadyate ।</q> asyārthaḥ&mdash;tatra sarveṃṣāṃ vyavahārāvagatilakṣaṇakāryamūlaṃ śabdārthasaṃbandhadarśanameva
vākyaprayogamūlam । <q>iha tu</q> tasya <note n="(1)"> B. adds <dn>kārya</dn></note>vākyārthadarśanasyābhāvaḥ । <q>tasmāt</q> pauruṣeyavacanaparaṃparāṃ

smaraṇavyavadhānāditi ?</q> uttaram&mdash;<q>idaṃ tat</q> smaraṇavyavadhānāditi <q>smaraṇaṃ hyatra pramāṇa-

tayopalabhyate<note n="(1)"> A. & B. <dn>palakṣyate</dn></note> ।</q> adhunātanapramātdṛṇāṃ smṛtivākyameva kāryāvagatau kāraṇam । na tu

yatkāryaṃ tat kāraṇakāraṇamapyavagamayati<note n="(1)"> A. <dn>anumāpayati ।</dn></note> ।</p> tena asaṃbaddhasyāpi kāraṇakāraṇasya
kāryato'numānamasti yathā paṭādibhyaḥ kuvindādeḥ । paṭasya hi sākṣāt tantavaḥ samavāyi-
kāraṇam tatsaṃyogastvasamavāyikāraṇam । kuvindādayastu asamavāyikāraṇabhūtatantusaṃyoga-
syotpattāvapi na kāraṇaṃ sākṣāt । tathā hi&mdash;tantukarmabhyaḥ tantusayogāḥ । tantukarmāṇi ca
kuvindahastatantusaṃyogebhyaḥ । paṭastu tantusaṃyogebhya iti । atha ca paṭādibhyaḥ kuvindā-
dayo'pyanumīyanta iti । pūrvapakṣī pariharati&mdash;<q>maivaṃ maṃsthāḥ asaṃbaddhaṃ</q> kāraṇakāraṇamapyanumīyata
iti । <q>etāvadeva hi tatra kāraṇam ।</q> tantutatsaṃyogakuvindādikameva paṭotpattau kāraṇam ।
nimittakāraṇasyāpi kāraṇatvāt kuvindādayaśca paṭotpattau nimittakāraṇam tena nāsaṃbaddhatvamiti
yuktameva teṣāmanumeyatvaṃ ca । pūrvapakṣī rāddhāntino matamāśaṅkate&mdash;<q>kimevaṃ smṛteḥ śabdakāraṇa-
kāraṇataivāsmin kārye ।</q> asyārthaḥ&mdash;yathā paṭādau janayitavye tantusaṃyogānāṃ kuvindakāraṇa-
karmakāraṇatā evaṃ smṛterapyasmin kāryāvagatilakṣaṇakārye janayitavye śabdakāraṇakaṃ yadvijñānaṃ
tatkāraṇataiveti kiṃ siddhāntin manyase yena śabdamanumāpayi<note n="(2)"> C. <dn>anumānumi</dn></note>tumicchasi । siddhāntī tūttara-
māha&mdash;<q>omityucyate ।</q> evamevāṅgīkaromītyarthaḥ । pūrvapakṣī dūṣayati&mdash;<q>siddhaṃ tarhi caitya-
vandanādīnāṃ prāmāṇyaṃ</q>, teṣāmapi śabdakāraṇakāraṇatvāt śabdānumāne sthite tanmūlatvena
prāmāṇyopapatteḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="r077"/>
<p>pūrvapakṣī rāddhāntino matamāśaṅkate&mdash;<q>na</q> siddhayati caityavandanādīnāṃ prāmāṇyaṃ, śabdamūlatvena
praṇetṛbhiranabhyupagamāt । tathā hyāha śauddhodani<note n="(1)"> A. <dn>buddhamuniḥ</dn></note>:&mdash;<quote>“paśyāmyahaṃ bhikṣavo divyena cakṣuṣā sugati
durgatiṃ ca”</quote> iti । na ca divyacakṣurupapadyate yadyogajaṃ sarvaviṣayajñānamabhimatam । na ca
tathāvidhasya jñānasya kāraṇamasti । ato nirmūlatvāt caityavandanādismṛtīnāṃ aprāmāṇyamiti
cet । dūṣayati&mdash;<q>na tarhi kāryato viśiṣṭakāraṇānumānam ।</q> yadi hi caityavandanādismṛtiṣu
śabdakāraṇakāraṇatā<note n="(2)"> A. & C. <dn>śabdakāraṇatā</dn></note> vyabhicaritā tadā smṛtiḥ vyamicāriṇī satī na śabdamanumāpayitumalam ।
tasmāt&mdash;<q>pramāṇāntaramatra mṛgyam ।</q> mūlabhūtaśabdasadbhāvāvadhāraṇe na <q>ca tadastītyuktam ।</q>
yatra na vaidikaṃ śabdamūlamupalabhata iti pramāṇāntareṇa vaidikaśabdopalaṃbhābhāva evedamadhi-
karaṇam । pūrvapakṣamupasaṃharati&mdash;<q>tadidaṃ vandhyāsutasmaraṇavadakāraṇaṃ</q>, yathā'tyantānupalabdha-
vandhyāsutādismaraṇaṃ na pramāṇasadbhāve kāraṇaṃ tathedamapyaṣṭakādismaraṇam । nanu mā bhūta smaraṇaṃ
pramāṇasadbhāve kāraṇaṃ, svayameva tu svatantramarthaparicchedakāraṇaṃ bhavatu ityatrāha&mdash;<q>na <note n="(3)"> A. <dn>na tu sma</dn></note>tat smaraṇa-
tayā karaṇībhavitumarhati</q> na svatantraṃ pramāṇaṃ bhavitumarhati । smaraṇatvādevetyarthaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="r078"/>
tasmāt duṣṭakāraṇataivātra sthitā । tataścāprāmāṇyaṃ codanāyāḥ ।</q> rāddhāntamāha&mdash;aho'na-
vasitanayanītikṣo <q>bhavān ।</q> na bhavatā nayo'vasita.; nāpi nītijñāḥ mīmāṃsakāḥ mīmāṃsakok‍to
nayaḥ, mīmāṃsakāśca nītijñāḥ । tena mīmāṃsakoktaṃ nayaṃ mīmāṃsakāṃśca nītijñān anādriyamāṇaḥ bhavāna
anavasitanayanītijñaḥ । pūrvapakṣī pṛcchati&mdash;<q>kimiti ।</q> rāddhāntī tṛttaramāha&mdash;<q>kāryatastāvat
smaraṇe śaktirasti ।</q> asyārthaḥ&mdash;aṣṭakāḥ kartavyā ityuk‍te kāryāvagatistāvadupajāyate ।
yathā ca pratyakṣamūlāni laukikāni vacāṃsi vaktrabhiprāyāntarbhāvadvāreṇa arthapratītimupajanayanti
sadva<note n="(1)"> B. <dn>tathā</dn></note>daṣṭakādivākyānyapi । tena kāryāvagatirevāsiddheti na śakyate vak‍tum । tena
kāryāvagatilakṣaṇakāryadarśanāt smaraṇasya tatra śaktirastītyavagamyate । smaraṇamidānīmakāraṇa-
mityakāraṇatā smaraṇe'dhyavasīyate । <q>na ca tadakāraṃṇatvaṃ smaraṇeśakyate'dhyavasātuṃ
saṃbhavādvedasaṃyogasya kāraṇāntarasyāsaṃbhavādasmin kārye ।</q> asyārthaḥ&mdash;evaṃ smaraṇasya
kāryāvagatau<note n="(2)"> B. <dn>smaraṇakāryāvagatau</dn></note> kāraṇatve pratibhāsamānepyakāraṇatvaṃ bhavet yadi smaraṇameva pramāṇalakṣaṇakāraṇaśūnyaṃ
﻿<pb n="r079"/>
bhavet । na ca smaraṇasyaivaṃvidhasya kāraṇaṃ nāsti smaraṇādeva kāryabhūtāt kāraṇānumānāt ।
kāraṇe cānumīyamāne kāryāvagatiśak‍tasmaraṇalakṣaṇakāryānuguṇatvena veda evānumīyate । pramāṇā-
ntarasyānanuguṇatvāt । na hi pramāṇāntarāṇi evaṃvidhasmaraṇakāraṇatāmāsādayitumarhanti
kāryaṃ prati tasya pramāṇatvābhāvāt । na ca vedānumānamapyasaṃbhavānnirastam; vedasaṃyogasya
saṃmavātsmṛtikārāṇāmapi । nanu na saṃbhavati smṛtikārāṇāmapi vedasaṃyogaḥ vedasyānupalabdheḥ ।
yatraiva hi viṣaye sarveṣāṃ vedānupalaṃbhaḥ tadviṣayasmṛtigocara evāyaṃ vicāraḥ । anyatra vicārasya
niravakāśatvāt । na ca tatra granthastvanumīyata iti granthānumānena rāddhāntopavarṇanaṃ yujyate ।
<note n="(1)"> A. <dn>nahyapratya</dn></note>na hi pratyakṣasya granthasyānumānaṃ yuktam । na cedaṃ vātyaṃ, yadyapi smṛtikārāṇāṃ pratyakṣaveda-
saṃyogo nāsti tathāpyanumānanibandhano vedasaṃyogo bhaviṣyatīti । liṅgābhāvāt । anumitaśca kathaṃ
vedo bhaviṣyati iti, kathaṃ ca tasyārthabodhakatvam ।</p>
<p>atrocyate&mdash;anumito'pi tāvacchabdo bodhaka<note n="(2)"> B. & C. <dn>vācaka eva</dn></note> eva, avagatasya sataḥ smaraṇārūḍhasya
vācakatvāt । ata eva lipyavagatebhyo'kṣarebhyo'rtha <note n="(3)"> C. <dn>kṣarapratipattiḥ</dn></note>pratipattiḥ । na cānumeyasyāvedatvam,
vedo hi nāma apauruṣeyaḥ śabda<note n="(4)"> C. <dn>sandarbhaḥ</dn></note>saṅghātaḥ । na cānumīyamānasya tadānīṃ aśrotragrahaṇatayā
śabdatvamevānupapannam । lipyavagatasyeva yogyatayā hi śrotragrahaṇatā tasya vidyate tasyāpi
kakārādivarṇamayatvāt । yacca liṅgābhāvādananumānamupanyastaṃ tadudāharaṇamātraniṣṭhatayā, yathaiva
hyasmākaṃ smṛtivākye darśanasamutthamanumānaṃ tathā manvādīnāmapi smṛtyantaradarśanasamutthitamityanena
krameṇāpareṣāmaṣyanumānamapareṣāmapītyanādismṛtiparaṃparāśrayaṇānna kaściddoṣaḥ । anāditvepi ca
smṛtiparaṃparāyāḥ <note n="(5)"> A. <dn>smṛti</dn></note>smṛtereva draḍhimā pramāṇaṃ; <note n="(6)"> C. <dn>tenātrāpya</dn></note>tenānādāvapyandhaparamparādidoṣo'pi nāsti । sarveṣāṃ
smṛtilakṣaṇaliṅgamayalocanaśālitvāt । śabdārthasaṃbandhavat । yathā hi śabdārthasaṃbandhāvagame
pūrvapūrvavṛddhavyavahāraliṅga<note n="(7)"> <dn>liṅgasaṃbandhasaṃbhavāt</dn></note>sadbhāvāt nāndhaparaṃparādoṣaḥ tathehāpi । na ca granthānumānābhyupagame'pa-
siddhāntadoṣaḥ । artho hyarthāpattau na śabdamupasthāpayati । tasyākāraṇatvāt । smṛtistu
<note n="(8)"> B. & C. <dn>prāmāṇyameva</dn></note>pramāṇamevopasthāpayitumalaṃ, tasyaiva taddhetutvāt । ata eva gautamaḥ <quote>‘pratyakṣavidhānādgārhasthyasya’</quote>
﻿<pb n="r080"/>
ityāha । anyathā pratyakṣavedamūlatve sarbasmṛtīnāṃ itarepyāśramāḥ pratyakṣavedavihitā eveti
gāīsthyasya viśeṣābhāvāt praśaṃsā nopapadyate । nanvevaṃ caityavandanādīnāṃ prāmāṇyaṃ kimiti na
bhavatītyatrāha&mdash;<q>caityavandanādiṣvasaṃbhavāt ।</q> labdhātmakaḥ kāraṇābhāvaḥ । asyārthaḥ&mdash;grantha-
praṇetṛbhiḥ caityavandanādiṣu yatkāraṇamabhyupagataṃ <note n="(1)"> C. omits <dn>tanna saṃbhavati</dn></note>tanna saṃbhavati yogipratyakṣādi tasya tena teṣāṃ
vandhyāsutasmaraṇavadaprāmāṇyam । manvādayastu vedamūlatvameva svavacasāṃ pratijānate ।
<lg><l>yaḥ kaścitkasyaciddharmo manunā parikīrtitaḥ ।</l>
<l>sa sarvo'bhihito vede sarvajñānamayo hi saḥ ।।</l></lg>
iti bruvāṇāḥ । tasmādvaiṣamyaṃ caityavandanādibhiḥ aṣṭakādīnām । ato bhavadīyamevātra
kāraṇadoṣānumānaṃ nirastaṃ, <q>na punarasmadīyaṃ kāryato granthānumānam । tasmādatantramanupalabdhiḥ,
granthaviṣayā</q>, na nirmūlatāṃ smṛterāpādayitumalamityarthaḥ ।</p>
<p>yadyapi hi kasyāṃcicchākhāyāmanāmnātatvāt । anabhivyaktatayā grantho nopalabhyate tathāpi
tasyānumānamaviruddhaṃ, anabhivyaktatayā yadapi vākyaṃ nopalabhyata iti । etadevopapāda yati
<q>vismaraṇopapatteśca pratipattaḥ ।</q> yadi hyanāmnāto'pi śabda upalabhyate tataḥ pratipat‍tuḥ
vismaraṇaṃ nopapadyate । dṛśyate ca pratipattdṛṇāṃ vismaraṇamapi । tato'vagacchāmo'nāmnātasya
satopyanupalaṃbhanaṃ bhavatīti । <q>tasmādavyāhatamanapekṣatvaṃ codanāyāḥ ।</q> yatpunaridamuktaṃ <quote>‘yāṃ
janāḥ pratinandantītyaṣṭakāliṅgā <q>mantrāḥ iti tadanupapannam; kutaḥ ? uttaram&mdash;tadeka-
vākyatayaivāprāmāṇyamuk‍tam । kathaṃ tadreva prāmāṇyahetutayopanyasyate</q> smṛtyekavākyatvā-
﻿<pb n="r081"/>
pannamantranirūpaṇenaivāprāmāṇyamuktam । kathaṃ tasyaiva prāmāṇyahetu(ka)tvenopanyāsaḥ । samartha-
yate&mdash;<q>naivedaṃ prāmāṇyahetutayopanyastam । vedasaṃyogasya tu saṃbhave liṅgam ।</q> ākṣeptā
pṛcchati&mdash;<q>kathaṃ kṛtvā</q>, kathamityarthaḥ anyathā evaṃ kathamitthamiti ktvāpratyayaḥ । uttaram&mdash;
<q>talliṅgāpekṣaṃ devatābhidhānaṃ <note n="(1)"> C. <dn>devatāvidhānaṃ</dn></note>karmaṇi ।</q> asyārthaḥ&mdash;yāṃ janāḥ pratinandantīti mantraliṅgālo-
canayā kvacitkarmāviśeṣe samavetā rātririti pratibhāsate । sā rātriḥ smṛtyā aṣṭakākarmaṇi
devatātvena samavetocyate । aṣṭakā hi rātridevatyā puṣṭikarmeti । tena vedādavagato'rthaḥ
rātreḥ samavāyaḥ smṛtyocyate । taddarśanānmanyāmahe anyadapi coditameva smṛtyā bodhyata ityasti
vedasaṃyogaḥ smṛtikārāṇāmityavagamyate । tadāha&mdash;<q>tasmānmāntravarṇikīṃ devatāmanuvadan</q>
smaran smṛtikāro <q>vedasaṃyogamātmana uyodbalayati ।</q> ye tu mantrādimūlāṃ smṛtimicchanti
teṣāṃ sarva evāyaṃ grantho viruddhayate । na ca mantrārthavādāḥ karmasvarūpaphalaviśeṣādiṣu prāmāṇyaṃ
pratipat‍tumalamiti । alamanenātisthūladoṣeṇa bālajanajalpitena pakṣeṇa dūṣitena । etenaiva
prayogavidhimūlatāpi smṛtīnāṃ vinivāritā । kiñca prayogavidhisaṃbandhepi smṛtyarthasya kiṃ pramāṇa-
mityapi cintanīyameva । <q>yatpunaridamuk‍tam&mdash;ye dṛṣṭārthāste tata eva pramāṇamiti । aśadida-
muktam ।</q> samarthayitā pṛcchati&mdash;<q>kimatrāsaduk‍taṃ</q>, na kiñcidasaduktamityarthaḥ । atrākṣeprā
āha&mdash;<q>bāḍhamatiśayenāsaduktam ।</q> yasmādevaṃ vadatā pramāṇāntarāpekṣā uktā bhavati yāni dṛṣṭā-
rthāni gurvanugamanādīni adhyayanavivāvaṅgatvena smaryante tatsmṛtiṣu prayojanadarśanameva mūlamityucyate
<q>tenādhyayanavidheḥ pramāṇāntarāpekṣitā uktā bhavati ।</q> aṅgagrāhakapramāṇāntarāpekṣitā uktā
mavati । aṅgagrāhakapramāṇāntarāpekṣitvāt । samarthayitā āha&mdash;<q>svarūpe vā kena vāritama-
﻿<pb n="r082"/>
vaghātāderiva dṛṣṭārthatvam ।</q> asyārthaḥ&mdash;yathā'vaghātādeḥ svarūpe dṛṣṭārthatvaṃ tathā gurvanugamanā-
dīnāmapi naiyogike tu svarūpe <note n="(1)"> B. <dn>nātraiva</dn></note>nāstyeva dṛṣṭārthatvam । tena svarūpe bhavatu pramāṇāntarāpekṣā ।

&mdash;tatraiva viśeṣaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ ।</q></p>
<p><b>virodhe tvanapekṣaṃ syāt asati hyanumānam । yadi saṃbhavati vedasaṃprayoge apratihataṃ

﻿<pb n="r083"/>
manayaiva yuk‍tyā prasaktam । katham ?</q> uttaram&mdash;virodhāt । virodho hi smṛtyā saha
<q>vedasyopalabhyate virodhe ca aprāmāṇyaṃ</q> sphuṭam <q>parasparabyāghātāt । yathā auduṃvaryāḥ
sarvaveṣṭanaṃ sparśanena saha</q> parasparavyāhatam । atrāyaṃ bhāvaḥ&mdash;yathā hyaviruddhā smṛtiḥ vedamupasthā-
payati<note n="(1)"> B. <dn>vedamanumāpayati</dn></note> tathā viruddhāpi tulyatvāddhetoḥ । manvādayo hi pratyayitā iti tadvacanādvedānumānam ।
tacca viruddhasmṛtiviṣayepi samānam । yadi parasparaviruddhārthāḥ śrutayo na saṃbhaveyuḥ tadā bhrāntyādi-
mūlā viruddhārthā smṛtiḥ syāt । tathā cok‍taṃ <q>mīmāṃsātantravārtike</q>&mdash;
<lg></l>parasparaviruddhatvaṃ śrutīnāṃ na bhavedyadi ।</l>

dṛśyante ca uditānuditahomavidhivat atirātre ṣoḍaśigrahaṇāgrahaṇavacca sahasraśaḥ śrutayopyasaṃbhavadyu-

durlabhaṃ prāmāṇyaṃ vedasya ।</p>
<p>atha manvādīnāṃ viruddhārthasmṛtiviṣaye pratyayitatvaṃ nāstītyananumānaṃ hanta tarhi<note n="(2)"> B. & C. <dn>uttaraṃ&mdash;na tarhi anyatrāpyanumānamiti</dn></note> anya-

<lg><l>kadācicchrutimūlatvamuktvā bhrāntyādimūlatā ।</l>
<l><note n="(3)"> B. <dn>śrutivipratipannā</dn></note>smṛtibhiḥ pratipannā cet kastāmindro'pi vārayet ।। iti</l></lg>
rāddhāntamāha&mdash;<q>satyamevaṃ</q> bhavedviroghādvedasyāprāmāṇyaṃ <q>yadyanyataḥ kāryānumānavighāto na syāt ।</q>
kuto'nyato'numānavighāta ityatrāha&mdash;<q>viruddhādeva vaidikādvacasaḥ ।</q> kathaṃ punaḥ tasyānumāna-
﻿<pb n="r084"/>
vighātakartṛtvamityatrāha&mdash;<q>sākṣādvedapratipādite hyarthe na tadvirodhi sāpekṣaṃ puṃvacaḥ pramāṇaṃ
bhavitumarhati ।</q> kuta ityatrāha&mdash;<q>pramāṇāntarānavacchinne hyarthe</q> pramāṇaṃ <q>pramāṇaṃ bhavitumarhati ।</q>
na punastadvayāghātena hi jātā pratītiḥ anyathā śakyā kartumiti pratītyantarameva nopajāyate ।
pratītyantare virodhini jāte hi <q>siddhasādhyavyavasthayā hi vādhaṃ naiyāyikā manyante na siddhaṃ
sādhyena vādhyate</q>, aśakyatvāt । <q>siddhenaiva hi sādhyaṃ bādhyate ।</q> utpattipratibandhanāt ।
<q>siddhaścāyaṃ vaidiko'rthaḥ pratyakṣāvagamyavedavākyakāraṇatvāt । paścāt na tadviruddhakāraṇa-
dhiṣayamanumānamātmānaṃ labhate vahnāviva śaityānumanam ।</q> yathā'smākamanumānaṃ nāsti tathā
pūrveṣāmapi । kiṃ nibandhanā tarhi smṛtiriyam ? tarhi bhrāntimūleti vadāmaḥ । yathā aviruddhā
smṛtiranumāpikā tathā viruddhāpi iti pūrvapakṣanyāyanibandhanayā bhrāntyā mūlānumānamaviruddhamiti
manvānāḥ smṛtīḥ praṇītavantaḥ । dṛśyante ca pūrvapakṣanyāyamūlāḥ smṛtayaḥ <quote>“aṅga vā samabhi-
vyāhārāt”</quote> iti piṇḍapitṛyajñasya darśāṅgatvasmṛtiḥ pūrvapakṣanyāyamūleti sphuṭataraṃ samabhivyāhārā-
diti hetvabhidhānāt । <quote>‘vedamadhītya s‍nāyāt’</quote> iti ca smṛteḥ pūrvapakṣanyāyamūlatā prathamasūtre
﻿<pb n="r085"/>
uktā । na cātra bhrāntimūlatābhyupagame sarvatra mithyābhāvaḥ । yatra hi vedamūlatvaṃ nāstīti
balīyasā pramāṇenāvagataṃ tatra mrāntimūlakatvakalpanā । anyatra nirbījameva bhrāntimūlatvabhiti
smṛtidāḍharyāt veda evānumīyate । anenedamapahastitaṃ yaduk‍taṃ&mdash;

iha cātyantāpratyakṣavedamūlā viruddhārthaviṣayā smṛtiḥ udāharaṇaṃ ; <q>tasmānna virodhe prāmāṇyaṃ
smṛteḥ । aprāmāṇyāccāvirodhaḥ avirodhe cāvyādhātaḥ । avyāghātāccāvihataṃ prāmāṇyaṃ
codanāyāḥ ।</q></p>
<p>adhikaraṇāraṃmamākṣipati&mdash;<q>nanu ca kāryārthatve śabdasya ko virodhaḥ ।</q> kasmāt

na parasparaṃ vyāhantumutsahate ।</q> svarūpavirodhe hi virodhaḥ । <note n="(1)"> B. adds <dn>kasmāt kāryārthatve cedvirodhonāstītyāha</dn></note>kāryadvayasya ca svarūpe

pattuṃ na śakyate । anubandhādibhiḥ</q> bhidyamānaiḥ medenāvagamāt । bhinnānubandhaṃ svarūpato

mavagamyate। kāryasya cedvitatiḥ na svatantrakāryatayā<note n="(2)">C.<dn>vitāti</dn></note> śak‍yate'vagantum । <q>tasmādanavagate

adhvaryurgṛhapatimityasya vidheḥ viṣayaḥ ।</q> uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>svāvasare</q> pañcame vakṣyāmaḥ । kāle'pi
cāyameva bhāṣyokta eva parihāraḥ । kathamayaṃ parihāraḥ ? uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>paurṇamāsīśabdābhidheyaṃ
kimabhipretamāyuṣmataḥ ।</q> yāvatā yadi tāvat kāla eko vibhurnityaśca abhidheyaḥ tadā tasya
dvitīyādiṣvap‍yaviśeṣāt anabhidheyatvāpattiḥ<note n="(3)"> B.<dn>avidheyāpattiḥ</dn></note>। sa evāha--<q>ato'trāpi kriyāpracitireva
grahāṇāṃ saṃyogavibhāgajā</q> paurṇamāsyādiśabdabācyā candrādityayoḥ saṃyogādyā kriyāpracitirjā&mdash;
yate sā pratipadādiḥ paurṇamāsīparyantā । yā ca vibhāgajā sā pratipadādiramāvāsyāparyantā ।
tasyāṃ satyāṃ kāle tadupādhibhinne pratipadādiśabdaprayogāt tasyā eva tacchabdavācyatā yuktā
sāmaśabdavat bhavatīti । gītiviśiṣṭe mantre prayujyamāno yathā sāmaśabdaḥ gītimātravācī,
tathā pratipadādiśabdo'pi । <q>iyāṃstu viśeṣaḥ</q>&mdash;kriyāpracayātmakatvepi <q>coditakāryapraciti-
﻿<pb n="r098"/>
revaikatrāṅgam ।</q> yo'sau pradhānakālatayā'ṅgānāṃ kāla ākṣipyate sa coditakāryapracityātmakaḥ ।
<q>kriyāntarapracitiḥ anyatrā</q>māvāsyādirūpāṅgam । kathaṃ punastasyā aṅgatvaṃ ? yadāsau tadā
karmānuṣṭhānāt tadviśiṣṭe kāle karmaṇaḥ karaṇāditi yāvat । na ca dravyabhūtakālāṅgabhāvo'trābhi-
pretaḥ । kintu paurṇamāsyādiśabdavācyatā tasya nāsti । śabdavācyasya cāṅgatā śabdena
bodhyate । <note n="(1)"> C. omits<dn>tena</dn></note> tena saṃbhavati kālāvacchedadvāreṇādityādigatipracayasyāpi karmāṅgatvamiti tatra
dakṣiṇācāreṇa<note n="(2)"> B.<dn>dakṣiṇakareṇa</dn></note> kriyamāṇeṣu padārtheṣu <q>kriyāntarapracityā tāvadavirodhaḥ ।</q> paurṇamāsīkālasya
tadyogitvāt । <q>coditakarmapracitistu karmottarakālabhāvinī</q> yathācoditaśrautasmārtapadārthā-
śrayā coditapracitiḥ । tasmāt tasyāḥ kramavadavirodhaḥ । atra bhāṣyaṃ&mdash;<quote>“na cācamanādayo 
vyavadhānaṃ kurvanti”</quote> iti tasyābhiprāyamāha&mdash;<q>pratipadārthāṅgābhiprāyaṃ</q>, ācamanaṃ kartṛsaṃskāraḥ
kartā na prayogāṅgatayā pratipadārthāṅgabhūtaḥ । tena dvāreṇācamanāderapi pratipadārthamaṅgabhāvaḥ ।
na ca svāṅgaṃ vyavadhāyakaṃ bhavati । kuta ityāha&mdash;<q>sāṅgasyaiva hi padārthasya padārthāntareṇa
kramāvagatiryuk‍tā</q><note n="(3)"><dn>tiryataḥ</dn></note> । tasmādavirodhitvādācamanādīnāṃ <q>ācamanādyanvitā eva vaidikāḥ
prayogāḥ pratipattavyāḥ</q> iti ।</p>﻿<pb n="r099"/>
<p><q>teṣ‍vadarśanāt । śabdārthavipratiyattau satyāṃ kimaprāmāṇyaṃ vedasya syāt ।</q> nā-
stītyabhiprāyaḥ । vyākaraṇaśās‍treṇaiva samastānāmabhidhānaśaṃsanasya[।t] saṃśayasya nirastatvāt
ubhayaniyamāt । uttaram&mdash;<q>saṃśayādapratipatteḥ ।</q> vācyavācakabhāvaḥ sandigdhaścet śabdārthāva-
gatirnāstītyaprāmāṇyam । na cākṣādiśabdavadubhayatra śak‍tikalpanāyāṃ pramāṇamasti śiṣṭānāma-
śiṣṭānāṃ ca atraiva śaktiritaratra lakṣaṇetyabhidhānāt । tatra ca kva mukhyaḥ kva gauṇa iti nādhyavasīyate
vyākaraṇaprāmāṇye'pi । nanu vyākaraṇaśāstrānabhyupagame yavavarāhādiśabdānāmudāharaṇatvaṃ
na syāt vākyaśeṣeṇaiva saṃśayavyāvṛtterityāha&mdash;<q>nanu ca sandigdheṣu vāk‍yaśeṣādityud‍dhūtam
aprāmāṇyam । pariharati&mdash;satyamud‍dhūtam । yatrānekārthatayaiva śabdasya sarvatra nimitta-
bhāvaḥ</q> prasiddhaḥ tatra kiṃparatvenātra prayukta ityetasmin saṃśaye vāk‍yaśeṣānnirṇaya uktaḥ
yathā akṣādiṣvanekārtheṃṣu । <q>yatra punaḥ vipratipattyaiva loke<note n="1"> B.<dn>laukikānāṃ</dn></note> kvacidarthe kasyacit</q> padasya
nimittatā nāvagatā, <q>na tatra prayogāt saṃśayaḥ</q>, prayogamadhikṛtya na tatra saṃśayo bhavati﻿<pb n="r100"/>
kutrārthe prayogo'yamiti । prayogāditi lyablope pañcamī । tathāpi kimityāha&mdash;<q>prayogasya ca
saṃśayaṃ vāk‍yaśeṣo vyāvartayati ।</q> yasminnarthe svīkriyamāṇe vāk‍yaśeṣasyopapattiḥ tatra
prayukta iti niścīyate । <q>nābhidhāne saṃśayaṃ</q> vāk‍yaśeṣo vyāvartayati । <q>abhidhāne cāyaṃ
saṃśayaḥ</q> abhidhānasaṃśayasya vyavahāravipratipattyā keṣāñcita dīrdhaśūke yavaśabdasya vyavahāraḥ
keṣāṃcit priyaṅguṣu; na ca gauṇamukhyaviśeṣāvadhāraṇaṃ ubhayatra tulyatvāt śabdavyavahārasya ।
<q>śabdārthavyavahāramūlaṃ ca vedārthajñānamityuktam</q> saṃbandhaparihāre । <q>tena vyavahārabaddhedārthe
prāptā viprātipattiḥ । na cātra virodhāt vedārthasya śak‍yate nirākartuṃ vipratipattiḥ ।</q> yathā
vedārthavirodhādaudumbarīsparśanena sarvaveṣṭanasmṛtiḥ nirākriyate tathā'tra nirākaraṇakāraṇaṃ nāsti ।
<q>ubhayathopapatteḥ vāk‍yārthasya । tasmāt nimittavipratipattyā'nadhyavasāyo</q> vāk‍yārthasya ।
ajñānaṃ anadhyavasāyaḥ ajñānācca aprāmāṇyam ।</p>﻿<pb n="r101"/>
<p><q>śāstrasthā vā ।।</q> rāddhāntamāha&mdash;satyaṃ vipratipattirnirākartuṃ na śakyate yadyavirodhaḥ syāt
atrāpi tu <q>virodho'vagamyata<note n="(1)">C. <dn>ta eva</dn></note> ityeva ।</q> śrūyate hi <quote>‘varāhaṃ gāvo'nudhāvanti’</quote> ityevamādiṣu
vākyaśeṣeṣu varāhasya gosādṛśyam । na ca kṛṣṇaśakunergosādṛśyamasti iti vedavirodhinī
nlecchānāṃ pratipattiḥ । <q>tataḥ kiṃ ?</q> uttaram&mdash;<q>viśiṣṭanimittako'nvayo'dhagamyate ।</q>
vedavirodhena mlecchapratipattau nirastāyāṃ ārya<note n="(2)">C. <dn>pratipattivaśena</dn></note>pratipattyavadhṛtasūkarārthapratipādakatayaiva varāhaśabdasya
vākyārthe nimittabhāva iti niścīyate tenādhyavasāyyeva vedaḥ । atra codayati&mdash;<q>nanu tadeveda-
māpatitaṃ vākyaśeṣānnirṇaya iti ।</q> tena yadyapyabhidhānasaṃśayo'yaṃ tathāpi vākyaśeṣānnirṇaya
iti paunaruktyameva । pariharati&mdash;<q>naivedamāpatitam ।</q> kuta ityāha&mdash;<q>sandigdhe hi
nimitte tatra nirṇayaḥ । atra punaḥ viparyaya eva nirākriyate । varāhādyeva</q> sūkarādyeva
autpattikam, na kṛṣṇaśakunādīti kṛṣṇaśakunyādyeva mukhyaṃ vācyamiti yo'yaṃ viparyayaḥ sa
﻿<pb n="r102"/>
nirākriyate na saṃśayaḥ । <q>nanu ca vedādeva nimittāvagamo<note n="(1)"> A. & C. <dn>nimittābhāvo</dn></note> 'bhyupagato bhavati na laukika-
vyavahārāt</q> yūpādīnāmiva । rāddhāntyekadeśyāha&mdash;yadi yūpādiśabdatulyatā <q>ebaṃ sati
ko doṣaḥ ।</q> ākṣeptā dūṣayati-<q>na khalu kaścidanyo doṣaḥ</q> brahmavadhādiḥ । <q>tadeva</q> hi <q>vaidika-
nimittatvaṃ na siddhayati<note n="(2)"> B. & C. <dn>kathaṃ na sidhyatīti</dn></note> । kutaḥ ? uttaram&mdash;apratipanne laukikanimittabhāve na vedāt
pratipattuṃ śakyate ।</q> yadyapi vedādidamavagataṃ gosadṛśo varāhaśabdavācya iti । tathāpi
sūkarapratipattiḥ aśakyā । anyasyāpi sādṛśyasaṃbhavāt । anye tu pratipanna iti paṭhanti
teṣāmayamarthaḥ । yukto yūpādiṣu vaidiko nimittabhāvaḥ loke atyantāprasiddhatvāt । iha
punarloke'nyatra prasiddhirastīti na vedānnimittāvagamaḥ । tadidamayuktam । trivṛcchabde pratipakṣa-
bhūte'pi laukike prayoge vedādeva nimittabhāvāvagamāt । paramasiddhāntī samarthayate&mdash;yata eva
vedānnimittabhāvāvagamo'yaṃ doṣaḥ <q>ata eva ca vaidikatvaṃ na brūmaḥ । kiṃ tarhi śiṣṭaprayoga
eva balavānityucyate vākyaśeṣānuguṇyāt । siddhe cāsya</q> śiṣṭaprayogasya anyato vākya-
śeṣānuguṇyādau<q>tpattikatve naiva tadvirodhinī mlecchapratipattirā<note n="(3)"> A. & B. add <dn>eva</dn></note>mātmānaṃ labhate । autpattika-
﻿<pb n="r103"/>
tayā gauṇenāpyarthena vyavahāropapatteḥ ।</q> nanu śiṣṭaprayoga eva kimiti gauṇo na bhavatī-
tyatrāha&mdash;<q>yadi vyavahārādeva dvayorautpattikatvakalpanā syāt tatretaretarāśrayatayā syāt
kalpanāvyāghātaḥ ।</q> āryavyavahāraprāmāṇyāt mlecchavyavahārasya vyāmohatvam । mlecchavyavahāra-

vyāghātaḥ । <q>atra tvanyataḥ śāstrīyasya prayogasya siddhamautpattikatvamityuktam ।</q>

gamyate ।</q> śabdasya vācyavācakaśaktya<q>numānavirodhāt ।</q> tasmāt gauṇo nāryavya-

﻿<pb n="r104"/>
<p><q>coditantu ।</q> pūrvādhikaraṇopajīvanena pūrvapakṣamāha&mdash;evamuk‍tena nyāyena yadyanāryavyavahāro
gauṇaḥ siddhaḥ <q>evaṃ tarhi ye śandāḥ āryavyavahāre nimittatayā na prasiddhāḥ teṣāmanimittataiva
vaidike vyavahāre syāt yathā pikanemasatatāmarasādīnāṃ</q>, anāryavyavahārasya śabdārthavya-
vasthāyāmakāraṇatvāt । āryavyavahāre ca teṣāmadaśanāt । anavadhāritanimittabhāvācca śabdāt
arthānavagateḥ nimittatā vedavyavahāre pikādiśabdānāṃ na syāt । <q>mābhūnnimittateti cet ।</q>
dūṣaṇamāha&mdash;tadevedaṃ codanāyā <q>aprāmāṇyaṃ prāpnoti</q>, yatpūrvamuktamanadhyavasāyalakṣaṇam ।
<q>nigamaniruk‍tavyākaraṇadivaśāt bhavatvarthāvagatiḥ</q> jarpharīprabhṛtīnāmiveti cet । dṛṣayati
<q>na tayorarthāvagatiḥ tayoḥ nigamaniruk‍tavyākaraṇayoḥ prayogamūlatvāt</q>&mdash;prayogādarśane
tayoreva nirmūlatvenānādaraṇīyatvāt ।</p>
﻿<pb n="r105"/>
<p>yadi prayogadarśanameva mūlaṃ tayoḥ <q>kathaṃ tarhi prakṛtipratyayārthohanam ।</q> ye'pi śabdā
loke dṛṣṭārthāḥ pragogamūlatvāt teṣāmapi prakṛtipratyayavibhāgāśrayaṇenārthehanaṃ nigamaniruk‍tavyā-
karaṇābhyāṃ kathaṃ kriyate jarpharīprabhṛtīnām । uttaram&mdash;<q>viniyogavaśādeva ।</q> etadeva
nivṛṇoti&mdash;<q>viniyuk‍tasya hi mantrasyā</q>vadhāritavākyatātparyasya <q>vākyaśeṣībhūtasya cārtha-
vādasyā</q>vadhāritatātparyasya <q>vṛddhavyavahāraprayogānuvarti prakṛtipratyayohanam । na punarūhyapada-
nimittaṃ vidhyuddeśavākyaṃ bhavitumarhati</q> tasya tātparyasyāvadhāraṇe pramāṇābhāvāt । yatra puna-
rūhyapadanimittaṃ vighyuddeśavākyaṃ tatrāpyanavasthaiva । <q>tasmāt</q> pikanemādipadamiśrāyāḥ <q>codanāyāḥ
aprāmāṇyam ।</q> rāddhāntamāha&mdash;satyamaprāmāṇyaṃ syāt <q>yadi sāmānyato dṛṣṭaṃ kāryānumāna-
virodhi syāt ।</q> pūrvapakṣe hi sāmānyatodṛṣṭamupanyastaṃ pikanemādiviṣayo'nāryavyavahāraḥ śabdārtha-
vyavasthāyāṃ animittaṃ, anāryavyavahāratvāt yavādiśabdaviṣayavaditi । tadetadyadi kāryānu-
mānamarthapratipattilakṣaṇāt kāryāt anāryavartināṃ yatpikādiśabdānāṃ kokilādivācakatbānumānaṃ
﻿<pb n="r106"/>
tannirākuryāt tadā syādaprāmāṇyam ? <q>atha tu yatraiva</q> yavādiviṣaye <q>pratyarthī</q> vedavākyaśeṣo
<q>vidyate tatraiva kāryānumānavirodhaḥ tadā vihatapratipakṣaṃ</q> kāryānumānaṃ <q>kena vāryate ।</q> yasya

nivāraṇaṃ bhaviṣyati । <note n="(1)"> A. <dn>tadāpi</dn></note>tadāha&mdash;<q>kiṃ punaḥ kāraṇaṃ sāmānyato dṛṣṭaṃ na bhavatīti ।</q>
uttaram&mdash;<q>sāmānyameva hi tanna syāt apratipakṣasiddhau ।</q> <note n="(2)"> A. <dn>satipratipakṣe anārtha</dn></note>sapratipakṣānāryavyavahāratvama-

siddhaṃ codanāyāḥ ।</q>
﻿<pb n="r107"/>
<p><q>prayogaśāstramiti cet । kiṃ punaḥ kāraṇaṃ pauruṣeyatayā siddhasya</q> prayogaśāstra-
syāna<q>pekṣatvamāśaṅkayate ।</q> māśakādīni pauruṣeyatvenaiva smaryante । yacca puruṣavākyaṃ
tatsāpekṣaṃ, ataḥ kathaṃ teṣāmanapekṣatvamāśaṅkayate । uttaram&mdash;<q>kāryataḥ pramāṇataścāśaṅkayate ।</q>
etadeva vivṛṇoti&mdash;<q>kāryaṃ paṭhitasya pāṭhaḥ śākhāntaravat । pramāṇaṃ punaḥ ācāryavacaḥ
pramāṇamiti ।</q> asyārthaḥ&mdash;yadidaṃ kāryaṃ paṭhitasyaiva vākyasya punaḥ pāṭhaḥ yathā
