ācāryavacaḥ pramāṇamityanenāpyanapekṣatvameva gamyate । <note n="(2)"> A. <dn>na hi pramāṇasya sāpekṣatvamasti</dn></note><q>na</q> hi sāpekṣasya prāmāṇyamasti ।
<q>nanu ca vipratiṣiddhamidaṃ pauruṣeyamanapekṣaṃ ceti ।</q> pariharati&mdash;<q>kimatra vipratiṣiddham ?
yathāvagamyante'rthāḥ tathā bhavanti । dvayaṃ cātrāvagamyate pauruṣeyatvamanapekṣatvaṃ ceti ।
smaraṇāt pauruṣeyatvaṃ</q> tenaiva tadupapadyate <q>kāryavacanābhyāmanapekṣatvam । tasmād‏dvayamastu ।</q>
<note n="(1)"> A. <dn>sāpekṣatvaṃ</dn></note>
﻿<pb n="r108"/>
atredamabhipretaṃ&mdash;ekaikaṃ vāk‏yaṃ vaidikameva tenānapekṣatvaṃ tāni tu nānāśākhāprakaraṇānārabhya-
vādaviprakīrṇāni puruṣeṇa naipuṇyāt anukrameṇa saṃhatya paṭhitānīti pauruṣeyatvam ।</p>
<p><q>nāsanniyamāt ।</q> rāddhāntamāha&mdash;<q>naitadupapadyate pauruṣeyatvamanapekṣatvaṃ ceti ।</q> na
ca vācyaṃ bhavatvapauruṣeyatvameveti yataḥ <q>siddhaṃ cāsya</q> prayogaśāstrasya <q>pauruṣeyatvaṃ</q> puruṣakūtatvena
smaraṇāt । <q>na ca kāṭhakādivat pravacanaparihāryam ।</q> yathā kāṭhakādisamākhyā
pravacanavaśenopapanna na tathā puruṣakṛtatvasmṛtiḥ । bhavatu puruṣakṛtatvameva tathāpi kimityāha&mdash;
<q>kṛtiścātra pramāṇāntaradṛṣṭārthābhidhānameva, na varṇādikāryatā ।</q> pramāṇāntareṇa yo dṛṣṭo'rthaḥ
tasya śabdenābhidhānaṃ tatparatvena śabdasya prayogo yaḥ saiva kṛtiḥ na punaḥ varṇādīnāṃ kāryatādi
﻿<pb n="r109"/>
nityatvādvarṇānāṃ varṇapadānupūrvyayośca vedepi dhvaninibandhanatvāt pauruṣeyatvameva । <q>tasmāt</q>
pauruṣeyatve siddhe <q>sāpekṣatvaṃ</q> tāvat duṣpariharam । <q>yatpunaḥ kāryamupanyastaṃ paṭhitasya
pāṭhaḥ śākhāntaravaditi</q> tatrocyate&mdash;<q>naitacchākhāntaratulyam ।</q> yathā śākhāntareṣu
sarvāṇyeva vāk‏yāni vaidikāni tathaiveha na bhavati vāk‏yāntaratvāt prayogaśāstravāk‏yānām ।
kathaṃ vāk‏yāntaratvaṃ ityatrāha&mdash;<q>prayogābhyāsaḥ kāryamasya svaravidhyarthavādaparisyāgāt</q>
svaravidhyarthavādān parityajya vāk‏yāntarāṇi kalpasūtrakāraiḥ praṇīyante vedāvagataprayogābhyāsāya
anuṣṭhātdṛṇām । tena vāk‏yāntarāṇyetāni arthavādasya vidheḥ svarāṇāṃ ca parityāgāt ।
sārthavādavidhisvareṇa vāk‏yena yo'rthaḥ pratipannaḥ tatraiva tadrahitāni vāk‏yāntarāṇi maśakādibhiḥ
praṇītāni । prayojanāntaraṃ cāha&mdash;<note n="(1)"> B. adds <dn>prayogaśāstraṃ prayogaśāstramiti</dn></note><q>tadānantaryapratītau padārthānāmavyavadhānamāvahati prayoga-
śāstram ।</q> padasvarādiparityāge hi vāk‏yasya śravaṇānantarameva padārthāḥ pratīyante ।﻿<pb n="r110"/>
avyavahitāśca pratīyamānāḥ sukhamanuṣṭhīyante iti paṭhitapāṭhaprayojanamācāryāṇām ।</q>
yata eva ca prayogābhyāsāya śīghrapratipattaye ca śāstramidam । <q>ata eva ca prayogaśāstramiti
vyapadiśyate<note n="(1)"> C. <dn>tathāṃ cānantaryaṃ</dn></note> ।</q> ata eva ca <q>kalpaśabdābhidheyatā । kalpanā hyatra padārthānāṃ na vidheyatvaṃ</q>,
racanā hyatra padārthānāṃ vedavihitānāmeva <q>na punarvidhānam ।</q> vidhānapakṣe kalpanāvyavahāro
nāstīti darśayati&mdash;<q>avagatasya</q> hi <q>klṛptirbhavati maṇeriva ।</q> yathā maṇerviracanā hāra-
grathanāya tathā'trāpi prayogagrathanāya racanā । yaduk‍taṃ&mdash;<q>ācāryavacaḥ pramāṇamiti pramāṇādava-
gamyata iti ।</q> tanna, asya vacanasyāsminnarthe'pramāṇatvāt । na hi vastusvarūpe śabda-
﻿<pb n="r111"/>
syānapekṣatvamastītyuktam । kintu kārye । tasmādanyaśeṣatvādasya vākyasya dṛṣṭānusāri
vyākhyānam ।</q> tatra <q>vedo vā ācāryaḥ</q> abhipretaḥ, yadvā ācāryāṇāṃ vacaḥ pramāṇamiti
pramāṇādavagamyaṃ satyārthaṃ tadabhipretam । tataścācāryavaco vedavacaḥ pramāṇamityuktam ।
atha vā <q>ācāryavaco</q> maśakādivaco yat tat <q>pramāṇam</q> satyamityarthaḥ । <q>kiṃ punaścintāyāḥ
prayojanam ?</q> ekagranthenāha&mdash;<q>vihitakalpanāparatvādasya śāstrasya na virodhamavagacchāmaḥ</q>
ya eva hi vihitāḥ padārthāḥ teṣāmeva racanāparatvādasya śāstrasya na vedavirodhaḥ saṃbhavati ।
uttaram&mdash;<q>astyatra vihitavirodhinī kalpanā sarvāsu tithiṣu darśapūrṇamāsādīnāṃ kalpanā ।
sā ca</q> kālaviśeṣasya paurṇamāsyādeḥ <q>śravaṇādviruddhayate । viruddhaṃ cānapekṣyaṃ</q> anādaraṇī-
yam <q>anyathāhyādare tena vyāghātādaprāmāṇyaṃ codanāyāḥ ।</q> tena vedavirodhe'nādaraṇīyatvaṃ
yathā syāditi sāpekṣatvaṃ kalpasūtrāṇāmucyate । tadādare hi ebhirvyāghātenāprāmāṇyamāpadyate
codanāyāḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="r112"/>
<p><q>anumānavyavasthānāt । iha tu vyavasthitaviṣayaṃ abyavasthitaṃ ca yat tatsardha-
mudāharaṇam ।</q> śākhāgṛhyasmṛtyācāragamyaṃ yatkilānuṣṭhānato<note n="(1)"> B. <dn>anupṭhānaṃ</dn></note>vyavasthitaviṣayaṃ kaiścidevānuṣṭhīyate
na sarvaiḥ । paramārthataścāvyavasthitam, vyavasthāyāṃ kāraṇābhāvāt tadihodāharaṇam ।
<q>kimidaṃ vyavasthitaviṣayamavyavasthitaṃ ceti ।</q> uttaram&mdash;<q>idamidam ।</q> eko'tredaṃśavda
uk‍taparaḥ । aparaśca vakṣyamāṇaparaḥ । yadidamuk‍taṃ tadidaṃ yadvakṣyāmaḥ । <q>prācyodīcyadākṣiṇā-
tyābhimāninaḥ kurvate</q> holākādīni । seyaṃ vyavasthā-prācyādīnāmidaṃ karma, vayaṃ ca prācyā
dayaḥ ityanenābhimānena holākādīni kurvate । na cāmimānasya niyāmakaṃ kiñcidastītyavyavasthā ।
﻿<pb n="r113"/>
kathaṃ punaḥ niyāmakaṃ nāsti ? uttaraṃ&mdash;vidhistāvanna niyāmakaḥ niyogārthamātraparyavasāyī-
hi saḥ ।</q> asyārthaḥ&mdash;ācāradarśanena yadvedavākyamanumīyate tadgatastāvadvidhiḥ na puruṣaviśeṣaṃ
prati tanniyāmakaḥ vidhimātraparatvāt । <q>karmaśabdo'pi holākādirna niyāmakaḥ karmaviśeṣā-
bhidhānāt । na cānyat kiñcit guṇo jātiḥ saṃsthānaṃ deśo vā niyāmakaḥ, tadabhāvāt ।</q>
yadīha anuṣṭhātṛmātravartī itarapuruṣavyāvṛtto guṇo jātirvā śarīrasanniveśo vā bhavet tato bhavenni-
yāmakaḥ । na cāsāvasti । <q>tathā samākhyāpi</q> dākṣiṇātyādikā na niyāmikā ।
<q>nanu yo yatra jātaḥ sa tena deśaviśeṣeṇa samākhyāyate prācya udīcyo dākṣiṇātya iti</q>
tena samākhyā niyāmikā bhavatu । pariharati&mdash;<q>na janmamātrāt samākhyeyamāgatādiṣvapi
﻿<pb n="r114"/>
tulyatvāt na niyāmikā samākhyā ।</q> nanu ca dakṣiṇāpathe jāta ityeṣā samākhyā
jātamātre bhavatīti sā niyāmikāstu ; ucyate, iyamapi na niyāmikā dākṣiṇātyasutaḥ
prāk‏kvacit jātaḥ paitṛkamevācāramanuvartate na prācyaṃ; tathā <q>itaro'pi itaratra jāta iti ।
lohitākṣādayastu niyāmakatvena vyabhicaritāḥ ।</q> tasmāt siddhamavyavasthitatvam ।</p>
<p><q>kiṃ punarasyāścintāyāḥ pramāṇalakṣaṇaupayikatvamasti ?</q> yeyaṃ holākādayaḥ padārthāḥ
prācyādibhireva kartavyāḥ uta sarvairiti asyāścintāyāḥ kiṃ pramāṇalakṣaṇaṃ pratyupāyatāsti yenātreya-
mārabdhā yāvatā tannāstyeva । uttaram&mdash;<q>kathaṃ vā nāsti</q> api tvastyeva । ākṣeptā
āha&mdash;<q>yadi niyāmakamasti yadi vā nāsti kiṃ jātamanapekṣatvasya ।</q> samādhātā āha
&mdash;<q>idameva vakṣyamāṇaṃ jātam । abhimāno vidyate na ca tasya mūlamupalabhyata ityaprāmāṇyaṃ
pūrvapakṣī manyate ।</q> yathābhūto'yamācāro'bhimānāliṅgito dṛśyate tathābhūtasya mūlaṃ codanā
na saṃbhavatīti kevalaholākādipratipādikā codanā ayathābhūtārthatayā na pramāṇam codanā tathā-
bhūtā na pramāṇam । atra ceyaṃ cintā&mdash;kiṃ yadyenānuṣṭhīyamānaṃ dṛśyate tattenaiva kartavyaṃ
utānyenāpi iti । sā viṣayaśuddhayarthatvena draṣṭavyā । <note n="(1)"> A. <dn>teṣāmevāvyavasthitamiti</dn></note>sarveṣāmanuṣṭheyamiti viṣayaṃ śodhayitvā
﻿<pb n="r115"/>
pūrvapakṣo hṛdi sthitaḥ <q>yadyavyavasthā aprāmāṇyaṃ</q> tarhi vedasyeti । <q>rāddhānte tu nābhimānaprabhavaṃ
vacanamiti parihṛtamaprāmāṇyam । yadi hi abhimānaprabhavaṃ vaidikaṃ vacanaṃ bhavet</q>
yādṛśo'bhimāno dṛśyate tādṛśo <q>vacanena</q> pratipādayitavyaḥ iti syāt । <q>tadā bhavedaprāmāṇyaṃ</q>
codanāyāḥ । na caitadasti svātantryāccodanāyā । <q>abhimānasya ca mūlaṃ nāstīti ।
bhavatvasau ayathārtho'bhimānaḥ ।</q> tathāpi karmasvarūpe codanāyāḥ prāmāṇyamastu tadāha&mdash;
<q>na punarayathārthatvaṃ codanāyāḥ śakyate'vagantum<note n="(1)"> <dn>vak‍tum</dn></note> ।</q></p>

﻿<pb n="r116"/>﻿<pb n="r117"/>
<p>prayogotpattyaśāstratvāt । <q>kathaṃ punaḥ vyākaraṇasmṛternirmūlatve sati vedasyā-
prāmāṇyaṃ śakya</q>māśaṅkituṃ yannivṛttyarthamidamadhikaraṇamārabhyate । ekagranthenāha&mdash;<q>yadi gāvyā-
dīnāmapyanādisattā syāt kiṃ jātaṃ codanāyāḥ । gavādiśabdā</q> apyasmin pakṣe
vācakā eva sāsnādimadādīnāṃ, na kevalaṃ gāvyādiśabdāḥ । tataśca sidhyatveva vedasya
prāmāṇyam । ucyate&mdash;<q>aśvagoṇyādiśabdānāṃ niyatārthatvaṃ smaranti vedavido vaiyākaraṇāḥ ।</q>
aśvaśabdo ghoṭakasyaiva vācako na niḥsvasya, goṇīśabda ścāvapanasyaiva vācakaḥ na goriti
vaiyākaraṇānāṃ smṛtiḥ । tataḥ phimityāha&mdash;<q>niyatārthatayā ca vedasya vyākhyānamapi kurvate ।</q>
ya evāsau ghoṭakāvapanādiḥ niyato'rthastadarthatayaiva vedagatānapyaśvādiśabdān vyācakṣate aśvamā-
﻿<pb n="r118"/>
labhetetyādiṣu । <q>yadi ca vyākaraṇaṃ pramāṇaṃ bhavet tadedatupapannaṃ syāt nirmūlatve</q> tu
sati niyatanimittārthatā niṣpramāṇikā prāpnoti । codayati&mdash;<q>bhavatu kā no bādhā ।</q> uttaraṃ
<q>&mdash;aniyatanimittako vedārthaḥ prāp‍noti tataścānadhyavasāyādaprāmāṇyaṃ syāt ।</q> aśvādi-
śabdo hi vede śrūyate upapadaprakaraṇādyabhāve prayogasaṃśayaḥ syāt । kiṃ ghoṭakādiparatvenāyaṃ
prayuk‍taḥ uta nisvādiparatveneti । tataścānadhyavasāyenāprāmāṇyaṃ syāt vyākaraṇasmṛternirmūlatve ।
samūlatve tu ghoṭādiparatvenaiva niścayādadhyavasāye sati yuktameva prāmāṇyaṃ codanāyāḥ । nanu
cobhayatra sādhutvepi śāstrasthanyāyena gauṇo nisvādiṣu prayogo bhaviṣyati, mukhyaśca ghoṭādiṣu, tena
mukhyārthagrahaṇenādhyavasāyo bhaviṣyatītyatrāha&mdash;<q>na ca śāstrasthanyāyo'tra <note n="(1)"> B. adds <dn>sādṛśyādgauṇo'tra</dn></note>saṃbhavati</q> gauṇamukhya-
viveke kāraṇābhāvāt । tatra hi vākyaśeṣānuguṇyādāryavyavahāratya mukhyatvamitarasya ca
gauṇatvamiti । iha tu vākyaśeṣo'pi nāsti । tathā tatra sādṛśyādgauṇīvṛttiḥ । iha tu
āvapanādīnāṃ gavādibhissaha sādṛśyaṃ nopalabhyate<note n="(2)"> A. adds <dn>gauṇamukhyaviveko nopalabhyate ।</dn></note> । tasmācchāstrasthanyāyenātra durlabhaḥ
﻿<pb n="r119"/>
tasmādvayākaraṇanibandhana evādhyavasāyaḥ । atastasya vyākaraṇasyopapattiḥ vicāraṇīyā ।
tadidaṃ vicāryate-kiṃ gaurityevamādīnāmanāditvaṃ sāsnādimati, gāvyādīnāṃ cādimatteti ।</q>
pratiyoginī cātra vacanavyaktiḥ&mdash;ubhayeṣāmapyanāditeti । etadeva bhāṣyaṃ vyācaṣṭe&mdash;<q>kimiyaṃ
smṛtiḥ saṃbhavanmūlā neti vicāryate ।</q> yadi vyākaraṇasmṛtiḥ saṃbhavanmūlā tadā sāsnādi-
mati gavādīnāmevānāditā । atha na, tadā abhayeṣāmapyanāditeti । <q>kiṃ tāvatprāptaṃ ?</q>
pūrvapakṣaṃ parigṛhṇāti-<q>āstāṃ tāvanmūlamūlicintā, śabdānuśāsanameva tāvadaniyatārtham ।
keyamaniyatārthatā'</q>nuśāsanasya ? uttaram&mdash;<q>iyamaniyatārthatā prayoganiyamārthaṃ hītaṃ śās‍traṃ</q>,
gavādīnāmeva sāsnādimati prayogaḥ sādhuḥ na gāvyādīnāmiti niyamārthamidaṃ śāstram । na
cānena <q>prayogo niyantu śakyate । atha prayogādeva prayoganiyamaḥ ।</q> yasya prayogo loke'sti
sa eva sādhuriti cet । dūṣayati&mdash;<q>siddhaṃ tarhi gāvyādīnāmapi sāsnādimatyanāditvam ।</q>
﻿<pb n="r120"/>
<p>teṣāmapi loke prayuk‍tatvāt । <q>kathaṃ punaḥ</q> vyākaraṇena <q>prayogo niyantuṃ na
śakyate ?</q> uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>itthaṃ na śakyate । prathamaṃ tāvadidamanuśāsanaṃ dhātoḥ pare pratyayā
bhavantīti । te ca kecit kartari</q> yathā tṛjādayaḥ । <q>kecitkarmaṇi</q> yathā tavyadādayaḥ
<q>kecit kartṛvarjiteṣu sarvakārakeṣu</q> yathā ghañādayaḥ ।</p> vyākaraṇecādhyāyadvayena pūrveṇa
sākṣācchabdānuśāsanaṃ na kriyata iti matvok‍tam । prathamaṃ tāvadidamanuśāsanamiti
<q>taccedaṃ sarvamanupapannam । kathamanupapannam ? evamanupapannam । dhātoḥ</q> pare pratyayā
bhavantītyucyate । ko nāmāyaṃ dhātuḥ yataḥ pratyayā bhavanti । rāddhāntyāha﻿<pb n="r121"/>
&mdash;nanu ca bhūvādayo dhātava ityanena sūtreṇa kāṃścicchabdān kayācit paripāṭyā paṭhitvā
dhātava iti saṃjñā kṛtā । atastayā dhātusaṃjñayā ye saṃjñino lakṣyante te bhyaḥ pare pratyayā
bhavantīti kiṃ nopapadyate ।</q></p>
<p>pūrvapakṣī dūṣayati&mdash;<note n="(1)"> B. <dn>gaṇḍayati</dn></note><q>gaṇḍatītyevamādīnāmapi sādhutvaṃ prāpnoti ।</q> na ceṣyate ।
kathaṃ punarasya sādhutvaprasaktiḥ ? ucyate bhavatīti bhūḥ iti k‍vip । kkibveti kviṣi kṛte <quote>“kvi-
bantā dhātutvaṃ na ahati”</quote> iti smṛteḥ <quote>“dhātvarthaḥ kevalaḥ śuddhaḥ bhāva ityabhidhīyate”</quote> iti
smaraṇāt bhāve lakāraḥ prāpnoti । tataścātmanepade yaki ca kṛte bhūyata iti prasajyate ।
ghaṭaśabdasya ca dhātvarthībhūta <note n="(2)"> B. reads <dn>kartṛ</dn></note>bhavitṛviśeṣaṇatvāt kriyāviśeṣaṇānāṃ karmatvaṃ napuṃsakatvaṃ ceti
smaraṇāt <note n="(3)"> C. <dn>vedamiti</dn></note>ghaṭamiti prasajyate । atra ca yadi ghaṭamiti na pradarśyate tadā bhūyata iti sādhutva-
prasaṅga ityucyamāne kasyacidiyamāśaṅkā syāt astyeva bhūyata ityasya sādhutvaṃ bhavateḥ bhāve-
lakārotpattāviti tannivṛttaye kartṛsādhanakvibante'pi bhūyata iti prāpnotīti darśayituṃ ghaṭamiti prayuk‍ta-
vān । <q>tathā sattādīnāmapi tārtīyapratyayaprasaṅgaḥ ।</q> bhū sattāyāmityatra sattāśabdasyāpi
﻿<pb n="r122"/>
paṭhitatvāt dhātusaṃjñāyāṃ satyāṃ tṛtīyādhyāyok‍tapratyayaprasaṅgaḥ । <q>anārṣaḥ sattādīnāṃ pāṭhaḥ</q>
bhūśabdādimātrasyaiva ārṣapāṭhe sati teṣāmeva dhātusaṃjñā na sattādīnā<q>miti cet ।</q> dūṣayati
<q>&mdash;bhavatvapyayaṃ parihāraḥ</q> sattādīnāṃ tārtīyapratyayāprasaṅge । <q>gaṇḍati</q> ghaṭaṃ bhūyata <q>ityevamādīnāṃ
punaraprayoga eva</q> parihāraḥ । atra ca bhavatvapītyapiśabdādetaddarśayati&mdash;anārṣatve pramāṇā-
bhāvāt na bhavatyevāyaṃ parihāraḥ । tathāpyabhyupagamyāpyucyate gaṇḍatyādiṣu tāvadayaṃ parihāro na
saṃbhavatīti । <q>atha kriyāvacano dhāturityucyate</q> tena gaḍervadanaikadeśe vartamānasya dhātusaṃjñā na
bhavati tadabhāvācca gaṇḍatīti na sādhuḥ syāt ; tathā kartari vartamānasya kvibantasya bhavateḥ dhātu-
saṃjñābhāvaḥ । tathā sattādīnāmapi iti na pūrvoktadoṣaprasaṅgaḥ । dūṣaṇamāha&mdash;<q>na, bhavati
tiṣṭhatītyevamādīnāmaprayogaḥ ।</q> bhavatyādīnāmakriyārthatvāt, <q>gaṇḍateśca pāṭho'narthakaḥ ।</q>
akriyāvacanatvena dhātusaṃjñā'bhāvāt tadarthatvācca gaṇapāṭhasya । <q>akriyāpi k‍vacit pratīyata
iti cet ।</q> asyārthaḥ&mdash;kvacidakriyāpi vyākaraṇe kriyāvat pratīyate svīkriyate । tena
﻿<pb n="r123"/>
bhavatyādīnāṃ <note n="(1)"> B. reads <dn>sādhutvaṃ</dn></note>dhātutvamiti cet । dūṣayati&mdash;<q>prayogāttarhi niyamaḥ na kriyātaḥ prayogaḥ ।</q>
iyamakriyāpi kriyāvadvayākaraṇe svīkriyata iti tābadvayākaraṇe smṛtirnāsti । kintu prayogaṃ
dṛṣṭvedamāśravaṇīyaṃ na punaḥ pūrvasiddhaṃ kriyātvamāśritya prayoganiyamaḥ । <q>kriyāvagatimātraṃ niyāma-
kamiti cet ।</q> asyārthaḥ, kriyāvagatimātraṃ dhātusaṃjñāyāṃ hetuḥ । vastuvṛttena kriyā vā bhavatu
akriyā vā; tena bhavatyādīnāmapi dhātutvamiti cet ; <q>nādhyāropānadhyāropayostulyatāvagatiḥ</q>
uk‍taṃ prathamapāde adhyārope avagatireva nāstīti । agrahaṇameva bhrāntiriti ।
tenākriyāyāṃ kriyāvagatireva nāstīti agrahaṇameva bhrāntiriti । viparītakhyātivādimate
syāṃdapyevam । nirākṛtā ca sā nayavīthīprakaraṇe । <q>tasmādidamapi na niyāmakam ।
pāṭhakriyāvacanābhyāṃ <note n="(2)"> C. <dn>niyama iti</dn></note>niyamyata iti cet</q> etacca yathāsaṃbhavaṃ vikalpābhiprāyeṇāśaṅkitam ।
﻿<pb n="r124"/>
dūṣayati&mdash;<q>tatrāpyetad‍dvayaṃ samuditaṃ sat niyāmakaṃ uta vyastamiti vak‍tavyam । tatra
samuditapakṣe gaṇḍatimavatyādīnāṃ tathaiva vyudāsaḥ ।</q> satyapi pāṭhe'kriyāvacanatvāt ।
atha <q>pratyekamiti cet</q> pāṭhādapi dhātusaṃjñā । tathā kriyāvacanatvādapīti cet । dūṣayati
&mdash;<q>pacatyādīnāṃ pāṭhānarthakyam ।</q> vināpi pāṭhena kriyāvacanatvenāpi dhātusaṃjñāsiddheḥ ।
<q>āgamayatyādīnāṃ nivṛttyarthamiti cet</q> siddhāyāmapi kriyāvacanatvena dhātusaṃjñāyāṃ yaḥ pacatyā-
dīnāṃ pāṭhaḥ sa niyamārthaḥ । kriyāvacanatvepi paṭhitānāmeva dhātusajñā yathā syāt nāgamayatyādī-
nāmiti cet । dūṣayati&mdash;<q>ubhayaṃ <note n="(1)"> C. <dn>tarhyatallakṣaṇaṃ</dn></note>tarhyāśritaṃ</q> lakṣaṇam । <q>sa eva bhavatyādiṣu doṣaḥ ।</q>
ubhayalakṣaṇatve । <q>tasmāllakṣa</q>ṇasyāniyāmakatve <q>punarapi prayoga eva śaraṇam ।</q> tasya ca
tulyatvānna niyama iti ।</p>
﻿<pb n="r125"/>
<p><q>tathākārakaniyamāsiddhiḥ ।</q> ekagranthenāha&mdash;<q>dhruvamapāye'pādānamiti dhruvatayā-

<q>athāyamabhiprāyaḥ, <quote>‘sārthāddhīnaḥ’</quote> <quote>‘rathāt patita’</quote> ityatra sārtharathayoḥ kriyā vidyata iti</q>
kārakatvamiti । dūṣayati&mdash;<q>nāsti kriyā sārthasya rathasya ca</q> hone patane ca । <q>kintu

kartā pacatītyasya kārakamabasīyate । tasmānniṣkriyaṃ kārakamiti badato</q> vaiyākaraṇasya

pūrvorkto doṣo na bhaviṣyatīti । dūṣayati&mdash;<q>kimasau</q> <note n="(1)"> C. <dn>dhātvarthaḥ</dn></note>rucyarthoṃ nirviṣaya eva । uttaraṃ&mdash;
<q>na nirviṣayaḥ yadyasmai rocate tasya tadviṣayo rucyarthaḥ ।</q> pratyuttaram-<q>avagatastarhi; modakā-
bhidhānāt ।</q> modakeṣvabhihiteṣu viṣayabhūteṣu viṣayiṇi rucyarthāvagatirasti । avagate ca
tasmin tadyoga eva caturthīti punarapi devadattāya modakā dīyantāmiti na prāp‍noti । dhātū-
ccāraṇaṃ saṃpradānasaṃjñānibandhanamiti cet । dūṣayati&mdash;<q>devadattāya modakāḥ kiṃ rocante iti

&mdash; na tadapekṣā prayuk‍tiḥ । kṛtaḥ ? <q>praśnottarānupapatteḥ ।</q> yadi tadapekṣaiva prayuk‍tiḥ tadā

﻿<pb n="r134"/>
tatrāha&mdash;<q>praśnanirākaraṇārthaṃ hi taduccāraṇaṃ na caturthīprayogasya sādhutvāya ।</q> tasmāt

syāt । vibhaktivyatyayānuśāsanasya <note n="(1)"> A. reads <dn>vyākaraṇe vedavākyārtha</dn> etc.</note>vyākaraṇavākyārthāvagamapūrvakatvāt <q>tatsiddheḥ tadavagamāt ।</q>

tiḍpratyayena nocyanta iti ।</q> uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>uktaṃ bhagavatā bhāṣyakāreṇa</q> patañ‍jalinā <q>bhūte dhātvarthe</q>

﻿<pb n="r136"/>
kathamasmāt taddhitasamāsayoḥ nirūpaṇamaśakyamityatrāha&mdash;<q>ekārthānvayitā ca sāmarthyam ।</q> ya

﻿<pb n="r137"/>
marhatīti । <q>tathā arthavadadhāturapratyayaḥ prātipadikamityatrāpi kiṃ kāryamarthavatvaṃ</q>,

<q>iti</q> vārtikaṃ <q>na ghaṭate । athautpattikamarthavatvaṃ tatkathanaparatvācchāstrasya na <note n="(2)"> <dn>śās‍trārthopāyatvaṃ</dn></note>śāstrārthau-
payikatvaṃ siddhayati ।</q> kimayaṃ śabdo gavādirarthavān na gāvyādirityetatkathanāya vyākaraṇaṃ

cedaṃ sūtre upeyamūlaṃ cetītaretarāśrayam । evaṃ cet</q> prātipadikameva na nirṇītam ।
<q>tannibandhane ca svarakāryapratyayavidhānaṃ ca na siddhayati । adhāturapratyaya iti cāvaya-
vātirekaḥ ।</q> asyārthaḥ । arthavadadhāturapratyayaḥ prātipadikamityasya sūtrasyāyamarthaḥ ।
arthavacchabdarūpaṃ dhātupratyayavyatirik‍taṃ prātipadikasaṃjñaṃ bhavatīti । atra ca apratyaya ityanena
pratyayamātrasya vyudāsaḥ na pratyayāntasya, antagrahaṇābhāvāt । na ca viśeṣaṇatvena kasyacit
pratyayaśabdaḥ prayuktaḥ yataḥ yenavidhiḥ iti tadantagrahaṇaṃ syāt, svarūpaparatvenāpi pratyayaśabdo-
vapatteḥ । saṃjñāvidhau ca pratyayagrahaṇe tadantavidhirnāstīti suptiḍantaṃ padamityatra pratipāditam ।
saṃjñāvidhirevāyaṃ na saṃjñāpratiṣedhaḥ paryudāsenaikavākyatvāt । tathā ca vṛttikāro'pi paryudāsameva
darśayati pūrvasūtre'pratyaya iti paryudāsāt । <quote>“kṛdantasya taddhitāntasya cānena prātipadikasaṃjñā
vidhīyata”</quote> iti kṛttaddhitasūtre vadati ।</p>
﻿<pb n="r138"/>
<p>nanu yadi pratyayamātraparyudāso'yaṃ kathaṃ tarhi uttarasūtre apratyaya iti paryudāsāt
kṛdantasya taddhitāntasya ca saṃjñāvidhiḥ, pratyayāntasya saṃjñāpratiṣedhe hi pratiprasavo'yaṃ kṛdantasya
taddhitāntasya ceti bhavet । ucyate, imāmevāśaṅkāṃ nirākartumidamuktam । <quote>“pūrvasūtre apratyaya
iti paryudāsāt kṛdantasya taddhitāntasya cānena saṃjñā vidhīyata”</quote> iti । asyārthaḥ । yadi
kṛnmātrasya taddhitamātrasya ca prātipadikasaṃjñā vidhīyeta tataḥ pūrvasūtre'pratyayagrahaṇaṃ na kartavyaṃ
syāt niyamenaiva vyāvṛtteḥ-yadi pratyayasya prātipadikasaṃjñā syāt tadā kṛttaddhitasyaiveti । kṛtaṃ
cāpratyayagrahaṇam । tato'vagacchāmaḥ kṛdantasya taddhitāntasya ca saṃjñā vidhīyate iti । yetu
pratyayāntasya saṃjñāpratiṣedhaṃ varṇayanti teṣāṃ pratyayamātrasya prātipadikasaṃjñā prasajyamānā kena
vāryate ।</p>
<p>tadevaṃ sthite sūtrārthe dūṣaṇamucyate&mdash;adhāturapratyaya iti <q>cāvayavātirekaḥ</q> iti ।
ekagranthenāha-<q>kimanena vyāvatyate ?</q> rāddhāntī vadati&mdash;<q>dhātorarthavattvepi pratyayasya prāti-
padikasaṃjñā mā bhūdityevamarthavada</q>dhāturapratyaya ityuk‍tam । pūrvapakṣī dūṣayati&mdash;yadyevaṃ <q>prāti-
svikamarthavattvamāśritya ādhāturapratyaya ityuk‍tam vākyasya</q> tarhi <q>prātipadikasaṃjñā
prāpnoti ।</q> tasyāpi prātisvikārthayogitvāt । <q>samāsagrahaṇaṃ tannivṛttyarthamiti cet</q>
arthavattvena prātipadikatve siddhepi yat samāsagrahaṇaṃ tanniyamārtham tena vākyasya na
bhavatīti cet । dūṣayati&mdash;<q>adhāturapratyayagrahaṇamanarthakam ।</q> tayorapi niyamena vyāvarti-
<q>tatvāt ।</q> tadāha&mdash;<q>tasyāpi samāsagrahaṇānnivṛtteḥ । ekārthatve sati nivartakaṃ nārthāntare</q>
﻿<pb n="r139"/>
iti cet</q> samāsaparisaṅkhayāyāṃ hi samānajātīyasya nivṛttaḥ vākyasamāsayoścaikārthatvena samā-
seṃna sajātīyatvamiti vākyasyaiva tena nivṛttiḥ nārthāntaravādino ghātoḥ pratyayasya cetyarthavadadhātura-
pratyayagrahaṇamiti cet । dūṣayati&mdash;<q>tadayuktam samāsasyāpyarthāntarābhyupagamāt ।</q> vāvaca-
nānarthakyaṃ manvānena kātyāyanena samāsavikalpārthavibhāṣāgrahaṇapratyākhyānāya vākyasamāsayorane-
kārthatvamuk‍tam । tena vākyasyāpi nivṛttirnopapadyate । atha vijātīyasya vākyasya nivṛttiḥ
tadā dhātupratyayayorapi syāt । <q>athārthavatsamudāyanirākaraṇatayā samāsagrahaṇaṃ;</q> samāso
hi arthabatsamudāyaḥ tena ca samānajātīyaṃ vākyaṃ arthavatsamudāyaṃ nivartayati, na dhātumātraṃ
pratyayamātraṃ vā । dūṣayati&mdash;<q>kṛttaddhitagrahaṇaṃ tarhi na kartavyam ।</q> tatkila evamartha
kriyate । samāsagrahaṇenārthavatsamudāye nivartamāne kṛdantasya taddhitāntasya ca nivṛttiḥ
prāpnoti sā mābhūditi । yadi samānajātīyasyaiva nivṛttiḥ tadā arthavatsamudāyātmakatvāt
samāsasya arthavatpadasamudāyātmakavākyasyaiva nivṛttyā bhavitavyam । na kṛdantataddhitāntayoḥ ।
tataśca <note n="(1)"> B. <dn>kṛtaṃ kṛttaddhitagrahaṇena</dn></note>kṛttaddhitagrahaṇamatiricyata eva । nanu ca kṛttaddhitagrahaṇaṃ kṛnmātrasya taddhita-
mātrasya ca saṃjñārthaṃ bhaviṣyatītyatrāha&mdash;<q>tatrāpi kṛdantāśca taddhitāntāśca</q> prātipadika-
saṃjñā bhavantītyabhidhānāta <q>samudāya eva</q> saṃjñī <q>iṣyate ।</q> yathā ca samudāyasya saṃjñitva-
siddhiḥ tethok‍tameva । yata eva svayaṃ vyākaraṇasya vyākulatā anaḥ <q>prayogasyābhyupāyatā
durghaṭā ।</q> na kevalaṃ vyākaraṇaṃ durghaṭaṃ upāyabhāvo'pi tasya prayogaṃ prati durghaṭaḥ । kasmāt

śabdārthe draṣṭavyaḥ । <q>duruk‍tānuk‍tanirīkṣaṇaṃ ca vyākhyātṛṇāṃ lakṣaṇe</q> prayoga <q>eva</q> prayoganipramaṃ

mūlabhūtaṃ prayogaṃ jānīyuḥ kathamativyāpakaṃ sūtraṃ praṇayeyuḥ । tenātivyāpakasūtrapraṇayanājjñāyate

pekṣāṇi santi svārthe prayujyante tadā laukikānyucyante । yadā nirapekṣāṇi tadā vaidikāni
ityanena bhedamāśrityānuśāsanaṃ vyākaraṇe śrūyate <quote>“bhāṣāyāṃ”</quote> <quote>“chandasī”</quote> ti ca ।</p>
<p><q>prayogacodanā ।</q> atra bhāṣyakāraḥ evaṃ vicāraṃ varṇayati । kimākṛtiḥ śabdārthaḥ
uta byak‍tiriti । tadayuk‍tam&mdash;yatyaro hi śabdaḥ sa śabdārthaḥ kāryaparatvaṃ ca sarvaśabdā&mdash;
nāmiti tatrāha&mdash;<q>uk‍taṃ tadbhūtānāṃ kriyārthena samāpnāya iti</q> tadidaṃ vicāryate-kva <q>bhūtānā-
miti na vipnaḥ kipākṛtau bhūtānāṃ</q> kāryaparatvaṃ uta vyak‍tau bhūtānāmiti । svārthe hi
vartamānāni padāni kāryamarthaṃ prati tātparyaṃ bhajante tatra vicāryate kutra vartamānānāṃ kāryaparatā
﻿<pb n="r153"/>
kimākṛtau vartamānānāṃ uta vyak‍tāniti । nimittabhūtārthacinteyam&mdash;kimākṛtiḥ śabdārthaḥ
uta vyak‍tiriti । <q>nanu ca yadyasmātpratīyate sa tadbhūtaḥ</q> ākṛtiścātrāvagamyate iti
bhāṣyakāro vakti । tena ākṛtibhūtatvameva । kathamatra saṃśayaḥ ? samādhatte&mdash;<q>ubhayaṃ cāsmāt
pratīyate</q> ākṛtivyaktyātmakam । yadyubhayamasmātpratīyate <q>kathaṃ tarhi</q> bhāṣyakāreṇok‍taṃ
<q>sāmānyapratyayādvayaktau ca kriyāsaṃbhavāditi ।</q> samādhātā āha&mdash;<q>kiṃcātra nopapadyate</q> yena
pṛcchasi ? ākṣeptā āha&mdash;<q>idaṃ nopapadyate vyak‍tau ca kriyāsaṃbhavāditi । kriyāsaṃbhavo hi
vyak‍tau tad‍bhūtatve heturutaḥ</q> na punaḥ pratyayaḥ । samādhātā āha&mdash;<q>kimanenāvagamo nirastaḥ ?</q>
na nirasta iti bhāvaḥ । akṣeptā āha&mdash;omityucyate । nirasta eva vyak‍tāvavagamaḥ
<q>ākṛtāvavagamābhidhānāt ।</q> yadi hi ubhayorapyavagamaḥ syāt tadā ākṛtibhūtatve avagamo
﻿<pb n="r154"/>
hetutvena noktaḥ syāt, anaikāntikatvāt । samādhātā āha&mdash;<q>agranthajño devānāṃ priyaḥ</q>
ākṣeptā pṛcchati&mdash;<q>kā'trāgranthajñatā ?</q> uttaraṃ samādhātuḥ&mdash;<q>iyamagranthajñateti ।</q> ekagranthe-
nāha&mdash;kriyārthena <q>samāmnāyaḥ</q> sarvapadānā<q>mityuk‍tam । kriyārthatayā ca tad‍bhūtatvaṃ nirūpi-
tam ।</q> yadapi svārthavartitvaṃ tadapi kriyārthatayā, svārthābhidhānadvārakaṃ hi kriyārthatvamiti ।
svārthābhidhānaṃ padaiḥ kriyate; vyak‍teśca kriyārthatā saṃbhavati nākṛteḥ <q>na cāpratītaṃ kriyārtha
bhavatīti vyak‍tāveva tad‍bhūtatvam</q> vyak‍timeva gavādiśabdaḥ pratipādayatītyarthaḥ । ida-
matrākṛtam&mdash;vyak‍tau ca kriyāsaṃbhavādityanena bhāṣyeṇa kriyāsaṃbhavapradarśanena vyak‍terevapratipādyatva-
miti darśitam । na punaḥ kriyāsaṃbhavamātram । yadi vyak‍tereva kriyāsaṃbhavaḥ avagatiśca,
<q>sāmānyāvagamastarhi kathaṃ ?</q> uttaram&mdash;astītyanena bhāṣyeṇa kriyārthatvasaṃbhavapradarśanena astī-
﻿<pb n="r155"/>
tyetāvacchakyate vak‍tuṃ na punaḥ kriyārthatayā tad‍bhūtatvam । nanu sāmānyāvagatau satyāṃ
vyak‍tāvavagamo na prāpnoti</q> bhinnatbāttayoḥ yadi śabdāt sāmānyāvagamaḥ tarhi vyaktyavagamo
na prāp‍noti bhinnatvāttayoḥ । pariharati&mdash;<q>aho batānubhavepyanavamarśaḥ !</q> etadeva vivṛṇoti
&mdash;yadi vyaktirnāvagamyate kasya saṃbandhinaḥ sāmānyamiti nābagamyate । kasmādityāha
&mdash;saṃbandhyantarasavyapekṣa<q>syāvagamaḥ ।</q> na kasyacitsaṃbandhitayā sāmānyamavagamyata ityarthaḥ ।
nanu mā nāma saṃbandhitayāvagamyatāṃ tathāpi kā kṣatirityatrāha&mdash;<q>saṃbandhitayā hyanavagamyamānaṃ
sāmānyaṃ sāmānyamiti nāvagamyate ।</q> kasmādityāha&mdash;<q>sambandhyantarasāpekṣā hi saṃba-
ndhini buddhirbhavati</q> saṃbandhisvabhāvaṃ ca sāmānyamiti saṃbandhitvenānavagamyamānamanavagamyamānameva<note n="(1)"> B. <dn>anavagatamena</dn></note>
syāt । <q>viśeṣatastvatra rūparūpitayā</q> saṃbandhitā <q>nāvagamyate</q> sāmānyaṃ hi rūpa tena vyak‍teḥ
rūpyamāṇatvāt rūpiṇī vyaktiḥ । <q>na hi rūpiśūnyā rūpe buddhirasti । yadi syāt rūpataiva na
syāt ।</q> svatantrapadārthātmakatā āpadyetetyarthaḥ । yadi vyak‍tāvapyavagamo'sti <q>kimiti
﻿<pb n="r156"/>
tarhi bhedenopanyāsaḥ</q> sāmānye pratyayāt vyak‍tau ca kriyāsaṃbhavāditi । uttaram&mdash;<q>kriyārthatvena
rūpasyānanvayapradarśanārthaḥ</q> vyak‍tāveva kriyā saṃbhavati nākṛtau kevalaṃ tatrāvagamamātramiti bhedeno-
panyāsaḥ । sāmānye pratyayāt vyak‍tau kriyāsaṃbhavāditi । bhavatu <note n="(1)"> <dn>kriyārthena</dn></note>kriyārthatvenānanvayaḥ
tathāpi kimityāha&mdash;<q>na cānanvitasya śabdārthatvaṃ yuk‍tam pañjarasyeva siṃhamānayeti
pañjarasthāvagatau ।</q> yena hi pañjarastha eva siṃho'vagataḥ tasya siṃhamānayeti yadyapi
pañjarāvagatirbhavati tathāpi pañjarasya na śabdārthatvaṃ, ānayatau tasyānanvitatvāt । evamatrāpi
kriyārthānanvitatvenākṛteḥ na śabdārthatvam । yadyananvitasya śabdārthatvaṃ na saṃbhavati <q>kimiti</q>
tarhi sāmānye pratyayādityupanyāsaḥ ? uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>amumeva vakṣyamāṇamarthaṃ pradarśayitum ।</q>
na tvākṛteḥ । kamartham ? uttaram&mdash;<q>ananvitanimittatayā aprāmāṇyābhidhānamākṛti-
vādināṃ</q> ye sāmānyasyāvagamamātreṇa śabdārthatvamicchanti tairevāvagamamātreṇānvayamantareṇā<note n="(2)"> <dn>anvaye'nādareṇa</dn></note>-
aśabdārthatvādananvitanimittatayā codanāyā aprāmāṇyamabhihitaṃ bhavatīti darśayitum । nanvā-
kṛtereva kriyānvayaḥ ityatrāha&mdash;<q>vyak‍teścānvayamicchanti vrīhīn prokṣatītyevamādiṣu
﻿<pb n="r157"/>
ākṛtivādino'pi । nanu yathā ākṛtivādināmaprāmāṇyaṃ tathā vyak‍tivādināmapītyāha
<q>&mdash;vyak‍titad‍bhūtapakṣe vā kimanapekṣatvaṃ siddhayati ?</q> na śiddhayatyeveti bhāvaḥ ।
uttaram&mdash;<q>siddhayatu vā māvā apanyāyāśrayaṇaṃ tāvajjātivādinaḥ</q> ananvitāyā jāteḥ
śabdārthatvābhyupagamāt । <q>vyak‍tipakṣe tu kāryānurūpā kāraṇakalpanā nyāyyā ।</q> vyak‍ti-
pratipattiḥ kāryabhūtā yathā śaṃbdānnirvahati tathā kāraṇaṃ kalpayituṃ nyāyyam । <q>nanu ca kathamayaṃ</q>
vyak‍tyabhidhāna<q>pakṣo nyāyyaḥ yasmāt<note n="(1)"> C. <dn>yasya</dn></note> vṛddhavyavahāraparaṃparā na vyutpattau kāraṇatāṃ pratipat‍tuṃ
śak‍noti । kathaṃ na śak‍noti ?</q> uttaram&mdash;<q>anvayavyatirekāśrayo</q> hi vṛddhavyavahāro'va-

vyatireke ca na prayujyate sa tasya śabdasyārthaḥ । tathā yasya śabdasyānvaye yo'rthaḥ pratīyate vyatireke
ca na pratīyate tasya śabdasyāsāvartho'vagamyate । <q>tau cāvayavyatirekau</q> vṛddhavyavahārāśrayau vṛddha-
vyavahāre cānvayavgatirekau <q>sāmānyanibandhanau</q> na vyaktinibandhanau vyaktyantarepi śabda-
prayogāt śabdaprayoge ca vyaktyantarapratīteḥ । sāmānye ca sati śabdāprayogāt, śabde ca
prayuk‍te sāmānyaṃ pratīyate । tena vṛddhavyavahāre tāvadvayak‍tinimittatā nāvagantuṃ śakyate ।
<q>na ca vṛddhavyavahārādanyat vyutpattikāraṇamupalabhāmahe karturasmaraṇā</q>tsaṃbandhasya । yadi hi
saṃbandhasya kartā smaryeta tadā saṅketavaśenaiva vyutpattiḥ syāt । na ca kartā smaryata <q>ityuk‍tam ।</q>
﻿<pb n="r158"/>
<p><q>nanu cākṛtāvapi tad‍bhūtatvaṃ</q> padānāmāmnāyasya kriyārthatvāditi nirākṛtam
ākṛteḥ kriyānvayitvābhāvāditi । ekagranthenāha&mdash;<q>kiṃ punaranayora</q>kriyārthatvavṛddhavyavahārā-
<note n="(1)"> C. <dn>rānuyāyitva</dn></note>nanuyāyitvayoḥ <q>balīyaḥ ?</q> akriyārthatvādākṛteraśabdārthatvaṃ pratibhāti । vṛddhavyavahārānanu<note n="(2)"> C. <dn>nupāyitva</dn></note>-
yāyitvādvayak‍teḥ tatra kasya balīyastvam ? uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>kāryaṃ balīya iti vrūmaḥ</q> kasmādityāha&mdash;

nyāyyā । <q>vṛddhavyavahārādi ca tad‍bhūtatayā saha kāraṇaṃ</q> vṛddhavyavahārādikaṃ tadbhatatvaṃ ca
kāraṇakoṭinikṣiptaṃ <q>kāryataścāsannataraṃ tad‍bhūtatvamavagamyate</q> kārya cālocya kāryasamanantaraṃ
vyak‍titastadbha‍ūtatvamevāvagapyate <q>tadanurūpā ca vyutpattiḥ kalpanīyā ।</q> ekagranthenāha&mdash;<q>sā cenna
vṛddhavyavahārapūrvikā saṃbhavati tarhi samayaḥ kalpyatāṃ kṛtakatvaṃ vā ।</q></p>
<p>atra codayati&mdash;<q>nanu vṛddhavyavahārādeva vālānāṃ</q> kāryāvagatiḥ dṛṣṭā । tena tata eva
kāryāvagatāvupapannāyāṃ samayasya kṛtervā kalpanā nopapadyate । <note n="(3)"> <dn>uk‍taṃ ca</dn></note>uttaram&mdash;<q>na hi dṛṣṭe'nupapannaṃ

upapannā</q> darśanaṃ paryālocya yathā dṛśyate tadanusāreṇopapanneva<note n="(4)"> A. <dn>upapannaiva</dn></note> pratibhāti <q>nimittatastu nopapadyate
﻿<pb n="r159"/>
vṛddhavyavahārasya vyutpattau nimittatvābhāvāt nimittaparyālocanayā vyutpattirnopapadyate । <q>na ca samayaḥ
kārya vopalabhyate । tasmāt</q> vyutpattau <q>nimittakalpanā nayānnirasteva<note n="(1)"> A. <dn>nirastai va । C. nayanirasteva</dn></note>lakṣyate ।</q> pariharati
&mdash;yadi punaḥ <q>sāmānyopalakṣitaṃ vyak‍tidravyameva</q> vākyārthapratipattau <q>nimittatāmāpadyate
tataḥ ko doṣaḥ ? naiva kaścit</q>, ekenopalakṣaṇena saṃbandhagrahaṇasya sukaratvāt ।
punaścodayati&mdash;<q>na khalu kaściddoṣo</q> bhavati, <q>upalakṣaṇatve tu pramāṇaṃ vak‍tavyaṃ</q> kimiti jāti-
rupalakṣaṇameva abhidheyaiva kasmānna bhavati ? pariharati&mdash;<q>kāryapratipattire</q>vātropalakṣaṇatve kāraṇaṃ ;
<q>na hi vyak‍tāvapratipannāyāṃ kāryapratipattiḥ ghaṭate ।</q> yadi hi vvak‍tirna pratīyate tadā tada-
nvitakāryapratipattirnopapadyate । tasmādupalakṣaṇamātraṃ tat । nanu kiṃ tayopalakṣaṇabhūtayetyatrāha

sarvamupapannamityarthaḥ । <q>ato vyaktyabhidhānaṃ manyate vyāḍiriti pradarśitam ।</q> yata eva ca
vyak‍tirarthaḥ <q>ata eva viniyojyatvamupādeyatvaṃ saṅkhayādīnāmupapannaṃ</q>, ākṛtau tu śabdārthe
tasyāḥ saṅkhayādyanāśrayatvāt <quote>‘ekā deyā’</quote> ityādau saṅkhayāyā viniyojyatvaṃ na syāt । saṅkhayā hi
﻿<pb n="r160"/>
sādhanatvena viniyujyate । sādhanaparicchedena ca tasyāḥ sādhanabhāvaḥ, yadi cākṛtireva śabda-

ghaṭate iti saṃkhyāviniyogo na ghaṭata iti । tathā paśunetyādau anenaiva prakāreṇa saṅkhayāyā

﻿<pb n="r162"/>

﻿<pb n="r163"/>
<p>atra pṛcchati&mdash;kiṃ <q>copamānopasarjanārthānāmapyanvayitvamasti ?</q> yepyupamāne upasarjanī-
bhūtā arthāḥ tevāmapi kimanvayitvamasti yena śyenākṛterapi <note n="(2)"> C. <dn>kāryānvayinā</dn></note>mavānanvayitvamicchati । anuṣṭhānā-
nanupraviṣṭatvācchayenākṛteranvayitā nāstīti । atrottaraṃ&mdash;<q>vāḍha</q>manvayitva<q>masti pratītau[pratipattau]
na kārye;</q> śyenākṛtisadṛśasthalasyānuṣṭheyasya pratīteḥ pratītyanvayitvamastīti nānuṣṭhānānvayitvam ।

yadi&mdash;yadi pratipattimātrānvayitvenāpyanvayitva<q>mākṛtestarhi</q> gavā yajetetyādiṣu 4svārthānvayitvaṃ
kimiti neṣyate । uttaram&mdash;<q>kāryapratipattāvākṛteranaṅgatvāt ।</q> yāgādikāryapratipattāvā-
kṛteḥ anaṅgatvāta । kāryapratipattikāle vyak‍tireva kāryānvayinī pratīyate । kevalaṃ vyutpattikāle
<note n="(1)"> B. <dn>bhavānananvayitvaṃ</dn></note>
<note n="(3)"> C. <dn>tatkimiti</dn></note>
﻿<pb n="r164"/>
<note n="(1)"> A. <dn>ākṛtirūpopi pratibhātīti bhāvaḥ</dn></note>ākṛtirupādhibhūteti bhāvaḥ । etadeva vivarītuṃ codyamāha&mdash;<q>nanu copalakṣaṇatve nākṛtiḥ kārya-
pratipattāvaṅga bhavati ।</q> uttaram&mdash;<q>nopalakṣaṇamaṅgaṃ vāsovadviśeṣāvagatau ।</q> asyārthaḥ&mdash;na
viśeṣāvagatāvupalakṣaṇamaṅgaṃ bhavati; vāsovat । yathā yo'yaṃ <note n="(2)"> B. <dn>vāsasvī</dn></note>śuklavāsāḥ sa devadatta iti

cinvītetyādābākṛteriti sādhayitvā saṃprati pūrvapakṣamāha&mdash;<q>tasmāt kvacidvayak‍tiranvayinī
kvacit sāmānyamiti</q> hetoḥ <q>na vidmaḥ</q> kva <q>tad‍bhūtatvaṃ nyāyya miti । tasmādanavadhṛta-

jñātatatsaṃbandhasya vastvantarasaṃbandhitā śakyate'vagantum । na cāsaṃbandhinaḥ prayogaḥ ।
prayujyate cedāśritaṃ tarhi vyaktivyatirik‍taṃ kiñcit । vyak‍terasādhāraṇataiva rūpam
sarvasāmānyaviśeṣaviyuktā hi vyaktirityanena darśitam ।</q> asyārthaḥ&mdash;-yadi sāmānyaṃ

śakyate vak‍tum । ajñātasaṃbandhaḥ śabdo na śakyate prayok‍tum । yadi ca prayujyate tadā ekaṃ
vastu vyaktyantaravarti samāśritya tarhi saṃbandho jñātavyaḥ tacca vastu vyaktito bhinnaṃ tasya vyak‏tyantare

vighaṭeta । asādhāraṇarūpatvādvayak‍teḥ । etacca darśitaṃ bhāṣye sarvasāmānyaviśeṣaviyuk‍tetyanena ।
﻿<pb n="r175"/>
<quote>“naiṣadoṣaḥ, vyak‍‍‏tyantarepi sarvasāmānyaviśeṣaviyukta eva vartiṣyata”</quote> iti <q>bhāṣyam ।</q> asyābhi-
prāyamāha&mdash;<q>naiṣa doṣaḥ</q> iti vadato bhāṣyakārasya sarvasāmānyaviśeṣaviyuktirevopalakṣaṇaṃ bhaviṣyati ।
tena tadupalakṣitavyaktyantarepi prayogo nānupapanna ityabhiprāyaḥ । atrottaraṃ bhāpyaṃ <quote>“yadi sarva-
sāmānyaviśeṣaviyuktaṃ sāmānyameva tat”</quote> iti <note n="(2)"> B. <dn>tadvayācaṣṭe</dn></note>tadvayākhyātumāha&mdash;yadi sarbasāmānyaviśeṣa-
viyuktamiti <q>evaṃ tarhi viyuktirvācyatayopanyastā na vyaktiḥ</q> viyuktirūpeṇaiva pratīteḥ viyu-
ktireva vācyā syāta <q>na vyaktiḥ ।</q> tadidamuk‍taṃ <q>sāmānyameva vācyamāpatati ।</q> gotvaṃ vā
bhavatu sarvasāmānyaviśeṣaviyuktirvā । atra bhāṣyaṃ <quote>“netyucyate”</quote> iti । tadākṣipati
<q>netyucyate yo'rthaḥ sāmānyasya</q> sādhāraṇasya dharmasya <q>viśeṣāṇāṃ</q> vā'sādhāraṇānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ

viśeṣaṃ vā gṛhṇāti</q> śabdaḥ kiṃ tarhi ? <q>āśrayamātrābhidhānaṃ śabdasya</q> sāmānyaviśeṣā-

vagateḥ prayogaḥ siddhayati ।</q> vyaktyantaramapi<note n="(1)"> B. reads <dn>vyaktyantaratvena nāva</dn></note> vyak‍terananyatvena nāvagamyata iti tatrāpi

﻿<pb n="r177"/>

<p><q>uktaṃ samāmnāyaidamarthyam । nanu cedaṃ pramāṇalakṣaṇam ।</q> asminnadhyāye <quote>‘yathāpramāṇaṃ śabdā-

samādhātā pṛcchati&mdash;<q>kiṃvā pramāṇalakṣaṇe'yamupanyāso na ghaṭate ।</q> ākṣeptā uttaramāha&mdash;

nirākiyate ? edamarthyāsaṃbhavāt</q> niyogārthatvāsaṃbhavāt । kathamaidamarthyaṃ <q>na saṃbhavati ?</q>
uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>niyogārthatayā</q> hi <q>vidhyuddeśamantrārthavādapadānāmarthavattoktā ।</q> niyogārthatayā yā
arthavattā uktā sā vidh‍yuddeśārthavādamantrapadānām । taccaitanniyogārthatvaṃ <q>nām‍no na
saṃbhavati avidheyatvāt ।</q> nanu mā nāma avidheyatayā vidheyatvena niyogādaidamarthyaṃ bhavatu
kintu śrutyā smṛt‍yā vā bhaviṣ‍yatītyatrāha&mdash;<q>nanu avidheyānāṃ hi</q> śrut‍yā <q>s‍mṛt‍yā vā'rthava-
ttoktā । taccaitada‍dvayamapi</q> nāmadheyatve <q>na saṃbhavati</q> tasmānnāmadheyapakṣe niyo&mdash;
﻿<pb n="r187"/> 
gaidamarththāsaṃbhavāt udbhidādyarthasya <q>vidheyatvam vidheyaścedruṇavidhiḥ ।</q> atra bhāṣya-
kāreṇoktam&mdash;<quote>“<note n="(1)">p. 182</note>kaścidasya bhāgo vidhiḥ yo'viditamarthaṃ <note n="(2)"><dn>vidadhāti</dn></note>vedayati yathā somena
yajeta”</quote> iti । tadākṣipati&mdash;<q>kathaṃ punaḥ somena yajeteti vidh‍yuddeśa udāharaṇam ?</q>
samādhātā āha&mdash;<q>kathaṃ vā na saṃbhavati ।</q> ākṣeptā''ha&mdash;<q>atrāpi yāgasyāvidhānāt</q>
upapadaśravaṇāt । samādhātā aha&mdash;<q>mābhūdyāgasya vidhānaṃ, guṇastāvadvidhīyate ।</q> tena tada-
bhiprāyeṇa bhāṣ‍yakāreṇa<note n="(3)">A. reads <dn>kāreṇa vidh‍yuddeśapadamuktam</dn></note> uktaṃ&mdash;kaścidasya bhāgo vidhiḥ । <q>nanu guṇa vidhirapi naiva saṃbhavati</q>
udbhidādiśabdānāṃ yāga<q>nāmadheyatayā prasiddheḥ ।</q> uc‍yate&mdash;<q>vṛddhavyavahāre hi prasiddhiḥ
prasiddhirit‍yucyate ।</q> na ca vṛddhavyavahāre <note n="(4)"><dn>somaśabdo</dn></note>ud‍‍bhicchab‍do yāgavacanaḥ । atra codayati
&mdash;<q>nanu yājñikavyavahāro'pi vṛddhavyavahāra eva</q> yājñikā hi ud‍bhidādayaḥ śabdāḥ
karmavacanā it‍yuktavantaḥ । tena tatprasiddhirapi prasiddhireva<note n="(5)">A. adds<dn>yadi karmavacanatvaṃ prasiddhaṃ teṣāṃ kimitiṃ guṇajñānam</dn></note> । pariharati&mdash;<q>na tat‍prasiddhiḥ
prasiddhiḥ । laukikavyavahārapūrvakatvādyājñikavyavahārasya । nahi loke</q> karmanāmadheya-
tayā prasiddhirud‏bhidādiśabdānāṃ, pratyutā<q>rthāntarābhidheyatayā</q> cod‍bhidādayaḥ prasiddhāḥ
khanitravacanatayā <q>prasiddheḥ tasmāda‍guṇavidhiḥ ।</q></p>
﻿<pb n="r188"/>
<p><quote>“prakṛtau j‍yotiṣṭome guṇavidhānamarthavaddhaviṣ‍yati”</quote> <q>ityayuktamidaṃ bhāṣyaṃ pratibhāti ।
kimi</q>tyayuktam ? uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>j‍yotiṣṭomepi j‍yotiṣṭomapadaṃ vidhāyakameva । tatrāpi</q>
hi yaj‍yartho'nyato <q>mṛg‍ya iti</q> ābhāṣānto granthaḥ <q>kena voktaṃ</q> tatrāpi yajyartho <q>na</q>
mṛg‍ya iti ? <q>yadyevaṃ tatra vidhānaṃ nopapadyate ।</q> samādhātā āha&mdash;<q>guṇavidhiprakṛtitā tatra
lakṣyate ।</q> etadeva vivṛṇoti&mdash;<q>etaduktaṃ bhavati&mdash;somena yajeteti guṇaṃ vidadhatā
pratipannā'nyato yāgasiddhiḥ pratiyannācet tatraivedamap‍yupapannaṃ bhaviṣyati ।</q> asyārthaḥ
somena yejetetyatra somākhyaguṇavidhau yo guṇavidherāśrayo'bhimataḥ sa yadi j‍yotiṣṭomo vā laukiko
vā tatraiva cod‍bhidādayo'pi guṇavidhayo bhavantviti । prakṛtiśabdaśca <note n="(1)">B.<dn>guṇavidheḥ</dn></note>guṇavidhau prakṛt‍yupa-
﻿<pb n="r189"/>
lakṣaṇārthaḥ । <q>tasmāj‍yotiṣṭomaśabdo'bhyupagataprakṛt‍yupalakṣaṇārthaḥ ।</q> yatraiva guṇavidherabhyu-
pagamaḥ tatraiva ud‏bhidādayo'pi guṇāvidhayaḥ sarve guṇavidhayo guṇaṃ vidadhatvityarthaḥ । atha
kasmādviśiṣṭavidhirna bhavatītyatrāha&mdash;<q>viśiṣṭavidhānāsaṃbhavaścoktaḥ ।</q> tarhi nāmadheyamastvi-
yatrāha&mdash;<q>nāmadheya pakṣe punaḥ niyogārthatā na saṃbhavati yajinā</q> yāgasya <q>vidheyasya upāttatvāt ।</q>
kiṃ nāmnā pareṇa, tadāha&mdash;samarpitavidheyavacanatayā na vidherupakaroti iti । nanu mā
nāma vidherupakārṣīt tathāpi kiṃ ityāha&mdash;<q>vidh‍yarthaupayikatayā ca prāmāṇ‍yaṃ</q> codanāyā uk‍tam ।
atastvadīyepi pakṣe prāmāṇ‍yaṃ <note n="(1)">B.<dn>pramāṇāntaramṛg‍yameva</dn></note>pramāṇāntarādavagamyate na sukhena labhyate । <q>asmadīye punaḥ
pakṣe padārtho'pi tāvad‍vṛddhavyavahāraprasiddha eva ।</q> <note n="(2)"><dn>t‍vanmate ca prāmaṇ‍yaṃ tāvattulyaṃ</dn></note>t‍vanmatep‍yaprāmāṇ‍yaṃ tāvat tul‍yaṃ yadi
paramalaukikī śabdaśaktirāśraṇīyā ।</p>
<p><q>api vā nāmadheyam ।</q> atrābhidhīyate-guṇaparametadvāk‍yamiti yaduk‍taṃ <q>sat‍ya-
metat viniyoge tu tat</q> viniyogālocanayā tu tathā pratīyate <q>na ca viniyaugāpekṣā kartavyā ।</q>
﻿<pb n="r190"/>
<q>kiṃ tarhi</q> bhāvāpekṣā bhāvaviṣayatvāttasyāḥ । <q>bhāvaścāyaṃ</q> yajeta iti । <q>tasmāt tadviṣayo'yaṃ
niyogaḥ ।</q> na caivaṃ viśeṣaviṣayo <q>niyogaḥ pramāṇāntaraprāpto'sti yena</q> tatparityāgena kevalaguṇa-
vidhānaṃ syāt । atra bhāṣyaṃ-j‍yotiṣṭomāt karmāntaraṃ iti । tadayuk‍taṃ; nahi j‍yotiṣṭomasaṃjñakaṃ
karmāsti yenaivamucyate j‍yotiṣṭomāt karmāntaramiti ityāśaṅkyāha-<q>j‍yotiṣṭomātkarmāntaramiti ।
etaduk‍taṃ bhavati । siddhaṃ laukikādvaidikaṃ karmāntaramiti ।</q> j‍yotiṣṭomaśabdo guṇavi-
dhyāśrayopalakṣaṇārthaḥ । <q>darśayiṣyati ca sūtrakāraḥ tebhyaḥ kriyā pratīyeta iti ।</q>
tena bhāvārtha eva vidhiviṣayaḥ । <q>kathaṃ tarhi guṇārthena punaḥ śrutiriti ?</q> yadi bhābārtha-
viṣaya eva niyogaḥ । uttaram&mdash;<q>kartavyatāprāp‍tyabhiprāyaṃ</q> na viniyogābhiprāyam ।
yat guṇārthatvaṃ punaḥ śruteḥ uk‍ta taddhomāvacchinnā kartavyatā prāptā, kevalaṃ guṇāvacchedo na
prāpta iti na punarguṇa eva vidhīyata ityabhiprāyeṇa prāptāprāptavivekena guṇānvayaparā punaḥ
śrutirityarthaḥ । atra pṛcchati&mdash;<q>kiṃ vā na yathāviniyogaṃ niyogaḥ</q> yena viniyoga-
nādareṇa niyogo varṇyate । uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>eṣā tāvat sūtrakārasya prakriyā bhāvārthāḥ karma-﻿<pb n="r191"/>
śab‍dāḥ tebh‍yaḥ kriyā pratīyeteti paṭhataḥ । kimidaṃ yathāviniyogaṃ viniyogaprat‍ya-
rthībhūtaṃ sūtram ?</q> uttaram&mdash;<q>bāḍhaṃ anyathā hi</q> yathāviniyoge hi <q>raktapaṭanyāyena śye-
nādi vidhānaṃ prāpnoti । nirākṛtaṃ caitadabhāvārthatayā</q> bhāvārthādhikaraṇe । <q>kiṃ punara-
sthāḥ prakriyāyā mūlaṃ ?</q> uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>avagatireva</q> mūlamiti <q>vramaḥ ।</q> bhāvārthaviṣaya eva
niyogo 'vagamyate yataḥ ।</p>
<p><q>nanu ca viniyoge'p‍yavagatireva;</q> tena tasyāpi t‍yāgo na yuktaḥ । pariharati

it‍yuktamasmābhiḥ । kāryasvabhāvatvādbhāvasya ।</q> kāryaviṣayatvānniyogasyetyuk‍taṃ <q>viṣaya-

vo'sau niyogaviṣayībhūto bhābaḥ tadarthaḥ । yadi viniyogo bhāvārthaḥ <q>kathaṃ tarhi guṇaparato cyate ।</q>﻿<pb n="r192"/>
atrāpi tāvadbhāvaparataiva syāt । uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>prāptau sat‍yāṃ bhāvasya</q> vāk‍yasya guṇa-

saṃbandhitā niruṇaddhi । kintu</q> raktapaṭavat <q>viśiṣṭavidhirevāvasīyate । kathaṃ puna-﻿<pb n="r193"/>

<note n="(1)">B. <dn>abhāvārthasya</dn></note>bhāvārthasya viśeṣaṇatvamāha&mdash;<q>yāvatā nāmno'pi</q> viśeṣaṇaviśeṣ‍yatvaṃ <q>dṛśyata eva ḍit‍tho'yaṃ

bhāvayediti gamyate । pūrvapakṣī dūṣayati&mdash;<q>tadidamayuk‍taṃ, na hyekavibhaktinibandhanaṃ sāmānādhi-

<p><q>yasmin guṇopadeśaḥ । uktaṃ nāmadheyamapi guṇaphalopabandhenārthavad‍bhaviṣyatīti

stuvata iti <q>stutyarthasāmānādhikaraṇyāt</q> stutināmatvam । <q>yatra punaḥ bhāvārthasāmā-

anugatārthatvepi sāmānādhikaraṇyānnāmatoktā ।</q> yeṣāmap‍yud‏bhidādīnāmanugatārthatvamasti

arthavattā na śakyate vak‍tum ।</q> atra codayati&mdash;<q>yuktaṃ tāvat guṇopavandhe</q> nāmno'rtha-
vattā nāstiti; <q>phalopabandhe punaḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyasaṃbhavāt</q> yājiśabdoccāraṇe sati
<q>kimityarthavattā na</q> śakyate vak‍tuṃ <q>citrayā yajeta paśukāma ityatra ।</q> pariharati&mdash;<q>ucyate
&mdash;nārthavattā</q> śakyate vak‍tuṃ <q>yajeta paśukāma ityeva</q> prakṛtavācinā yajinaiva
biśiṣṭasya yāgasya phalopavandhasiddheḥ । kuta ityāha-<q>tatra hi sannidhānādeva yāgaviśeṣo labhyate
na nāmataḥ ।</q> atra codayati&mdash;<q>mā</q> bhṛnnāmato yāgaviśeṣāvagatiḥ । <q>nāmatā tāvanni-﻿<pb n="r200"/>
vārayituṃ na śak‍yate</q> sāmānādhikaraṇyāt । pariharati&mdash;<q>kena coktaṃ nāmatvaṃ nirā-
kriyata iti । prayojanaṃ nāstītyetāvatā''kṣepaḥ । kathaṃ punarguṇavidhānaṃ citrayā yajeta
paśukāma iti ?</q> ayamabhiprāyaḥ&mdash;yadyapi prayojanaṃ nāsti tathāpi kimiti nāmadheyatvaṃ na
syāt । kathaṃ guṇavidhiriti । uttaram&mdash;<q>evaṃ guṇavidhānam । atra hi nirjñāto
yāgaviśeṣaḥ phalāya codyate ।</q> bhavatvevaṃ tathāpi kimityāha&mdash;<q>nirjñāte hi viśeṣe padānta-
rāvagatiḥ <note n="1">B.<dn>nāviśeṣāya</dn></note>na viśeṣāyopapadyate;</q> kutaḥ ? uttaram&mdash;<q>nirjñātatvādeva ।</q> dadhimadhudhṛtamiti
vāk‍yānnirjñāto viśeṣarūpo yāgaḥ yajeta paśukāma iti prakṛtavācinā yajinaiva viśeṣo nirjñātaḥ ।
<q>yatra hi vidheryo'rthaḥ</q> <note n="2">C.<dn>svabāk‍yānvita padābagabhya</dn></note>svabidhivāk‍yānvinapadārthāvagamya eva bhavati tatra tata eva viśoṣā-﻿<pb n="201"/>
vagamaḥ ।</q> yathodbhidā yajeteti । <q>vākyāntaranirjñātastu nātmaparijñānāya svavākye<note n="(1)"> <dn>svavākyānvitapadāvagamya</dn></note> padā-
nvayamapekṣate । anapekṣitasya ca sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ śābdaṃ na bhavati ।</q>
ākāṅkṣāsannidhiyogyatā hi saṃbandhe hetavaḥ । yajeta paśukāma ityatra ca na yajirnāmadheyamākāṅ-
kṣati viśeṣaparijñānāya; vākyāntara eva viśeṣaparijñānāt । ataścānvayābhāvānna nāmadheyatā ।
tasmāt 'citrayā' ityatra vidheyatayā citratvamavagantavyam । tatra codayati—<q>yatra tarhi upapadā-
deva viśeṣāvagamaḥ vihitasya aprakṛtatvāt bhavatu tatra nāmadheyasya prayojanaṃ</q> tadbale-
naiva viśeṣāvagamāt । parihahati—<q>iha tāvadekāntato nāstītyetāvadudāhṛtam । aprakṛtepi ca
naiva nāmadheyatopakaroti ।</q> yadapyaprakṛtanāmadheyayuktaṃ vākyaṃ phalāya yāgaṃ vidadhāti
tatrāpi na nāmno nāmadheyatayānvayaḥ । kasmādityāha—<q>aprakṛte hi karmāntarataiba,</q> phalaṃ
prati karmaṇo vidheyatvāt । aprakṛtatvācca karmaṇaḥ karmāntaratvam । <q>tatra ca padadbayārtha-
vidhānam ।</q> nāmnāpi mukhyakarmasādṛśyamupakāranibandhanaṃ vidhīyate । bhāvārthaśabdenāpi
bhāvārthavidhānamiti<note n="(2)">C. <dn>bhāvārthaḥ pradarśitaḥ</dn></note> darśitam <q>agnihotraṃ juhotīti kuṇḍapāyināmayane ।</q> tasmā-
dutpannasya prakṛtasya karmaṇaḥ phalopabandhena utpadyamānasya vā karmāntarasya phalopabandhena arthavannāma

<p>samādhatte—<q>ayamabhiprāyaḥ-yaugikatve hi prakṛtayāgābhidhānasiddhiḥ syāt yathā

uttaraṃ—<q>anākāṅkṣitatvaṃ<note n="(2)">A. <dn>anākāṅkṣitatvānnāmnaḥ</dn></note> nāmnaḥ citrāpadasya ।</q> yasmādayamanuvādaḥ tasmānnirjñātaviśeṣatvāt
viśeṣajñānāya nāma nākāṅkṣati । <q>anākāṅkṣitasya ca sāmānādhikaraṇyābhāvaḥ ।
tadabhāvānna nāmateti । tasmātphalavidhau na nāmadheyatayopakāritā'vagamyata iti ।

guṇaphalakalpanāyāṃ</q> na nāma śakyate nivartayituṃ tena pūrvapakṣī guṇaphalasaṃbandhaṃ nirākaroti ।
kuto nivartayituṃ na śakyate<note n="(1)">B. <dn>śakyata ityāha</dn></note> । uttaraṃ—<q>yasmādyajateravivakṣā । avivakṣāyāṃ ca anāśritaḥ</q>
bhāvārtho, na ca bhāvārthānāśrito <q>guṇaḥ phalāya vidhātuṃ śakyate ।</q> kasmāt punaḥ

karmaṇo'nyataḥpravṛttatvādavidhīyamāne guṇāt phalamitirbhavati । <q>na ca paśukāmavidhānādṛte<note n="(2)">B. <dn>yarjyasyānyatpravartakamasti</dn></note> yajya-
rthasya kṛte anyasya pravartakatvamasti ।</q> tasmādyajateravivakṣā । citrāśabdasya tu paśukāmasaṃbandhaḥ ।
<q>tasmāt paśukāmasaṃbandhāparityāge citrāpadasya nāmataivāvaśiṣyate<note n="(3)">A. <dn>vasīyate</dn></note> ।</q> tena pūrvapakṣī
citrāśabdasya guṇaphalasaṃbandhāśrayaṇenāpi paśukāmasaṃbandhamekāntato nirākaroti । sa hi manyate

nāmataiva citrāśabdasyāpadyeta । tena prayatnena guṇaphalasaṃbandhenāpi ekavākyatāṃ dūrata eva

mapi pūrvapakṣopodvalakaṃ bhāṣyaṃ vyācaṣṭe—<q>guṇavidhikalpanāyāmapi na lakṣaṇeti । lakṣaṇāśrayaṇe

guṇa eva sādhyatayā na vidhīyata ityarthaḥ । <q>tataḥ kim ? idaṃ tato bhavati yatrāyaṃ guṇavidhiḥ
siddhaḥ san karmaupayikatāṃ pratipadyate tatra vidhātavyo</q> guṇaḥ <q>paśāvasya vidhānaṃ</q>

atra bhāṣyakāreṇa coditam । atha kasmāt na pañcadaśasaṅkhyāviśiṣṭānyājyāni stotreṣu vidhīyanta

tathehājyāni pañcadaśānyeveti <note n="(1)">B. <dn>pañcadaśānītyeva</dn></note>siddham । tadāha—<q>na tvasāvastīti । tasmādvidhyuddeśani-

<p><q>atha kasmādagniprajāpatyorivāsaṃbandhayorapi vidhānaṃ na saṃbhavati ?</q> yathā'gnihotre
yadagnaye ca prajāpataye cetyanenānyonyāsaṃbandhayoragniprajāpatyorekenaiva vidhinā vidhānaṃ tathehāpi
kasmānna bhavatītyarthaḥ । <note n="(3)">B. <dn>uttaraṃ-na</dn></note>pariharati-na sambhavatyayamasaṃbandhayorvidhānaṃ <q>pramāṇāntarasiddho nāsti iti vidhyuddeśanimittaka eva parigrahītavyaḥ ।
tasmātsiddhaṃ nāmadheyamidamapīti ।</q></p>﻿<pb n="211"/>
<p><q>tatprakhyaṃ cānyaśāstram । kena punarviśeṣeṇātra guṇavidhyāśaṅkā yāṃ</q> nivartayitumidamadhi-

katham ?</q> uttaraṃ—<q>naivātra sāmānādhikaraṇyena prayojanaṃ, karmavacanataivātra na pratīyata

vidhiraviruddha ityuktam ।</q></p>﻿<pb n="213"/>
<p><q>atrocyate—nātra guṇavidhiḥ saṃbhavati,</q> prāptatvādguṇānām । etadeva vivṛṇoti
-ye'tra guṇā vidheyatayopanyastāḥ te'nyata eva prāptāḥ । <q>agnistāvat <quote>yadagnane ca prajāpataye

tyānarthakvaṃ yuktam । saṃbhavati cāghāramāghārayatītyasya yāgavidhāyakatvenārthavattvam । yadi hi sa na﻿<pb n="214"/>

udaiharaṇabhūteṣu bhāṣyakāreṇa yatra siddhāntepi1 rūḍhitvānapāyaḥ tadevodāhṛtam । pūrvapakṣā-

lopabhayāllopāntarāśrayaṇaṃ,</q> śyene matublopabhayena vatilopāśrayaṇam gauṇapakṣe na yuktaṃ

syāt tadā tatparatvāt ākhyātaparatā nāstīti sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ na syāt । yadā tu vatyartho nā-
vidheyaḥ kintu karmaṇi pravṛttinimittamātraṃ tadā karmaparatvāt sāmānādhikaraṇye sati nāmadheyatvaṃ
bhavati । <q>matublope punaḥ bhinnādhikaraṇatā'parihāryaiva vidheyatvānmatvarthasya<note n="(1)">B. <dn>vidheyatvātkarmaṇaḥ</dn></note> ।</q> tenā-
nekārthavidhānādekārthāvagamavirodhādvaraṃ vaterlepaḥ <q>na matublopa iti siddhaṃ nāmadheyatvaṃ</q> śyena-
śabdasyāpi ।</p>
<p><q>nāmadheye guṇaśruteḥ । kimarthamidamadhikaraṇam ?</q> yadi guṇavidhiryāvat saṃbhāvyeta
tadā tannirākaraṇārthamidamadhikaraṇaṃ bhavet । na cāsau saṃbhāvyate । <q>yato yaugikaprāptārtharūḍhīnāṃ
nāmatvaṃ pratipāditam । śakyate ca vājapeye tatprakhyatā vaktum, surāgrahavidhānāt ।</q>
<note n="(2)">A. <dn>peyarūpā surā syāt tasyā vihitatvāt</dn></note>peyarūpasya vājasya vihitatvāt । parihāramāha-<q>sarvanāmākṣepakamidamadhikaraṇaṃ</q> pūrvapakṣadaśāyām ।﻿<pb n="223"/>
kuta ityāha—<q>yajestantrābhidhānopanyāsāt ।</q> tantreṇa yajiḥ phalaguṇau prati svārthaṃ samarpayati ।

pekṣataiva śabdasya ।</q> sakṛduccāraṇa eva vidheyoddeśyatvayoravagatatvāt vidhīyamānasyaivoddeśyatvasaṃbhavānna
guṇavidhāvāśrayāntarāpekṣānti iti na śakyaṃ nāmābhidhānam । <q>tasmāttantrābhidhānanirā-

ntaropādānaṃ vyarthamiti bhāvaḥ । pariharati—<q>bāḍhamu</q>dbhidādayopyatrodāharaṇam । ākṣeptā āha

tasmādacodyamevaitat yaccodyāmahe ।</q> parihārāntaraṃ cāha—<q>śakyate cātra viśeṣo'pi kaści-

prabhavaḥ saṃskāranimittakaśca prayogaḥ sārvabhaumaḥ ।</q> <note n="(1)">A. <dn>ye saṃskṛte śabdaṃ prayuñjate teṣāṃ tāvatsaṃskāranimittatā</dn></note>ye tāvadasati saṃskāre śabdaṃ na prayuñcate
teṣāṃ sphuṭaiva saṃskāranimittatā । ya'pi jātimātre prayuñcate te saṃskṛte'pi prayuñjate iti
saṃskṛtaviṣayatvaṃ sārvabhaumam । tadeva ca śrautam । ekadeśe yajjātibacanatvaṃ tadgauṇam ।
kasmādevaṃ ? uttaraṃ—<q>prasiddhasya</q> hi padasya <q>śraute'rthe gauṇatā saṃbhavati</q> nāprasiddhasya ।
yathaiva hi jvalane prasiddho'gniśabdo māṇavake tatsādṛśyena prayujyamāno gauṇo bhavati । sarveṣāṃ
saṃskāranimittatā prasiddheti jātimātre gauṇaḥ ekadeśabhavaḥ prayogaḥ । yeṣāṃ tu saṃskṛtamātra
eva prayogaḥ teṣāṃ prayogadvayābhāvānmukhyaḥ prayogaḥ । <q>na cāyaṃ sarvatra ghṛtavacanatayā prasiddhaḥ ।
aprasiddhasya ca ghṛte'nyatra gauṇatvaṃ nopapadyate ।</q> ye saṃskāranimittaṃ śabdaṃ manyante te
jātyantarepi śabdaṃ na prayuñjate tatra sa gauṇo na yuktaḥ anyatra mukhyaprayogādarśanāt । <q>karma-
nimittatve</q> yatra punaḥ ekadeśe ghṛte <q>prayujyate</q> asaṃskṛte'pi <q>tatra karmanimittake'pi prayogāt
siddho</q> gauṇaḥ, anyatra mukhyaprayogasiddheḥ siddho ghṛte gauṇaḥ । tasmāt saṃskāranimittatvā-﻿<pb n="236"/>
dājyādiśabdānāṃ <q>kāryārthataiva yuktā । atrocyate । kāryārthatayā'nvayo na ghaṭate itareta-
rāśratvaprasaṅgāt । barhiṣaḥ</q> sataḥ <q>prokṣaṇaṃ prokṣaṇena ca barhiriti ।</q> yadvai prokṣaṇādinā
saṃskriyate tadbārhirityucyate । barhiruddeśena prokṣaṇādayo vidhīyanta iti na jñāyate kasya
prokṣaṇādayo vidhīyanta iti । yadyevamitaretarāśrayatvaṃ <q>kathaṃ tarhyaṣṭākapāle</q> netaretarāśrayaḥ ?
uttaraṃ—<q>na cetaretarāśrayamabhidhānataḥ prasiddherityuktam । śha punaḥ kāryata evābhidhānaṃ,
tenetaretarāśrayatvamiti vaiṣamyam ।</q> pūrvapakṣī tvāha—<q>yūpe kathaṃ ?</q> yūpaṃ takṣatīti śrūyate ।
yūpaśabdaśca kāryasaṃskāravacanaḥ tatra vyaktamitaretarāśrayatvam । <q>anyataḥ prasiddhyabhāvāt
agatikā gatiriyam ।</q> yathā barhirādāvanyataḥ prasiddhirasti jātimātre prayogadarśanāt tathā
yūpe nāsti tena asati gatyantare eṣāgatirāśrīyate yattakṣaṇārhaṃ yattakṣaṇakarmabhūtaṃ tat takṣaṇena yūpaṃ
karotīti । <q>keyamagatikā gatiḥ ।</q> ekagranthenāha—<q>kiṃ na śāstrādevāvagamyate ?</q>
ayamāśayaḥ—yadi śāstrāt avagamyeta tadā barhirādiṣvapi tathāstviti । uttaraṃ—satyāṃ
prasiddhau na śāstrādavagamyate yatrānyataḥ prasiddhirasti tatra sāmānyena vyavahāro na yuktaḥ ।
viśeṣasyaivāvagamāditi tatreyaṃ śāstrādgatirnāvagamyate । yatprokṣaṇārhaṃ prokṣaṇe karmabhūtaṃ tadbārhiḥ
tat prokṣaṇena saṃskriyata iti । <q>aprasiddhe punaḥ padārthe apratihatatvādvidhyarthasya kalpyate ।﻿<pb n="237"/>
anyathā vidhyarthapratighātaprasaṅgāt । <q>yaduktaṃ sārvabhaumaprayogo gauṇo na saṃbhavati
śrautasyāprasiddheriti ekadeśasthastu</q> gauṇassaṃbhavatīti atrocyate—<q>nāvaśyaṃ prasiddhaśrautārtha-
meva gauṇaṃ prayuñjate lokikaḥ</q> rājaśabdamiva । yathā rājaśabdāmāryā aprasiddhaśrotārthamapi
gauṇaṃ prayuñjate tathā barhirādiśabdamapi । codayati—<q>tatrāpi</q> rājaśabde'pi tulyo doṣaḥ ।
ekagranthenāha—vācya<q>sādṛśyapratipattyarthaṃ hi gauṇaṃ prayuñjate । atadbuddhyāpi gauṇaḥ
prayujyata iti haṭho'yaṃ;</q> vācyārthasādṛśyapratipādanāya hi gauṇaḥ śabdaḥ prayujyate । mukhye
cārthe'vijñāte na tatsādṛśyaṃ jñāyata iti sādṛśyabuddhāvasatyāṃ gauṇasya prayogo <note n="(1)">C. <dn>'nimittakaḥ</dn></note>nirhetukaḥ ।
atrābhidhīyate—<q>na prayokturvivakṣāmapekṣate śabdārthasaṃbandhaḥ । saṃbandhāpekṣā hi vivakṣā ।</q>
asyārthaḥ—yadyapi prayoktā gauṇabuddhyā prayuṅkte prayojyaśca tathaiva pratipadyate tathāpi pārśvastho
bālaḥ mukhyārthe prayogamadṛṣṭvā mukhyatāmevāvagacchati । sa tathā pratītya vyavahāramapi pravartayet ।
tena prayoktṛvivakṣāṃ nāpekṣate pārśvasthasya śabdārthasaṃbandhaḥ, kintu yādṛśaṃ mukhyaṃ śabdārthasaṃbandhaṃ
pratipadyate tādṛśameva punarvyavahārakāle'pi pārśvastho vivakṣati । etadeva dṛṣṭāntapurassaraṃ﻿<pb n="238"/>
darśayati—<q>uktaṃ hi gopotalikādiṣu aśaktijatvāparijñānādanādiśabdamiva<note n="(1)">C. <dn>anādṛgiva</dn></note> prayuñjate । eva
matrāpi vivakṣā'parijñānāt kasyacit prayoktuḥ vivakṣāśūnyamarthāntare prayuñcate</q> । jāti-
viṣaye mukhyaṃ śabdārthaṃ jānatā kenacidekadeśajātena gauṇaḥ<note n="(2)">C. <dn>gauṇasaṃskāra</dn></note> saṃskārayoginyatajjātīye'pi
barhirādiśabdaḥ prayuktaḥ । atra mukhyamanyamarthamaviduṣo gauṇārthavivakṣā'sti । evamajānato
mukhyabuddhiḥ pravṛttā । yathā gopotalikādiṣvanāditvabuddhiraśaktijatvamaviduṣaḥ tannibandhanaśca
śabdārthavyavahāraḥ । <q>kathaṃ punaridaṃ vijñāyate</q> bhrāntimūlo'yaṃ saṃskṛtaviṣaye mukhyaśabdavyavahāra
iti । uttaraṃ—<q>loke vede ca vyavahāradarśanāt । vede tāvadājyaṃ vidhāya kvacit ghṛta-
śabdena stauti</q> tatra yadi saṃskāravacanaḥ ājyaśabdaḥ syāt tatra stutau ghṛtaśabdaḥ upa-
lakṣaṇārthaḥ syāt । jātivacanatve tu svārthaḥ, tena jātivacanataiva vedālocanayā'vasīyate ।
<q>loke'pyājyaṃ krayyamiti krayyamiti kriyāsādhananirapekṣaḥ prayogaḥ ।</q> kriyāsādhanaṃ kriyaiva
saṃskārarūpā sādhanaṃ yasya tannirapekṣaḥ prayogo lokepi dṛṣṭaḥ । <q>nanu ca tatrāpyajñātavivakṣātvaṃ
śakyate vaktum ।</q> <note n="(3)">A. <dn>saṃskṛtasya mukhyārthatvepi tatsaṃbandhādgauṇaḥ</dn></note>kenacitsaṃskāramātravācitve'pi tadarhatāmātreṇa gauṇo jātau śabdaḥ
prayuktaḥ tatra <note n="(4)">B. <dn>vivakṣāmaparijñāya</dn></note>vivakṣā'parijñānāt kasyacinmukhyārthabuddhirutpannaivetyatrāpi śakyate vaktuṃ; tena﻿<pb n="239"/>
kathaṃ niścayaḥ ? pariharati—<q>ukto vetasādiṣu parihāraḥ iti ।</q> <note n="(1)">B. <dn>laukikavyavahārācca jātisaṃskārarūpavipratipattau</dn></note>laukikaviṣayavyavahāra-
<q>vipratipattau vaidikavyavahārasāmānyānnirṇaya iti ।</q> tenātrāpi vaidikavyavahārasāmyāt
jātau mukhyatā । saṃskṛtaviṣaye tu tadīyasaṃsaskārayogādnauṇaḥ prayoga iti । yadyevaṃ tenaiva
tarhyadhikaraṇena gatam । ucyate—jñātamukhyaprayogasyaiva gauṇaḥ prayoga itīmāmāśaṅkāmapanetumida-
madhikaraṇamārabdham । udāharaṇaṃ tu barhirādayo vetasādayaścomayatrāpīti । <q>kiṃ punaḥ prāsaṅki-
syāsya</q> pramāṇalakṣaṇe <q>prayojanaṃ ? uttaraṃ—anadhyavasāya eva</q> śabdārthānadhyavasāya eva ।
śabdārthavyavahāre ko mukhyaḥ, ko vā gauṇa ityanadhyavasāyaḥ syāt । tataśca vede'pyanadhyava-
sāyādaprāmāṇyaṃ syāt । tenānadhyavasāyo hyadhikaraṇasya prayojakaḥ । <q>nanu ca bhāṣyakāreṇa
karmaṇyeva viśeṣo darśitaḥ ।</q> nāvagatau । pariharati—yata eva karmaṇi viśeṣaḥ <q>ata evā-
nadhyavasāyaḥ prayojanaṃ</q> tannivṛttaye'nadhyavasāyo'dhikaraṇasya prayojakaḥ । karmaṇi yadi viśeṣo
na syāt tadā anuṣṭhānaviśeṣo na syāt । anuṣṭhānaviśeṣābhāvādanadhyavasāyo<note n="(2)">A. <dn>'napaneyaḥ</dn></note> na doṣaḥ iti
tannivṛttaye'dhikaraṇamārabdhaṃ, <q>niścaye tvadhyavasāyāt sthitameva prayojanam ।</q></p>﻿<pb n="240"/>
<p><q>prokṣaṇīṣu ।। kimarthamidaṃ pṛthagadhikaraṇaṃ ? uttaraṃ—sārvabhaumaikadeśabhavayoḥ</q> prayo-
gayoḥ <q>smṛtito'pavādaḥ kathyate ।</q> saṃskāranimittaḥ sārvabhaumaḥ prayogaḥ jātinimittastvekadeśa-
prabhavaḥ । tayoḥ smṛtimālocyāpavādaḥ kathyate, yaugikaḥ prokṣaṇīśabda iti । pūrvapakṣamāha
—<q>kathaṃ punaḥ prayogasya smṛtito'pavādaḥ kathyate</q> prayogamūlā hi vyākaraṇasmṛtiḥ sā kathaṃ
prayogamapavadatīti bhāvaḥ । rāddhāntamāha—<q>saṃbhavati hi smṛterānuguṇyaṃ prayogasya ।</q> smṛtyanu-
guṇo hi prayogo bhavatyeva । kuta ityāha-<q>yasmāt dvayorapyavayavayogaḥ saṃbhavati ।</q> yo'pi
saṃskāranimittakaḥ prayogaḥ tatrāpi yogaḥ saṃbhavati yaśca jātinimittakaḥ tatrāpi । tataśca
yogāvirodhī prayoga iti na yogaṃ bādhate tatra prokṣaṇīrāsādaya</q> iti saṃskāranimittakaḥ prayogaḥ
<q>prokṣaṇībhirudvejitāḥ smaḥ'</q> iti jātinimittakaḥ । <q>tasmāda</q>virodhitvāt <q>smṛtito nirṇayaḥ ।</q>
śeṣamuktam ।</p>﻿<pb n="241"/>
<p><q>tathā nirmanthye ।। kimatrātiricyate ?</q> uttaraṃ—<q>idamatrātiricyate । smṛtirapyati-
vyāpikā ।</q> aciranirmathite prayogadarśanāt । <note n="(1)"> <dn>tathā</dn></note>tathā asaṃskṛte'pi prayogadarśanāt
<quote>nirmanthyamānaya pakṣyāmaḥ</quote> iti । tena saṃskāranimittatā nāsti । tathā yaugikatvamapi
na saṃbhavati । aciranirmathitepi prayogadarśanāt । yaugikatve ciranirmathitamātre prayogaḥ
syāt । na ca jātinimittatā, agnimātre prayogāt । <q>tasmāt smṛtito'pi na nirṇaya﻿<pb n="242"/>
iti manyate pūrvapakṣavādī ।</q> rāddhāntamāha—<q>aviśeṣābhidhānāt smṛteḥ na viśeṣaprayogo
vihantuṃ kṣamaḥ ।</q> yadi hi smṛtau ciranirmathite aciranirmathite ca nirmanthyaśabdaḥ sādhuriti
smṛtaṃ syāt tadā viśeṃṣaprayogaḥ smṛtiṃ vihanyāt । na caitadasti । <q>vihantyaviśeṣajñānamiti
cet</q> smārtamaviśeṣajñānaṃ prayogo vihantīti cet । pariharati-<q>na vihanti viśeṣapari-
samāpteraviśeṣasya ।</q> yo'sau smṛtāvaviśeṣaḥ sa yadi viśeṣa upasaṃhriyeta prayogabalena tadā na
kaściddoṣaḥ । <q>tasmāt pūrvavadidamapi । tena tathetyuktam ।</q></p>
<p><q>vaiśvadeve ।। kathaṃ punaḥ guṇavidhināmadheyatayā'tra saṃśayaḥ ?</q> yāvatā bhāvārthasāmānā-
dhikaraṇyānnāmadheyatvamevātra yuktam । uttaraṃ—<q>guṇavidhipakṣa evātra sāmānādhikaraṇya-﻿<pb n="243"/>
mupapannataraṃ, pratyayārthatvādbhāvārthasya</q> na nāmadheyatā yuktā guṇavidhipakṣa eva tāvadyuktaḥ
guṇavidhāvapi matvarthalakṣaṇābhāvāt viśvedevā devatā asyeti yāgasyaiva pratyayārthatvāt mukhya-
yā vṛttyā sāmānādhikaraṇyasyopapatteḥ । punarākṣipati—yadi guṇavidhirevopapannataraḥ <q>kimiti
nāmadheyatayopanyāsaḥ</q> samādhatte—<q>viṣayābhāvāt guṇavidhānasya</q> guṇasya vidheyasya viṣayā-
bhāvādguṇavidhirapi na yuktaḥ । kimiti viṣayābhāvaḥ । uttaraṃ—<q>agnyādibhi</q>rdevatābhiḥ
<q>śrutyā'varuddhatvāt prakṛtānāṃ karmaṇām ।</q> yāni tu prakṛtāni karmāṇi tānyutpattiśiṣṭairabhnyā-
dibhiravaruddhāni na tatra devatāntaraṃ śakyate vidhātum । yadi prakṛte devatāntaravidhiraśakyaḥ
<q>karmāntaraṃ tarhi devatāviśiṣṭaṃ kimiti na bhavati ? tadapi nādhyavasīyate prakṛtatvā-
dāmikṣāyā</q> vaiśvadevyāḥ । karmāntaravidhau hi <note n="(1)"> <dn>viśeṣavidhānaṃ</dn></note>viśiṣṭavidhānam । tacca gatyantarābhāve﻿<pb n="244"/>
sati yuktam । asti cātra gatyantaraṃ, vaiśvadevyāmikṣāyāgasāhacaryāt prakṛteṣu yāgeṣu daṇḍinyāyena
nāmadheyatayāpyanvayasaṃbhavāt । ato'tra nāmatāpi na saṃbhavati guṇavidhānenāpi sāmānādhi-
karaṇyopapatteḥ । nāpi guṇavidhiḥ prakṛteṣūtpattiśiṣṭaguṇāvarodhāt । tadāha-<q>tasmānna nāmato
nāpi guṇato'napekṣatvaṃ śakyate'vagantumiti</q> pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । rāddhāntaikadeśyāha—iti
<q>cenmanyase anapekṣatvādhyavasānaṃ na śakyate kartumiti bhavatu guṇavidhānenādhyavasānaṃ
tathā'vagamānnāmākhyātārthasaṃbandhasya । nanu cokto viṣayābhāvaḥ ।</q> pariharati—durukto hi
saḥ । punaścodayati—<q>kathaṃ duruktaḥ ।</q> uttaraṃ-<q>śrutāddhi kāryakalpanā, na kāryataḥ śrutam ।
kimidamucyate ?</q> uttaraṃ—idamidaṃ, <q>utpattiśiṣṭaguṇāvarodho hi anavagame hetuḥ, na puna-
ravagatasya vighāte</q> utpattiśiṣṭaguṇāvarodhena guṇāntarasaṃbandhāvagatireva virudhyate, na punarava-
gatasya vighātaḥ kriyate । bhavatvevaṃ tathāpi kimityāha—<q>vaiśvadevaśabdaścāyamākhyātārthe eva
prakṛte vartate, nāgnyādayaḥ <note n="(1)">A. <dn>saṃbandhinaṃ</dn></note>saṃbandhinaḥ ākhyātārthaṃ vaiśvadevaśabdābhidheyatayā nivārayituṃ﻿<pb n="245"/>
kṣamāḥ ।</q> ekagranthenāha—<q><note n="(1)">B. <dn>saṃbandhyantaraṃ</dn></note>sambandhyantaraviṣayatāṃ nivārayanti, nābhidheyatāma</q> nivāra-
bhānti । <q>tataḥ kiṃ ? uttaraṃ—idaṃ tato bhavati abhidheyopapattyarthaṃ saṃbandhyantarasya
devatāntarasya prāptiṃ notpattisambandhino'gnyādayo vighnanti । yathā saṃskāryatayā</q> yāga-
śeṣasaṃskāra(śeṣa)bhūtabhakṣaṇasambandhitayā'nyathānupapadyamānayā''<q>kṣiptaṃ phalacamasasya yāgasādhanatvaṃ
somo na</q> vihantīti । tena śrutavaiśvadevaśabdābhidheyatvopapattyarthaṃ viśveṣāṃ devānāṃ kāryakalpanā
yuktā । prakṛteṣu yāgeṣu devatātvenānupraveśo yukta ityarthaḥ । na punaryāganirvṛttiḥ kārya-
meṣām । sā cāgnyādibhireva siddhyatītyālocya śrutasya vaiśvadevaśabdābhidheya<note n="(2)">B. <dn>dheyatvasyāyathātvakalpanaṃ</dn> C. <dn>dheyasyānyathātva</dn></note>syāyathārthatva-
kalpanaṃ yuktam । yasmādabhidhānopapattyarthaṃ devatātvena sambandhaḥ <q>tasmā</q>dagnyādibhiḥ sahānuṣṭhāne
vikalpenānapekṣātvādhya<q>vasānam<note n="(3)">A. <dn>adds yuktam</dn></note> ।</q> paramasiddhāntamāha—<q>yadyevaṃ</q> śabdapravṛttimātrasiddhaye
guṇavidhikalpanaṃ-<q>evaṃ tarhi nāmadheyataivāstu । abhidhānopapattyarthaṃ hi guṇāntarasaṃbandhaḥ﻿<pb n="246"/>
parikalpyate'nupapattyā । atulyapramāṇaśiṣṭānāṃ tvavikalpaḥ ।</q> agnyādayo hi śrutyā
śiṣṭāḥ, viśvedevāstu vākyena । tatra vidhānaṃ <q>nāmadheyatayopapadyate । nanu</q> nāmadheyamātratve
<q>'vayavārtho'vagamyamānaḥ kārye'nanvayī</q> syāt । avayavārthānusāreṇa hi viśveṣāṃ devānāṃ deva-
tātvaṃ pratīyamānaṃ kāryeṇānanvitaṃ syādityarthaḥ । pariharati-<q>nānvitasyānvayo nyāyyaḥ, anvi-
taścāmikṣāyāmayamarthaḥ tasmātkāryānanvayo nābhidhānaṃ vārayitumutsahate ।</q> ekasminnapya-
pyanvitasya । anyatrānanvitasya daṇḍinyāyena nāmadheyatayopapatteḥ nimittatvaṃ daṇḍavadaviruddham ।
<q>tasmānna vikalpaḥ kalpayituṃ śakyate, nāpyāvṛttiḥ karmaṇaḥ । ato nāmadheyatayā'dhyavasānaṃ
nyāyyam ।</p>﻿<pb n="247"/>
<p><q>kathaṃ punaḥravaiśvadeve</q>'myādiyāge <q>vaiśvadevābhidhānaṃ</q> pravṛttinimittaśūnyaṃ
<q>guṇavidhau punarvidhānāt</q> pravṛttinimittasaṃbhavāt sidhyati । pariharati—<q>satyamevaṃ yadye-
kāntato vidhānataḥ siddhyati । āmikṣāyāṃ tvanabhidhānaprasaṅgāt ।</q> āmikṣāyāṃ hi
viśvedevāḥ prāptatvānna vidheyā ityekāntato vidheyatayā'bhidhānapravṛttirna siddhyati । nanvābhikṣā-
parityāgena vidheyatayā'bhidhānaṃ setsyati ityatrāha—<q>tulyaṃ ca prakṛtatvaṃ</q> tenābhikṣāyāgo na
na śakyate varjayitum । atra codayati—<q>kataratpunaranayorbalīyaḥ iti ।</q> yadidamavaiśvadevasya

vidheyābhidhānaṃ</q> saṃbhavati । vidheyo hyajñāto jñāpyate abhidheyaśca jñātaḥ । na caika
evārthaḥ sakṛt jñātaścājñātaśca saṃbhavati । <q>saṃbhavati ca tulyayogināṃ lakṣaṇayābhidhānam ।

vartate tathehāpyavaiśvadeve vaiśvadeve ca vaiśvadevaśabdo vartiṣyate । <q>tasmājjyāyānayaṃ pakṣaḥ</q>
avaiśvadevasya vaiśvadevābhidhānamiti śreyānayaṃ pakṣaḥ ।</p>﻿<pb n="248"/>
<p>idaṃ punaratra vaktavyam—vaiśvadevena yajeteti kasmādāmikṣāyāga eva na vyapadiśyate ।

haviṣi vā mukhyayā vṛttyā vartate । yajatinā sāmānādhikaraṇyāt tasya yāgavṛttitvena na śaknoti
eṣa yajatiśabdaṃ niyantum । na ca vaiyadhikaraṇyena vaiśvadevaśabdasya yajinā saṃbandhaḥ
āmikṣāśabdasāmānādhikaraṇyena tasya strīliṅgatvāpatteḥ । sāmānādhikaraṇyenānvayopapattau
vyadhikaraṇānvayānuṣapatteḥ ।</p>

bhavati yathā khapuṣpamiti jñānaṃ tathā khapuṣpamiti śabdaprayogaḥ1 । tathā hi jñānaṃ caikaṃ khamātra-
viṣayaṃ aparaṃ ca puṣpamātraviṣayam । tatra tayoranyonyasaṃbandhapratipattyabhāvepi asaṃbandhamaprati-
padyamānaḥ saṃbandhapratipattivyavahāraṃ karoti । tayoḥ sannidhānoccāraṇaṃ saṃbandhisādhāraṇaṃ pratipadyamāna
iti <q>nayavīthīnibandhana</q>nyāyānusāreṇa varṇanīyam । <q>tasmāt siddho'rthavādaḥ । kiṃ bhavati
prayojanaṃ kathaṃ ceti dartiśaṃ bhāṣye ।</q></p>
<p><q>jātiḥ ।। jātyādiṣyapyevameva prāmāṇyaṃ yojyam ।</q> tatrāpyarthavādatvāśrayaṇena prāmā-
ṇyam । yadyevaṃ kimiti tarhi pṛthagadhikaraṇānītyatrāha—<q>pṛthagadhikaraṇāni tu parihārānyatva-
<note n="(1)">B. <dn>prayogo'pīti</dn></note>﻿<pb n="263"/>
pradarśanārthāni ।</q> tatrāgneyo brāhmaṇa ityekasthānaprabhavatayā sādṛśyādgauṇīvṛttiriti parihāraḥ ।
'ādityo yūpa' iti yūpasādṛśyāt । 'apaśavo vā anye go aśvemyaḥ paśavo go aśvā' iti
praśaṃsayā go aśveṣveva paśuśabdo gauṇaḥ । tathā sṛṣṭīrupadadhātīti bhūmnā, prāṇabhṛta upadadhātīti
liṅgasamavāyena lakṣaṇeti parihāraṃ darśayituṃ pṛthagadhikaraṇānīti । <q>tasmādgauṇārthānāmapi prāmāṇya-
marthavādatayā sthitam । lākṣaṇikārthānāṃ ca । kathaṃ punaḥ sṛṣṭyādiṣu lakṣaṇānāmapi lakṣya-
tvam । na hi gaṅgāyāṃ ghoṣa iti lakṣaṇabhūtā gaṅgāpi lakṣyā bhavati । <q>uttaraṃ—lakṣyaiḥ sahaikakriyā-
yogāt ।</q> yāni tāvallakṣyāṇi taiḥ sahaikakriyāyogo lakṣaṇasya । tasyāśca kriyāyā lakṣyatve
nimittatvāt upadhānayogitā hi lakṣyatve hetuḥ । asti copadhānayogitā lakṣaṇabhūtānāmapi
sṛṣṭyādīnām । <q>ato <note n="(1)">B. <dn>lakṣyalakṣaṇatvena</dn></note>lakṣyalakṣaṇateti na virodhaḥ । <note n="(2)">B. <dn>apaśvādiṣu kathaṃ paśuśabdo lakṣaṇayā aśvādiṣu</dn></note>aśvādiṣu paśuśabdaḥ kathaṃ﻿<pb n="264"/>
lakṣaṇayā;</q> aśvādiṣu yāvatā mukhya eva yuktaḥ । atra ca lakṣaṇāgrahaṇamatantraṃ, gauṇasyābhi-
matatvāt rāddhānte । sarvathā mukhyataivāva na gauṇatā, nāpi lākṣaṇikatetyarthaḥ । <q>uttaraṃ
pratiṣedhapūrvakatvāt prayogasya pratiṣiddho hi tajjātīyeṣu jātiśabdo'pareṣu tajjātī-
yeṣu prayujyamāno gauṇatayaiva prayogaṃ labhate ।</q> atra hyanyeṣu paśuṣu paśavo na bhavantīti
pratiṣedhaṃ kṛtvā paśujātīyeṣveva gavāśveṣu paśuśabdaḥ prayujyata iti gauṇa eva tasya prayogaḥ ।
<q>kasmāt ? jātiśabdo hi tajjātīye pratiṣidhyamānaḥ samavetasya guṇasya pratiṣedhyatayaiva
pratiṣedhaviṣayo bhavati</q> jāteranapagamānna jātiḥ pratiṣeddhuṃ śakyate; tathāpi kimityāha
—<q>guṇapratiṣedhācca</q> punastajjātīyāntare <q>prayujyamāno gauṇārtha eva pratīyate ।</q> pūrvavākyeṣu
guṇeṣu pratiṣiddheṣu pratiprasavo guṇānāmeva yuktaḥ ityarthaḥ । <q>tasmājjātiśabdo'pi gauṇaḥ</q>
vācyaguṇayogena pravartanāt <q>ityavirodhaḥ । ataḥ siddhamanapekṣatvam ।</q></p>﻿<pb n="265"/>
﻿<pb n="266"/>﻿<pb n="267"/>
<p><q>sandigdheṣu । nanu ca yavavarāhavetasādiṣu vākyaśeṣāt sandehāyapanayaḥ kṛtaḥ</q>
tena punaruktametaditi bhāvaḥ । pariharati—<q>satyaṃ padārthaviṣayastu saḥ । autpattikānautpatti-
katayā tu sandihyamānaḥ padārthaḥ</q> tatra tatra vākyaśeṣeṇa <q>nirṇītaḥ</q> । atra codayati
—<q>asti vā padasyārthaḥ</q> yadviṣayaḥ sandeho'panīyate । nāstyeveti bhāvaḥ । pariharati
—<q>bāḍhamasti ।</q> āvāpoddhārabhedena padārthayorvācyavācakabhāvāvagamāt । yadi padaṃ padārthamātra-﻿<pb n="268"/>
mabhidhatte padavyatireki ca vākyaṃ nāstītyeṣa niścayaḥ <q>kathaṃ tarhi vākyavākyārthayorautpattikatvaṃ
vṛddhavyavahārāt ।</q> parihati—<q>satyaṃ vākya</q>vākyārthayorautpattikaḥ saṃbandhaḥ <q>sa tvavayavaśo</q>
vākyena vākyārthaḥ pratipādya <q>ityuktaṃ tadbhūtānāṃ</q> kriyārthena samāpnāya iti । <q>vākyārthamātṛ-
kāyāṃ</q> ca asmābhiḥ । <q>tasmāttadbhūte tatra sandehaḥ । iha tu kriyārthe</q> vākyārthe ।
<q>so'yaṃ</q> vākyavākyārthayoḥ padapadārthābhyāṃ <q>viśeṣaḥ । pratipāditaścāyaṃ vistareṇa । ataḥ
kriyārthe saṃśayādapi aprāmāṇyam ।</q> upakramopasaṃhārayorvirodhādvākyārtha eva sandehaḥ ।।
<q>evaṃ sthite</q> pūrvapakṣe <q>upakramavaśādupasaṃhāranirṇayo yuktaḥ kaścit</q> rāddhāntaikadeśī iti <q>manyate
avirodhāt ।</q> kathamavirodha ityāha—<q>sāmānyaṃ hi svātmani viśeṣe ca vartate ।</q> yadi yena
kenacidaktaṃ gṛhyate tadāpyaktā iti ghaṭate । tathā ghṛtenāktatve'pi 1tenopakramavaśenopasaṃhāre
ghṛtaśabdo varṇanīyaḥ sṛṣṭīrupadadhātīti <q>sṛṣṭyarthavat ।</q> yathā sṛṣṭīrupadadhāti iti sṛṣṭiṣvasṛṣṭiṣu
ca sṛṣṭiśabdastathā ghṛte cāghṛte ca ghṛtaśabdo varṇanīyaḥ । <q>atrocyate—syādetadevaṃ yadi
<note n="(1)">B. <dn>tenaitadvaśena</dn></note>﻿<pb n="269"/>
<q>vākyāntaravihitaṃ sāmānyaṃ syāt । ihapunarviśeṣaparyantaivānvayāvagatiḥ ekavākyatvāt ।</q>
ekasmin vākye padānāṃ parasparaṃ vṛttimālocya vākyārtho'vagamyate । tatrāktaśabdasya
ghṛtapadasaṃbandhāt ghṛtaviṣayatvamevāvagamyate । anyathā ghṛtaśabde lakṣaṇā syāt aktaśabde tu na
kaścicchabdārthavirodhaḥ । <q>tasmādvākyaśeṣa</q>nimittā<q>pekṣaṃ kriyārthatvamiti siddhaṃ</q> vākyaśeṣe
yadghṛtapadaṃ tadapekṣaṃ vākyasya vākyārthabodhakatvamiti siddham ।</p>
<p><q>arthādvā ।। yatrāpyanuṣṭhāne saṃśayastatrāpi śāstrameva sandigdhaṃ manyate ।</q> tenā-
prāmāṇyaṃ pūrvapakṣe ।</p>﻿<pb n="270"/>
<p><q>nanu caitadayuktamanuṣṭhānasandehāt śāstrameva sandigdhamiti ।</q> śāstrapūrva-
katvādanuṣṭhānasya (vākyārthabodhakatvamiti siddham ।) yadyapyanuṣṭhānaṃ sandigdhaṃ tathāpi <q>na</q>
śāstraṃ sandigdhamityarthaḥ । pariharati—<q>satyaṃ yathā bhavānāha ।</q> siddhānuśāsane'nuṣṭhāna
sandehe'pi siddhānuśāsanaṃ na sandigdham । <q>kāryānuśāsane tu āskandatyanuṣṭhānasandeho'pi
śāstram ।</q> ākṣeptā āha—<q>kimanuṣṭhānaṃ na śāstrapūrvakaṃ</q> yena tatsandehe śāstraṃ sandigdham ।
tatpūrvakatve hyanuṣṭhānamapi sandihyeta na śāstraṃ sandihyate । <q>satyamanubandhe śāstrapūrvakam ।</q>
utpattidaśāyāṃ śāstrapūrvakamityarthaḥ । <q>niyogārthasatvanuṣṭhānaṃ;</q> na niyogo'nuṣṭhānaṃ pramāpayati ।
tena tasminnapi sandigdhe śāstrameva sandigdhaṃ 1tatparyantatvācchāstrasya । <q>tasmādupapanno
niyogārthasandehaḥ ।</q> anuṣṭhānasandehādapi tatparyantatvāttasya । rāddhāntamāha—<q>sa punaḥ</q> yo ni-
gārthaḥ <q>sāmarthyato nirṇetavyaḥ ।</q> nirṇītaśca bhāṣyakāreṇa । adhyāyārthamupasaṃharati—
<note n="(1)"> <dn>tatparyāyatvāt ।</dn></note>﻿<pb n="271"/>
ato vidhyarthavādamantrasmṛtināmadheyānuṣṭhānato'napekṣatākṣepaṃ kṛtvā sthāpitaṃ prāmāṇyaṃ
codanāyāḥ ।</q> prāmāṇyamityuktaṃ prāmāṇyāyatasya nimittaparīṣṭiriti pratijñātam ।
<trailer><q>iti mahopādhyāyaśālikanāthakṛtāyāṃ</q>
<q>ṛjuvimalāyāṃ prathamasya caturthaḥ pādaḥ</q></trailer>﻿<pb n="272"/>
<head>ṛjuvimalāpañcikāyāṃ</head>
<head>dvitīyādhyāyasya</head>
<head>prathamaḥ pādaḥ</head>
<p><q>bhāvārthāḥ</q> ।। <quote>prathamādhyāye pramāṇalakṣaṇaṃ<note n="(1)">G. <dn>pramāṇaṃ vṛttaṃ</dn></note> vṛttaṃ</quote>ityuktam—idaṃ bhāṣyam ।
prathamādhyāyo hi hetutayā kīrtanīyaḥ । na ca sarveṇaivādhyāyena <note n="(2)">G. <dn>pramāṇamu</dn></note>pramāṇalakṣaṇamuktam । kiṃ
tarhi ? tadekadeśena pratyakṣādilakṣaṇena । nāpi ca tasya śāstrabhedaṃ prati hetubhāvaḥ ityā-
śaṅkyāha</q>—<q>prathame'dhyāye pramāṇalakṣaṇaṃ vṛttamiti, yathā pramāṇaṃ śabdaḥ tathoktamityarthaḥ ।</q>
asyārthaḥ—prathame'dhyāye ityasya bhāṣyasyāyamarthaḥ—yena prakāreṇānapekṣatvākhyena <note n="(3)">G. <dn>anapekṣaṃ</dn></note>śabdaḥ
pramāṇamiti lakṣyate tadanapekṣatvaṃ pramāṇalakṣaṇa <note n="(4)">G. <dn>lakṣaṇaṃ</dn></note>muktamiti । tena kṛtsnaścādhyāyārthaḥ kīrtito
bhavati । bhavati cānapekṣatvasya śāstrabhedaṃ prati hetuteti vakṣyāmaḥ । nanu ca vidhyarthavādādi-
nirūpaṇaṃ prathame'dhyāye kṛtaṃ, na tu yena prakāreṇa śabdasya prāmāṇyaṃ sa ukta iti mattvā
pṛcchati<q>—kuta</q> iti । uttaratvena bhāṣyamavatārayati—<q>yasmādvidhyarthavādasmṛtayastattvatonirṇītāḥ﻿<pb n="273"/>
guṇavidhirnāmadheyaṃ ca parīkṣitam । sandigdhānāmarthānāṃ vākyaśeṣādarthāccādhyavasānamuktam ।</q>
tasmātpramāṇalakṣaṇamuktam । kathaṃ punretāvatyukte<note n="(1)">G. <dn>tyarthe ukte ।</dn></note> pramāṇalakṣaṇamuktaṃ bhavati ? tatrāha—
<q>ete ca</q> arthavādādayaḥ । <q>anyathā gṛhyamāṇāḥ</q> prāmāṇyasya <q>tattvatastu
parijñātā na prāmāṇyaṃ vighnanti । atastattvato nirṇītā yasmāttasmāduktaṃ pramāṇalakṣaṇami-
tyuktam ।</q> vidhyarthavādāditattvanirṇayaḥ prāmāṇyasidhyartha evokta iti prathame'dhyāye pramāṇa-
lakṣaṇamevoktam । tena sādhūktaṃ prathame'dhyāye pramāṇalakṣaṇamuktamiti । 'tanna prasmartavyaṃ'ityanena
bhāṣyeṇa tat anapekṣatvaṃ na vismartavyamiti vadatā <q>anapekṣatvasavyapekṣaṃ bhedābhedakathanamiti</q>
darśitaṃ, tatsmaraṇasyaivopayogitvapradarśanāt <q>kasmādana</q>pekṣatvasavyapekṣaṃ bhedābhedakathanam ?
<q>uttaraṃ—kāryasya hi bhedābhedaḥ kathyate । sa cānapekṣatvanibandhanaḥ</q> । kasmādityāha—<q>anya-
savyapekṣe hi śabde śabdādeva kāryavibhāgo na śakyate vaktum ।</q> upasaṃharati—tasmāttanna
prasmartavyamityanenā<q>na pekṣatvāditi<note n="(2)">G. <dn>anapekṣatvādi yaduktaṃ</dn></note> yaduktaṃ tanna prasmartavyamityuktam ।</q> <note n="(3)">G. <dn>tatrāyaṃ</dn></note>atrāyamabhiprāyaḥ﻿<pb n="274"/>
śāstramedo'dhyāyārthaḥ sādhyabhedo'nubandhabhedaśca taddhetutvenātra kathyate । tacca sādhyaṃ śabdaika-
samadhigamyaṃ tena śabdasyānapekṣatvamapekṣyate । yopyasāvanubandhabhedaḥ śāsrabhedahetuḥ sopi kārya-
bhedāpekṣaḥ । yadi hi yāgādisaṃbandhenāpūrvaṃ bhidyeta, tadā yāgādīnāmanubandhabhāvo bhidyate
bhinnānubandhasamarpakatayā śāstramapi bhidyeta । yāgānubandhena tu yadyapūrvaṃ na bhidyate tadā anubandhabhedā-
bhāvāt na śāstraṃ bhidyate । tasmādanubandhabhedasidhyarthamapi kāryabheda eva kathanīyaḥ । na
cāsau <note n="(1)">G. <dn>apekṣāṃ</dn></note>anapekṣatvaṃ vinā śakyate vaktumiti tasyānapekṣatvasavyapekṣatvam । <quote>anantaraṃ pradhānā-
pradhānāni parīkṣyante bhinnānyabhinnāti ca</quote> iti bhāṣyam śāstrabhedānantaraṃ <note n="(2)">G. <dn>śāstrabhedo'nantaraṃ</q></dn></note>vaktavya iti
vakti । tatra hetuṃ pṛcchati—<q>anantaramiti kasmāt ?</q> ekagrahaṇenāha—<q>anyadapi hi
lakṣaṇāntaraṃ śeṣādyanapekṣatvasavyapekṣameva<note n="(3)">G. <dn>kṣatvameva</dn></note> śabdānnirṇetuṃ śakyate ।</q> tasmātkena viśeṣeṇa
śāstrabhedalakṣaṇamevānapekṣatvalakṣaṇānantaramārabhyate ? uttaraṃ—<q>satyaṃ</q> śeṣādyapyanapekṣatva-
savyapekṣameva śabdānnirṇetuṃ śakyate, <q>na punaranantaraṃ;
<note n="(4)">G. <dn>na punaruttaraṃ</dn></note> idameva tvanantaramityanenābhiprāyeṇa
bhāṣyakāreṇoktam <quote>anantaraṃ pradhānāpradhānāni</quote> iti । <q>kasmātpunaridamevānantaraṃ na
śeṣalakṣaṇādi ?</q> uttaraṃ—<q>kāryabhedapūrvakatvātsarvasyoparitanasya ।</q> kāryabhedapūrvakatvaṃ tu
śāstrabhedapūrvakatvāt, kāryabhedasya ca śāstrabhedaṃ pratihetutvāt । yathā ca śāstrabhedapūrvakatvaṃ﻿<pb n="275"/>
śeṣalakṣaṇasya tathā tṛtīyādye darśitam । <quote>pradhānāpradhānāni parīkṣiṣyante bhinnānyabhinnāni
ce</quote>ti bhāṣyamanubhāpitam ākṣipati—<q>kimidaṃ pradhānāpradhānānīti ।</q> ekagranthenāha—<q>yadi
tāvat pradhānāpradhānāni parīkṣiṣyanta iti saṃbadhyate anyatpratijñātaṃ anyatparīkṣitaṃ
syāt ।</q> tataśca pratijñāparīkṣayorvirodhaḥ । etadeva vivṛṇoti-<q>bhedābhedaparīkṣā hyanantaraṃ
dṛśyate na pradhānāpradhānaparīkṣā ।</q> nanu cetarattadarthe, <quote>yaistu dravyaṃ cikīrṣyate <q>guṇastatra
pratīyate</quote> iti ca pradhānāpradhānaparīkṣāpyanantaraṃ dṛśyata eva ।</q> pariharati—<q>tṛtīyasiddhaṃ hi
tat saṃvyavahārārthamihānītaṃ kāryabhedaprasiddhaye</q> śāstrabhedahetubhūtakāryabhedaprasiddhaye ।
<q>tathā ca bhāṣyakāreṇa,</q> tṛtīye'dhyāye <q>svayamevoktam । atha tatra kiṃ vṛttaṃ yaistu dravyaṃ
cikīrṣyate guṇastatra pratīyeteti tatrāpūrvārthatā vyāvartitā bhavati dṛṣṭaprayojanānā-
mākhyātārthānām । iha tu sarveṣāmeva śeṣāṇāṃ lakṣaṇamucyata iti । <note n="(1)">G. <dn>pradhānānītyasaṃ ।</dn></note>tasmātpradhānāpradhānā-﻿<pb n="276"/>
<q>nītyasaṃbaddham ।</q> ucyate—<q>pradhānāpradhānānīti sādhyānubandhāvabhidhīyete1 ।</q> sādhya
śabdena cotpattyādicatuṣṭayaṃ karaṇopakāraḥ karaṇāvāntaravyapāraḥ aiśvaryalakṣaṇādhikāra-
ścocyate । tāni sādhyāni pradhānaśabdenocyante tathā apradhānaśabdenānubandhā niyogasya
viṣayabhūtāḥ । <q>atastāni pradhānāpradhānāni parīkṣiṣyante, bhinnānyabhinnāni ceti</q> sādhyā-
nāmanubandhānāṃ ca bhedābhedau parīkṣiṣyete ityarthaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>anubandhabhedastāvat—yajati dadāti juhotīti ।</q> tadbhedena śāstrāṇāṃ bhedaḥ ।
<q>anubandhābhedo'pi-ya evaṃ vidvān paurṇamāsīṃ yajata iti ।</q> tadabhedācca śāstrasyābhedaḥ । tathā
kāryabhedopi vrīhīnavahanti, vrīhīn prokṣatītyanayoḥ śāstrayorbhedaḥ । avaghātasya niyamādṛṣṭānu-
viddhaḥ tuṣakaṇavimokaḥ kāryam । prokṣaṇasya tvadṛṣṭaṃ saṃskāraḥ । tena vrīhīnavahanti vrīhīn
prokṣatītyanayoḥ śāstrayorbhedaḥ । ete ca śāstre yadyapi parasparaṃ bhinne tathāpi kevalabhāvārtha-
vidherna bhidyete, anubandhabhedābhāvāt । niyogaviṣayo hyanubandhaḥ na cāvaghātādīnāṃ niyogaviṣaya-
tvamiti vakṣyāmaḥ । sādhyabhedo'pi parasparānapekṣaḥ śāstrabhedahetuḥ । na ca āgneyādyapūrvānapekṣaṃ
avaghātādikāryaṃ sādhyam । guṇakarmaṇāṃ tu anyonyanirapekṣasādhyabhedāt śāstrabhedo yukta eva ।
taduktaṃ prakaraṇāntarādhikaraṇe <quote>nanu camasaguṇavidhānepi śāstrāntaramevaitat, na, vākyā-
taramevaitat na śāstrāntaram । tulyakāryaguṇāntaravidhānāpekṣaṃ tu bhavati śāstrāntaraṃ na
kelalabhāvaguṇavidhānāpekṣam</quote> । (bṛ-2-3-24)</p>
<p>atra ca parasparanirapekṣatākāryāṇāṃ tulyatā abhipretā । etena dadhnā juhotītyādīnāṃ
niyamādṛṣṭarūpasādhyabhedena śāstrabhedo veditavyaḥ । tathā paurṇamāsyadhikaraṇe karaṇetikartavyatā-
<note n="(1)">R. <dn>ndhā abhidhīyante ।</dn></note>﻿<pb n="277"/>
śāstrayorapi<note n="(1)">G. <dn>kartavyatayorapi śāstrabhedena ।</dn></note> sādhyabhedena bhedo'bhidhāsyate । itikartavyatāyā hi karaṇopakāraḥ sādhyaḥ ।
karaṇānāṃ tu karaṇāvāntara<note n="(2)">R. adds <dn>vyāpārāntara</dn></note>kāryāṇi vyāpārarūpāṇi । tathā yāvajjīviko'bhyāsa ityatra
jīvanādhikārakāmādhikārayoḥ sādhyabhedena śāstrabhedo varṇayiṣyate<note n="(3)">G. <dn>vartiṣyate ।</dn></note> । abhedaśca sādhyasya
'samidho yajati' 'tanūnapātaṃ yajati' [ityatra] 'āgneyo'ṣṭākapāla' ityadhikārākhyaikasādhyayo-
gitvāt । yadyapi anubandhabhedena samidādyāgneyādiśāstrāṇi bhinnāni tathāpi sādhyābhedāda-
bhinnāni । <q>tasmāt sūktaṃ pradhānāpradhānāni parīkṣiṣyante bhinnānyabhinnāni ceti । eṣa
evārtho varṇanīyo nānya ityanantaraśabdavyākhyānabhetat । eṣa cādhyāyasaṃbandha ityānantaryasya
hetvabhidhānam ।</q> bhāṣye caśabdo yasmādarthe-yasmādeṣo'dhyāyasaṃbandhaḥ tasmādanantaraṃ śāstrabheda-
lakṣaṇaṃ kartavyam । yathā cāyaṃ heturbhavati <q>tathā darśitamasmābhiḥ ।</q></p>
<p><q>tadiha ṣaṅvidhaḥ karmabhedo vakṣyate—śabdāntaraṃ abhyāsaḥ saṅkhyā guṇaḥ prakriyā
nāmadheyamiti</q> bhāṣyānubhāṣaṇam । ākṣipati—<q>kathaṃ karmabhedaḥ śabdāntaram ।</q> bhāva-﻿<pb n="278"/>
sādhanaṃ bhedaśabdaṃ gṛhītvā'yamākṣepaḥ । samādhatte—<q>bhidyatte'neneti bhedaḥ</q> tena karaṇasādhano
bhedaśabdaḥ । yattchabdāntarādiniḥ bhidyate <note n="(1)">G. <dn>yacca</dn></note>tacca karma bhāvārtha ityarthaḥ । śabdāntarādibhiḥ
ṣaḍbhiḥ bhāvārthamātrabhedaḥ nānubandhabhedaḥ, nāpi śāstrabhedaḥ, na ca niyogabhedaḥ । saṅkhyayā
hi saptadaśa prājāpatyānityatra nānubandhabhāvo bhidyate, prājāpatyaprātipadikasamarpitānāṃ dravyadevatā-
saṃbandhānāṃ <note n="(2)"> <dn>tatsannidhikṛnniyoga ।</dn></note>sakṛnniyogaviṣayatvāt । tantrasaṃbandhe ca viṣayabhāvo na bhidyate darśapūrṇamāsābhyāmitivat ।
dravyadevatāsaṃbandhaśca vidhiviṣaya iti nibandhakāraḥ śabdabalavādī manyate । ślokāścātra bhavanti—
adhyāyena dvitīyena gururbhāṣyanibandhane ।
sādhyānubandhabhedābhyāṃ śāstrabhedamavarṇayata ।।
anyonyanirapekṣaṃ tu yatsādhyaṃ śāstrabhedakam ।
sādhanānāṃ viśeṣeṇa tadbhedā bahudhoditāḥ ।।
abhidhānāntarābhyāsaguṇākhyāprakriyāntaraiḥ ।
anubandhāstu bhidyante śāstrabhedasya hetavaḥ ।।
anubandhātmanaikyepi bhāvamātrāṇi bhindati ।
<note n="(3)">G. <dn>tadbhedatvā.</dn></note>tadbhettṛttvāviśeṣeṇa saṃkhyāpyatraiva sūtritā ।।
yasmāt karaṇasādhano bhedaśabdaḥ tasmātkarmabheda ityuktam । <q>vakṣyamāṇakramānapekṣaṃ śabdānta-
rādīnāṃ vyutkrameṇoccāraṇaṃ kramasyānaupayikatvapradarśanārtham ।</q> bhāvārthabhedakatve śabdā-
ntarādīnāṃ parasparakramāpekṣā nāstītyarthaḥ ।</p>
<p>atra codayati—<q>vakṣyamāṇamatrānusaṃkīrtyate pratijñārūpeṇa<note n="(4)">G. <dn>pratijñābhiprāyeṇa kīrtitamiti</dn></note> । kimarthaṃ ? hetvabhidhāna-
kāla eva pratijñābhidhānaṃ nyāyyaṃ naiyyāyikāḥ ।</q> nyāyavyavahāriṇo manyante । hetvavatārāya<note n="(5)"> <dn>hetvabhidhānāya</dn></note>﻿<pb n="279"/>
hi pratijñā ucyate sa tu hetvabhidhānakāla evocitā । pariharati—<q>satyaṃ</q>sādhyatayā yatra prati-
jñeyo'rthaḥ ucyate tatraivaṃ, <q>suravagrahaṇārthañcaitat<note n="(1)"> <dn>sukhagrahaṇārthatve</dn></note> । śrotṛbuddhisamādhānāt</q> śāstrabhedahetu<note n="(2)"> <dn>hetutayā'nu</dn></note>-
bhūtānubandhabhedapratipādanaṃ kariṣyata<note n="(3)">G. <dn>kariṣya i</dn></note> ityukte tajjijñāsākṣiptacetasaḥ śrotuḥ buddhiḥ samāhitā satī
sukhena śāstrabhedamucyamānaṃ prati pravartate । tadetannānākarmalakṣaṇamadhyāyamācakṣata iti vadan
<q>pūrvācāryāṇāmabhidhānaprasiddhiṃ darśayati । anāditāṃ nyāyasya kathayitum ।</q> anādirayaṃ
nyāyaḥ jaiminiprabhṛtibhiḥ kenacideva viśeṣeṇa svagranthena nibadhyate । <q>ato'nyadupoddhātātpra-
saktānuprasaktaṃ ceti apratijñātārthacintādoṣaparihārārtham ।</q> yadapi pratijñātācchāstra-
