bhedādanyaccintyate tadupoddhātatvena yathedamevādyam । prasaktānuprasaktañca—yathā mantratadbheda-
lakṣaṇādi । ato na kaściddoṣaḥ । <q>prathamaṃ tāvadidaṃ cintyate prathame'dhyāye idamuktaṃ codanā-
lakṣaṇo'rtho dharma iti । codanā ca kriyāyā abhidhāyakaṃ vākyaṃ; vākye ca padānāmarthaḥ ।﻿<pb n="280"/>
tatra kiṃ padena padena dharmaḥ ucyate uta sarvaireka iti</q> bhāṣyānubhāṣaṇam । ākṣipati
—yuktaṃ tāvat prathamaṃ tāvadidaṃ cintyate kiṃ padena padena dharmaḥ ucyate uta sarvaireka ityevaṃ
saṃbandha iti iti śabdaścātra draṣṭavyaḥ । <q>prathame'dhyāye idamuktamityasya granthasya1 kaḥ
prasaṅgaḥ</q> kena cāyaṃ granthaḥ saṃbadhyate । <q>ato na vidmaḥ kathamidaṃ vyākhyeyamiti ।
atrābhidhīyate-kiṃ padena padena dharmaḥ</q> ucyate ityetāvatyukte svasiddhānta<q>prakriyāvirodhaṃ</q>
kaścinmanyate <q>vākyavākyārthayoḥ autpattikasaṃbandhābhidhānāt ।</q> yadā hi vākyenaiva
vākyārthaḥ ucyate tadā padārtho nāmāsya pṛthagartho nāsti । tatkathaṃ padena padenābhihi-
tasyārthasya niyogaviṣayatā śaṅkyata iti । <q>tasyaivaṃ</q> prakriyāvirodhaṃ <q>manvānasyaitaduttaraṃ pratha-
me'dhyāye</q> ityādibhāṣyam । asyārthaṃ vyācaṣṭe—<q>satyaṃ prathame'dhyāye idamuktaṃ codanā-
lakṣaṇo'rtho dharma iti । codanā ca vākyam ।</q> tena vākyalakṣaṇa eva vākyārtha
ityuktaṃ codanālakṣaṇasūtre । tathāpi <q>vākye ca padānāmapyartho'stītyuktam । tadbhūtānāṃ</q>
kriyārthena samāmnāya iti padānyeva padārthānanvitānabhidadhati vākyaśabdābhidheyāni vākyārthamabhi-
<note n="(1)"> <dn>granthakalpakaḥ</dn></note>﻿<pb n="281"/>
dadhati tena na prakriyāvirodhaḥ । <q>ato yuktamidaṃ—kiṃ padena padena dharmaḥ ucyate uta
sarvereka iti ।</q> nanvetadayuktam । na hi pratipadaṃ dharmābhidhāyakatvaṃ, kiṃ tarhi liṅādi
śabda eva dharmamapūrvātmānamācaṣṭe ityāśaṅkya vyācaṣṭe—<q>etaduktaṃ bhavati । kiṃ padena padena abhi-
hitasyārthasya kāryayogitā uta parasparasaṃbandhasavyapekṣasyeti</q> yatpadābhihitasyārthasya kārya-
yogitā niyogaviṣayatā tena padena niyoga ukto bhavati kevalānniyogaśabdānniyogajñā-
nānutpatteḥ । <q>kathaṃ punaḥ parasparasaṃbandhitayā'vagamyamānasyārthasyānyapadārthāsaṃbandhina
eva kāryayogitā</q> śaṅkyate parasparaṃ saṃbandhāvagateḥ sarveṣāṃ niyogasaṃbandho nāvagamyate ।
pariharati—<q>dṛṣṭā hi aruṇādiṣu</q> kāryasaṃbandhāvagatiḥ <q>dravyaguṇayoḥ</q> parasparasaṃbandhinorapi ।
tena kāryayogitve parasparasaṃbandhāvagamāvirodhaḥ । <q>nanu ca</q> tatra dravyaguṇayoḥ parasparasaṃbandhā-
<q>vagatirnāsti ityuktam ।</q> tṛtīyāvibhaktibalena krayasaṃbandhāvagamāt । pariharati—<q>satyameva-
maidamarthyena nāsti</q> parasparasaṃbandha ityuktam । <q>na punarguṇaguṇitayāpi</q> nāsti; api tu
astyevetyarthaḥ । <q>anyathāpi hi</q> yadi parasparasaṃbandho nāvagamyate tadā <q>niyama eva na syāt ।</q>
anaruṇayāpyekahāyanyā krayaḥ syāt । anekahāyanyāpyaruṇayā iti । asti ca niyamaḥ
iti tenāstyeva parasparasaṃbandhāvagatiriti । <q>evamatrāpi nāmākhyātayoḥ</q> kiṃ kriyākāra-
kayoḥ <q>saṃbandhanirapekṣa eva niyogasaṃbandhaḥ utājahatkriyākārakasaṃbandha evetyupapannaḥ﻿<pb n="282"/>
<q>saṃśayaḥ ।</q> na jahāti kriyākārakasaṃbandhaṃ yaḥ so'jahatkriyākārakasaṃbandhaḥ sa hi niyoga-
saṃbandhaḥ । <q>kintāvatprāptamiti । asmin saṃśaye kintāvadyuktamityarthaḥ ।</q> prāptaśabdo'yaṃ
yuktaśabdārthe vartate । uttaraṃ—<q>pratipadaṃ dharmasaṃbandha iti yuktam । kasmāt ?</q> uttaraṃ—<q>niyo-
gārthatvāduccāraṇasya sarvapadānām ।</q> sarvāṇyeva padāni niyogaidamarthyāpannapadārthapratipādana-
parāṇi । kāryārthatvāduccāraṇasya padānāṃ sarveṣām । <q>nanu kriyākārakasaṃbandhopyatrābagamyate
tena</q> kriyākārakayorapyaidamarthyāvagamāt tadaparityāgena ca sarveṣāmeva sākṣānniyogaidamarthyaṃ yujyate ।
pariharati—<q>satyaṃ</q> saṃbandho'vagamyate kriyākārakalakṣaṇaḥ <q>na tu kriyārthatve kārakāṇāṃ pramāṇa-
masti । niyogārthasya nirapekṣasya sādhyatvenāvagamāt ।</q> yadi parasparaṃ kriyākārakayo raidamarthyaṃ
nāsti tadā kriyākārakasambandhopi nāstīti matvā kaścinmandadhīścodayati-<q>kathaṃ punaḥ nirvyāpārameva
kārakaṃ niyogārthamabhiniṣpādayati</q> kārakībhūtaṃ hi niyogaidamarthyāpannatayā niyogārthābhi-
niṣpādakam । 1kathaṃ kriyākārakasaṃbandhaṃ vinā kārakatvaṃ ? <q>karma vā akriyamāṇaṃ</q> svayamalabdha-
sattākaṃ kathaṃ niyogamabhiniṣpādayati ? pariharati—<q>bhavatvarthādayaṃ</q> kriyākārakasaṃbandhaḥ
<q>dravyaguṇayoriva</q> guṇaguṇitayā <q>saṃbandhaḥ । tādarthyaṃ tu 2niyogāyaiva</q> anyaddhi tādarthyam ।
<note n="(1)">G. <dn>karma.</dn></note>
<note n="(2)">G. <dn>niyogārthataiva</dn></note>﻿<pb n="283"/>
anyaśca kriyākārakasaṃbandha ityāśayaḥ । <q>tasmātpratipadaṃ dharmaḥ । atrocyate—naitadupapadyate ।</q>
kasmādityāha—<q>yadi hyajahatāṃ pratītamarthaṃ niyogārthatā na syāt syātpratipadaṃ dharmaḥ ।</q> asyārthaḥ
-sarvatra tātparyasya balīyastvāt pratīto'pi parasparasambandhaḥ yujyate yadi tasmin svīkriyamāṇe
niyogaṃ prati tātparyaṃ hīyeta । <q>yatra punarapekṣitaiva saṃbandhāvagatiḥ ānuguṇyena tatra tattyāge
śrutahānameva syāt । na caitat</q> <note n="(1)">G. adds <dn>na caitadvijñānaṃ</dn></note>śruterhānaṃ yuktam । pratipadaṃ dharmasambandhe parasparasambandhāvagatiḥ
tyaktā syāt kāraṇābhāvādeva । ekakrayākhyakriyānupraveśo hi dravyaguṇayoḥ parasparaṃ sambandhā-
vagame kāraṇam । iha tu pratipadaṃ anubandhabhedena niyogabhedāt bhinnaniyogānupraveśinoḥ
nāmākhyātayoḥ nirbījaḥ parasparasaṃbandha ityavagamyamāno'pi tyajanīyaḥ । sa ca vidhinā'pekṣitaḥ ।
na hi kriyāmantareṇa kārakatvaṃ saṃbhavati । na ca kārakamantareṇa kriyāniṣpattiriti । tasmā-
danyatarānugṛhīto'nyataro vidhyartha iti yuktam । nirvahati ca paraṃparayāpi tātparyamityadoṣaḥ ।
<q>evaṃ cādṛṣṭānumānaprasaṅkalpanā'lpīyasī bhaviṣyatīti</q> bhāṣyam । atra kila bhāṣye evaṃ
pratīyate yadi pratipadaṃ dharmaḥ syāt tadā pratipadamapūrvāṇi kalpanīyāni । tāni cādṛṣṭānu-
mānagamyāni । sāmānyato dṛṣṭaṃ hi tārkikāṇāmadṛṣṭānumānaśabdenābhihitam । tathoktam
sparśaśca na dṛṣṭānāṃ iti <quote>adṛṣṭaliṅgo vāyuḥ</quote> iti । tenāyaṃ granthasaṃbandhaḥ— evamalpīyasyadṛṣṭānu-
mānasyāpūrvaviṣayasya sāmānyato dṛṣṭānumānasya prasaṅgakalpanā bhavatīti । atra codayati—<q>kā﻿<pb n="284"/>
punaratrādṛṣṭānumānaprasaṅgakalpanā ? śabdādapi hi dṛṣṭaṃ dṛṣṭameva</q> । yadi hyadṛṣṭakalpanā bhavet
tadaivaṃ yujyate vaktuṃ <note n="(1)">G. adds <dn>evamalpīyasī</dn></note>evamadṛṣṭānumānaprasaṅgakalpanā bhaviṣyati' iti । na cātrādṛṣṭakalpanāsti
śabdābhidheyatvādapūrvasya । pariharati—<q>satyaṃ yathā bhavānāha</q> nāmnādṛṣṭakalpaneti । <q>pratipadaṃ
dharmakalpanāyāṃ āśrayāśrayiprasaṅge niyamānumānamadṛṣṭaṃ apramāṇakaṃ<note n="(2)">G. <dn>adṛṣṭapramāṇakaṃ</dn></note> prāpnotītyarthaḥ ।</q>
kriyāśūnyasya kārakatvānupapatteḥ kārakeṇa<note n="(3)">G. <dn>kārakatvena</dn></note> kriyā āśrayitvena grāhyā । kriyayāpi <note n="(4)"> <dn>svayamapi</dn></note>svayaṃ
niṣpannayā kārakamāśrayabhūtaṃ grāhyam । tatra ca niyamāvagatiḥ । imāmeva kriyāmāśritya
kārakametanniyogaṃ niṣpādayati । etadeva ca kārakamāśrityeyaṃ kriyetyevaṃrūpā adṛṣṭāśrayā-
śrayiprasaṅgakalpanā niṣpramāṇikā syāt । aruṇaikahāyanīnyāyavailakṣaṇyāt । <q>tatra ca bahva-
dṛṣṭānumānaprasaṅgakalpanā kathaṃ ? uttaraṃ—evaṃ tāvadāśrayatvaṃ kārakāṇāṃ āśrayitvaṃ ca
karmaṇāṃ punaśca tatsiddhaye sādhyasādhanatvaṃ viśeṣaniyamaśceti । anyatarānugṛhītapakṣe punaḥ
alpīyasyadṛṣṭānumānaprasaṅgakalpanā bhaviṣyatīti । <quote>kimidaṃ adṛṣṭānumānaprasaṅgakalpaneti ?
uttaraṃ—adṛṣṭamapramāṇakaṃ</q> yatkilādṛṣṭaṃ tadapramāṇakaṃ anumānaṃ niyamānumānaṃ yasya āśrayāśrayitva-
prasaṅgasya asau adṛṣṭānumānaprasaṅgaḥ adṛṣṭānumānaśvāsau prasaṅgaśceti tasya kalpanā alpīyasī ।﻿<pb n="285"/>
<q>nanu ca naiva bhavati kalpanā kimidaṃ alpīyasīti ?</q> pariharati—<q>anyatarānugṛhīta-
pakṣe'pi vidhyarthasyaiva</q> vidheyaṃ vidhyarthaḥ tasyaivānugraha iti <q>vidyate kalpanā ।</q> anugraho'pi
kriyamāṇo na svarūpamātrasyābhyupeyaḥ niyogārthavirodhāt । <q>nanu ca śābdamevedaṃ kimatra
kalpyate</q> ? pariharati—<q>kāryato'vagamaṃ navame vakṣyāmaḥ</q> apūrvaprayuktatvābhyupagamena । tena
kalpanāvācoyuktirghaṭate । yadi kāryato'vagatiḥ na tarhi śābdatvamityāśaṅkyāha—<q>śabdā-
vagatakāryamūlatvāttu śābdam । tasmātsādhūktam evamalpīyasyadṛṣṭhānumānaprasaṅkalpanā
bhaviṣyatīti</q> tasmādekamapūrvaṃ iti bhāṣyakāreṇopasaṃhṛtamākṣipati—<q>kimidamekamapūrvamiti ।</q>
pariharati—<q>nanvidameva,</q> suvyakta evāyamarthaḥ । punarākṣipati—<q>naivaṃ<note n="(1)">G. <dn>mevaṃ</dn></note> ekasmādapūrvamiti
prakamāt ।</q> tasmādekasmādapūrvamityupasahartavyam । naikamapūrvamiti । <q>atrābhidhīyate—yadā
pūrvapakṣe pratipadaṃ dharmaḥ tadā pratipadaṃ niyogabhedena bhavitavyam ।</q> kasmāt ?
uttaram—<q>pratipadamanubandhabhedāt ।</q> yadā punaḥ parasparasaṃbaddhānāṃ vidhinā yoga<note n="(2)">G. <dn>vidhiniyogaḥ</dn></note>;
tadā eka evānubandhaḥ । ataścaikamapūrvamityupasaṃhṛtam । nanvevamapi ekasmādapūrvamiti
kimiti nopasaṃhṛtam yena phaladvāreṇopasaṃhāraḥ<note n="(3)">G. <dn>upasaṃhiṛyate</dn></note> ityāha-<q>amumeva ca pūrvapakṣe kāryabhedaṃ darśayituṃ﻿<pb n="286"/>
<q>bhagavatā bhāṣyakāreṇa phalenopasaṃhṛtam tasmādekamapūrvamiti,</q> kāryabhedadarśanaṃ ca
pūrvapakṣe<note n="(1)">G. <dn>parasparāsaṃbandhā</dn></note> parasparasaṃbandhāvagatiḥ nirbījā prāpnotīti siddhāntayuktisiddhyartham । atra ca niyo-
gārthatvāduccāraṇasya sarvapadānāṃ sākṣānniyogasaṃbandho bhavati । sākṣātsambandhasaṃbhave ca
paramparāśrayaṇānupapatteḥ sarveṣāṃ niyogaviṣayatvamiti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । rāddhāntastu sarveṣāṃ
niyogaviṣayatve parasparasaṃbandhāvagamavirodhāt pratipadaṃ niyogabhede bhinnaniyogānupraveśināṃ
sambandhānupapatteḥ yathāviniyogaṃ viṣayabhāvo<note n="(2)">G. <dn>viṣayabhedo</dn></note> nyāyya iti anyatarānugṛhītasyānyatarasya
viṣayatvam । parasparasaṃbandhāśrayaṇe ca (vi)niyogāvagama<note n="(3)">G. <dn>niyogāvagatameva</dn></note>eva pramāṇamiti ।</p>
<p><q>yadā ekasmādapūrvaṃ tadā saṃdehaḥ । kiṃ bhāvaśabdebhyaḥ uta dravyaguṇaśabdebhya iti</q>
atra pṛcchati—<q>bhāvaśabdagrahaṇena kasya grahaṇaṃ ?</q> ekadeśyuttaramāha—<q>ākhyātānāmeva ।</q>
punaścodayati—<q>evaṃ tarhi sandehaṃ darśayatā kiṃ</q> <q>nāmaśabdebhyaḥ utākhyātaśabdebhya iti
vaktavyam । kimidamucyate—kiṃ bhāvaśabdebhyaḥ uta dravyaguṇaśabdebhya iti ।</q> ākṣeptāraṃ﻿<pb n="287"/>
pṛcchati—<q><note n="(1)">G. <dn>kiṃ tatra</dn></note>kiṃ vātrātiricyate</q> bhāṣyakārīyepi sandehopanyāse kiñcidadhikaṃ nāsti yena
lābhena kiṃ nāmaśabdebhya utākhyātaśabdebhya iti kartumucitamiti codyate । ākṣeptā''ha
<q>—dvirukto nāmaśabdo'</q>tiricyate । dravyaguṇaśabdagrahaṇe kriyamāṇe <note n="(2)">G. <dn>nākhyātaśabdānāṃ</dn></note>nāmaśabdānāṃ śabda-
dvayenopasaṅgrahaḥ । bhāvaśabdagrahaṇe<note n="(3)">G. <dn>bhāvaśabdāśrayaṇe</dn></note> kriyamāṇe pratiyogitayā dravyaguṇagrahaṇaṃ kartavyam ।
vācyāvacchedena hi tadā śabdo nirdiśyata iti bhinnau dravyaguṇaśabdau vācyau śabdopasthāpa-
nāyoccārayitavyau । ākhyātagrahaṇe tu svarūpeṇa śabdanirdeśāt śabdasvarūpanirdeśako nāma-
<q>śabda</q> eva prayoktavyo bhavati । tataśca śabdadvayānuccāraṇaṃ lāghabārtham । paramasamādhātā
āha—<q>anabhiprāyajño hi bhavāt yadi hi kimākhyātaśabdebhyaḥ uta nāmaśabdebhya ityucyate
tataśca nirṇīyate</q> ākhyātaśabdebhya evāpūrvamiti tadā āgneyo'ṣṭhākapāla ityakriyārthaḥ
syāt । dravyadevatāsambandho niyogaviṣayo na syāt nāmatvādāgneyaśabdasya; bhavatīti ca
bhavatyarthaḥ kriyārtho niyogaviṣayaḥ syāt <q>ākhyātatvāt</q> bhavatiśabdasya । aniṣṭaṃ caita-
dubhayamapi । <q>bhavatyarthasyavidheyatvāt</q> । na hi bhūto bhavatyartho niyoktuṃ śakyate amṛtaśca
svayamavidyamānatvāt । tena bhavatyartho na vidheyaḥ । <q>dravyadevatāsaṃbandhasya ca vidheyatvāt ।﻿<pb n="288"/>
<q>tasmāda</q>niṣṭāpattirmābhūditi <q>nāmākhyātagrahaṇaṃ na kṛtaṃ</q> bhagavatā <q>bhāṣyakāreṇa । kiṃ tarhi ?
yenaiva svabhāvenākhyātārthasya vidhyarthatā saṃbhavati yena ca svabhāvena nāmno</q> vidhyarthatā
<q>na saṃbhavati tenaiva svabhāvenopanyāsaḥ kṛto</q> bhagavatā bhāṣyakāreṇa । <q>kena svabhāvenā-
khyātārthasya vidhyarthatā, kena vā nāmno na <note n="(1)">G. <dn>nivartiteti</dn></note>saṃbhavatīti</q> praśnadvaye yathā saṅkhyamuttaradvayam ।
<q>bhāvārthatayā ākhyātārthasya vidhyarthatā, dravyaguṇābhidhānatayā ca nāmno</q> na vidhyarthatā ।
yathā caitattathopariṣṭādvyākhyāsyāmaḥ<note n="(2)"> <dn>vakṣyāmaḥ</dn></note> । atra bhāṣyam—<quote>kaḥ punarbhāvaḥ ke vā bhāvaśabdā</quote>
iti tadvyācaṣṭe—<q>kaḥ punarayamākhyātārthavyatirikto bhāvo nāma ? kaścākhyātaśabdavyati-
rikto bhāvaśabdo nāma ।</q> uttarabhāṣyaṃ vyācaṣṭe—<q>prativacanantu</q> uttaraṃ tu <q>yajeta dadātijuhotī-
tyeṣāṃ</q> yo'rthaḥ sa bhāvārthaḥ ete ca bhāvaśabdā iti <q><quote>nanu ca yāgadānahomaśabdā eta</quote></q>
iti parihārabhāṣyam । tadvyācaṣṭe—<q>nanu sa evāyamākhyātārthaḥ ta evāmī ākhyāta-
śabdāḥ ityākṣepaḥ <quote>naitadevaṃ, yāgādiśabdāścaita</quote></q> iti parihārabhāṣyaṃ vyācaṣṭe—<q>samādhānaṃ
tu nākhyātārthamātraṃ yajeta dadāti juhotītyatra</q> gamyate kiṃ tarhi ? <q>arthāntarotpāda-﻿<pb n="289"/>
<q>katvamapi,</q> karturanyo yo'rthaḥ tadutpādakatvamapi gamyate । <q>na kevalaṃ pūrvāparībhāva evā-
vagamyate yathā bhavatīti ।</q> pūrvāparībhāvamātraṃ ākhyātamātrārthaḥ<note n="(1)">G. <dn>ākhyātārthaḥ</dn></note> । na tathā bhāvayedityatra<note n="(2)">G. <dn>pacatītyatra</dn></note>
anyotpādakatvaṃ tu bhāvārthaḥ<note n="(3)">G. <dn>bhāvārthatvaṃ</dn></note> tacca bhavatītyatra nāsti । kartureva tatrotpattyavagamāt । yadeta-
duktamasmābhiḥ taduktaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇāpi <quote>yajyādyarthaścāto'vagamyate bhāvayediti ca</quote> ityanena
bhāṣyeṇa । nanvanya evārtho'sya bhāṣyasyeti matvā pṛcchati—<q>kimuktamanena</q> bhāṣyeṇa । uttaraṃ
<q>—pūrvāparībhāvaścāto'bagamyate anyotpādakatvaṃ ceti</q> tatra <note n="(4)">G. <dn>yatra kāryaścāto</dn></note><q>yajyādyarthaścāto'vagamyata</q>
ityanena pūrvāparībhūtayāgādyavagatiruktā । <q>bhāvayedi</q>tyanyotpādakatvāvagatiḥ । <q>punaścāyamartho</q>
bhāṣyakāreṇa <q>prakaṭīkṛtaḥ । tathā yateta yathā yatkiṃñcidbhavatīti ।</q> anyotpattyanuguṇaḥ puruṣa-
prayatno'vagamyata ityarthaḥ । <q>tenaite ākhyātaśabdā api bhāvaśabdā ityucyante ।</q> yataḥ pūrvā-
parībhūtānyotpādakatvasvabhāvo yo'rthaḥ sa bhāvārthaḥ tadarthāśca śabdāḥ bhāvaśabdāḥ । <q>ato dravyaguṇa-
śabdagrahaṇamapi ।</q> nāmaśabde hi kriyamāṇe pratiyogyartho na nirdiṣṭaḥ syāt nāmaśabdānāmapi keṣāṃ
cidbhāvārthatvāt । nanvevamapi yena svabhāvena kriyārthatvaṃ<note n="(5)">G. <dn>akiyārthatvaṃ na ni</dn></note> tanna nirdiṣṭaṃ syāditi yadi kaścinmanyate﻿<pb n="290"/>
taṃ pratyāha—<q>dravyaguṇapratyayotpākatvādakriyārthatvaṃ na nāmatvāt ।</q> nāmnaḥ āgneya ityādeḥ
kriyārthatvadarśanāt । <q>kiṃ tāvatprāptamaviśeṣeṇeti । ko'bhiprāyaḥ</q> evaṃ vadato bhāṣyakārasya ।
<q>uttaraṃ—dravyaṃ vā bhavatu kriyārthaṃ kriyā vā bhavatu dravyārthā । sarvathā tāvadaparityakta-
kiyākārakasambandha eva kāryasaṃbandhaḥ ।</q> yadi kriyāviṣayo niyogaḥ tadā itarattadarthamiti
nyāyāt dravyaṃ kriyārtham । yadā tu dravyaṃ niyogaviṣayaḥ tadā kriyā dravyārthā । pakṣadvayepi
cāsmin kriyādravyārthapakṣe kriyākārakasambandho na virudhyate । tenāgṛhyamāṇaviśeṣatvādanyatarasya
vidhiviṣayatvam । na caivamanadhyavasāyenāprāmāṇyam । anuṣṭhānasyādhyavasitatvāt । ekarūpameva
hi pakṣadvayeṣyanuṣṭhānaṃ anuṣṭhānānadhyavasāyena cāprāmāṇyam । <q>atrocyate । naivaṃ sidhyati
kriyākārakasaṃbandhaḥ । yadā hi kriyā dravyārthā</q> tadā dravyaviṣayo niyogaḥ <q>tadā kriyā-
kārakasambandhastyakta eva bhavati । kasmāt ?</q> uttaraṃ—<q>dravyaṃ hi tadā karmabhūtaṃ kriyāyāṃ</q>
pradhānabhūtaṃ dravyaṃ, kriyayā īpsyamānatvāt । īpsyamānaśca karmāpadyeta । <q>na ca karma kārakaṃ
kārakasthā hyutpattiḥ karmeti vakṣyāmaḥ</q> । kāraka<note n="(1)">M. <dn>kārakasthā</dn></note>sya yā avasthotpadyate sā karma na kārakāvasthaiva ।
yadi karma kārakaṃ na bhavati <q>kathaṃ tarhi karmaṇi kārake dvitīyetyāgamaḥ । tathā karturīpsita-</q>﻿<pb n="291"/>
<q>tamaṃ karmeti ca kārakādhikāre</q> । etadāgamaparyālocanayāpi karmaṇaḥ kārakatvamavagamyate karmaṇi
kārake dvitīyeti sāmānādhikaraṇyanirdeśāt । tathā īpsitatamaṃ yatkārakaṃ tatkarmetyabhidhānāt ।
samādhatte—<q>yatra kriyāphalamabhiniṣpadyate</q> tat kārakaṃ <q>karmeti sūtrārthaḥ</q> । kriyāphalabhāgitvaṃ
kārakasya karmatvaṃ; na punaḥ kriyāniṣpādakatvaṃ kriyāniṣpādakatayā ca kārakatvaṃ nānyathā । kasmādevaṃ
vidhaḥ sūtrārthaḥ ? ityatrāha<q>—anyathāhīpsitatamagrahaṇamanarthakaṃ syāt</q> । na hi kriyāniṣpādakaṃ
kriyayā īpsitatamaṃ bhavati । kriyājanyaphalabhāgitvāvasthā ca kriyayā īpsitatamā bhavati ।
<q>tasmāt karmaṇi kārake dvitīyetyapi siddham</q> । avasthādvayayogitvāt । <q>tasmāt
kriyārthaṃ</q> niyogārthaṃ niyogaviṣayasamarpakaṃ <q>yadā''khyātaṃ</q> bhavati <q>tadaiva dravyaguṇayoḥ kāra-
katvasiddhiḥ kārakatvena ca</q> tayoḥ śravaṇaṃ; naitadanugrahāya ākhyātārthasyaiva niyogārthatvaṃ
niścīyate ata āha—<q>ye bhāvārthāḥ karmaśabdāstebhyaḥ kriyā pratīyeta yajetetyevamādibhyaḥ ।</q>
atra sūtrakāreṇa bhāvārthebhyaḥ kiyā pratīyeteti vadatā hetvantarānupādānāt bhāvārthatvameva heturukta
iti matvā pṛcchati—<q>kutaḥ iti ।</q> tadvyācaṣṭe—<q>kuta iti praśnaḥ <note n="(1)">G. <dn>kimatra</dn></note>kimanyathā bhāvārthatvaṃ hīyeta</q>
tadapi bhāvārthasyāniyogaviṣayatve bhāvārthatvameva hīyeta tadā syādayaṃ hetuḥ na caitadastīti bhāvaḥ ।﻿<pb n="292"/>
uttaraṃ—<q>bāḍhaṃ hīyate pūrvāparībhāve hi bhāvārthatvaṃ bhavati</q> bhāvaśabdasya pūrvāparībhāva-
vācitvāt । tathāpi kimityāha—<q>sa ca pūrvāparībhāvo'tra dravyaguṇayoḥ tadarthatve sati</q>
bhavati । <q>anyathā hi godohanena paśukāmasya praṇayeditivadāśrayāvagatireva syāt । na
ca godohanasādhyaṃ praṇayanamavasīyate</q> । asyārthaḥ-sādhyatve hi bhāvārthatvaṃ bhavati bhāvārthasya
ca niyogaviṣayatve dravyaguṇayośca tadarthatve sādhyatvaṃ bhāvārthasya sampadyate । dravyaguṇavostu
niyogārthatve āśrayamātratayaivāranmātārthavatvamavagataṃ<note n="(1)">R. <dn>khyātārthānāmavagatiḥ</dn></note> syāt na sādhyatvena godohanena paśukāmasya
praṇayeditivat । <q>nanu ca godohanena paśukāmasya praṇayedityapi pūrvāparībhūtameva praṇayanaṃ
pratīyate । godohanaṃ ca</q> karaṇameva । ato'siddho dṛṣṭāntaḥ । pariharati—<q>satyaṃ pratīyate na
punaḥ godohanena praṇayedityevadvākyārthatayā,</q> asminvākye godohanasya vākyārthatvāt tadupa-
kārakatvācca praṇayanasya viparītaḥ sādhyasādhanabhāvo'vagamyate । laukikastvayaṃ kriyākārakabhāvaḥ
śabdenopādīyate । <q>tasmādaniyamapakṣe na niyamena kriyākārakabhāvamajahato vidhyarthatvaṃ
vākyasya pratīyate</q> । yadā tāvat kriyāniyogārthā tadā pratīyamānakiyākārakabhāvā-
parityāgaḥ । dravyaguṇayostu kiyārthatvena uktena nyāyena kiyākārakabhāvaparityāga eveti
nāniyamaḥ । api tu bhāvārtha eva niyogārtha iti । <q>ata idamuktaṃ bhāvārthatvādeveti ।﻿<pb n="293"/>
<q>etaduktaṃ bhavati—evameva saṃbandhāvagamāditi ।</q> bhāvārthasya niyogārthatayā sādhyatvaṃ
dravyaguṇayostu sādhanatvamevetyevameva<note n="(1)">G. <dn>tyeva</dn></note> sambandho'vagamyate, nānyathetyarthaḥ । <q>tadidānīṃ<note n="(2)">R. <dn>tamidānīṃ</dn></note>
pūrvāparībhūtabhāvavyatirekiṇamarthaṃ bhāvaśabdavācyaṃ prapañcayati</q>—yatpratipādanāyākhyātaśabdo-
pādānamakṛtvā bhāvārthagrahaṇaṃ kṛtaṃ taṃ pūrvāparībhūtārthavyatirekiṇaṃ anyotpādakatvamarthaṃ prapañcayati
—<q>yaḥ āhuḥ kimupi bhāvayediti te svargakāmapadasaṃbandhāt svargaṃ bhāvayediti brūyuriti ।</q>
atra cedamabhimataṃ—liṅādiyuktavākyaṃśravaṇasamanantarabhāvinīṃ pravṛttimavagamya pravartakārthābhidhā-
yitā liṅādīnāmavasīyate । kāryasya ca pravartakatvāvagamāt tadeva liṅādayo'pyavabodhayantīti
niścīyate । kāryaṃ ca kṛtisādhyaṃ kṛtipradhānamucyate । taduktam । <quote>kṛtisādhyaṃ pradhānaṃ
yat tatkāryamabhidhīyate</quote> iti । tasya cābhidhānaṃ kṛtimanabhidhāya nopapadyate iti liṅādayaḥ
kṛtimapyabhidadhati । kṛtireva ca bhavituḥ prayojakavyāpāra iti bhāvanocyate । ato yajetetyeva-
mādibhyo'nyotpādanā'vagamyate । yā ca sā'nyotpādanā sā svargakāmapadasaṃbandhāt svargabhāvanā
'vasīyate । atra codayati—<q>kimidaṃ svargakāmapadasaṃbandhāt svargaṃ bhāvayediti .
svargakāmaṃ bhāvayediti yuktaṃ vaktum । padārthasya hi padārthāntareṇa saṃbandhaḥ । svarga
kāmaścātra padārthaḥ na svargaḥ ato'sadevedaṃ pratibhāti । atrocyate । satyaṃ svargakāmaḥ
padārthaḥ</q> puruṣapradhānatvādasya śabdasya । <q>sa eva ca puruṣaḥ padārthāntareṇa</q> liṅādivācyena﻿<pb n="294"/>
kāryeṇa niyojyatayā <q>sambadhyate । svargaparastvasau saṃbandhaḥ</q> svargabhāvanāparyantaḥ sambandhaḥ
<q>ityaidaṃparyaṃ</q> svargasambandhaparyantatvaṃ<note n="(1)">G. <dn>paratvaṃ</dn></note> <q>atra bhāṣyakāreṇa darśitam ।</q> nanu kimarthaṃ svargāśrayaṇe-
nānyotpādakatā prapañcitā । yāvatā sākṣādapūrvamevāśritya kimiti na punaḥ prapañcyata ityatrāha
<q>—dhātvarthasya karaṇatvapradarśanārtham</q> । ayamabhiprāyaḥ—yadi ca svargakāmaśabdaḥ svarga-
(kāmanā)bhāvanāparyanto bhavati tadaivāpūrvādhikaraṇasiddhāntanyāyenāpūrvaṃ kriyāvyatiriktaṃ kāryaṃ
prasiddhyati । anyathā kriyaiva kāryaṃ syāt । tataśca dhātvarthasya karmataiva bhavet na karaṇatā,
kriyātirikte kārye tatprati phalaṃ ca prati dhātvarthasya karaṇatā siddhyati । nanu ca karaṇatva-
pradarśanasyaiva kiṃ phalamityatrāha—<q>vakṣyati hi sthita etasminnadhikaraṇe guṇavidhirnāmadheya-
miti vicāro bhaviṣyatīti ।</q> etaduktaṃ bhavati । nāmadheyanirākaraṇārthaṃ bhāvārthagrahaṇamiha kṛtam ।
nāmadheyatayā siddhiśca śyenādīnāṃ śabdānāṃ sāmānādhikaraṇye sati bhavati । sāmānādhikaraṇya-
siddhiśca yāgasya karaṇatve sati, śyenādiśabdānāṃ karaṇavibhaktiyogitvāt । tena karaṇasidhyā
vinā bhāvārthagrahaṇameva na śakyate vyākhyātuṃ iti karaṇatvapradarśanārthaṃ svargaṃ pratyutpādakatvaṃ
darśitam । <q>kathaṃ punaḥ svargaṃ bhāvayedityevaṃ paratā</q> darśapūrṇamāsābhyāṃ svargakāmo yajetetyevamāde-
rvākyasya । uttaraṃ—<q>yathaivaṃparatā tathā'dhikāralakṣaṇe vakṣyāmaḥ</q> <quote>vṛtyarthañcābhisaṃyogāt</quote>
ityatra । <q>tasmāttebhyaḥ kriyā pratīyeteti nigamitaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa । kā punaratra kriyā ?</q>﻿<pb n="295"/>
uttaraṃ—<q>vidhyarthaḥ</q> vidhirūpo yo'rthaḥ । <q>nanu phalasya karaṇaṃ kriyetyuktaṃ</q> <q>phalasya ca
yāgaḥ karaṇaṃ, na vidhyarthaḥ</q> tasya karaṇatve avākyārthatvaprasaṅgāt । <q>ucyate । yathā vidhyarthaḥ
karaṇaṃ tathā'dhikāralakṣaṇe vakṣyāmaḥ</q> na ca vākyārthatvaṃ<note n="(1)">G. <dn>vyākhyārthatvaṃ</dn></note>, ātmārthameva karaṇatvāvalambanāt ।
taduktam—</p>
ātmasidhyanukūlasya niyojyasya prasiddhaye ।
kurvatsvargādikamapi pradhānaṃ kāryameva naḥ ।। iti ।
<q>ihāpi ca bhāṣyakāreṇa te ca yāgadānahomasambaddhāḥ svargasya utpattiṃ vadantīti vadatā
vidhyarthasyaiva karaṇatoktā</q> । asya bhāṣyasyāyamarthaḥ—te ca bhāvaśabdāḥ yāgadānahomairabhi-
dheyairabhidhāyakatayā'bhisaṃbaddhāḥ santaḥ<note n="(2)">G. <dn>tadviṣayīkaraṇaṃ vidhyarthaṃ vadanti</dn></note> tadviṣayābhidhānadvāreṇāpūrvārthaṃ vadanti । tatra ca vidhyarthe
svargotpattiśabdaṃ prayuñjānena vidhyarthasya svargotpādane karaṇatoktā । utpadyate yayā sotpattiriti
utpattiśabdaḥ karaṇasādhanaḥ । nanu yāgādeḥ karaṇatvābhyupagamāt vidhyarthasya karaṇatvaṃ
nopapadyate ityatrāha—<q>tatsambandhāddhi yāgādeḥ</q> karaṇatā karaṇībhūtāpūrvaniṣpādakatayaiva dhātvarthasya
karaṇatvaṃ nānyatheti na doṣaḥ । <q>kuta iti praśno'yaṃ kathaṃ punarniyogārthasya <note n="(3)">G. <dn>karaṇatā</dn></note>karaṇabhāvo'va-
gamyate ityabhiprāyaḥ ।</q> kāryātmā vidhyarthaḥ phalasiddhau kathaṃ karaṇamityarthaḥ । <q>uttaravādī tu﻿<pb n="296"/>
<q>eṣahyartho vidhīyate yathā yāgādinā svargakāmaḥ svargaṃ sādhayedityadhikāralakṣaṇasiddhamarthaṃ
darśayati ।</q> paṣṭhādye hi karmaṇi niyujyamānasya kāminaḥ kāmasiddhau yāgaḥ karaṇamiti kasya
śabdasya vyāpāra iti codayitvā'yamarthaḥ prayatnenoktaḥ । <q>kena sādhayetsvargaṃ yāgādineti ।
kimanena granthena pradarśitam</q> ? uttaraṃ—<q>saivādhikārikī yuktiḥ</q> । yā'sāvadhikāralakṣaṇe
vidhyarthasya karaṇatve yuktiḥ saivoktā'nena granthena । kuta ityāha—<q>svargaṃ sādhayato'dhikāra
iti hi sthāsyāti ।</q> kāmyasiddhiparyantaḥ kāmino'dhikāraḥ iti vakṣyati । tenāyaṃ bhāṣyārthaḥ
svargakāmo hi svargaṃ sādhayitumicchati । sa kena sādhayetsvargamityasyāmākāṅkṣāyāṃ yajeteti
vidhīyate । <q>yasya ca śabdasyārthena phalaṃ sādhyate tenāpūrvaṃ kṛtvā nānyatheti tato'pūrvamavagamyate</q>
ato yastasya vācakaḥ śabdaḥ tato'pūrvaṃ pratīyata iti । <q>pūrvāparavirodhaparihāro'yam</q>
kutaḥ pūrvāparavirodha āśaṅkyate ityatrāha—<q>pūrvaṃ hi niyogātphalamityuktam idānīṃ yāgā-
tphalamiti</q> vadato virodhaḥ । taṃ pariharati—<q>tenāpūrvaṃ kṛtvetyavirodhaḥ ।</q> yāgasyāpi
karaṇatā karaṇībhūtāpūrvasiddhidvāreṇetyānuguṇyānnāsti virodhaḥ । <quote>tato'pūrvaṃ gamyata</quote> iti
sopaskāraṃ bhāṣyaṃ vyācaṣṭe—<q>tato'pūrvameva phalasādhanamiti gamyate phalasādhanamityupaskāraḥ</q> ।﻿<pb n="297"/>
yasmādapūrvasiddhiddhāreṇa yāgādeḥ karaṇatā ato'pūrvameva paramakāraṇam । <quote>ato yastasya vācakaḥ
tato'pūrva pratīyata iti tena bhāvaśabdā apūrvasya vācakā iti brūma</quote> iti bhāṣyaṃ pratīkenānubhāṣya
tātparyamāha—<q>ato yastasya vācaka iti nigamanametat</q> । upasaṃhāro'yamityarthaḥ । akṣa-
rārthamāha'—<q>yasmādapūrvaṃ sādhayan bhāvārthaḥ phalaṃ niṣpādayati nānyathā kṣaṇikatvāt tena
tadviṣayo vidhyartho liṅgādibhiḥ pratyāyyate tasya ca</q> tatpratipādyamānasya <q>viṣayādhīnaprati-
pattittvāt bhāvarthānāṃ ca viṣayabodhakatvāt tato'pūrvaṃ pratīyata ityucyate na punara</q>pūrvasyāmī1
bhāvaśabdā <q>vācakā iti ।</q> evaṃ ca darśayan bhāṣyakāraḥ tebhyaḥ kriyā pratīyeteti sūtraṃ
vyācaṣṭe-yadbhāvārthebhyaḥ kriyā pratīyata ityucyate tanna sākṣādvācakatvābhiprāyeṇa, kintu viṣayā-
bhidhānadvāreṇeti ।</p>
<p>nanu kasmādevaṃ sūtraṃ vyākhyāyana ityatrāha bhāṣyakāraḥ <quote>na tu kaścicchabdaḥ sākṣāda-
pūrvasya vācako'stī</quote>ti । tadidaṃ bhāṣyaṃ kecidayuktaṃ manyante । anenaiva hi bhāṣyeṇa sarvathaiva
apūrvasya vācakaḥ śabdo nāstītyucyate । taccāyuktam । liṅādīnāṃ tadvācakatvāt ityā-
śaṅkyāha—<q>na tu kaścicchabdaḥ sākṣādapūrvasya vācako'stīti bhāvārthābhiprāyametat ।</q>
<note n="(2)">R. <dn>bhāvārtha</dn></note>/?/ coll out show 1 in para﻿<pb n="298"/>
bhāvārthān śabdānabhipretya vācakatvaniṣedhaḥ na śabdamātrābhiprāyeṇa । tadāha—<q>na punarliṅādi-
śabdo'pi niyogaṃ nācaṣṭe</q> । nanu yadyapi sūtre tebhyaḥ kriyā pratīyata iti bhāvārthānāmeva
niyogābhidhāyakatā'vasīyate tathāpi pramāṇābhāvānneyamāśaṅkocitā yannirākaraṇāyedamucyate na tu
kaścicchabdaḥ sākṣādapūrvasya vācako'stīti । tadāha---<q>kathaṃ punarbhāvārthe vācakatvāśaṅkā</q> ?
uttaraṃ---<q>kevalasyāprayogāt niyogaśabdasya</q> liṅādeḥ । yadi bhāvārthavyatirekeṇa keva-
lena prayuktena liṅādinā vidhyartho'vasīyate<note n="(1)">G. <dn>vidhīyate</dn></note> tadā bhāvārthevācakatvāśaṅkā na syāt । na ca
kevalasya prayogo'sti nityaṃ prakṛtiparasyaiva <note n="(2)">G. <dn>niyoga</dn></note>prayogaviyamāt । <q>tiḍantasyaiva prayogāt
tiṅanta eva prayujyate bhāvārtho'pi na śuddhaḥ । <q>tena yāvatprayogānuvartinyeva vācakateti
bhrāntānāṃ</q> yāvadeva prakṛtipratyayātmakaṃ padaṃ prayujyate tadanusāryeva vācakatvaṃ <note n="(3)">G. <dn>tathaiva</dn></note>tasyaiva
vācakatvamiti bhrāntānāṃ <q>arthāvagamaṃ muktvā</q> anyena prakāreṇa <q>prayogeyattā na siddhyati</q>
yadi kevalasyāpi vācakatvaṃ tadā kimiti kevalo'pi na prayujyate । na hyanyonyārthāvagamaṃ
muktvā prayogaparimāṇopāyaḥ yāvatā hyarthaḥ pratyāyyate tāvadeva prayujyata itīdaṃ mataṃ nirākartuma-
<q>vācaka ityuktam</q> । nanu yadi prayogektāyā anyathānupapattyā vācakatvamāśaṅkitaṃ tarhi <q>na yuktaṃ
nirākartum</q> ekena granthenāha-<q>kiṃ vā prayogeyattā anyathā sidhyati</q> yena<note n="(4)">G. <dn> yena vā yatprayo</dn></note> yāvatprayogānuvartinī
vācakatā nirākiyate । pariharati---<note n="(5)">G. <dn>arthāvagamo'pi bhāvāda</dn></note><q>arthāvagamo vā vibhāgādavagamyamānaḥ kimapahnotuṃ</q>﻿<pb n="299"/>
<q>śakyate ।</q> liṅādipratyayamantareṇa<note n="(1)">G. <dn>prathamatareṇa</dn></note> juhoti yajatītyādau bhāvārthāḥ pratīyante prakṛtyantarapare ca
liṅādau prayukte'pūrvamavagamyata ityanvayavyatirekābhyāṃ liṅāderevāpūrvavācakatvam । dhātostu
bhāvārthābhidhāyakatvamavagamyamānaṃ na śakyate'pahnotum । tena bhāvārthānāṃ nāpūrvaṃ prati vācakatā ।
yadi vibhāgena <q>vācakatvaṃ kiṃ tarhi prayoganiyame kāraṇaṃ ?</q> kimiti kevalo liṅādiśabdo
na prayujyate ? <q>uttaram---prayoga eva</q> prayoganiyame kāraṇam । nanu prayoga eva kāraṇe pṛṣṭe
prayoga eva heturiti na yuktamuttaramityatrāha---<q>vācakatvasyeva prayogasyāpyanāditoktā</q> yathā
vācakatvaṃ śabdānāṃ anāditayā, prayogopi vṛddhavyavahāraparamparayā, <q>vimalāñjane</q>'nāditvasya jñāpi-
tattvāt । tenottareṣāṃ pusāṃ pūrvapūrvapuruṣaprayoga eva niyame kāraṇam । yo hi yathābhūtaḥ
prayujyamāno vācako dṛṣṭaḥ śabdaḥ sa tathābhūta eva prayujyata iti niyamasiddhiḥ । <q>tasmāt
sūktaṃ na bhāvaśabdena niyogo'rtho'bhidhīyata iti । bhāvārthaiḥ kimapi bhāvayitavya-
mityevamādimiravaibhaktikasaṃbandhaṃ</q> phalaniyogabhāvārthānāṃ darśayati । yasmādayamavaibhaktikaḥ
saṃbandhaḥ tasmādaya<q>mavainiyogika iti siddham । anyathā hi yadyevaṃ</q> na pradarśyate tadā﻿<pb n="300"/>
<q>viniyogābhāvāt vibhaktavidhānānusārī kaścit bādaririvāsaṃbandhaṃ manyate ।</q> nanu
manyatāṃ nāma tathāpīha kā kṣatirityatrāha---<q>tataśca sthita etasminnadhikaraṇe guṇavidhirnāmadheya-
miti vicāro bhaviṣyatīti na śakyate vaktum ।</q> na hi karaṇatāmantareṇodbhidādīnāṃ
nāmatetyuktametatpurastāt । <q>kiṃ punaḥ kāraṇaṃ</q> kena punaḥ kāraṇenetyarthaḥ <q>viniyojakalakṣaṇo'yaṃ</q>
saṃbandho na bhavati । uttaraṃ---<q>viniyojakānāṃ śrutyādīnāmabhāvāt । kathamabhāvaḥ ?</q> ayamāśayaḥ
pṛcchakasya---yajyādiśrutireva śrutiḥ kasmānna bhavati । uttaraṃ---<q>saṃbandhasyānavagamāt
yadi</q> yajyādiśrutisamanantaramaidamarthyalakṣaṇaḥ saṃbandho'vagamyate tadā bhavet śruti-
saṃbhavaḥ । na cāsāvavagamyate । sāmānyenaiva saṃbandhāvagamo<note n="(1)"> <dn>sabandhenā</dn></note> nāstītyuktamiti matvā coda-
yati---<q>nanu cāyamasti saṃbandhaḥ yajeta svargakāma iti ।</q> pariharati---<q>bāḍhamasti na puna-
raidamarthyalakṣaṇaḥ kiṃ tarhi adhikāralakṣaṇaḥ</q> । nanu yadi śrutyādayo na saṃbhavanti kathaṃ tarhi
adhikāralakṣaṇo'pi saṃbandho'vagamyate ityatrāha---<q>aidamarthye ca viniyogāvagamyamityuktaṃ śeṣaḥ
parārthatvādityatra</q> । tatra ca śrutyādīni viniyoge kāraṇānīti pārārthyalakṣaṇaṃ śeṣatvaṃ
tasmiṃśca śeṣatve aidamarthyalakṣaṇe śeṣatvena viniyoge1<note n="(2)"> G. <dn>viniyogeṣu</dn></note> śrutyādīni kāraṇānīti vadatā aidamarthyaṃ﻿<pb n="r301"/>
<p>viniyogāvāvagabhyamityuktam। na punaradhikāralakṣaṇo'pi saṃbandhaḥ। tenāsatsvapi viniyojakeṣu
bhavatyadhikāralakṣaṇaḥ saṃbandhaḥ। yadi phalaniyoge bhāvārthānāmavainiyogikaḥ saṃbandhaḥ <q>kathaṃ
tarhi <quote>“karmāṇyapi jaiminiḥ phalārthatvāt”</quote></q> phalaṃ ca puruṣārthatvāt”</quote> iti। etadeva
vivṛṇoti---<q>dravyaguṇasaṃskāreṣdheva</q> kevaleṣu <q>na pārārthyama</q> api tu yāgaphalapuruṣeṣvapī
tyanenādhikaraṇena <q>bādaripakṣaṃ</q> dravyaguṇasaṃskāreṣveva śeṣabhāva ityevaṃrūpaṃ <q>nirasyatā pārārthya-
lakṣaṇasaṃbandho'trābhyupagataḥ</q>। tena vainiyogikasaṃbandhāvagamādayuktametadvainiyogiphasaṃbandho
nāstīti। pariharati---<q>satyamabhyupagataṃ</q> pārārthyalakṣaṇaḥ saṃbandhopyatnāstīti। <q>na punaḥ
stacchabdedaṃparatayā</q>। ārthoyaṃ pārārthyalakṣaṇaḥ saṃbandhaḥ na vainiyogika ityavirodhaḥ।
<q>naṣṭāśvadagdharathavatsaṃbandha</q> ityanenārtho'yaṃ saṃbandha iti darśitam। <q>nanu bhāvārthaiḥ kimapi
bhāvayitatavyam svargakāmasya ca kenāpi bhāvyateti guṇapradhānabhāvaṃ darśayati</q>। śābda-
saṃbandhakathanaṃ cedam। sa ca guṇapradhānabhāvaḥ <q>pārārthye sati</q> bhavati iti <q>punarapyaidaṃparyamevaśabdasya
prāpnotīti</q>। pariharati---na prāpnotyaidaṃparyaṃ śabdasya। kuta ityāha---<q>bhāvasvabhāvo hyayamiti
kathyate</q> anyotpādakatā nāma bhāvasvabhāva iti kathyate। <q>nedaṃparatā śabdasya</q> kathyate।
yata evāyamavainiyogikaḥ saṃbandhaḥ <q>ata eva ca dravyaguṇaśabdebhyaḥ tṛtīyāyuktebhyopi</q>pratī-
yamānasyārthasya <q>vidhyarthatā nābhyupagatā</q>। vainiyogikasaṃbandhe tṛtīyāvibhaktivaśena dravyaguṇa-
﻿<pb n="r302"/>
<p>yoreva vidhinā saṃbandhaḥ syāt। nacaitadasti <q>tasmānna viniyogādyāgasvargayoḥ sambandhaḥ kiṃ
tarhi ? bhāvārthatvādevettyuk‍tam</q> bhāvārthatvādeva viniyogaviṣayatā bhavati। tasyāṃ ca
satyāṃ phalabhāvanāṃ prati karaṇateti bhāvārthatvādeva yāgasvargayoḥ sambandhaḥ। yata eva cānyathāpi
saṃbandhāvagatiḥ <q>ata eva cākhyātaṃ sambandhe pāṇinirna smarati</q></p>
<p><q>nanu ca kartari karmaṇi bhāva iti smarati</q> ayamāśayaḥ---kartari karmaṇi bhāve
cārthe cākhyātamiti smaratā saṃbandha evākhyātaṃ smṛtaṃ bhavati। yathā subbibhaktiḥ kartṛkarmaṇoḥ
smṛtā saṃbandhitve smṛtā bhavati। pariharati---<q>satyaṃ smarati, na teṣāmanyasambadhitāṃ
teṣāṃ</q>---ākhyātārthānāṃ tiṅ‍‍vibhaktiḥ anyasaṃbandhitāṃ na pratipādayati। <q>yathā prātipadi-
kādavagamyamānasyārthasya anyasaṃbandhapratipādinyaḥ subbibhaktayaḥ na tathā''khyātāda-
vagatasyārthasya</q> tiṅ‍‍vibhaktayaḥ। <q>nanu ca tṛtīyādibhirdviṣṭhatvāt saṃbandhasya dvayorapi
saṃbandhitoktā bhavati</q>। tena tṛtīyādismaraṇenākhyātārthasyāpi śābdī saṃbandhitā'styeva।
pariharati---<q>satyaṃ dviṣṭhaḥ saṃbandhaḥ saṃbandhitā punaḥ nāmārthasyaiva tṛtīyādibhiḥ</q> pratipādyate
nākhyātārthasya arthāttu tasya saṃbandhitā <q>yathā pumān sadvitīyo dvivacanasyaukārāntasyārthaḥ na
punaḥ dvitīyopyarthaḥ</q> pumāneva। api tvasau sadvitīyatvasidhyartha arthād‍gṛhyate। yata
﻿<pb n="r303"/>
<p>evākhyātārthasyānyasaṃbandhitā tiṅ‍‍vibhaktibhirnocyate <q>ata eva cākhyātārthe kartṛkarmagatā
saṅkhayaivocyate vacanaiḥ na punaḥ kartnādayaḥ</q>। yadi yathā subbibhaktayaḥ prakṛtyarthasya anya-
<q>saṃbandhitāṃ</q> vadanti tathā tiṅ‍vibhaktayo vadeyuḥ tathā subbibhaktivadeva kartṛtvādikamapi tā
ācakṣiran। nanu yadyapi prakṛtyarthasya kartṛtvādikaṃ na vadanti tathāpi prakṛtyarthasaṃbandhina eva
kartṛtvādikamapi kimiti na vadantītyatrāha---<q>pramāṇāntaragamyā hi te kartrādayaḥ</q> ataḥ
śabde nocyante। kutaḥ pramāṇāntarātte gamyante ityatrāha---<q>niyogataḥ pratyakṣādibhirvā</q> vede
niyogataḥ karturavagamaḥ yatya niyojyatvaṃ tasyaiva kartṛtvaṃ tena niyogataḥ karturavagamaḥ। pratyakṣādi-
bhistu laukikakarmaṇāṃ kartrādyavagamaḥ। yata eva ye kartrādayo'nyato'vagamyante ata eva te śabda-
vācyā na bhavanti iti। <q>ata eva tu niyogo</q> liṅādiśabdaḥ <q>kāryepyarthe</q>। yadyapi
tasyārthaḥ kāryarūpaḥ tathāpi <q>bhaviṣyantamarthaṃ</q> na vadati। bhaviṣyadviṣayāyāmapi kāryatāyāṃ
na padena bhaviṣyatvāvagamasiddhiḥ।</p>
<p>nanu ca na paropādhikī niyogārthasya bhaviṣyattā kiṃ tu svabhāvata eva tatrāha---<q>kāraka-
vyāpāro hi kālatrayāvacchedyo bhavati nādhikāraḥ</q> na niyogārtha ityarthaḥ। tena paropādhi-
kaiva bhaviṣyattā, kārakavyāpāravyatirekeṇa ca anyeṣāṃ dravyaguṇāmāmapi na kālasaṃbandhaḥ tena
yaducyate kālatrayaviyuktañca khapuṣpavaditi, tatkhapuṣpavadeva asaṃbhavidūṣaṇam।</p>
<p><q>kathaṃ tarhi prayājāderviniyojyatvaṃ ?</q> ekagranthenāha---<q>ākhyātāttasya</q> hi ca viniyo-
gāt <q>pārārthyaṃ nāvasīyata ityuktam</q>। tena pārārthya nopapadyete। <q>pariharati</q>---
﻿<pb n="r304"/>
<q>kimetāvantyeva pramāṇānītyatra</q> tṛtīye parihāraṃ vakṣyāmaḥ। prakaraṇādhikaraṇe parihāraṃ vakṣyāmaḥ
ityarthaḥ। atra bhāṣyam---<q><quote>“naivaṃ dravyaguṇaśabdā”</quote> iti</q>। tatra pṛcchati---<q>kiṃ naivaṃ</q> ? kiṃ
bhūtāste na bhavantītyarthaḥ। uttaraṃ---<q>naivamadhikāralakṣaṇasaṃbandhamarhantītyarthaḥ</q>। yathā bhāvārthā
adhikāralakṣaṇasaṃbandhamarhanti naivaṃ dravyaguṇaśabdāḥ teṣu puruṣasyādhikāralakṣaṇamaiśvarya na
bhavatītyarthaḥ<note n="1">G. <dn>nāstītyarthaḥ</dn></note>। <q>sarvathā hi <note n="2"> G. <dn>niyoga</dn></note>2viniyogapramāṇaviṣayā evaite</q> dravyaguṇāḥ। na ca
 puruṣasyaiśvarya vainiyogikam। kiṃtu naiyogikam। tacca<note n="3"><dn>viṣayasyo</dn></note>3 cikīrpitasyopapadyate nānyasyeti svargakāmādhikaraṇe vakṣyāmaḥ। ataḥ siddhaṃ bhāvārthatvādeva niyogaviṣayatāṃ pratipadyate। na
vibhaktivaśeneti। yadi vainiyogikasaṃbandho yāgasya nāsti <q>kathaṃ tarhi</q> bhāṣyakāreṇoktam---<q>“svargakāmaḥ”</q>
kena sādhayetsvargaṃ yāgādineti। atra svargasiddhau vainiyogikaḥ saṃbandhaḥ yāgasyāvagamyate।
<q>uttaram---viṣayamaṅgīkṛtyaitaduktam</q>। <q>na viniyojyatāṃ</q> niyogaviṣayasyaiva sataḥ ārthaṃ karaṇatvaṃ
bhavati। tadabhiprāyeṇa karaṇatoktā। <q>yathā caitadevaṃ tathā svargakāmādhikaraṇe nipuṇatara</q>---



﻿<pb n="r305"/>
<p>mupapādayiṣyāmaḥ। bhavanti kecitkarmaśabdā na bhāvārthāḥ yathā śyenaikatrikādayaḥ।
kecidbhāvārthā na karmaśabdāḥ yathābhāvo bhavanaṃ bhūtiriti iti bhāṣyamanubhāṣitaṃ vyācaṣṭe
---<q>bhāvārthāḥ karmaśabdā iti padadvayābhidhāne bhāvārthasya</q> bhāvārthasaṃbanghipadadvayābhidhāne kiṃ
<q>prayojanam</q>। prayojanamevāha---yadi karmaśabdebhyaḥ kriyāpratīyetetyucyeta <q>tadā śyenaikātri-
kādibhyo'pūrvasyotpattirityuktaṃ syāt ete'pi hi karmaśabdā</q> nāmadheyatvāt। atra codayati
---yadi hi karmaśabdāḥ śyenaikatrikādayaḥ tadā <q>etebhyopi kimityapūrvotpattirnabhavati</q> ?
<q>dravyaguṇaśabdanivṛttyarthaṃ bhāvārthāḥ karmaśabdā</q> ityadhikaviśeṣaṇamuktam। na karmaśabda-
nivṛttyartham। karmaśabdāścaite, tasmātkathameṣāṃ nivṛttiḥ <q>tasmādabhidhīyamāne viśeṣaṇe</q>
bhāvārthagrahaṇena <q>naiva śyenādīnāṃ nivṛttiḥ</q>। <q>ete hi bhāvārthasyaiva karmaṇo vācakā yāgādeḥ</q>
﻿<pb n="r306"/>
<q>idamaparaṃ kha/?/rparaṃ</q> visaṃsthulaṃ <q>sthita etasminnadhikaraṇe nāmadheyatvamiti na hi punarasyāṃ
cintāyāṃ</q> vartamānāyāṃ <q>karmavacanatvaṃ śyenāderupapadyate</q> sāmānādhikaraṇyābhāvāt।
<q>yadā''khyātārthena vidhiḥ sādhyata iti sthitaṃ</q> tadā tṛtīyārthalābhe<note n="1">G. <dn>tṛtīyārthatve</dn></note> sati tṛtīyāntānāṃ sāmānādhikaraṇye sthite <q>matvarthalakṣaṇābhayānnāmadheyatvamityuktam</q>। tenāsminnadhikaraṇe'sati
nāmadheyatvameva nāsti kintu dravyaguṇavacanataiva। tadvacanatayā nivṛttiḥ <note n="2">G. <dn>bhāvārthagrahaṇenaiva</dn></note> karmaśabdagrahaṇenaiva kṛtā। <q>ataḥ śyenādinivṛttyarthamabhidhānadvayaṃ śakyamucyate</q>। <q>atrābhidhīyate</q>। <q>nedaṃ
śakyaṃ yadi karmaśabdebhya ityucyate tadedamevādhikaraṇaṃ sthitiṃ na labhyate</q> ? kasmādityāha
sthāpyamānaṃ hyetajjyotiṣṭomādeḥ karmaśabdatāmāvahati ataśca nāmākhyātayorviśeṣo na
labhyate</q>। asyārthaḥ---yadi karmaśabdebhyo'pūrvamityucyate tadaivedamadhikaraṇaṃ sthatiṃ na labhate
cakrakadoṣaprasaṅgāditi---tathā hi jyotiṣṭomena yajetetyatra prathamaṃ dravyaguṇaśabdatvāta
jyotiṣṭomādiśabde'karmaśabdatayā niraste yajetetyetadviṣaya evārparve sthite tatsāmānādhikaraṇyena
karmanāmadheyatve jāte karmaśabdatayā punarapūrvārthatā prāpnoti। tasyāṃ ca satyāṃ yāgasāmānādhi-


﻿<pb n="r307"/>
karaṇyaṃ nāsti। na hi tadā bāge tṛtīyārtho'sti। tataśca karmavacanatvānupapatteḥ dravyaguṇa-
vacanatāpatteḥ yāgāderevāpūrvamiti cakrakeṇa adhikaraṇameva na vyavatiṣṭhate। <q>bhāvaśabdābhi-
dhāne<note n="1"><dn>bhāvaśabdebhya ityucyamāne</dn></note> punaḥ</q> satyapi karmavacanatve <q>siddhavatkarmābhidhānāt prāpnoti jyotiṣṭomādernivṛttiḥ sakarmake hi pūrvāparībhūte bhāvaśabdo vartata</q> ityuktam। <q>etaduktaṃ bhavati</q>। uttarakāla-
bhāvinīmapi<note n="2 ">G. <dn>uttarakālavācināmapi</dn></note> karmavacanatayā jyotiṣṭomādipadānāṃ apūrvārthatāṃ nivartayituṃ bhāvārthagrahaṇaṃ kṛtam। yata eva ca nāmadheyanivṛttisiddhipyadhikaraṇavyavasthāpanārthameva ato nādhikaraṇabhedaḥ।</p>
<p><q>evaṃ tarhi sarvanivṛttisamartho</q> bhāvārthaśabda eva kevalaḥ sūtro'stu tenaiva dravyaguṇānāmadhe-
yānāṃ <note n="3">G. omits<dn>siddheḥ</dn></note> nivṛttisiddheḥ <q>karmaśabdagrahaṇamatiricyate</q>। kuta ityāha---<q>idameva hi na<note n="4">G. omids <dn>na</dn></note> labhyate pūrvāparībhūte sakarmake bhāvaśabdo vartata iti</q>। <q>anyatrāpi</q> darśanāt <q>bhāvo bhavanaṃ bhūtiriti bhāvaśabdasya</q> tena śiṣṭaviṣayatāmevāpādayituṃ<note n="5"><dn>kartuḥ śabdagrahaṇaṃ</dn></note> bhāvaśabdagrahaṇaṃ kṛtam। <q>kiṃ punarihodāharaṇam</q> ?
﻿<pb n="r308"/>
<p><q>yadi śyenaikatrikādayo'pi karmaśabdāḥ naiva dravyaguṇaśabdānāṃ nivṛttyarthaṃ sūtra-
mupapadyate</q> nivartanīyābhāvāta। <q>sarvatrādhikāracodanāsu nāmaivopapadamupalabhyate na<note n="1">G. omits <dn>na</dn></note></q> dravyaguṇaśabdāḥ। nanu bhavatu sarvāsvadhikāracodanāsu nāmaivopapadaṃ<note n="2">G. <dn>dravyaguṇaśabdopapadaṃ</dn></note> somena yajetetyādyā utpatti-
codanāḥ dravyaguṇaśabdopapadabhāja udāharaṇaṃ bhavantu। kathaṃ ca sarvādhikāracodanāsu nāmaivopapada-
miti। ucyate। sarvāsu tāvadadhikāracodanāsu viruddhatrikadvayāpattyā vākyabhedaprasaṅgānmatvartha-
lakṣaṇādoṣaprasaṅgācca upapadānāṃ nāmatayaivānvayo nānyathā। yā eva adhikāracodanāstā evodā-
haraṇam। sarvāsu khalūtpatticodanāsu adhikāravidhisannidhisamāmnātāsu na prathamamapūrvāntarāṇi
pratīyante। kintu <note n="3">G. <dn>svakriyā</dn></note> svakīyakārakavargāvacchinnāni karmamātrāṇyeva pratīyante। adhikāracodanāvartī ca niyogaśabda aidamarthyamātreṇa tairanvitaṃ niyogamācaṣṭe। karaṇopakārakatayā ca teṣāmai-
damarthyopapattiḥ। na ca kṣaṇikāni tāni karmāṇi saṃbhūyaikamupakāraṃ janayitumīśate।
kṣaṇikānāṃ yugapadbhāvāsaṃbhavāt। atasteṣvapyavāntarāpūrvāṇi kalpyante iti na tatra dravyaguṇa-
śabdebhyo'pūrvotpattisaṃbhāvanā। etena pradhānotpattayo'pi vyākhyātāḥ। tāsvapi prathamamadhikāra
vidhyapekṣitaṃ karmasvarūpamātrasamarpaṇam<note n="4"><dn>pekṣita-rpaṇaparatvāta</dn></note> । utpattiniyogānāmanavagamāt। kṣaṇikasya karmasvarūpasya prācyodīcyakālayoraṅgayoḥ upakāryatā na saṃbhavatītyaparvāntarāśrayaṇamiti tatra tatrātikṣuṇṇo'ya-
marthaḥ tasmānnirvipayamidaṃ sūtraṃ manvānaḥ ki punarihodāharaṇamiti pṛcchati। nanu nāma-
vyatirik‍tamapyupapadaṃ adhikāracodanāsu dṛśyate<quote>‘etasyaiva revatīṣu vāravantīyamagriṣṭomasāma’</quote>
﻿<pb n="r309"/>
<p>kṛtvā paśukāmo hyetena yajeteti tadāha---<q>kā vārtā etasyaiva revatīṣvityevamādiṣu</q> ? uttaraṃ---<q>yathā-
vyākhyātāddate'nyasya vidhyarthatā tatra na saṃbhavati tathā tatraiva</q> revatyadhikaraṇe vakṣyāmaḥ
tena tadapyudāharaṇaṃ na saṃbhavati। atrottarabhāṣyaṃ<note n="1">Page 305---<quote>“śyenainābhicaran yajetetyevamādi”</quote> tadvayācaṣṭe
---<q>evaṃ tarhi nāmopapadānyevātrodāharaṇāni</q> kathaṃ tānyudāharaṇānītyatrāha---<q>anenaiva sūtreṇa
nāmākhyātayorvidhyarthatve vivekaḥ</q>। asyārthaḥ---anenaiva sūtreṇāyaṃ vivekaḥ kriyate nāmnāṃ
vidhyarthatā nāsti ākhyātārthānāmeva vidhyarthateti। sthite cāsmin viveke nāmadheyata-
yānvayaḥ śyenādiśabdānām। prāk‍cedasmādvivekāt dravyaguṇaśabdataiva tadā''ha
<q>viveke hi nāmataiva na syāt dravyaguṇaśabdataiva syāt</q> tasmātprathamameṣāṃ dravyaguṇaśabdatveno-
dāharaṇatvaṃ <note n="2"><dn>paścāda‍bhūtārtha</dn></note> paścādabhāvārthakarmaśabdatvena nivartyatvam। tasmātsiddhaṃ dravyaguṇaśabda-<q>nivṛttyarthamudāharaṇam</q>। kathaṃ punarnāmākhyātayorvidhyarthatve viveka ityatrāha---<q>ākhyāti-
kyo vibhak‍tayaḥ pūrvāparībhāvaṃ pratipādayantītyupariṣṭādvakṣyati</q>। tenākhyātānāmeva
vidhyarthatā। kāryabhūto hi vidhyarthaḥ puruṣeṇa pratīyate। naca paravyapārasādhyaṃ paraḥ sva-
saṃbandhitayā kāryaṃ pratipadyate। puruṣasya ca prayat‍nalakṣaṇaḥ svavyāpāraḥ। tena prayat‍narūpa-
kṛtīp‍sito vidhyarthaḥ śrūyate। prayat‍naśca sarvaḥ sādhyaviṣayaḥ। tena prayat‍nāvacchedadvāreṇa
sādhyo'rtho vidherviṣayaḥ। <note n="3">G <dn>saddaśa</dn></note><q>visaddaśavibhaktiyogācca jyotiṣṭomāderna pūrvāparībhūtapratipādana-
﻿<pb n="r310"/>
<p><q>atha</q> na santi sarvatra nāmadheyānyevopapadaṃ tadā nāmadheyanivṛttyarthamevedaṃ sūtram।
tathāpi sulabhamudāharaṇaṃ karmaśabdamātrānmāmūdapūrvasyotpattirityevamarthamupapadyata evaitatsūtram।
evañca sulabhe udāharaṇe yadidaṃ nibandhane kimihodāharaṇamityevamādinā granthena
kimihodāharaṇamiti bhāṣyasyābhipāyavarṇanaṃ kṛtam---udāharaṇābhāsābhiprāyeṇa ayaṃ praśna iti
tadanarvakam। sbarūpajñānārtha evāyaṃ praśna iti kṛtvā kimihodāharaṇamityevamādeḥ granthasyeti
kartari ṣaṣṭhī na śeṣalakṣaṇe। nahyasya granthasyāyamarthaḥ kimihodāharaṇamityevamāderbhāṣyasyābhi-
prāyavarṇanamiti। ādiśabdasyānanvayaprasaṅgāt। na hi tatrāparaḥ praś‍navartī
grantho'sti।</p>
<p><q>atrocyate</q>। <q>nahi karmaśabdāda‍vyudāsaḥ śakyate kartuṃ karmaśabdena।
abhinnatvānnāmanābhipadayoḥ</q>। asyārthaḥ---yāvanti padāni sūtre prayujyante tāvatāṃ vyā-
vṛttyarthatā aṅgīkaraṇīyā। karmaśabdagrahaṇena dravyaguṇā vyāvṛttāḥ na nāmadheyāni
teṣāmapi karmaśabdatvāt। ye ca te dravyaguṇā vyāvṛttāḥ te adhikāracodanāsu na santīti
﻿<pb n="r311"/>
<note n="1"><dn>manvānaḥsamāhārābhiprāyeṇa</dn></note> manvānasyābhāvābhiprāyeṇa yuk‍taiva codanā। yadi nāmanāmipadayorabhinnatā <q>kathaṃ tarhi śyenai-
katrikādayo nirasyante</q> ? uttaram---<q>anākhyātārthatvādeva</q>। anākhyātārthatvena hi
siddhavatteṣu <note n="2">G.<dn>G.karmāvagati</dn></note> karmārthāvagatiriti na vidhyarthatā। yadyanākhyātārthatvaṃ nirākaraṇakāraṇaṃ bhāvārthagrahamidānīṃ <q>kimartham</q> ? uttaram---<q>karmaśababdatvepyabhāvārthatvenānākhyātārthataiveti</q>।
karmaśabdatvepyeṣāmanākhyātārthatvaṃ apūrvāparībhūtārvatvamiti<note n="3">G. <dn>bhūtartthatva</dn></note> kathayituṃ bhāvārthagrahaṇam। bhāvārthagrahaṇe hi jñāyate nūnamabhāvārtha api kecitkarmaśabdāssantīti। tenaiṣāmapūrvā---
paribhūtārthatvapratipādanārthaṃ bhāvārthagrahaṇamapi sārthakam। <q>tasmāt sūktametadasmākaṃ---yo'yaṃ
<q>kimihodāharaṇamityevamādeḥ nibandhanagranthasyopanyāsaḥ</q>।'</p>
<p>sarveṣāṃ bhāvo'rtha iti cet। iti sūtramanubhāṣyākṣipati---<q>kimanena pūrvok‍tamākṣiptam</q> ?
uttaram---<q>yatpūrvoktaṃ tadevākṣiptam</q>। ākṣeptā āha---bhāvārthebhyaḥ kriyā pratīyata iti
﻿<pb n="r312"/>
pūrvamuktam। <q>sarveṣāṃ bhāvo'rtha iti vadatā kathamidamākṣiptaṃ bhavati</q>। ekagranthenāha
---<q>/?/vadi hyabhāvārthānāmapūrvārthatāṃ vadet tadā''kṣepaḥ saṃbhavati</q>। nanu dravyaguṇaśabdebhyo
'pūrvaṃ nāstītyādi pūrvamevoktam। tatra yadi sarveṣāṃ ityanena sarveṣāmevāpūrvārthatocyate
tadā'styevākṣepa ityāśaṅkyāha---<q>sarveṣāṃ bhāvo'rtha iti vadato naiva dravyaguṇaśabdāḥ
santītyabhiprāyo gamyate। na punardravyaguṇaśabdā api bhāvārthā iti pratipat‍tuṃ śakyate।
karmaśabdasāmānādhikaraṇyācca viśeṣataḥ</q>। asyārthaḥ। sarveṣāṃ bhāvo'rtha iti vadato'-
yamabhiprāyo'vagamyate dravyaguṇavācinaḥ śabdā na santyeveti; na punardravyaguṇavācakā-
ścāpi śabdāḥ bhāvārthā iti। viśeṣataśca bhāvārthaśabdasya karmaśabdena<note n="1">R. <dn>karmaśabdagrahaṇena</dn></note> saha samānādhi karaṇyāt। yasya hi śabdasya karma abhidheyaṃ sa karmaśabdaḥ। yaśca karmaśabdaḥ nāsau
dravyaguṇaśabdo bhavitumarhati। tatra ca dravyaguṇaśabdāpalāpena na kiñcidākṣiptaṃ bhavati।
samādhatte--- <q>ayamabhiprāyaścodakasya dravyaguṇaśabdā api bhāvarūpāpannā eva vidhyarthā bhavanti</q>
asyārthaḥ। avivādaṃ tāvadidaṃ vidhiṃ pratyaidamarthyaṃ yat dravyaguṇaśabdānāmapi tadbhāvarūpāpannā
﻿<pb n="r313"/>
nāmeva। <q>taccedaṃ tadhnājuhotītyatra darśayiṣyāmaḥ। evañcet sarveṣāṃ bhāvo'rthaḥ dravyaguṇā-
vagatiḥ nāntarīyakī। tasmānna svarūpataḥ kriyānvayo dravyaguṇānām। abhidhānavat</q>
yathā'bhidhānamantrasya svarūpataḥ kriyānvayo nāsti tathā dravyaguṇayorapi। <q>tasmādbhābārthā</q>
ityevaṃ sūtraṃ na dravyaguṇaviśeṣāvagatāvalam। sarveṣāṃ bhāvārthatvāt na kaścit bhāvaśabdena
viśeṣo gṛhyate। yāvaduk‍taṃ bhavet sarvapadānāṃ vidhyanvayināṃ vidhyarthateti tāvadevoktaṃ bhavati
bhāvārthebhyaḥ kriyā pratīyata iti। tena sūtrākṣepo bhavatyeva; aviśeṣakatve bhāvārtha-
grahaṇasyānarthakyaprasaṅgāt।</p>
<p><q>yeṣāmutpattau। satyaṃ sarvaiṣāṃ bhāvārthatā। kintu ekasya svataḥ anyasya tadyogāt</q>।
bhāvārthasya svato bhāvārthatā। dravyasya guṇasya ca tadyegāt। <q>kimidaṃ tadyogāditi ?
tadarthānupraveśādityarthaḥ</q>। kriyānupraviṣṭā hi dravyaguṇaḥ sādhyā bhavanti kārakatvasya
<note n="1"><dn>taccabhāva</dn></note>
﻿<pb n="r314"/>
sādhyatvāt। <q>kathaṃ punaridamavagamyate ekasya svato'nyasya tadyogāditi</q>। uttaraṃ
---<q>tatsvabhāvādeva</q>। etadeva vivṛṇoti---<q>ekasya</q> dravyasya guṇasya ca <q>siddha eva svabhāvaḥ।
anyasya ca</q> bhāvārthasya <q>sādhyaḥ। tatra na sādhyaḥ sādhyatāmanyato'pekṣate। siddhaḥ
punaḥ na sādhyayogāddate sādhyatayā pratipat‍tuṃ śakyate</q>। atra codayati-<q>kiṃ jahatsvabhāvā
sādhyānvayitā siddhasya</q> bhavati। kiṃ svabhāvabhūtāṃ siddhatāṃ parityajya sādhyānvayī
siddho bhavati। uttaram---<q>bhavatu ko doṣaḥ</q>। ākṣeptā''ha---<q>ayameva doṣaḥ siddhataiva
nāvagamyate</q> so'pi bhāvārthavat sādhya eva pratīyate। athānanvitāvasthāyāṃ siddhatā nāsti
tadayuktamityāha---<q>ananvitānāñcāyaṃ vivekaḥ sūtrakāreṇa pradarśitaḥ</q>। tasyāñcāvasthāyāṃ
sarvameva sādhyamiti nāsti vivekaḥ। <q>tasmānnamaḥ śaydavidbhayo yairevaṃ viveko niścīyate</q>।
﻿<pb n="r315"/>
<p>samādhatte---<q>yathāhācāryavān bhavān kintu nimittagataiṣā kathā</q>। siddha eko'paraḥ sādhya
iti yeyaṃ kathā sā nimittagatā। ananvitāvasthā hi saṃbandhagrahaṇopāyatāṃ gacchantī vākyārtha-
pratipattau nimittam। evaṃ sambandhagrahaṇam। ayamartho'nena śabdenākāṅkṣitasannihitayogyārthānta-
reṇānvitassannabhidhīyata iti। tenāsti nimittam। bhavatu nimittāvasthāyāṃ vivekaḥ tathāpi
kimityata āha---<q>nimittataśca kāryamakāryeveti parīkṣakairvaktavyam</q>। nimittāvasthāyāṃ yasya
kāryatā<note n="1">G. <dn>yakāryaṃ sannihitaṃ</dn></note> naimittikāvasthāyāmapi tasya svabhāvikī kāryatā<note n="2"><dn>G. tadevakāryaṃ sādhyamiti vaktavyam</dn></note>। anyasya tadayogāt। tathāca
<q>bhagavatā sūtrakāreṇa nimittāvasthopavarṇitā utpattisaṃbandhaśabdaṃ prayuñjānena। utpattau
nimittābasthāyāmityarthaḥ</q>। śabdoccāraṇamātreṇa hi ananvitasvarūpeṇa padārthaḥ smaryate iti
nimittāvasthaivotpattirucyate। nimittāvasthāyācca dravyaguṇayoḥ sādhyāvasthā<note n="3">G. <dn>sādhyāvagatiḥ</dn></note> nāstīti darśayati-
<q>nimittato hyakāṅkṣā cākhyātārthasyaiveti darśitaṃ bhāpye</q> nimittāvasthāyāmākhyātārtha evādhi-
﻿<pb n="r316"/>
kāriṇamapekṣate। na dravyaguṇaśabdārthaḥ। yasya cādhikārākāṅkṣā sa sādhyaḥ। anuṣṭhānāya
hyasāvapekṣyate। tenādhikāryapekṣāpradarśanena bhāṣyakāreṇa ākhyātārthasyaiva nimittāvasthāyāṃ
sādhyatetyuk‍tam। bhāṣye ca pradhānākāṅkṣā'dhikāryākāṅkṣā'bhimatā। evantāvat nimittāśrayaṇena
viveko darśitaḥ। samprati naimittikāvasthāyāmapi darśayitumāha---<q>kārye punaḥ</q> naimittikevākyārthe
tasyāṃ daśāyāmityarthaḥ। <q>kiṃ siddhasādhyaviveko naivāsti</q> ? uttaram---<q>astitāvat
āśritatvāt prayogasyeti। ucyate---bhāvārthānāmeva prayogaḥ puruṣeṇāśrita iti</q>।
﻿<pb n="r317"/>
pṛcchati---<q>kimidamucyate bhāvārthānāmeva prayogaḥ puruṣeṇāśrita iti। yāvatā dravya-
guṇānāmapi kimiti nāśrita iti</q>। uttaram---<q>nimittāśritattvātkāryasya yathānimitta
mavabhāsate</q>। nimittāśrito hi vākyārthaḥ tena yaḥ siddharūpaḥ sa siddhatayā sādhanatve-
nānvayaṃ yāti। yaḥ sādhyaḥ sa sādhyatayaivetyarthaḥ। <q>tadidaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa kiñcetyuk‍tvā
kāryādapyevaṃbhūtanimittataiveti pratipāditam</q>। kāryānniyogādapi evaṃbhūtanimittataiva
vākyārthasyāvagamyata iti pratipāditaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa। yadā hi bhāvārthaviṣayo niyogaḥ tadā
dravyaguṇaśabdārtho bhāvārthaniṣpādakatayaiva vākyārthe'nvayaṃ<note n="2">G.<dn>bhāvārthānvayaṃ</dn></note> yāti। bhāvārthatve sādhyatayā। anyathā dravyaguṇaśabdānāṃ niyogārthatānupapatteḥ। tena niyogādapi siddhasādhyatayaivāvagatiḥ
vākyārthadaśāyāmapi। kasmātpunarevaṃbhūtetyāha---<q>sāpekṣanirapekṣatvātkāryāvagateḥ</q>। ekasya
﻿<pb n="r318"/>
sāpekṣā kāryāvagatiḥ। sāpekṣo niyogasaṃbandhāvagamaḥ। anyasya nirapekṣaḥ। <q>kva sāpekṣatvaṃ
kva vā nirapekṣatvam</q> ? uttaram---<q>siddhasādhyayormadhye sādhyasyānapekṣatvaṃ</q> sādhanasya
sāpekṣatvaṃ vidhyarthe niyogasaṃbandhe। kuta ityāha---<q>sādhyaviṣayatvānniyogasya
<note n="1">G.<dn>niyogaviṣayasya</dn></note>। sādhyā-
pekṣitā tu siddhasyeti guṇavidhau darśayiṣyāma ityuktam</q>। bhāvārthatvādeva bhāvārthaviṣaye
niyoge sati yadaikasmādapūrvaṃ tadetarat tadartamiti nyāyena dravyaguṇayorbhāvā[rthā]rthatayaiva niyoga-
saṃbandhaḥ। tena bhāvārthasādhanatvenaiva tayoḥ vidhyanupraveśo nānyatheti guṇavidhau darśayiṣyāma
ityuktamatraiva। taccedaṃ dadhnā juhotīti pratipādayipyāma iti। tena siddhasādhyārthadvayaśabda-
saṃbhavāt bhāvārthāḥ karmaśabdā iti viśeṣāvagatau samarthaṃ sūtram। adhikaraṇārthamupasaṃharati
---<q>eṣa vinigamanāyāṃ hetuḥ</q>। atra ca naimittikāvasthāyāṃ dravyaguṇabhāvārthānāṃ sarveṣāmeva
sādhyārthatvāt<note n="2"><dn></dn>sādhyatvāt</note> sādhyārthaviṣayattvācca niyogasyāviśeṣeṇa vidhiviṣayasamarpakatvamiti pūrbaḥ pakṣaḥ
rāddhāntastu dravyaguṇayorvidhiviṣayatve kriyāyāśca tādarthye yathāpratīyamānakriyākārakabhāvāvagama-
viroya iti bhāvārthaviṣaya eva niyogo na dravyaguṇaviṣaya iti।</p>
﻿<pb n="r319"/>
<p><q>codanā</q>। <quote>“kathaṃ punaridamavagamyate asti tadapūrva”</quote>iti bhāṣyanubhāṣaṇam।
ākṣipati---<q>nanu cāyaṃ praś‍no nopapadyate</q>। kuta ityāha---<q>apūrvaṃ hi vidhyarthaḥ</q>। na
pūrvamapūrvam। pūrva taducyate yadavagataṃ prāk। yat‍tu kena citprāganavagataṃ pratīyate tadapūrvam।
tathābhūtaśca vidhyarthaḥ। tathāpi kimityāha---<q>vidhitaśca pramāṇyamityuktam</q>। pramāṇā-
ntaragamyā hi kriyā bhāvanā vā yadi vākyārthaḥ syāt tadā vedasyāprāmāṇyameva syāt।
tayorhi pramāṇāntaragamyena ced‍rūpeṇa vedādavagatiḥ tadā'nuvādādaprāmāṇyam। atha
pramāṇāntarāvagamyarūpaviparītena rūpeṇa tadā viparyayādaprāmāṇyam। vidheḥ punaḥ pramāṇānta-
rāvedyasya yathaiva śabdādavagatiḥ tathaiva prāmāṇyaṃ nyāyyam। pramāṇāntaravedye cārthe pauruṣeyatvaṃ
cedasyāpadyata iti prathamapāda uk‍tameva। atrocyate---<q>ayamabhiprāyaś‍codakasya niyogo hi
karmaṇi puruṣaṃ niyuṅkte na svārthe</q>। asyārthaḥ--loke hi kārbāvagatiḥ pravṛttau nimittam।
bālo'pi hi yāvata kāryatayā stanapānādikaṃ nāvabudhyate tāvanna pravartate। tena vṛddhavyavahārepi
prayojyasya liṅādiśabdānvitavākyaśravaṇasamanantarabhāvinīṃ pravṛttimupalabhya kāryāvagatinimittatā-
<note n="1">G. <dn>sādhyatvāt</dn></note>
﻿<pb n="r320"/>
liṅāderavasīyate। tatrāpi cintyam---kiṃ karma gavānayanādikaṃ kāryatayā pratyāyyate ?
yadi vā karmātiriktamanyaditi ? tatra karmaṇi pravṛttidarśanāt tadeva kāryatayā'vagatamiti
pratīyate। pratītipravṛkattyoḥ samānaviṣayattvāt। ācāryavākyānantarapravṛttāvapyevameva।
tasmālliṅādiḥ karmaṇa eva kāryatāmavagamayati vyutpattipratipattyorekaviṣayattvāt।
ācāryavākyānantaraṃ yadeva kāryatayā śabdo'vagamayati tatraiva puruṣo niyujyate। anyathā
niyogāsambhavāt। tena karma kāryatayā liṅādiravagamayan karmaṇyeva puruṣaṃ
niyuṅkte। nānyatra karmavyatirik‍te svārthe। anyasya svārthatvenānavabodhyamānattvāt।
etañca kriyaiva vākyārthaḥ। tasyā eva śabdena kāryatayā pratyāyyamānattvāt।
tataścaitadadhikaraṇasiddhāntasiddhamevāpūrvasya vākyārthatvamāśritya prāmāṇyamityuk‍tam।
nanvevamapi phāmināṃ karmaṇi niyuktau phalasiddhirna syāt; kṣaṇikatvātkarmaṇām।
kālāntarabhāvittvācca phalasiddheḥ। tadidamaṅgīkṛtyaivāha---<q>karma cānityam। na ca svargādya-
nantaramupalabhyate। tasmādyāgasya vā nityatvaṃ kalpayitavyam। ātmano vā saṃskāraḥ kaścit।
devatāprasādo vā na punastenāpūrvaṃ kṛtvetyetat sūktamiva pratibhāti</q>। paraṃ phalasidhyanya-
thānupapattyā karmaṇo vā nityatvaṃ, ātmano vā saṃskāraḥ kaścit, devatāprasādo vā kalpyatām।
﻿<pb n="r321"/>
apūrvantu kāryarūpaṃ śabdenāvagamyata iti vyutpattiviparītaṃ aśakyādhyasānam। ato yasya ca
śabdasyārthena phalaṃ sādhyate tenāpūrva kṛtvā nānyatheti yaduk‍taṃ tada‍duruktamiva pratibhāti।
<q>codanā punarārambhaḥ। atrābhidhīyate। niyogaḥ karmaṇi puruṣaṃ niyuṅktai iti samyagava-
dhṛtaṃ bhavatā। ārambhe hi puruṣaṃ niyuṅkte na karmaṇi</q>। ayamāśayaḥ---yadā tāvat ṣaṣṭhādya-
siddhāntabalena bādaryadhikaraṇasiddhāntabalena ca phalasiddhisamarthe kārye kāmī niyujyata iti
sthitaṃ tadā na karmaṇi <note n="1">R.<dn>kāmīniyojyatayā'nvayamanubhavati</dn></note>kāmīno niyojyatā saṃbhavati। tasya kālāntarabhāviphalasādha-
katvābhāvāt। ato niyojyānvayayogyaṃ yāgādivyatirik‍taṃ kālāntarāvasthāyi kāryaṃ liṅādibhiḥ
pratyāyyate। ato liṅādayaḥ svārthe puruṣaṃ niyuñ‍jate natu karmaṇi। kasmāt karmaṇyeva na puruṣaṃ
niyuñjata ityatrāha---<q>ārambhaviṣayaṃ hi karma</q>। kāryabhūtasya vidhyarthasya viṣayobhāvenānvayaṃ
yāgādikarma yātīti na tatra puruṣo niyujyate। nanvevamapyārambhaḥ kāryatayā pratīyate na vidhyarthaḥ
tatrāha---<q>sa cārambho vidhyarthaḥ</q>। ārabhyate aneta iti vyutpattyā ārambhaḥ ārambhārthaḥ punarvidhyarthaḥ
tasya phalasādhanatā'vagamyate phalakarmeti bā। kathaṃ viṣayamiti napuṃsakaliṅgatā ? karma-
śabdasāmānādhikaraṇyāt। tadyathā pradhāno'yaṃ lakṣaṇārtha iti pulliṅgatvam। kathaṃ punarvidhyarthasya
phalasādhanatā'vagamyate ? phalasādhanatve vā kimiti phalasya vākyārthatā na bhavatītyatrāha
﻿<pb n="r322"/>
---svargakāmasya cāsāvityārambhāt svarga iti brūmaḥ। basmātsvargakāmasya niyojyasya aso
niyogaḥ। na cāsau phalamasādhayastasya bhavati। ato niyojyaviśeṣasaṃbandhanniyogaḥ phala-
sādhanatāmavalamvate। ātmana evāso saṃvidadhīnaḥ phalasādhaka iti <note n="1">G. <dn>pradhāna bhāvanā</dn></note> pradhānabhāvaṃ nātivartate। nahi niyojyasambandhaṃ vinā niyogasya siddhirupapadyate। taduk‍tam---
ātmasiddhayanukūlasya niyojyasya prasiddhaye।
kurvan svargādikamapi pradhānaṃ kāryameva naḥ।। (pra. pa. bākyārthamā)
kena punarupāyena tasyāpūrvasya siddhiḥ tatrāha---<q>karmaṇāñcārambhaḥ</q> viṣayabhūtaṃ karmaiva<note n="2"><dn>karmeva tatsukaramiti</dn></note> tasya
karaṇamiti darśitaṃ <q>viṣayakaraṇīye</q>। nanvevamapi karmaṇā vidhyarthe siddhe kimiti karmānantaraṃ
phalaṃ na bhavati ? sahakāryapekṣaṇāditi brūmaḥ। darśitañca tat <quote>“tac‍caiva hi kāraṇaṃ śabdaśceti”</quote>।
bhāṣyaṃ (1-1-5) evañ‍ca kāmādhikāre yāgādivyatiriktakāryavacanā liṅgādayo vyutpannāḥ।
nityādhikāre niṣedhādhikāre<note n="3">G. Omits this</note> ca tadevāvabodhayanti anekārthakalpanāyā anyāyyatvāt। loke tu pramāṇāntareṇa tasyānupalambhāt na tatpratipādakatayā liṅādayaḥ prayok‍tuṃ śakyāḥ। kintu
pramāṇāntaragamye karmaṇaḥ kāryatve lakṣaṇayā prayujyante। karmaṇo hi kāryatā। bidhyarthaḥ
kāryatāṃ na vyabhicarati। tena tāmavyabhicāriṇīṃ kāryatāṃ lakṣayituṃ liṅādeḥ prayogaḥ। lākṣaṇi-
kābhimānastu laukikānāṃ nyāyamaviduṣāṃ nāsti। viduṣāṃ punarastyeva। kasmātpunaḥ karmādī-
nāmeva nityatvādikaṃ na parikalpyate atrāha---<q>karmādinityatvaparikalpanā punaḥ pramāṇāntara-
viruddhaiva; animittā ca ārambhe pratyarthini। kathaṃ punaḥ pramāṇāntaravirodhaḥ</q> ? uttaram
﻿<pb n="r323"/>
---<q>bhaṅgitvaṃ hi karṇāṃ prasiddhameva kṣaṇāntaranupalambhācca</q>। svabhāvata eva tāvat karmaṇāṃ
kṣaṇabhaṅgitā prasiddhā। tathā''śrayavināśādapi vināśitvam। kathaṃ punarāśrayasyaiva vināśa
ityatrāha---<q>ātmanaśca niṣkiyatvaṃ sarvagatattvādātmanaḥ</q>। yadi hi karmaṇaḥ āśrayaḥ ātmā syāt
na syādāśrayavināśādvināśaḥ। na tvātmanaḥ karmāśrayatvaṃ niṣkriyatvādātmanaḥ। niṣkriyatā ca
sarvagatattvāt। upapāditā ca sarvagatatā'smābhiḥ <q>pariśiṣṭe</q>। etacca calanātmikāṃ kriyāmaṅgī-
kṛtyocyate। yāpi ca yāgādikriyā sāpi śāstrīyarūpā nānāvidhā'nekaparispandābacchinnā
nātmani samavaiti। <q>puroḍāśādeśca karmavadvināśadarśanāt</q>। tadāśritasya karmaṇaḥ spaṣṭa
eva vināśaḥ āśrayavināśāt। athocyeta <note n="1">G.<dn>purastādabhāvāt</dn></note> sūkṣmībhāvāt puroḍāśāderanupalabdhiḥ na puna-rvināśādityatrāha---<q>saukṣmyādeśca viśeṣasyārambhe pratyarthini nāsti kalpanetyuktam। darśi-
tañca bhāṣye sāmānyakalpanāyāmasti pramāṇaṃ na viśeṣakalpanāyāmiti</q>।
﻿<pb n="r324"/>
<p>asyārthaḥ। saukṣmyādikamapi puroḍāśādīnāṃ kalpyate karmaṇāñca sthāyitvaṃ yadyanyathā-
nupapattiḥ syāt। na cāsāvasti iti kriyātiriktaṃ sthāyikāryaṃ kiñcidastīti sāmānyakalpana-
yauvopapatteḥ। devatāprasādātmasaṃskārau ca navamaikādaśayornirākariṣyamāṇatvādiha na
nirākṛtau।</p>
<p><q>tāni dvaidham।। avagatametat bhāvaśabdāḥ pradhānakarmaṇo vācakā iti</q> bhāṣyamanubhā-
ṣitamākṣipati---<q>kva punaridamavagataṃ ? bhāvaśabdāḥ pradhānakarmaṇo vācakā iti। karma-
śabdā bhāvārthā ityetatsamadhigatam</q>। etadeva bivṛṇoti---<q>karmaṇaḥ pūrvāparībhūtasya</q>
<note n="1">G. <dn>guṇabhāvādarśanāt</dn></note>
﻿<pb n="r325"/>
<q>vācakā iti na punaḥ prādhānyaṃ kacinnirdiṣṭam। athāyamabhiprāyaḥ itarattadarthamiti vadatā
nāmārthaṃ pratyākhyātārthasya prādhānyamuktamiti</q> yadaikasmādapūrvaṃ tadā itarattadarthamiti vadatā'pūrva-
viṣayabhūtānāmākhyātārthānāṃ dravyaguṇāpekṣayā prādhānyamuk‍tamiti। <q>tadayuk‍taṃ svargakāmapadārthaṃ
puruṣaṃ prati guṇabhāvadarśanāt। tathocoktam te svargakāmapadasambandhāt svargaṃ bhāvayediti
vrūyuriti। tasmānna vidmaḥ kimidamavagatametat bhāvaśabdāḥ pradhānakarmaṇo vācakā
iti। atrābhidhīyate---prādhānyaṃ hi niyogaviṣayatvamabhipretam</q>। tenāyamarthaḥ---avagata-
metat bhāvaśabdāḥ niyogaviṣayībhūtasya karmaṇo vācakā iti। kasmātpunaḥ pradhānaśabdena
niyogaviṣayaḥ ucyate ? tadāha <q>kuta iti</q>। uttaram---<q>viṣayatvādeva</q>। niyogaviṣayo
hi nānyo'rtho bhavati। nanu niyogaviṣayo niyojya eva tāvat guṇabhāvena pratīyate
﻿<pb n="r326"/>
anyathā niyogasiddhayanupapatteḥ ityatrāha---<q>niyogaviṣayatayā hi yāgādayaḥ pratīyante na kasya-
cidutpattyādyarthatayā</q>। yathā'vadhātādayaḥ kasyacidutpattyādyarthatayā pratīyante na tathā
yāgādayaḥ। kintu viṣayatāmātreṇa teṣāmavagatiḥ śabdataḥ। tathā'vagatānāñca teṣāmārthikī guṇa-
bhūtatā। yathā caitattathā'dhikāralakṣaṇe vakṣyāmaḥ। tena śābdīmavasthāmāśritya pradhānavyapadeśaḥ।
<q>tasmād‍yuktamevaitadavagatametaditi। cintā copapadyate</q>। yadaivaṃbhūtaḥ pradhānaśabdasyārthaḥ
tadā cintāpyupapadyate। <q>kiṃ sarvāṇyeva niyogaviṣayatayā pratīyante ? utotpattyādyarthatayā
keciditi</q>। anyathā hi yadi dravyaguṇāpekṣayā śoṣitayā pradhānatvamāśrīyate
tadā peṣaṇāderapi pradhānatā dṛṣadupalādyapekṣayeti sarvameva pradhānaṃ syāt। tataśca
koṭidvayābhāve cintānupapattiḥ। atra cādhikaraṇe śrūyamāṇāmapi dvitīyāṃ aśrūya-
māṇāmiva kṛtvā cintā। ata eva ca bhāṣyakāreṇa dogdhi pinaṣṭi vilāpayatī---
﻿<pb n="r327"/>
syevamādaya ityevok‍tam। dvitīyāṅgīkāre hi pūrvapakṣayitumeva na śakyate। tatra
pūrvapakṣī manyate। sarveṣāntāvadanyotpādakatā। ato yuk‍tā sarveṣāmeva niyogaviṣayatā।
na hi sākṣātsambandhasambhave paramparāśrayaṇaṃ nyāyyam। na ca śabdāvagatakriyākārakabhāva-
virodhaḥ। dvitīyāmanaṅgīkṛtya vicārābhyupagamāt। rāddhāntastu---loke tāvat pramāṇāntareṇotpa-
ttyādisambandhitā godohanādīnāmavagatā। ghaṭate ca taddvāreṇa niyogārthatvam। na ca
dṛṣṭasvabhāvānusāreṇa niyogārthatve upapadyamāne adṛṣṭaśrayaṇaṃ yuk‍tamiti cikīrṣitotpattyādyarthataiva
eṣām। pūrvapakṣamāha---<q>yuk‍taṃ tāvat keṣāñcidutpattyādyarthatā kalpayitum। yadyevambhūtā-
nāmapi</q>, kāryāntare vyāpṛtānāmapi <q>niyogasaṃsparśitopapadyate। na tu tadadyāpi
nirṇīyate। <note n="1">G.<dn>ayaṃ tu</dn></note> atha tu nirṇaye heturasti tato na sarvasyāpūrvārthatā nyāyyā</q>। na cāsā-
vasti। na ca sākṣātsambandhasambhave paramparāśrayaṇaṃ yuk‍tamiti bhāvaḥ। rāddhāntabhāṣyamākṣipati
---<q>evamalpīyasyadṛṣṭānumānaprasaṅgakalpanā nyāyyeti bhāṣyam। tatpunarasaṅgatārthamiva
pratibhāti</q>। niyogārthatve'pi hi niyogaviṣayatve'pi hi <q>naivādṛṣṭānumānakalpanā। ucyate</q>।
﻿<pb n="r328"/>
parihṛtametadevamalpīyasyadṛṣṭānumānaprasaṅgakalpanetyatra। <q>nanu yuk‍taṃ tatra pramāṇāntaradṛṣṭa-
kriyāniṣpattiparityāgena nāmārthānāṃ śabdato niyoganiṣpādakatvaṃ</q> ?। na yuktam,
evamapi kriyāniṣpādakatvenāpi niyogārthatve upapadyamāne iti; iha tathā nāstīti bhāvaḥ।
pariharati---<q>atrāpi tulyaṃ kriyāntarasya yatsādhanaṃ</q> vrīhyādi tadutpattyādyarthatayā sambhabati
niyogasaṃsparśini <q>śabde niyogasādhanatā sākṣāt na yuk‍tā। nanu ca niyogaśūnyānāṃ niyoga-
viṣayo</q> yo yāgaḥ tasya vrīhyādi <q>tadupattyādyarthataiva</q> avaghātādīnāṃ <q>nāvasīyate</q>।
vrīhyādiśabdānāṃ jātimātravacanatvāt। <q>nacāvihitamaṅgaṃ bhavatīti vakṣyati</q>। vidhiśūnyañca
na vihitaṃ bhavati। pariharati---<q>satyam niyogādṛte nāṅgatā</q>। astyevātrāpi niyogo-
'dhikāravidhirūpaḥ sannidhisamāmnātasakalapadārthagrāhī। tad‍grahabalenaiva tadīye sādhane viniyoga
<q>itya ṅga pā rāyaṇe nirṇītam</q>। yadi niyogādṛte aṅgatā nāsti bhavatu tarhi aṅgeṣvapi niyoga
﻿<pb n="r329"/>
ityatrāha---<q>na ca niyogārthateti tṛtīye vakṣyāmaḥ</q> teṣāmarthādhikaraṇe। <q>ke punaste bhāvārthāḥ</q>
ye kriyāntarasādhanotpattyādyarthatayā niyogasaṃsparśinaḥ। uttaram---<q>ya eva loke cikīrṣito-
tpattyādyarthatayā prasiddhāḥ</q>। te ca <q>darśitā bhāṣyakāreṇa</q> dohanapeṣaṇavilayanādayaḥ।
<q>prayojanamuktaṃ</q> bhāṣyakāreṇa।</p>
<p><q>dharmamātre tu karma syāt। uktamajahatkriyākārakasambandha eva niyoga-
sambandhaḥ kārakāṇāṃ bhāvārthānāṃ ca cikīrṣitārthānām। ihedānīṃ yatra dṛṣṭaḥ
saṃskāro nopalabhyate, cikīrṣitapratipādikā ca vibhaktirasti tatrāpi kimajahatkriyā
﻿<pb n="r330"/>
<q>kārakasambandhaiva niyogārthatā uta yāgāderiva niyogaviṣayataiva dhātvarthasyeti</q> cintyate।
anenāvāntarasaṅgatiḥ saṃśayabījaṃ saṃśayasvarūpañcopanyastam। <q>kiṃ punaratna yuktam</q> ? pūrva-
pakṣamāha---<q>dṛṣṭasyābhāvānniyogasiddhirevāvaśipyate</q>। yathā pūrvatra kāryāntaraṃ dṛṣṭaṃ tatheha
nāsti prokṣaṇādīnāṃ tena niyogasiddhireva kevalaṃ kāryam। yasya ca niyogasiddhireva kāryaṃ sa
viṣaya iti viṣayatvameva prokṣaṇādīnām tadāha---<q>tasmātprayājādivanniyogārthataiva saṃmārgādeḥ।
nanu cikīrṣitārthapratipādikā dvitīyāvibhaktiḥ avivakṣitā bhavati</q>। pariharati
---<q>na ceyamaikāntikī। balbajān śikhaṇḍakān kurvīṃtetyevamādiṣu vyabhicāradarśanāt</q>।
na hi balbajāḥ tatra cikīrṣitāḥ। kintarhi śikhaṇḍakāḥ। tenāsatyapi cikīrṣitārthatve
﻿<pb n="r331"/>
dvitīyāvibhaktirbhavati iti na cikīrṣitārthatvaṃ pratipādayitumalam। tathā vede ca sak‍tūn
juhotīti <note n="1">G. omits this</note> dhyabhicāriṇī dvitīyā। <q>tasmātkaraṇārthepyasyāḥ prayogo dṛṣṭaḥ</q>। tenādṛṣṭa-
kāryakalpanāyāṃ neyaṃ pramāṇamiti niyogārthatvameva sammārgādeḥ tulyaśrutitvāt। ucyate।
<q>yattāvalloke vyabhicāradarśanamupanyastam tadayuk‍tam। loke hi vivakṣātaḥ kārakāṇi
bhavanti</q> yādṛśaṃ kārakaṃ puruṣo vivakṣati anevarupepyarthe tādṛśameva śabdenocyate। vivakṣā
ca puruṣavaśānuvartinī-puruṣasyecchānuvartinī। vaśaśabdenecchā'bhidhīyate। <q>ataścikīrṣita-
vibhak‍tidarśanāt tathaiva vivakṣeti yuktaṃ pratipat‍tum</q>। tena balbajāneva śikhaṇḍākāreṇe-
ṣṭān pratipat‍tuṃ dvitīyeyaṃ prayukteti kalpyate। tena loke tāvat vyabhicāradarśanaṃ nāsti।
tena cikīrṣitārthavācinyeva dvitīyeti niścīyate। <q>vede tu kathaṃ</q> ? uttaram---<q>uktamasmābhiḥ</q>

﻿<pb n="r332">
<q>kāryarthatayā prāmāṇyaṃ</q> sarveṇa padajātena niyoga eva pratipādyate। tatra tu
kenacita sākṣāttasyaivābhidhānam। kenacicca tadanvitārthābhidhānam। <q>iha ca cikīrṣitārthā-
parityāgena niyogasaṃsparśitā na śakyate</q> juhotītyasya <q>vak‍tum</q>। kasmādityāha---<q>kriyā-
ntarasādhanatvena aśravaṇāt sak‍tūnām</q>। yathā vrīhyādayo niyogaviṣayībhūtayāgasādhanatvena
śrūyante na tathā saktavaḥ। tena nāsti tanmukhena niyogasaṃsparśitā juhoteḥ। nanu yadyapi
sak‍tavaḥ kriyāntarasādhanatvena na śrūyante tathāpi prayājādivanniyogānupraveśitvaṃ bhaviṣyati।
tataśca taddvāreṇa juhoterapi niyogānupraveśitā ghaṭiṣyate। atrāha---<q>na ca saṃktavo niyogauk‍yena
itikartavyatāṃpratipat‍tuṃ kṣamāḥ</q>। yathā prayājādayo niyogauk‍yena itikartavyatāṃ karaṇo-
pakārakarāṃ pratipat‍tuṃ kṣamāḥ na tathā saktavaḥ niyogaik‍yābhāvāt। <q>kimiti niyogaik‍yaṃ na
<q>bhavatīti</q> ? uttaram---<q>abhāvārthatvāt sak‍tūnām</q>। yeṣāṃ hi eko'dhikāraniyogaḥ

﻿<pb n="r333">
sādhyaḥ teṣāmitikartavyatātvam। na ca sak‍tūnāmabhāvārthānāṃ anyotpādakatvabhāvahīnānāṃ
adhikāraniyogaḥ sādhyatayā śakyate vak‍tum। prayājādīnāntu bhāvārthānāṃ śakyate'vyabhi-
cāreṇānyotpādakatayā utpādyasvabhāvasannihitādhikāraniyogasaṃbandho'dhyavasātum। nanu vināpi
niyogaik‍yena kimiti netikartavyatātvam ? tatrāha---<q>kāryārthasya hi karaṇāṃśopanipātitā।
kimityaṃśopanipātitā vā</q>। yasya hi kāryārthatvaṃ tasya karaṇāṃśopanipātitā sākṣātkaraṇatayā
vā tadanugrāhakatayā vā tadanugrāhako'pi karaṇāṃśa eva। kimityaṃśopanipātino'dhikāriviśeṣa-
ṇāṃśe। akāryārthasya tvetadubhayamapi nopapadyate। tenākāryārthatvātsak‍tūnāṃ svatastāvadanubandhabhāvo<note n="1">G.<dn>anubandhābhāvaḥ</dn></note>
nāstīti। tadāha---<q>ato na svato'nubandhabhāvaḥ</q> niyogasaṃbandhitvamityarthaḥ। na ca <note n="2">G. <dn>sak‍tuhoma</dn></note> sak‍tvartha-
homadvāreṇāpītyāha---<q>bhinnānubandhānāñca kimityaṃśabhāva evaik‍yam</q>। sak‍tūnā hi bhinnā-
nāmutpattiniyogānāmiva ye'nubandhāsteṣāṃ sādhyāṃśa evaik‍yam yathā'dhikāraniyoge।
<q>bhidyate cātra kimityaṃśabhāvaḥ</q> sādhyāṃśaḥ ekatra saktavaḥ sādhyāḥ। aparatrādhikāraḥ।
<q>ato naik‍yaṃ vidheḥ anekatvācca jetikartavyatātvaṃ sak‍tūnāṃ tasmādalaukiko'yaṃ cikīrṣitārtha-
saṃyogaḥ cikīrṣitatvena sak‍tūnāmanavagamāt। na caitāvatā vyabhicāritā śak‍yate vak‍tuṃ
<note n="3"><dn>anubandhānāṃ ca</dn></note>
﻿<pb n="r334">
<q>dvitīyāyāḥ</q> kasmādityāha---<q>yāvaddarśanabhāvī hi chāndasaprayogaḥ yāvatyeva dṛśyate tāvatyeva
chāndasaprayogo bhavati tatra saktūnāṃ mārutaikakapālādiṣu <note n="1">G.<dn>kriyāpi</dn></note>vināpi cikīrṣitatvena dvitīyā dṛṣṭeti teṣveva tathāstu। anyatra tu cikīrṣitārthavāvinyevāsau। <q>tathā ca vyākhyātāro</q>
vyākaraṇa-vyākhyātāro <q>dṛṣṭānuvidhiḥ chandasītyupadiśanti</q> yata eva <note n="2">
<dn>G.<dn>ceyamapi</dn></note> ceyamacikīrṣitārthe dvitīyā
<q>ata eva bhagavatā</q> sūtrakāreṇa <q>tṛtīyā ca hośchandasīti tṛtīyārthe chandasi dvitīyā
dṛṣṭetyuktam</q>। sūtrasya cāyamarthaḥ---chandasi viṣaye juhoteḥ prayoge dvitīyā bhavati, tṛtīyā ca। yadi
dvitīyā bhavatyevetyetāvadevocyate tadā iha dvitīyāyāḥ tṛtīyayā bādhitatvāt<noten="3">G.<dn>adhikṛtatvāta
</dn></note> satyapi karaṇatve tṛtīyā na syāt। tena sāpi tasya vidhīyate। anena cābhiprāyeṇa vṛttikāreṇāpyuktam
dvitīyāyāṃ prāptāyāṃ tṛtīyā vidhīyata iti। cakārātsāpi bhavatīti। asyāyamarthaḥ---yadi cakāraḥ

﻿<pb n="r335">
sūtre na prayujyate katadā tṛtīyaiva kevalā sūtreṇoktā bhavati। tataśca dvitīyāvidhirna jñāyate। ata
eva prādhānyena dvitīyāvidhānārthatvāt sūtrasya dvitīyādhikāro'yamityuttarasūtrepi dvitīyaivā-
nuvartate। <q>yattu kātyāyanenoktam</q>---karmaṇāṃ karaṇasaṃjñā vak‍tavyā saṃpradānasya ca karaṇasaṃjñeti
tata asadvāditvādasya anādaraṇīyam। na hi yāge haviṣaḥ karmatā। <q>ata eva copapada-
vibhak‍titulyaiṣā draṣṭavyā</q>। yathā antarāntareṇaśabdaprayoge dvitīyā tathābhūtaiṣā draṣṭavyā।
lokaprasiddhadvitīyārthābhāvāt। lokataśca sambandhādhyavasāyaḥ tatra<note n="1>R.<dn>cāvyabhi</dn></note>
ca vyabhicāro darśitaḥ। <q>tasmādajahatsvārthavṛttitvānniyogārthasya</q>। ajahat svārthavṛttiḥ yaḥ so'jahatsvārthavṛttiḥ
niyogārthaḥ tasya bhāvastattvam। tasmāt cikīrṣitārthaiveyaṃ grahaṃ sammārṣṭi vrīhīn prokṣatī<note n="2">R. add<dn>nāsti</dn></note>tyeva-
mādiṣu <q>dvitīyā</q>। tena niyogaviṣayatā sammārgādīnāmapi। <q>nanu ca dṛṣṭo'rtho nāstī-
tyuktam</q>। ato na cikīrṣitārthatvasambhavaḥ। pariharati---<q>niyogārthasya ca sātvaṃ na cikīrṣi-
﻿<pb n="r336">
<q>tārtheṣu sambhavatītyapyuktam</q>। asyārthaḥ---yathā dṛṣṭārthoṃ nāstīti bhavadbhiruktam tathā'smā-
bhirapyetaduktam ye bhāvārthāśca cikīrṣitārthāḥ teṣu niyogārthasya sādhyatva nāstīti। ekagranthenāha
---<q>nacānyat pramāṇamasti yena kāryakalpanā syāt</q> niyogāṅgagrahādigataṃ parityajya yena
pramāṇāntareṇa kāryāntarakalpanā syāt tat pramāṇāntaraṃ nāstīti। <q>tataścikīrṣitārthābhidhā-
nāt niyogārthasaṃsparśitvācca siddhamadṛṣṭakāryatvam। lokavatkāryāntarasaṃyogāt</q>
grahaṇādīnāṃ, yathā cikīrṣitārthābhidhāyinī dvitīyopapadyate yathā ca niyogasaṃsparśitā bhavati
tathā'nusaratāṃ niyogasaṃsparśānuguṇagrahādigatādṛṣṭakalpanaiva nyāyyā'vabhāti। saṃbhavati ca
niyogānuguṇaniyogāṅgagrahādīnāṃ kāryānyarayogitvāt। lokavaditi dṛṣṭānta vyācaṣṭe---<q>loke'pi
kāryāntarayogitvāt hastyādīnāṃ siddhaṃ nīrājanāderadṛṣṭārthatvaṃ prayojanam। varuṇa-
pradhāseṣu śrūyate <quote>“śamīmayyaḥ sruco bhavanti hiraṇmayyovā’</quote> iti। prakṛtau nānāvṛkṣīya- ﻿<pb n="r337"/>
<q>sruk‍sammārgavyaṅgamapūrvamiti nānāvṛkṣīyāḥ sruca utpādayitavyāḥ। sammārgārthena yathā
pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ yathā tarhi siddhāntaḥ śamīmayya eva hiraṇmayyo vā sammārjayitavyā iti tathā
paridhyādiṣu</q>, anena bhāṣyeṇok‍taṃ prayojanamanubhāṣitam। <q>nanu ca pūrvapakṣe'pyaṅgapradhānārtha-
metadvidhānaṃ bhaviṣyati barhirvat</q>। anena srugudāharaṇaprayojanamākṣipati। arthastu yathā barhiṣi
havīṃpyāsādayatītyaṅgapradhānārthabarhirvidhīyate tathā śamīmayatvaṃ hiraṇmayatvaṃ vā। tataśca sammārge'pi
tadvidhānāt tatsammārga eva kartavyaḥ na nānāvṛkṣīyasammārga iti na prayojanasiddhiḥ। pariharati
<q>naivam। yatra hyaṅgapradhānārtha evopadeśavidhiḥ kāryavidhirapi tatra tathaiva। yatra punaḥ
﻿<pb n="r338"/>
upadeśavidhibhedaḥ tatra kāryavidhiḥ prakaraṇāt pradhānasyaiva</q>। asyārthaḥ। prakṛtau yo vidhiḥ
sa upadeśavidhiḥ upadiśyata ityupadeśaḥ padārthaḥ tasmin yo'sau vidhiḥ na kārye। padārtho-
padeśapūrvakatvāt tatkalpanāyāḥ। vikṛtau tu yo vidhiḥ sa kārye prākṛtopadeśaprakalpye
vidhānāt। tatra yadi prakṛtāveka eva vidhiraṅgapradhānārthaḥ tadā tatkalpyaṃ kāryamapi aṅga-
pradhānārtham। kāryavidhirapi tatra kāryasyaikatvāt aṅgapradhānārtha eva bhavati। yathā śaravidhiḥ
<q>yatra punarupadeśavidhibhedaḥ</q> tatra bhinnaṃ kāryam। kāryavidhiśca<note n="1">G.<dn>kāryavidhinā। tataśca</dn></note> ekasminneva kārye yuktaḥ। ekatraiva bādhena caritārthatbānna śakrotyanekatra bādhitumiti। kāryavidhinā hi bādhamānenānu-
praveṣṭavyam। tatra ca prakaraṇabalena pradhānasambandhinaiva kāryavidhinā bhavitavyam। <q>darśita-
mānarthakyāttadaṅgeṣviti</q>। nanvaṅgeṣu vidhiranena darśitaḥ na pradhāne ityatrāha---yatra hi
<q>pradhānasya tatkāryaṃ na sambhavati tatrānarthakyāttadaṅgānām। yatra punassambhavati tatra
﻿ <pb n="r339"/>
<q>pradhānārtha eva bhavati prakṛtatvāt ityuktam। yathā sahasradakṣiṇādayaḥ pradhānadakṣiṇāsu
ānarthakyāṃt tadaṅgeṣvityanena arthādidamuktam</q>। pradhānasya sambhave nāṅge vidhānam। kintu
pradhānasyaiva yathā sahasradakṣiṇā ahīnānāmiti pradhānadakṣiṇākārye sahasradakṣiṇāvidhānaṃ
nāṅgadakṣiṇākārye। iha juhā juhotītyupadeśena ekaṃ pradhānasambandhi k‏lṛptam। sruca-
ssambhārṣṭītyanenāparamaṅgasambandhi। tatra vikṛtau śamīmayatvañca vidhīyamānaṃ pradhānakārya eva vṛkṣa-
jātaṃ vikāroti nāṅgakārye। tataścābādhitatvāta parṇādivṛkṣāṇāṃ sammārga[rgārtha]tvena nānāvṛkṣīyāḥ
srucaḥ utpādyāḥ। prakṛtau tu parṇamayatvādisruk‍padārthoddeśenaiva vidhīyamānaṃ homādau
sammārge ca bhavatīti pradhānaṃ samarthitaṃ prayojanam। evantāvat srugudāharaṇaṃ samarthitam।
nanu paridhyudāharaṇe yadyapi pradhānakārya eva bāṇavidhiḥ tathāpi sammārgopi tenaiva(veti) vakta-
vyam paridhessatastatra viniyogāt। tathā'gnyudāharaṇamayuktam। apūrvatvādavabhṛthasyetyatrāha
---<q>na codāharaṇamādaraṇīyaṃ madhvaśanādiṣu darśanāt</q> udāharaṇānādarasya। puroḍāśodāharaṇe
tu yāgoddeśena vrīhividhināt paryagnikaraṇe vrīhayo nāṅgamiti bikṛtāvapi na vrīhīṇāṃ
prāptiḥ।</p>

﻿<pb n="r340"/>
<p><q>stutaśastrayoḥ</q>।। atra bhāṣyakāra evaṃ vicārayati---yadetat guṇavacanaṃ tat guṇinīṃ
devatāṃ prati guṇabhūtaṃ uta pradhānabhūtamiti। tadanupapannam। nātra niyogaviṣayatvāviṣayatvalakṣaṇaḥ
pradhānaguṇabhāvaścintyate। kintu devatāpekṣaḥ śeṣaśoṣibhāvarūpaḥ। sa cāsaṅgato'trādhyāye
niyogaviṣayavastuvicārastu upoddhātatvena saṅgataḥ। sati viṣayabhāve tadbhedena śāstrabhedo bhavati
anyathā neti matvā''ha---<q>atrāpi sa eva saṃśayaḥ। kintu stutaśastrayoḥ cikīrṣitārthatvaṃ
uta vidhiviṣayataiveti</q>। bhāṣye niyogaviṣayatvapakṣe stutaśastrayoḥ devatāpekṣayā tayoḥ pradhāna-
bhāvaḥ। aviṣayatvapakṣe tu guṇabhāva ityuktam। atra codayati---<q>nanu cikīrṣitārthatve
stutyartho'pi hīyate stauti śaṃsatīti ca tadarthānidhānam</q>। asyārthaḥ---yāgadevatāsaṃskārā-
rthatayā stutaśastrayościkīrṣitārthatvam। tatra mantravākyena yadi yāgadevatāprakāśanaṃ kriyate tadā-
'bhidhānataiva syāt yājyāvat, na stutirūpatā। yadi punaḥ <note n="1">R.<dn>stutigatadeva</dn></note> stutiḥ na ca devatāprakāśanaṃ mantravākyena kriyate tadā yāgīyasmaraṇānupapatteḥ na cikīrṣitārthatvam। <q>tasmānnātra saṃśayaṃ

﻿<pb n="r341"/>
<q>paśyāmaḥ। ajahatsvārtha2 tṛṣṇayā hi cikīrṣitārthatvaṃ gṛhyate viparītaśca tadatra</q> stuti-
rūpatāhāniprasaṅgāt। <q>athāyamabhiprāyaḥ paśupuroḍāśavat cikīrṣitārthatā</q>। dṛṣṭāntaṃ vivṛ-
ṇoti---<q>yāgasya sato devatārthatvaṃ devatārthatve ca cikīrṣitārthatvam। na ca yajyartho'-
paiti</q>। upasaṃharati---<q>tasmāt stutereva devatāsmaraṇaṃ prayojanaṃ bhaviṣyati yajeriva</q>।
dūpayati---<q>viṣama upanyāsaḥ</q>। vaiṣamyameva darśayati---<q>tatra hi devatāsādhanako yāgaḥ</q> yo'sau
puroḍāśayāgaḥ sa devatāsādhanakaḥ tena devatāṃ saṃskartuṃ śaknoti। <q>ato'jahatsvārtha-
vṛttitvaṃ yujyate yajerna devatāsaṃskārakatve kaścidvirodhaḥ। iha punaḥ stutiḥ stutyama-
pekṣate na devatām</q>। tena stutiḥ stutyamātraprakāśane samarthā na devatāsmaraṇe। <q>evañca
devārthatve hīyate stutyarthaḥ। nanu ca stutibhājo'pi devā iti devatāvidaḥ</q> tena stutyo'pi
<note n="1">G.<dn>svārthavṛttyāhi</dn></note>

﻿<pb n="r342"/>
devātārūpa iti tena stutirapi stutyamapekṣamāṇā devatāmevāpekṣate। ato bhavatyevāsau devatā-
prakāśanasamarthā। na ca svarūpamapi jahāti tadāha---<q>devatā cet stutyā tarhi sāmyaṃ paśu-
puroḍāśena। maivaṃ vocaḥ ghoṭārūḍhasya vismṛto ghoṭaḥ</q>। vismṛta iti karmakartari niṣṭhā
vismṛtaḥ cittādapakrānta ityarthaḥ। ekagranthenāha---<q>stitibhājaśca devatā iti vravīṣi
havirbhājaśca saṃskāraṃ manyase</q>। uddeśyatayā hi yāge devatābhāvaḥ, prakāśyamānaguṇatayā ca
stutau devatā। tena yasyāḥ saṃskāramicchasi saiva devatā vismṛtā। stutibhājo'pi devatā
iti vadatā stutibhāji devatāyāṃ prakāśitāyāṃ na havirbhāk prakāśitā bhavati, devatābhāvabhedāt।
<q>puroḍāśe<note n="1">G.<dn>tvahavirbhāgād‍yuktam ।</dn></note>tvavibhāgād‍yuktam।</q> paśāvapi ivirbhāktayaiva
devatātvaṃ puroḍāśe'pi। tena tatra yuktaṃ puroḍāśayāgasya paśudevatāprakāśakatvam। iha punaḥ grahayajidevatāprakāśakatvaṃ (a)
stuteranupapannaṃ devatābhāvaprakārabhedāt। <q>tasmānnātra pūrvapakṣaṃ paśyāmaḥ</q> samādhatte---<q>aya-
﻿<pb n="r343"/>
<q>mevātra pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ stautiśaṃsatī stutyārthe iti। na cācikīrṣitaḥ stutyaḥ sak‍tuvat
---yāgasaṃbandhitvena</q> stutyasya। nanu nānena rūpeṇa dravyatyāga prati hetutā। kuto yāgasaṃbandhite-
tyāha---<q>abhidheyābhedāt</q>। indrādiśabdānāmabhidheyaṃ yadindrādisvarūpaṃ tat stutau yāge ca
na bhidyate devatābhāvaprakārabhede'pīti yāgasaṃbandhitā stutyasya। <q>na tu purojāśavaddevatā'bhe-
dāt</q> yāgasamvandhiteti brūmaḥ। yathā paśupuroḍāśayordevatābhāvaprakārabhedo nāsti।
tatheha nāsti। <q>tatra hi devatāpratyabhijñānamevābhipretam</q>। yenaiva rūpeṇa dravyatyāgaṃ pratyudde-
śyatayā paśāvagnīṣomayoḥ devatābhāvaḥ tenaiva puroḍāśe'pīti devatāpratyabhijñānam। tacca tatraiva
vakṣyāmaḥ। <q>atra tu abhidhānābhedamātreṇeva ajahatsvārthabṛttitvamupapadyata iti pūrva-
pakṣavādī manyate</q>। abhidhānābhedena svarūpasya buddhisthatvāt। yāgagatāpi tasyāvasthā smaryate
prayojanākāṅkṣāyāṃ ca stuteḥ tadeva prayojanaṃ bhaviṣyatīti। guṇaprakāśane tu mantravākyasya
tātparyamiti na stutirūpatāhāniḥ।</p>
﻿<pb n="r344"/>
<p><q>itarastu</q> rāddhāntekadeśī <q>codayati---yadyava māhendragrahayajeraindrī stutiḥ tatraikābhidhā-
nābhāvāt na cikīrṣitārthā syāt</q>। indramahendrābhidhānayorbhedāt। tataśca tatra niyogā-
viṣayatvam। tathā viṣayatvamevotkarṣaḥ kalpanīyaḥ syāt। na cāsau yuktaḥ। tasmānni-
yogaviṣayatvameva pūrvapakṣaikadeśī tāvat samarthayate---<q>notkarṣaḥ kalpanīyaḥ</q>। kuta ityāha
---<q>indra eva hi mahendraḥ</q>। kutaḥ ityāha---<q>abhinnārthābhidhānaṃ hi sāmānādhikaraṇya-
mucyate</q> mahendra iti mahacchabdasyendraśabdena saha sāmānādhikaraṇyam। ekārthābhidhānañca
sāmānādhikaraṇyam। tena ya evāsāvindraśabdārthaḥ sa eva mahacchabdasyāpīti indramahendrayoḥ
samānārthatvāt notkarṣaḥ kalpanīyaḥ। atra rāddhantaikadeśyāha---<q>nanu ca nīlotpalamiti
bhinnārthāvagateḥ kathamabhinnārthābhidhānam</q>। nahi utpalaśabdena kevalena yādṛśo'rthaḥ
pratyāyyate jātimātraṃ tādṛśa eva nīlotpalaśabdādapi pratīyate guṇādhikyāt। tataśca katha-
mabhinnārthābhidhāyitā। pūrvapakṣaikadeśyāha---<q>bhinnārthabhidhāne vā kathaṃ sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ</q> ?
saṃmānādhikaraṇasamāso'yamiti sarvavādināṃ sammatam। tatra yadyarthabhedaḥ kathaṃ sāmānā-
dhikaraṇyam ? artha eva hi śabdasyādhikaraṇamucyate। rāddhāntekadeśyāha---<q>utpalagata-
﻿<pb n="r345"/>
<q>guṇābhidhānāditi brūmaḥ। āgato'si tarhi madīyaṃ panthānam</q>। ekagranthenāha---pūrvapakṣai-
kadeśyāha---tatrotpale prayuktaḥ sa nīlaśabdaḥ <q>tadaguṇābhidhānasamartho bhavati</q>। anyathā hi
yasya kasyacid‍guṇaḥ pratyāyyeta viśeṣābhāvāt। astu tatra prayuktaḥ tathāpi kimityāha
---<q>yatraśabdaḥ prayujyate tamācaṣṭe</q>। prayogāyattatvādabhidhānasya। yata eva guṇavacanā api
nīlādiśabdāḥ guṇinyeva vartante। <q>ata eva guṇamabhidhāya guṇini vartante ye guṇa-
śabdāsta iha gṛhyante guṇavacanatayeti samāsapratiṣedhe</q> pūraṇaguṇetyatrokaṃ vyākhyātṛbhiḥ।
<q>tasmātsiddham</q> indramahendrayorekābhidhānatbam। yadi guṇinyeva prayogaḥ tadabhidhānañca
tadā guṇāvagatiḥ kathaṃ tatrāha---<q>guṇāvagatirhi vājinasthānīyā sāmānādhikaraṇye</q>।
﻿<pb n="r346"/>
yathā āmikṣārthe dadhyānayane'cikīrṣita vājinamapi niṣpadyate vastusvabhāvena tathā guṇāva-
gatirapi। na punaḥ sāpi kartumabhimatā। yata ekārthābhidhānatendramahendraśabdayoḥ।
<q>ataḥ cikīrṣitārthatvaṃ stuteraindyāḥ</q>। rāddhāntaikadeśī dūṣayati---<q>tadidamayuktam</q>। yasmā-
nnirasto'yamarthaḥ ananvito'pyavasīyata iti। asyārthaḥ। mahacchabdena tāvat
vṛddhavyavahārānusāreṇa mahatvamabhidhīyate। tena mahacchabdaprayoge tadeva pratīyate। pratīyamāne
cānenānvayimā bhavitavyam tena māhendragrahayajau saguṇasya devatātvāt na tasya indraśabda-
vācyatvam। nacedaṃ vācyam yadyapi mahacchabdena mahatvamucyate tathāpi tasya yāge anvayitā
na sambhavatīti। nirastatvādasyārthasya। anvitameva hyartha padamabhidhatta iti <q>tada‍bhūtādhi-
karaṇe</q> darśitam।</p>
<p>nanu rājapuruṣamānayetyādau rājña ānayane'nanvitasyāpi abhidhānamityāśaṅkyāha
