---<q>kāryetu kadācidanveti kadācinneti। avagatau punarna taṭasthaṃ<note n="1"><dn>pū. mī.1-1-25.</dn></note>padārthāvavodhanamityuktam</q>।
﻿<pb n="r347"/>
sarvathā tāvat padārthasyāvagatidaśāyāṃ anvitasyaivābhidhānam। na taṭasthasya। kāryāvasthāyāntu
kadācidanvayaḥ kadācinna। rājapuruṣādāvapi pratītyanvayitā rājño na śakyate'panhotum।
tenā<note n="1">G.<dn>tenānanvitasya</dn></note>nvitasyābhidhānamasiddham। punaḥ pūrvapakṣaikadeśyāha---<q>mābhūt padārthāvagatāvananvayaḥ। kārye punaruttarapadārthapradhānatvāt</q> asya samānādhikaraṇasamāsasyendra eva kāryabhāk, sa
eva kevalo devatetyarthaḥ। <q>anyathā hi</q> yadi punarupasarjanapadārthasyāpi kāryānvayitā
<q>tathāpyanupapannaiva śabdavidāṃ vāgiyam---ayaṃ pūrvapadārthapradhāno'yamuttarapadārthapradhāna iti</q>।
rāddhantaikadeśyāha---<q>kiñcijjño devānāṃ priyaḥ</q> kaścitsamāsaḥ pūrvapadārthapradhānaḥ kaściccottara-
padārthapradhāna ityetāvanmātraṃ bhavān jānāti, na punaryathā pradhānatā taṃ prakāram। kuta
ityāha---<q>samāso hi nāma parasparānugamapūrvakaṃ padārthāntarānugamanam। tatrāpi kadācit
﻿<pb n="r348"/>
<q>pūrvaṃ padamuttaraṃ padamanveti kadāciduttaraṃ pūrvam</q>। etadeva vivarītuṃ praśnamāha---<q>kimida-
manvetīti</q>। uttaram---<q>idamidaṃ idamāśrityāyaṃ padārtho'rthāntarānvayī bhavati iti</q> tatra ca
yamāśritya padārthāntarānvayitā sa pradhānabhūtaḥ yaścānyamāśrirityānvayī bhavati sa guṇabhūtaḥ। tena
yadyapi mahendraśabda uttarapadārthapradhānaḥ tathāpi mahacchabdasya kāryānvayitayā svārthābhidhāyakatvam।
tataśca māhendragrahayajane mahatvasyāpi devatābhāvenānvayaḥ। yadi paramuttarapadārtha pradhānabhūtamāśritya
tataḥ kiṃ ? uttaram---<q>tata idaṃ bhavati nānābhidhānataiva sthāsyati saguṇasyānvayāt</q>।
māhendragrahayajau mahendraśabdo'nyāṃ saguṇāṃ devatāmabhidhatte। aindrayāṃ tu stutau indraśabdo'nyāṃ
nirguṇāmiti। rāddhāntaikadeśī pūrvapakṣaikadeśino matamāśaṅkate---<q>atha mataṃ arthāntarasambandhaḥ
punaḥ arthāntareṇa kevala eva sambadhyata iti</q>। mahatvenārthāntareṇa saṃbandho yadyapi indraśabda-
syārthaḥ tathāpi kevala eva taddhitārthena saṃbadhyate। atha vā taddhitārthena kevalassambandhaḥ
﻿<pb n="r349"/>
paścānmahatvena। tena<note n="1">B. adds<dn>na</dn></note> saguṇasya devatātvenānvaya iti। dūṣayati---<q>uk‍taṃ <note n="2"><dn>samasthamānapadārthayorasamatttayo</dn></note>parasparānvaye
samāsaḥ tato'rthāntarānvayaḥ</q>। yatraiva parasparasaṃbaddhayoreva samasyāmānārthayorarthāntarasambandhaḥ tatraiva
samāsa ityuktam। tasmānnārthāntarāpekṣasyārthāntarasaṃbandhasya pūrvaṃ paścātsamāsaḥ<note n="3">G.
<dn>paścānna samāsaḥ</dn></note>। nāpi samastasya pūrva
paścāt kevalasyārthāntarasaṃbandha iti। ataḥ saguṇādevatā kevalenendraśabdena na śakyāgidhātumityu-
tkarṣaḥ prāpnoti। pūrvapakṣaikadeśyāha---<q>bhavati vai pradhānasya sāpekṣasyāpi samāsa iti samāsavidāṃ
giraḥ śrūyante</q>। tathāpi kimityāha---<q>pradhānaṃ cendrārthaḥ। ato dravyasaṃbandhasyāpīndrasya
﻿<pb n="r350"/>
<q>mahattvena saṃbandha upapadyate</q>। taddhitārthasaṃbandhasyāpi mahacchabdena samāso bhaviṣyati। tataśca
kevalasya taddhitārthasaṃbandhānnirguṇā devatā bhavitviti। rāddhāntaikadeśī dūṣayati---<q>na samyaga---
vadhṛtaṃ bhavatā samāsavidvacaḥ</q>। kastasyārtho vacasa ityatrāha---<q>padārthāntarasaṃvandhapradhānasya
samastasyāpi samāso niruṇadvīti tasyārthaḥ</q>। na punaḥ samāsapadanirapekṣasyārthāntarasaṃbandha
iti। yathā kila samastasyāpradhānapadārthasyārthāntareṇa saṃbandho na bhavati ṛddhasya rājapuruṣa iti
na tathā pradhānasya bhavati rājapuruṣaḥ śobhana iti। pradhānapadārthasyāpi yaḥ padārthāntarasaṃbandhaḥ
nāsau padārthāntaranirapekṣaḥ। na ca śobhanatā puruṣasaṃbandhinī pratīyate। api tu rājīya-
puruṣasaṃbandhinī tadrītyā atrāpi bhavatvindrasya taddhitārthasaṃbandhaḥ na tvasau nirapekṣaḥ iti saguṇaiva
devatā। pūrvapakṣaikadeśyāha---<q>nanu cāsamarthasamāsā api vyākhyātṛbhiruditāḥ</q>। tena yadyapi
mahatvasyendraśabdena saha saṃbandho nāsti tathāpi samāso bhavivyati iti mahatvanirapekṣaiva devatā'ntu।
rāddhāntaikadeśyāha---<q>satyamuditaḥ yatraiva</q> tatraiva te bhavantu। <q>atra punaḥ samarthaḥ padavidhiritye-
tadeva nyāyyam। asāmarthyasyādarśanāt</q>। yatra hi pramāṇāntareṇāsāmarthya pratīyate
samāsaśca tatrāsamarthrasamāsaḥ iha punarasāmarthyasya pramāṇaṃ nāsti। tena samarthasamāsa evāyam।


﻿<pb n="r351"/>
pūrvapakṣaikadeśyāha---<q>nanu cedamevāsāmarthyaṃ māhendro grahayajiḥ aindrī stutiriti। evañcā-
jahatsvārthatopapannā</q>। cikīrṣitārthatve bhavatīti। yadyayaṃ samarthasamāsaḥ syāt tadā
cikīrṣitārthatvaṃ na bhavati stutisvabhāvena stutyarthatā pratibhāti। tena sa yathā nirvahati
tathā''śrayaṇīyamityasamarthasamāso'yamityasti pramāṇāntaram। rāddhāntaikadeśyāha---<q>eva-
mitaretarāśrayaṃ prāptoti। cikīrṣitārthatvena mahendrasyāsāmarthya asāmarthye cikīrṣitārtha-
tvam</q>। asamarthasamāse niścite anayā stutyā mahendrasya cikīrṣitārthatvaṃ mahendrasya
cikīrṣitārthatve'samarthasamāso'yamityastītaretarāśrayatvam। <q>itaretarāśrayaṇāṇi vastūni</q>
﻿<pb n="r352"/>
śāstreṇa na prakalpyanta <q>ityuk‍tam</q>। pūrvapakṣaikadeśyāha---<q>yadyevamasamarthasamāso'pi
na prāpnoti prādhānye bhāvārthasya sāmarthyaṃ</q> samarthasamāsaniścaye <q>sāmarthye ca prādhānyamiti</q>।
rāddhāntaikadeśyāha---<q>maivam। abhidhānataḥ sāmarthyāvagateḥ</q>। sāmarthyaṃ parasparasaṃbandhaḥ।
sa cābhidhānata evāvagamyate। <q>tasmāt saguṇaiva devatā</q>। yuk‍tyantaraṃ cāha---<q>avaśyaṃ caitade-
vamabhyuyagantavyam</q> saguṇaiva devateti। <q>anyathā</q> hi guṇavacanamaniyogasaṃsparśi-
syāditi। <q>na ca saṃbhavantyāṃ gatau tadyuk‍tam। tasmādutkarṣa eva prāptoti। evaṃ nirākṛte
pūrvapakṣaikadeśini paramapūrvapakṣyāha---<q>bhavatu tarhya‍ut‍karṣaḥ naitāvatā cikīrṣitārthaḥ śakyate tyak‍tum</q>।

﻿<pb n="r353"/>
nanutkarṣa evāpramāṇakaḥ paramapūrvaviṣayatvamevetyatrāha<note n="1"><dn>tyāha</dn></note>---<q>atantre hi kramasannidhī (vivakṣite)</q> vipakṣabhūte sāmarthye। sthānaprakaraṇayoḥ sāmarthyarūpālliṅgato durbalatvāddhetoryatra sāmarthya-
kalpitaṃ na kārya tatrotkarṣo yuk‍taḥ। stuterhi stutyapratipādanaṃ liṅgena kāryamupagamyate।
samākhyā ca sāmānyasaṃbandhupratipādikā<note n="2">B.<dn>sāmānyaprati</dn></note> bhaviṣyatīti na doṣaḥ। <q>nanūtkarṣe bahūnāṃ niṣprayoja-natā prāpnoti maṇḍūkasūk‍tādīnām</q>। pariharati---<q>na niṣprayojanatā। yasya yatra karmaṇyarthaḥ<note n="3">G.<dn>sa na tatra</dn></note>sa tatra yātīti darśitaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa। kathaṃ punarvācastome āśvine ca sāmarthyaṃ bhinnārthānāṃ</q> sūk‍tānāṃ ? pariharati---<q>vacanādekārthatā</q> prāpnoti
<q>aindrīvat</q>। yathaindrī ṛk vacanāt gārhapatye viniyuk‍tā satī gauṇyā lākṣaṇik‍yā vā vṛttyā pratipādikā bhavati। tathā'trāpītyadoṣaḥ।</p>
<p><q>api vā।। apa stautiśaṃsatī cikīrṣitārthau na bhavataḥ</q>। kasmāt ?
﻿<pb n="r354"/>
uttaraṃ---devatāyā apratyabhijñānāt। na devatābhāvaprakāraḥ pratyabhijñāyate yataḥ। anyathā hi
yāge devatābhāvaḥ anyathā ca stutau। yadyapi stutau stutyaprakāśanamapyasti tathāpi yāgīya-
pratyabhijñānābhāvānna tādarthya stuteravagamyate। <q>nanvabhidhānataḥ pratyabhijñānamuditam</q>। pariharati
---<q>tadayuk‍tamuk‍tam</q>। kuta ityāha---<note n="1">G. adds<dn>tarhi</dn></note><q>yatra hi pramāṇāntareṇa pratyabhijñānamasti tade-vedamiti <note n="2">G.<dn>tenābhidhānaṃ ca tadādānāyālaṃ</dn></note>tatrābhidhānaṃ na bhedāyālaṃ bhavati। tathā ca darśitam---vaśāyāmarthasamavāyāditi yatra punarabhidhānādeva pratyabhijñānaṃ tatra yāgānvayī stutyanvayīti na </q> śakyate <note n="3">R.<dn>vakm‍tu</dn></note>pratipattum। asyārthaḥ। abhidhānaṃ pratyabhijñāne kāraṇaṃ yadi hi tathā <note n="4">G.<dn>tathārthajñānāmapi</dn></note>syāt। yatrāpi pramāṇāntareṇa tadevedamiti niścayaḥ tatrāpyabhidhānabhedāt bhedaḥ syāt। na caitadasti। yatra punarabhidhāna-meva pratyabhijñākāraṇaṃ tatra pratyabhijñā nāsti। na hi yāgānvayī yaḥ sa eva stutyanvayīti
śakyate vak‍tum। nanu cānanvitena sādhāraṇena rūpeṇabhidhānāt bhaviṣyati pratyabhijñānamiti
﻿<pb n="r355"/>
<q>atrāha---na cānanvayino'bhidhānamasti iti tatra tatrok‍tam। tasmāt</q> pratyabhijñā'bhāvāt
<q>na cikīrṣitārthatvaṃ stauteḥ śaṃsateśca। ato niyogaviṣayataivāvasīyate</q>। yata eva ceyaṃ
mulyuk‍tirasti <q>ata evāmī bhāṣyakāreṇa śrutisaṃyogā darśiṃtāḥ stuteḥ prādhānyāvagama-
hetavaḥ</q>। yaiḥ stutau niyogaviṣayatvamavagamyate te śrutisaṃyogā darśitāḥ। kathaṃ punaḥ
saptamīśrutisaṃyoge prādhānyaṃ aprādhānyaṃ kuto na syāt ityāha---<q>saptamīśrutisaṃyogo
'bhidhāne'pi tulyaḥ</q>। kavatīṣu stuvata iti saptamīśrutiḥ devatābhidhāne'pi tulyā। ato
na siddhāntasiddhaye samarthā। uttaraṃ---<q>na, abhidhānasya parārthatvāt। abhidheyabhāvasthaṃ
hyabhidhānaṃ</q> abhidheyo yo bhāvaḥ tasminnabhidhānaṃ sthitaṃ tadviṣayamityarthaḥ। <q>stutau punaḥ stutyārthe

﻿<pb n="r356"/>
stavanaṃ tacca stutyaṃ kavatīṣveva nānyatra। pramāṇāntarānavagamāt</q>। yathā'bhidheyaṃ
pramāṇāntarabhūtayāgacodanayā'vagamyate, na tathā stutyaṃ kavatīvyatirekeṇānyatra। evañca
<q>kavatīṣu stuvata iti yuk‍tam</q>। nanu vivakṣāvaśenābhidhānapakṣe'pi kavatīnāmadhikaraṇanirdeśo
bhaviṣyati। tatrāha---<q>na cātra puruṣavaśādvivakṣātaḥ kārakābhidhānaṃ śakyate</q>। puruṣasya
vivakṣiturabhāvāt। kathaṃ tarhi ? <q>abhidhānata eva</q> yādṛśamevābhidhānaṃ tādṛśamevābhidheyam।
na devatābhidhānāpekṣayā vibhak‍tyantaraṃ prayuktam। <q>taccābhidhānaṃ kavatīsthamityuktam</q> tena
yujyate saptamīśrutisaṃyogaḥ siddhānte। pūrvapakṣe tu tṛtīyā syāt। <q>tathā dvitīyāśruti-
saṃyogaḥ prādhānyaṃ</q> pradhānakarmatvamutsargāt gamayati। <q>anyato hi guṇabhāvo vak‍tavyaḥ</q>।
tena praugaṃ śaṃsatīti dvitīyāśrutisaṃyogāt pradhānakarmatayā'dhyavasānam<note n="1">G.<dn>abhidhānam</dn></note>। <q>tathā indrasya nu vīryāṇīti</q> ṣaṣṭhīśrutisaṃyogo'bhidhāne indrābhidhāne abhidhānasya <q>paryavasānaṃ nāstīti kathayati</q>
﻿<pb n="r357"/>
pratipadikārthamātre prathameti prathamāsaṃyogāt। nanu yatra prathamā tatra tarhi bhavatu devatā-
prādhānyaṃ tatrāha---<q>prathamā punarliḍādyabhihite padārtha upapadyate</q> lakāreṇa yadā hyarthaḥ pratipādyate
tadapekṣayāpi prathamopapadyate abhihite karmaṇi kartari vā prathamopapadyata ityarthaḥ। [a]-
<q>jahatsvārthatā ca stuteḥ prāpnoti। stutyābhidhānāt</q> devatābhidhānarūpāpatteriti <q>pradarśitam</q>।
bhāṣye śabdapṛthak‍tvāt iti vyākhyeyānubhāṣaṇam। vyākhyānamāha---<q>śāstrapṛthak‍tvaṃ ca darśayati</q>
dvādaśastotraśastro'gniṣṭomaḥ। tacca śāstrapṛthak‍tvaṃ <q>viṣayabhūte bhāvārthe</q> upapadyate
<q>na guṇabhūte niyogaśūnyatvāditi pradarśitam</q>। anubandhabhedena hi śāstrabhedo bhavati।
niyogaviṣayabhāvaścānubandhatvam। yatra ca niyogo'sti tatra niyogaviṣayatvam। na ca
guṇakarmasu niyogo'stīti darśitaṃ <q>tāni dvaidhamityatra। niyogaśūnyatvaṃ ca tṛtīye vakṣyāma
﻿<pb n="r358"/>
<q>ityapyuk‍tam। kiñcāgniṣ‍ṭuti āgneyīvidhānāt pradhānārthataivāvagamyate</q>। kuta ityāha
---guṇapakṣe hi kāryata eva prāpnoti। āgneyatvād‍grahāṇāmāgneyya evarcaḥ syuḥ kāryeṇohasya
prāptatvāt। <q>anyaścārthaḥ pratīyata iti</q> vyākhyeyānubhāṣaṇam। etadākṣipati---<q>anenāpi
śāstrabheda eva kathyate</q>। tena śāstrapṛthak‍tvādityanena paunaruk‍tyam। pariharati---<q>iyān
viśeṣaḥ pūryatra svato bhedaḥ</q> dvādaśasaṅkhayāśravaṇāt। <q>iha tu saṃbandhopādhikaḥ</q> saṃbaddhe
vai stotraśastre iti saṃbandhaṃ vadan bhedaṃ darśayati। yadyekatvaṃ na saṃbandha upapadyata ityarthāt
bheddaḥ। <q>pradhānakarmavadabhidhānamiti</q> vyākhyeyānubhāṣaṇam। tadeva vyācaṣṭe---<q>pradhānasyocitaṃ

﻿<pb n="r359"/>
nāmeti। kutaḥ</q> ? uttaraṃ---<q>bhedāvagamāt</q>। pradhānapakṣe bhedo'vagamyate। <q>guṇa-
karmaṇāṃ tu bhedo nāstīti somaṃ krīṇātītyatra darśayiṣyāmaḥ</q> dvādaśe krayāṇāṃ samuccayaṃ varṇayi-
ttum। tathāpi kimityāha---<q>bhedānupāti ca nāma</q>। bhinnā hi saṃjñā saṃjñinorbhede satyucitā।
<q>tasmādanucitaṃ bhinnaṃ nāma guṇakarmaṇāṃ<note n="1"><dn>guṇakarmaṇī</dn></note> phalanirvṛttiṃ ca karmaṇaḥ
sakāśāddarśayati</q>---stutasya stutamasītyādinā। <q>na punaḥ cikīrṣitādvastunaḥ</q>। atha na kasmāccikīrṣitādityāha
<q>devatātaḥ</q>। guṇakarmapakṣe na karma phalāntarayogyaṃ kintu yadetat cikīrṣyate tata eva phala-
mucitam। <q>tasmādacikīrṣitārthatvaṃ siddham। prayojanamanyatretyuk‍taṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa।</q>
daśame prayojanaṃ sūtropanibandhanaṃ tatra saṅgatatvāditi।</p>
﻿<pb n="r360"/>
<p><q>vidhiḥ</q>। kiṃ yadvat brāhmaṇeṣu gataḥ bhāvaśabdo vidhāyakaḥ tadvanmantre'pi, uta
mantre'<note n="1">G.<dn>'bhidhāyaka</dn></note>vidhāyaka iti bhāṣyamanubhāṣyākṣipati-<q>kimidamupanyastam</q> ?
samādhātā āha---<q>nanu na śrutaṃ bhavatā yadupanyastaṃ</q> yenaivaṃ pṛcchasi। ākṣeptā āha---<q>satyaṃ śrutaṃ kintu asaṃbaddha-
miva pratibhāti</q>। samādhātā āha---<q>kathamasaṃbaddham</q> ? ākṣeptā āha---<q>viniyuk‍to
hi mantra iti sthitam</q>। asyārthaḥ---yasya mantrasya viniyogo nāsti vasantāya kapiñjalānāla-
meta ityādeḥ so'trodāharaṇaṃ na bhavati। kintu yo viniyuktaḥ। tathāpi kimityāha---<q>prayoga-
samavāyī ca mantraḥ smaraṇenopayujyata iti sthitam</q>। yo hi mantro viniyuk‍taḥ sa karma-
ṇyaṅgīkṛtaḥ prayogakāle smaraṇenopayujyata iti। <q>ataḥ kā'tra vidhāyakāśaṅkā</q>। na hi
smārakasya vidhāyakatvāśaṅkā। ākṣeptā samādhāturāśaṅkāntaramāha---<q>atha manyase niyogaśabda-
﻿<pb n="r361"/>
śravaṇāt</q> liṅādiśravaṇāt <q>bhavatyāśaṅketi</q>। dūṣayati---<q>tadapi nirākṛtam</q>।
satyapi niyogaśravaṇe <q>paurṇamāsīṃ yajata iti ekārthatāvagamāt</q>। yathā tatraikārthāva-
gamādvivāyakatvaṃ na bhavati tathā'trāpīti yuk‍tamityarthaḥ। samādhātā āha
---<q>evaṃ tarhyekārthatayaivā'tra vidhāyakatāśaṅkā</q>। etadeva vivṛṇoti---<q>brāhmaṇa-
pratipāditamarthaṃ</q> mantro'bhidhatta iti। ato'bhinnārthatā mantrabrāhmaṇayoḥ। <q>abhinnasya
cārthasya vidhānamabhidhānaṃ ca na saṃbhavatīti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ</q>। yathā vidheyatayā so'rtho brāhmaṇe
pratīyate tathā mantre'pi vidhāyakatayaiva pratyetavyaḥ ekārthatvāt। tathā brāhmaṇavanmantra-
syāpīti vidhāyakatvameveti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ। abhyuccayamāha---<q>arthataścaikatvaṃ nānātvaṃ vā śabdānām
yadaikārthatvaṃ tadaikaśabdatvamupapadyate। arthabhede tu śabdabheda eva yuk‍taḥ। ekaścāyaṃ liṅgādi-
śabdaḥ tenātrāpi eka eva yuk‍taḥ। <q>nanu caivamabhidhāyakatvaṃ hīyate mantrāṇāṃ samidādī-
nāmiva parasparam</q> yathā samidho yajatīti pratyabhyāsamarthabhedaḥ tathā'trāpi vidhāyakatvapakṣe'rthabhedena
bhavitavyam। tataśca yatrārthe mantraviniyogo mantrasya tadabhidhāyakatvameva hīyate।
﻿<pb n="r362"/>
tathā ca sati viniyogavirodhaśca āpadyata iti। ucyate। nābhidhāyakatvaṃ hīyate।
<q>tannimittatvāt</q> <note n="1">B.<dn>abhidhāyakanimi</dn></note>abhidhāyakatvanimittatvādvidheḥ nimittaṃ vidhirna bādhata ityuk‍taṃ śabda-nyāyavidbhiḥ। ata siddhamaviśeṣāt</q> dvayormantrabrāhmaṇayorvidhāyakatvam।</p>
<p><q>apivā। ucyate---abhidhāyakatayā hyekārthatvaṃ mantrasya pratipattavyam</q>। vini-
yogaparyālocanayā mantrasyābhidhāyakatvena brāhmaṇena sahaikārthatvaṃ pratipannam। nanu bhavatvabhidhāya-
katvaṃ tathāpi vidheyatayā'bhidhāyakatvena vidhāyakatvamevāstviti matbā pṛcchati---<q>kasyābhidhāya-
katayaikārthatvaṃ</q> ? kiṃ vidheyasyābhidhāyakatayā ? rāddhāntī vadati---vihitasyābhidhāyakatayā
brāhmaṇenaikārthyaṃ mantrāṇām। yad‍brāhmaṇena bihitaṃ tadabhidhāyakatayā viniyogāvagamācca।
na ca vihitābhidhāne vidhānaṃ pratipat‍tuṃ śakyate vihitasya vidhānāsaṃbhavāt। kasmāt
punarvihitasyaivābhidhāyakatā ? yāvatā vidheyatvenaiva kimiti na bhavati। tataśca
mantreṇa vidhānameva tasyārthasyetyatrāha---<q>vidhāne hi karmāntarāpattirvidhibalādāpadyate</q> vidhā-
﻿<pb n="r363"/>
nasya vihitādbhedakalpakatvāt। <q>karmāntaratve<note n="1">B.<dn>ca</dn></note>vā'<note n="2">G. omits<dn>na</dn></note>nabhidhāyakatvaṃ khamidādīnāmiva para-sparam। tataśca viniyogaśruterbādhaḥ</q>। ayamabhiprāyaḥ। ekārthaṃ
tāvat viniyogavaśena pratīyate। tatra yadi vidheyatvenocyeta tadā ekārthatbameva bādhyate। tasmāt
bihitatayaivābhidhānenaikārthatvamāśrayituṃ yuk‍tamavirodhaāt। bhavatu viniyogaśruterbādho vidheya-
tvenābhidhānamiti <q>cet</q>। dṛṣayati---<q>na</q> yuk‍to viniyugaśruterbādhaḥ vihitābhidhāyakatayā
niyogārthasaṃsparśasiddheḥ। yadi hi mantrāṇāṃ vihitasmārakatāyāṃ bhiyogasparśoṃ na siddhayet
tadā vidheyābhidhāyakatāmāśritya viniyogaśruterbādha āśrīyeta। upapadyate vihitasmārakatayāpya-
dhikārasaṃsparśaḥ। <q>tasmānna niyogāntaramarhati</q>। na ca vidheyatvābhidhānapakṣe'pyarthavādo<note n="3">G.
<dn>arthabhedo</dn></note> na bhaviṣyatyekārthatvādvidheriti śakyate vak‍tuṃ vidhisvabhāvavirodhāt। tasmādvidhisvabhāvāvirodhāya
vihitatvenaivābhidhānamāśrayituṃ yuk‍tam। na tu vidheyavihitābhidhāyakayoḥ mantrabrāhmaṇayoḥ
arthabhedaḥ smṛtipramāṇayorivāvasthāmātrabhedāt। <quote>“stutyarthatāyāmapyānarthakyaṃ”</quote> iti bhāpyamanu-
bhāṣyākṣipati---<q>keyamakāṇḍe'prastāve stutyarthatāśaṅkā</q> pūrvapakṣiṇo vidhāyakatvamabhimatam।
tasyeyaṃ stutyarthatā''śaṅkā nopapadyate। uttaraṃ---<q>ucyate stutāvapi hi vihitābhidhānaṃ
﻿<pb n="r364"/>
<p><q>dṛṣṭam</q>। yathā vāyavyaṃ śvetamālameta iti vihitasya vāyorabhidhānam। etaduk‍taṃ bhavati।
rāddhāntābhāsinaṃ kasyacidiyaṃ stutyarthatāśaṅkā bhavati vihitābhidhānaṃ yadi mantre kriyate tadā
stutyarthatāpi kimiti na bhavati। nanu stutyarthatā bhavatu na kāpi kṣātiḥ ataḥ kimiti
nirākriyate iti manvānaḥ pṛcchati---<q>tataḥ kimiti</q>। uttaraṃ---<q>ekavākyatāyāmevaita---
dupapannaṃ bihitābhidhānaṃ nāma na vāk‍bhede</q>। yatstutau vihitābhidhānaṃ nāma tadeka-
vākyatāyāmevopapannam, na vākyabhede। <q>abhinnaṃ ca vighivākyanmantravākyam।
tasmādabhidhāyakatvaṃ duśśakamupapādayitum। atrāyaṃ bhāvaḥ---yadi stutaye vihitābhi-
dhānamiti pakṣaḥ svīkriyate tadā vihitābhidhānalakṣaṇo rāddhānta eva na siddhayet।
ekavākyatve hi stutaye vihitābhidhānaṃ na bhinnavākyatve। spaṣṭaśca vidhi-
mantrayorvākyabhedaḥ। tataśca vihitābhidhānameva bhajyeta। vidhāyakatvamevopapadyeteti।
<q>nanu viniyogena vihitābhidhāyakatvaṃ</q> stutaye bhaviṣyati। pariharati---<q>ucyate, aidamarthye hi
biniyogasya prabhaviṣṇutā nedaṃ kāryatve</q> viniyogena hyasyātra śeṣabhāva ityetāvanmātra
pratipādyate na punaḥ stutirasya kāryamiti śakyate kalpayitum। upādānenāpi śakyameva
kāryamupādīyate na punaraśakyam। bhinnavākye ca stutirūpaṃ kāryamaśakyam। ato rāddhānta-
siddhayarthaṃ stutaye vihitabhidhānamiti rāddhāntābhāsanirākaraṇam। kaḥ punaḥ nirākaraṇe
﻿<pb n="r365"/>
heturityāha---<q>satyam। stutāvapi yatra padanivandhanamekārthatvaṃ tatra śrutyaiva</q> vihitābhidhānam।
yathā vāyurvai kṣepiṣṭheti। <q>iha punarupādānanaḥ</q> ekārthatvam। grāhakalakṣaṇena vidhivyāpāreṇa
svīkṛte mantre brāhmaṇena sahaikavākyatvam। <q>tasmānna stutiḥ saṃbhavati padanibandhanottarakāla-
bhāvitvāt</q>। idaṃ cākṛtaṃ vidhiśeṣabhūtā stutirbhavati iti। yacca bhinnena brāhmaṇavākyena
vihitaṃ tatra stutirarthavatī। tasmānna stutyarthatayā vihitābhidhānam। kintu smṛtyarthatayā।
adhikaraṇārthamupasaṃharati---<q>ato bhinnavākyānāmapi bhavati vihitābhidhāyakatvam। idaṃ
kāyatve hya‍upādānaṃ prabhavati</q>। grāhakeṇa gṛhītasya mantrasya svato'bhidhānasamarthasya
prayogakālāpekṣitārthābhidhānameva kāryaṃ kalpyate grāhakagrahaṇabalenaiva। <q>tasmāt siddhaṃ vihitā-
bhidhānaṃ mantrāṇāṃ kāryam</q>।</p>
<p><q>taccodakeṣu। <quote>‘uk‍t‍taṃ mantragato bhāvaśabdo'bhidhāyaka iti ’</quote></q> bhāṣyamanubhāṣyākṣi-
pati---<q>abhidhāyako'yaṃ na vidhāyaka ityetāvadvak‍tavyam</q>। viniyuk‍tavākyagato bhāvaśabdo'bhi-

﻿<pb n="r366"/>
dhāyako na vidhāyaka ityetāvadvak‍tavyam । <q>kiṃ mantraśabdena ।</q> yadyapi mantraśabdastatra na bhavati
tathāpi rāddhānto labhyata eva । viniyuk‍tatvaṃ hyabhidhāyakat‍ve hetuḥ । na ca viniyogo'pi
 <q>mantraśabdābhidheyatayā । kathaṃ tarhi ? iṣetvetyevamādibhiḥ pratīkaiḥ । tasmānmantraśabdābhidhā-
namatiricyate</q> na cābhidhāyakatvasiddhayarthameva mantraśabdābhidhānam । <q>yataḥ kiyamāṃṇe'pi
mantraśabdābhidhāne na mantratvādabhidhāyakatvaṃ bhavati । vidhāyakatvamapi mantreṣu vasantayā
kāpiñjalānālabhata ityebamādiṣu dṛṣṭam । yadapi bhāṣyakāreṇocyate ajñāte mantre kathaṃ tadgataḥ
bhāvaśabdo vicāryo bhaviṣyati iti । idamarthato'dhikaraṇaṃ pūrvaṃ draṣṭavyamiti । etadapyayukta-
mevok‍tamiti ।</q> kuta ityāha-<q>na mantratvādevābhidhāyakatvam । ki tarhi ? viniyuk‍tatvāditi ।</q>
tenājñāte'pi mantratve śak‍yata evābhidhāyakatvamupapādayituṃ <q>viniyogaśca pratīkādibhiriti ।</q>
<note n="(1)">B. <dn>kiṃ tarhi</dn></note>﻿<pb n="r367"/>
tatrāpi mantratvamanupayogi। ākṣepāntaramāha---<q>anyathāpi cāyaṃ sūtrārtho gacchatyeva।
mantraśabdo'pyabhidhāyakeṣu prayuk‍taḥ pūrvasminnadhikaraṇe sūtre tadvayākhyānārthaṃ sūtraṃ abhi-
dhākeṣu kiṃ mantraśabdābhidhānamasti। bāḍhamasti। taccodakeṣu mantraśabdamabhiyuk‍tāḥ
prayujjate। evaṃ ca prāyikametadityetadapi na vak‍tavyam yasmāt mantrābhidhānaprasiddhi-
kathanārthametatsūtraṃ na mantralakṣaṇārtham</q>। lakṣaṇārthatve hi prāyikatvakathanamupapadyate, nābhi-
dhānaprasiddhikathane। yasmādidaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ na bhavati tasmāllakṣaṇena tu siddhānāmityevamā-
dyasamañjasam। ato'vyāpitālakṣaṇadoṣakathanena svakauśalapradarśanārthaṃ lakṣaṇa-
sūtratvamadhyāropyate। atrābhidhīyate। bhāṣyakārasyāpi pūrvok‍tamantraśabdavyākhyānametaditi
sammatamabhiyuk‍tā upadiśanti। mantrā āvartanta ityevaṃ vadatā</q> bhāṣyakāreṇāpyabhiyuk‍ta-
﻿<pb n="r368"/>
kathanārthaṃ sūtramityuk‍tam। <q>padārthakathanaparaṃ caitat bhāṣyamevañjātīyakeṣvabhiyuk‍tā upadi-
śantītyādi। ato yadanyattallakṣaṇadūṣaṇaparamevaitat</q>। ye ca lakṣaṇaparamevaitatsūtramiti
manyante tanmataṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa dūṣyate। <q>prāyikamityanena prakaṭimetat। ata eta
vṛttikāreṇodāharaṇaprapañcok‍tirapi na mṛṣyate bhāṣyakāreṇa। lakṣaṇābhidhānapakṣe
hi lakṣaṇaviśeṣābhidhānamupapadyetāpi। padārthavyākhyāne punaranavasara eva tallakṣaṇa-
viśeṣābhidhānasya</q> vṛttikārakṛtasya। taccedaṃ vṛttikāreṇodāharaṇāpadeśena iti vadatā
vṛttikārakṛtalakṣaṇaviśeṣasyāsaṃbaddhataiva kathitā। <q>tasmānmantrapadasya prayogakathanaparametat
sūtraṃ na mantralakṣaṇaparam</q>।</p>
﻿<pb n="r369"/>﻿<pb n="r370"/>
<p><q>śeṣe । taccodakeṣu mantrākhyeti mantraśabdārthakathanapare sūtre kaḥ prasaṅgaḥ śeṣe brāhmaṇa-
śabda</q> iti । asya <q>lakṣaṇapare</q> tu sūtre prasaṅgādapyupapadyate eva brāhmaṇalakṣaṇam । ekagranthenāha
&mdash;<q>lakṣaṇapare'pyuk‍to doṣaḥ</q> pūrvamate <q>na vidmaḥ kathamidamiti । atrocyate । śabdārtha-
kathanaparamevaitatsūtradvayam ।</q> etadeva vivṛṇoti&mdash;<q>vidhimantrayoraikārthyamiti । kimidaṃ﻿<pb n="r371"/>
vidhimantrāvityevamāśaṅakyate ?</q> tatredamuttaraṃ&mdash;<q>asti dvayaṃ vede । kecinmantrāḥ kiñcit
vrāhmaṇaṃ iti । yatrābhiyuk‍tā mantraśabdaṃ prayuñjate sa mantraḥ । yatra ca vidhiriti
vruvate taddrāhyaṇam । bṛttikāramatasya yo'yamupanyāsaḥ saḥ pūrvavad draṣṭavyaḥ</q> asaṃbaddha
ityarthaḥ ।</p>﻿<pb n="r372"/>
<p><q>anāmnāteṣu । ūhapravaranāmadheyāni cintyante-kiṃ mantraśabdābhidheyāni ? uta neti ।</q>
anenākṣep‍tuṃ sandeho'nubhāṣitaḥ । ākṣipati&mdash;<q>nanu taccodakeṣu mantrākhyetyanena yatrābhiyuk‍tāḥ
mantraśabdaṃ prayuñjate sa mantra ityuk‍tam । na cābhidhāyakatvaṃ mantratve lakṣaṇam ।</q> yenohādī-
nāmapi mantratvaṃ syāt । <q>nacohādīnyabhiyuk‍taiḥ mantratvenābhilapyante । tasmādanupapannaḥ
saṃśayaḥ । atrābhidhīyate । ūhapravaranāmadheyairhi kratuṣu mantrakāryaṃ kriyate । nacāmantraiḥ mantra-
kāryaṃ niṣpadyata iti pūryapakṣavādino'bhiprāyaḥ ।</q> mantrakāryakāritvādeṣāṃ valāt mantratvamabhyupa-
gamanīyam । anyathā tatkāryānupapatteḥ । <q>rāddhāntavādī tu manyate satyaṃ, amantraiḥ
mantrakāryaṃ na bhavati । na punaḥ amantrānugṛhītaiḥ ।</q> ya eba mantrāḥ ta eva mantrakāryaṃ kurvanti ।
amantrāstu teṣāmanugrahaṃ kurvanti । na cāmantrānugṛhītatvena mantrāṇāmapyamantratā । nanṛhapravarā-
dīnyevārthābhidhānaṃ kurvanti na punarmantrānugrahaṃ ityatrāha&mdash;<q>ūhapravaranāmadheyāni ca mantrāṇā-﻿<pb n="r373"/>
mupakāraṃ kurvanti santyanugrāhakāṇi prayat‍nakaraṇādivat । tasmādamantratvamūhādīnām ।
na cānugrāhakaṃ mantrābhilapyaṃ prayat‍nakaraṇamiva । tasmādamantratva</q>mūhādīnām । <q>kaḥ punare-
bhiranugrahaḥ ? yathaiva tāl‍vādibhirarthābhidhāne sāhāyyam ।</q> yathā tāl‍vādīnyapya-
bhivyañjakāni santi arthābhidhāne sāhāyyaṃ kurvanti tathohādīnyapi । <q>nanu coha-
pravaranāmadheyāni svayamabhidhānaṃ kurvate na sāhāyyaṃ</q> tāl‍vādikamiva । ataḥ kathamanugrāha-
katvam । pariharati&mdash;<q>na khal‍vatra kaścidviśeṣaḥ ।</q> kecidanugrāhakā <q>api pradhānakārye upa-
kurvanti । kecidaṅgakāryam । yathā svāmisaṃskārāḥ prayājādayaśca । tasmādupapanna-
mamantratvaṃ</q>, abhidhāyakatve'pi mantrānugrāhakatvena svayaṃ mantrakāryakaratvābhāvāt । <q>sbāmi-
saṃskārāṇāmiva na prādhānyaṃ</q> yathā kārye anugrāhakā api svāmisaṃskārā na pradhānaṃ,
tathohādayo'pi । <q>prayojanaṃ bhāṣyok‍taṃ</q> mantratipattau yatprāyaścitaṃ tat amantre na
bhavatīti ।</p>﻿<pb n="r374"/>
<p><q>teṣām ।। kena prasaṅgenedamāyātam ? uttaraṃ&mdash;anenedamāyātam । mantrabrāhmaṇaśabdayoḥ
vedābhidheyasyārthasya vācyatayā niyama uk‍taḥ ṛgādidiśabdaiścasa vyavahāro dṛśyate vedaśabdā-
bhidheya evārtha ṛco yajūṃṣi sāmānītyagyajussāmaśabdairabhidadhāti</q> vedaśabdavācyamevārtham ।
tatrāśaṅkeyamāpadyate । atha ko bhāga ṛkśabdenocyate । <q>ko vā yajuśabdena, ko vā
sāmaśabdeneti tatra ṛkśabdābhidheyapradarśanārthamidamāravdham ।</q> prasaṅgāt saṅgatirityarthaḥ ।﻿<pb n="r375"/>
yatra pādavyavasthā sa ṛk‍śabdābhidheyo'rtha iti nirūpitam । arthagrahaṇaṃ cānuvāda ityuk‍taṃ
bhāṣyakāreṇa ।</q> tena vṛttavaśenāpi yatra pādavyavasthā sā ṛk । <q>kaḥ punarayaṃ pādo nāma ?</q>
uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>gāyatryādīnāṃ chandasāṃ bhāgasammito'kṣarasamūhaḥ pādaḥ</q> tādṛśo pādaśabdaprayogādabhi-
yuk‍tānām ।</p>
<p><q>gītiṣu । pragīto mantraḥ sāmeti vak‍tavye gītiṣu sāmākhyetyucyate</q> mantratraividhye
pratipādye pragīto mantraḥ sāmeti vak‍tavyam । na gītimātraṃ sāmeti । tathāpi gītiṣu
sāmākhyetyucyate । <q>tatkathaṃ nāma rathantarādayaḥ sāmaviśeṣaśabdā gītiviśeṣasya﻿<pb n="r376"/>
bācakāḥ syuriti । ye rathantarādayaḥ śabdāḥ sāmaviśeṣasya bācakāste kathaṃ gītiviśeṣasya
vācakāḥ syuḥ iti ।</q></p>
<p><q>nanu ca gītimātre sāmaśabdamabhiyuk‍tā na prayuñjate yato rathantaramadhīṣvetyuk‍taḥ
sarkī gītimadhīte loke na gītimātram, na cākṣarāntareṣvavasthitam । akṣarāntare punaḥ</q>
sāmataiva <q>nāsti anyatra vacanāt ।</q> asyārthaḥ&mdash;yadi gītimātrameva sāma tadā ṛgantareṣu
cādhyetavyam । na punaḥ ṛcyādaraḥ kartavyaḥ । akṣarāntaragatāpi gītiḥ vācyaiva । nacaitadubha-
yamapi dṛśyate । kintu gītiviśiṣṭāṃ ṛcamevādhīte yatra bacanaṃ nāsti । sati vacane ṛgantara-
mupādīyate । tatra rathantarādiśabdo gītimātre lākṣaṇiko draṣṭavyaḥ । <q>athāyamabhiprāyaḥ na ca
padaśūnyaṃ gītakamasti</q> tena ṛcyādara iti । dūṣayati&mdash;<q>sarkā hi gītiḥ sāmaśabdavācyā</q>,
ṛgavyabhicārāt, gītimātre prayogādarśanānna gītimātraṃ sāmaśabdābhidheyam । kintu gītivi-
śiṣṭā ṛk । <q>gītisvarūpābhivyak‍tyarthamakṣaropādanamiti cet</q> yadidaṃ rathantaramadhīṣvetyuk‍te
ṛgupādānaṃ tadgītisvarūpābhivyak‍tyarthaṃ, ṛgabhāve ṛgantaropādāne vā gītisvarūpaṃ nābhivyajyate﻿<pb n="r377"/>
tena niyatargupādānamiti cet । dūṣayati&mdash;<q>viparītaṃ tat । yathā'kṣarābhivyañjitā gīti-
stathā navame vakṣyāmaḥ । ato gītimātravacanatve pratibhāmātraṃ</q> sūtrakārasya । atrābhidhīyate
&mdash;anbayavyatirekagamyaṃ hi <q>padapadārthanirūpaṇam । tatra yā abhivatī ṛkasamāmnāyate paṭhyate
sā na rathantaraśabdābhilapyā । kiñca rathantaravuddheḥ utpādikā gītiḥ</q> na punaḥ ṛgeva ṛgādi
<q>ṣvapi prayujyamānā adhyetdṛṇāṃ rathantarabuddhimutṣādayati । bruvateca rathantaramanena lokena na
gītamiti ।</q> tena ṛcaṃ vināpi gītau rathantaraśabdaprayogāt gītiṃ vināpi ca kevalāyāṃ
ṛcyaprayogāt gītireva rathantaraśabdavācyā । yattu rathantaramadhīṣvetyuk‍te niyatāmeva yonimupādatte
tat saukaryāt । tasyāṃ hi tadabhyastaṃ, ṛgantaropādāne ca saṃśaravileśau vikārabhūtau kauci-
dāpadyete । nacāśruto vikāra āśrayituṃ nyāyya iti yonerādarāt । <q>tasmāt sūk‍taṃ gītiṣu
sāmākhyeti ।</q></p>﻿<pb n="r378"/>
<p><q>śeṣe ।। gītipādavaddhābhyāṃ yadanyanmantrajātaṃ tadyajuḥ । anayoḥ punarlakṣaṇaṃ tacchūnyataiva
yajuṣo lakṣaṇam ।</q> ṛk‍sāmavyatirik‍to mantro yajuśśabdenocyate । uk‍tāstriprakārā mantrāḥ
<q>ṛco yajūṃṣi sāmānīti ।</q></p>
<p><q>nigado bā ।</q> avāntarasaṅgatiṃ vadan pūrvapakṣamāha&mdash;<q>uktametat ṛco yajūṃṣi sāmānīti
trividhā mantrā iti । ayamaparaścaturtho vyapadeśaḥ śrūyate nigadā iti ।</q> nanu vede vyapade-
śo na śrūyate <quote>“yamṛṣayastrauvidā viduḥ ṛcassāmāni yajṛṃṣi”</quote> ityetāvanmātraśravaṇāt ityatrāha﻿<pb n="r379"/>
&mdash;evamadhyetāro vyapadiśanti nigadā vartante na yajūṃṣi, yajūṃṣi vartante na nigadā iti ।</q>
yadyapi vede na śrūyate tathāpyadhyetṛvyapadeśaḥ śrūyata eva tena te yajurbhyo'nye nigadā iti gamyate ।
yuk‍tyantaraṃ cāha&mdash;<q>uyāṃśutvena prayogo neṣyate nigadānām ।</q> yadi te yajūṃṣi bhaveyustadā teṣā-
mupāṃśutvaṃ prasajyeta, yajuṣāṃ upāṃśu yajuṣetyupāṃśutvavidhānāt । rāddhāntaikadeśyāha-<q>kimityupāṃśutvaṃ﻿<pb n="r380"/>
nigadānāṃ <q>neṣyate</q> upāṃśu yajuṣeti śravaṇāt । <q>kāryasya</q> puruṣāntarabodhanalakṣaṇasyā-
siddherupāṃśutvaṃ nigadānāṃ <q>neṣyate</q> iti cet nopāṃśutve'pi vacanasyāsiddhiḥ । <q>vacanapūrvakatvāt
kāryasya</q> parasaṃbodhanameva nigadānāṃ kārya na bhavati । yadyapi teṣāṃ svarūpamātrālocanayā
tatkāryaṃ pratibhāti tathāpi vācanikopāṃśutvadharmayogāt tatkāryamasaṃbhāvyamānatayā tyajyeta ।
anyacca kalpyate vaidike vyavahāre vacanamūlameva kāryaṃ yataḥ pūrvapakṣyāha&mdash;yata eva vatanabalena
yajurapekṣe laiṅgikakāryabādhaḥ <q>ata evedaṃ caturthaṃ mantrajātamiṣyate mābhūt kāryeṇa saha vacana-
virodha iti ।</q> caturthe hi mantrajāte upāṃśutvāprasak‍teḥ kāryeṇa saha vacanavirodho na bhavati ।﻿<pb n="r381"/>
ato'virodhasiddhayarthaṃ caturtha mantrajātamiṣyate । nanu bhavatu virodhaḥ bādhyatāṃ ca kāryaṃ
vacanabalenetratyāha&mdash;<q>bhajahatsvārthaṃ ca vacanamiti sthitam ।</q> yo yasya svārthaṃ kāryaṃ so'jaha-
dyasmin vacane tadajahatsvārtha vacanamiti sthitam । yathā godohanādivacanaṃ dohanādikāryā&mdash;
parityāgenaiva varṇyate, tathā'trāpi varṇanā yuktā । <q>nanu coccairnigadeneti vacanamasti ।</q> tena
vacanena viśeṣaviṣayeṇa sāmānyavihite upāṃśutve bādhite sati kāryasyāpi virodho nāsti ।
tena bhavatu yajuṣṭa‍vaṃ tathāpi na kaściddoṣaḥ । pariharati&mdash;<q>ayamaparo'sya doṣaḥ । avibhāge
hi vikalpaḥ prāpnoti ।</q> yo vādī yajuṣṭ‍vaṃ nigadānāmicchati tasya tāvatkāryeṇa saha virodha-
lakṣaṇo doṣo'sti upāṃśu yajuṣetyanayā tāvatprāp‍tyā kāryaṃ viruddhayate । yadi paraṃ tasyāṃ
bādhitāyāṃ kāryasyāvirodhaḥ । aparo'pi tasyāyaṃ doṣo'sti । yajurbhyo nigadānāmavibhāge
abhede vikalpaḥ prāpnoti । upāṃśutvoccaiṣṭvayoḥ vacanadvayena samarpitatvāt । na ca padādibhi-
rivāhavanīyasya upāṃśutvasyoc‍caiṣṭ‍vaina bādhaḥ । upāṃśutvavidhisāpekṣatvāduccaiṣṭ‍vavidheḥ yāvadipāṃ-
śutvavidhirnāśrīyate tāvat parasaṃbodhanakāryanibandhanamuccaiṣṭ‍vaṃ prāptameveti na virodhāvakāśaḥ । tena﻿<pb n="r382"/>
bacanabalena kārye prāpte uccaiṣṭ‍ve nirākṛte vacanasyāvakāśa iti । tadapekṣatvānnaikāntataḥ upāṃśutvasya
bādhaḥ । vācanikaprāp‍tyupajīvanenoccaiṣṭ‍vavidhiriti । tasmādvikalpaparihārāya caturthaṃ mantrajātamiṣya-
tām । tasmiṃśca pakṣe uccairnigadeneti vacanamanuvādakam । upasaṃharati&mdash;<q>tasmātsiddhaṃ
nigado vā caturthaṃ mantrajātaṃ syāt</q> iti ।</p>
<p><q>atrābhidhīyate&mdash;nedaṃ caturthaṃ mantrajātaṃ yaṃjūṣ‍yeba nigadāḥ apādabaddhatvāt
apragītatvācca । trayībyapadeśaścaivamupapadyate</q>, anyathā catuṣṭayī syāt ।</p>
<p><q>yaduk‍taṃ byayadeśādanyatvamiti tatprakarṣābhidhānāt parihṛtam ।</q> tadanyatvaṃ bhāṣya-
kāreṇa prakarṣaṃ vyapadeśahetumabhidhāya parihṛtaṃ nirākṛtam prakarṣalakṣaṇadharmayogena satyapi yajuṣṭ‍ve
vyapadeśabhedo yujyata eveti । <q>yaduk‍taṃ upāṃśutvaṃ vacanāt prāpnotīti tadapyuccairnigadeneti
prakarṣābhidhānopapatteḥ parihṛtam ।</q> gobalīvardavat । yathā gopadaṃ balīvardasannidhāne tadatirik‍ta-
vyak‍tiparamevāvatiṣṭhate tathopāṃśu yajuṣetyatrāpi yajuśśabdaḥ sannihitauccairnigadenetyenacchrutyupa-
nipātamātreṇaitatparityāgena viśeṣāntaramupalabhate । iyaṃ ca laukikī vyutpattiḥ tena kāryaprāpte
uccaiṣṭ‍vai'niraste vacanamidamuccairnigadeneti anuvādavākyamityabhiprāyaḥ । akṣarārthastu yadapyupapāṃśutvaṃ
pūrvapakṣe uk‍taṃ tadapi uccairnigadena karma kriyate ityetādṛśasya prakarṣasya yadabhidhānaṃ kṛtaṃ
tasyopapannatvāt parihṛtaṃ gobalīvardayoriva । yadi nigadaḥ uccaiḥ paṭhyate tadā ṛgeva kimiti﻿<pb n="r383"/>
na bhavatītyatrāha&mdash;<q>nacoccaiṣṭ‍vena ṛk‍tvaṃ</q> nigadānāṃ, <q>apādabaddhatvādityuk‍taṃ pūrvam । tasmātsiddhaṃ
ṛco yajuṃṣi sāmānīti</q> mantrā iti ।</p>
<p><q>arthaikatvādaṃ ।</q> nanu yathā ṛcaḥ sāmāni ca pāṭhata eva parimāṇato jñāyante tathā
yajūṃṣi । kathamidamucyate ityatrāha&mdash;<q>uk‍taṃ triprakāro mantraḥ। pāṭhādeva jñātaparimāṇaṃ
dvividhaṃ mantrajātaṃ</q> ṛcaḥ sāmāni ca । <q>yaṃjūṣi punaḥ pāṭhataḥ</q> parimāṇato na jñātuṃ
<q>śak‍yante iti kiyadekaṃ yajuriti ।</q> parimāṇajñānopāyābhāvānna śakyate vak‍tuṃ iyadekaṃ﻿<pb n="r384"/>
yajuriti । ata idamārabdham । <q>nanu viniyogādyajūṃṣyapi jñātuṃ śak‍yante parimāṇataḥ
iṣetveti śākhāmācchinatti । ūrjetvetyanumārṣṭi iti ।</q> yāvata ekatra viniyogastāvadekaṃ
yajuriti viniyogavaśena yajuḥ parimāṇaṃ jñātuṃ śak‍yate । pariharati&mdash;maivaṃ viśvasīḥ । <q>viniyo-
gāddhi tādarthyamavagamyate na parimāṇaṃ tadarthaścāyaṃ prayāsaḥ</q>, na tādarthyaparijñānārthaḥ । nanu
yāvato viniyogastadaidamarthyaṃ tāvadekaṃ yajuriti atrāha&mdash;<q>jñātaparimāṇasya viniyogādaidamarthyam ।</q>
naidamarthyāt parimāṇajñānam । <q>nanu cetiśabdaḥ purvok‍tasya karaṇatāmāpādayati ।</q> tena
yatpūrvamuk‍taṃ tasya itiśabdena karaṇatayā viniyogaḥ । tena jñāyata eveyato viniyogaḥ
iti । yāvataśca viniyogaḥ tāvadekaṃ yajuriti । pariharati&mdash;<q>kasya pūrvok‍tasya</q> varṇasya
padasya vāk‍yasya veti na vidmaḥ । satyam । pūrvok‍tasya itiśabdaḥ karaṇatāmāpādabati ।
tadeva pūrvok‍taṃ na jñāyate kiṃ varṇaṃ padaṃ vāk‍yaṃ veti । nanu yāvataḥ parasparasaṃbandhaḥ tāvataḥ
pūrvok‍tasya karaṇatā itiśabdenocyate ityatrāha&mdash;<q>nacārthasaṃbandhādṛte</q> varṇo varṇasyānvayī
bhavati । <q>padaṃ vā padasya ।</q> yadi hyarthasaṃbandhavyatirekeṇa varṇānāṃ parasparasaṃbandho bhavet tadā﻿<pb n="r385"/>
arthaikatvādityato'nyat upāyāntaramekayajuṣṭ‍ve bhavet । na caitadasti । <q>tasmāt tasyaikasya
pūrvoktasya karaṇatāmāpādayati itiśabdaḥ sa tvanyato vijñeyo varṇapadavāk‍yatayā ।</q> atiśayamāha
<q>na hyarthādṛte śak‍yate varṇavyatirekeṇa varṇasamūhasyeti śabdasaṃbandho vak‍tum ।</q> asyārthaḥ
-itiśabdasaṃbandhena karaṇatayā viniyogaḥ । sa cetiśabdasaṃbandhaḥ ekasyaiva varṇasya pratīyate । na
varṇasamūhasya । arthāvacchedaṃ vinā samūhānupapatteḥ । tasmāditiśabdena varṇasyaiva viniyogo'rthāvacche-
damantareṇa syāt । <q>nanu ca brāhmaṇavāk‍yavanmāntravāk‍yamap‍yekavākyatayā'vasīyata eba ।</q> yathā
brāhmaṇamekārthapratipādakatayā ekavāk‍yamavasīyate tathā mantravākyamapi । kimatra parimāṇajñānāya
prayat‍nena । pariharati&mdash;<q>satyaṃ yadi svatantrānmantrādarthapratipattiḥ syāt</q> brāhmaṇādivat ।
<q>viniyogasavyapekṣaṃ tu mantrāṇāmarthapratipādanamityuk‍taṃ mantrādhikaraṇe ।</q> tena yāvato
viniyogo yasminnarthe tāvatastadarthapratipādakatvaṃ; tataśceyato viniyoga ityanyato vijñeyam ।﻿<pb n="r386"/>
jñāte ca tasmin tāvat ekārthatvamiti । atra codayati&mdash;evaṃ cedyadi viniyogādarthaprakāśanaṃ
mantrāṇāṃ tadā <q>ṛco'pi viniyogāpekṣatvāt arthasya, arthaparatvācca mantrāṇāṃ anyata eva
parimāṇāvagatiriti</q> iyato viniyoga iti । tataśca yajurmātraviṣayo'yaṃ vicāro na yuk‍taḥ ।
uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>satyaṃ arthaparijñānamanyataḥ ।</q> ṛcāmapi <q>parimāṇaṃ tu chandasaḥ sakāśādvijñeyami-
tyuk‍tam ।</q> chandovaśena hi ṛk‍parimāṇaniścayaḥ । <q>tasmāt kiyadvāk‍yaṃ yajurityetāvānasya</q>
vyāpāraḥ । arthavaśena hi yajuṣaḥ parimāṇaṃ na ṛca ityarthaḥ । <q>sāmāni tu gītakānyabhiyuktaiḥ
parimāṇataḥ smaryante ।</q> tena teṣ‍vapi parimāṇajñānopāyānveṣaṇaṃ nāsti । <q>tasmādidaṃ
parimāṇalakṣaṇaṃ yajuṣāmucyate, arthaikatvāt, sākāṅkṣatvācceti । kimidamarthaikat‍vaṃ ?</q>
uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>anuṣṭheyasya</q> padārthasya <q>smaraṇameko'rthaḥ ।</q> yadyanuṣṭheyasmaraṇamatraiko'rthastarhi <q>padaṃ padamātra-﻿<pb n="r387"/>
mekaṃ</q> vāk‍yam । ekameva hi padaṃ svamarthaṃ smārayati । tadāha&mdash;<q>padena padena hyanuṣṭheyasmaraṇaṃ
na vāk‍yena ।</q> samādhātā ekadeśī codayati&mdash;<q>nanu cānanvitasya padābhidheyatā
nāsti ityuk‍tam ।</q> nacānvitābhidhānaṃ dvitīvārthopādānamantareṇa । naca padāntaravyatirekeṇa
padārthāntaropasthāpanamiti vāk‍yenaivārthaprakāśanam । ākṣeptā āha&mdash;<q>evaṃ tarhi dvayora-</q>
rthayora(na)nvitayoḥ <q>ekārthatvam । padārthena hi padārtho'nvīyate na padārthasamudāyena ।
upapadyate caitat</q> sūtrakārīyamapi mantralakṣaṇaṃ <q>arthaikatvāt sākāṅkṣatvācceti ।</q> tena sūtrakārasyāpi
dvayordvayorekavāk‍yatvaṃ sammatam । samādhātā āha&mdash;<q>evaṃ tarhi prayojanavācyo'yamarthaśabdaḥ
parigṛhyate ।</q> prayojanaṃ vācyaṃ yasya saḥ prayojanavācyaḥ । na pratipādyo'rthaśabdenocyate ।
yāvatāmekaṃ prayojanaṃ tāvadekaṃ vāk‍yamityarthaḥ । yadi pratipādyo'rtho nābhimataḥ kathaṃ tarhi
sākāṅkṣatvaṃ, na hi devasyeti pūṣ‍ṇa ityākāṅkṣaṃ bhavati । bhavati tu tena śabdenaikaprayojanatvaṃ﻿<pb n="r388"/>
militaṃ caikavāk‍yatve kāraṇam । ataḥ kathamatraikavāk‍yatā । <q>ucyate&mdash;dvayordvayoḥ saṃbandhaḥ</q>
tena vibhāge'styeva sākāṅkṣatvam । <q>evaṃ cedamupapannameva sākāṅkṣatvam ।</q> yena
saha yasya saṃbandhaḥ tasya yadi vibhāge sākāṅkṣatvaṃ evaṃ cedupapannameva sākāṅkṣatvaṃ bhavati tadā
arthaikatvenaikavāk‍yatetyarthaḥ । <q>kintu pradhānapadena na</q> guṇabhūtaṃ <q>sakalaṃ padajātamabhisaṃbadhyate</q>
na guṇabhūtena bhavatyekārthatvam । <q>tasmāt prayojanavācye</q>'rthaśabde <q>siddhaṃ sākāṅkṣatvam ।
kimarthamubhayaṃ sūtritami</q>tyatrok‍taṃ bhāṣya eva prayojanam ।</p>
<p><q>sameṣu ।</q> nanu kathamatraikādhikaraṇyaṃ yataḥ iṣetvetyudāharaṇe'dhyāhārāpekṣatvena pūrvapakṣakaraṇaṃ
k‍lṛptīrityudāharaṇe tu adṛṣṭārthatayā ityāśaṅkayaikādhikaraṇatāṃ samarthayate&mdash;<q>yatredānīṃ vidhyantara-﻿<pb n="r389"/>
vihitaprayojanasaṃbandho nasti yajuṣaścaikārthatvaṃ viniyogādityuk‍tam । tatra kiṃ tata eva
viniyogādekārthatvaṃ, utānyato mṛgyamiti ।</q> ayamabhiprāyaḥ&mdash;ubhayasmin‍nudāharaṇe
śāstrāntaravihitaprayojanasaṃbandho nāsti । (na tarhi) [yadi] iṣetvetyācchinatti, urjetvetyanumārṣṭi
iti śrūyate tadā syādeva<note n="(1)">G.<dn>tasyādeva</dn></note> yajuṣāṃ vibhāgaḥ । tathā <quote>‘āyuryajñena kal‍patāṃ prāṇo yajñena kal‍patām
ityapi yadi śāstrāntaravihito'nuṣṭheyavibhāgaḥ śrūyate tata ekema padārthaprakāśanaṃ kṛtamiti
yajurbhedaḥ syāt । atra tvadṛṣṭārthaṃ k‍lṛp‍tyardhaprakāśanamityekena kṛtārthatā na śak‍yata iti
na bhede pramāṇamasti । tena śāstrāntaravihitaprayojanābhāvatul‍yatayā ekādhikaraṇatvamiti ।
akṣarārthastu yatra śāstrāntaravihitaṃ yat‍prayojanaṃ tanna śrūyate yajuṣaścaikārthatvaṃ viniyogāt ।
yāvatāṃ ekatra viniyoga: tāvatāṃ ekārthatvamityuktam । tatra kiṃ tata eva viniyogādekārthatvaṃ﻿<pb n="r390"/>
utānyato mṛg‍yamiti । <q>pūrvapakṣavādino'bhiprāyaḥ-yajuṣa evaikārthatā yuktā'vagantuṃ na vini-
yogataḥ<note n="(1)">G. <dn>parārtha</dn></note> pārārthyamātraparyavasānādviniyogasya ।</q> asyārthaḥ । yajuṃṣi tāvat praśleṣapari-
paṭhitāni । tatra viniyoge'pi yāvat praśleṣe'nugṛhyate tāvadekaṃ vāk‍yaṃ yuktam । na ca
viniyogasya kasyacidvirodhaḥ । tādarthyamātraparyavasānāt । kal‍pyaṃ ca prayojanapadaṃ tatra
<note n="(2)">R. <dn>yathā</dn></note><q>yadi iṣetvetyadhyāhārādekārthatvam । evamūrjetvetyevamādisahitasyāpi । tasmādekaṃ
vāk‍yam ।</q> nanvevamubhābhyāmadhyāhārābhyāṃ paripūritaṃ vāk‍yamabhuyatra prayojyam । tatraikasmin
vāk‍ye yuktaḥ ekasyaivādhyāhārasya saṃbandhaḥ । aparasya kā gatirityatrāha&mdash;<q>pratipattiprayojanaṃ
ca vāk‍yārthe guṇapradhānabhāvo bhaviṣyati ṛcāmiva kāryāntare prayujyamānānāmiti ।</q>
yadyadā prakāśyate tattadā pradhānabhūtaṃ itaracca guṇabhūtaṃ yathā ṛcāṃ kāryāntare viniyujyamānānāṃ
yo'rtho'viniyojakaḥ sa pradhānabhūtaḥ anyad‍guṇabhūtam ।</p>﻿<pb n="r391"/>
<p><q>atrābhidhīyate&mdash;viniyogādevaikaṃ prayojanaṃ yuktam । kasmāt ?</q> uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>yatra
viniyogastatprayojanam ।</q> tasmādekaprayojanatayā caikayajuṣṭ‍vam । tatra iṣetveti cchinatti
ityetāvanmātrasyaiva chedane viniyogaḥ na punarubhayasyānupraveśe pramāṇamasti <note n="(1)">G. <dn>yathāśāstraṃ</dn></note> yathāsvaṃ viniyogenaiva
kṛtārthatvāt । yadyekaprayojanatayā yajuṣa ekatvaṃ <q>na tarhi pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । śākhā hi
tatprayojanam । vacanāntaravihitatvānnirvāpavat ।</q> <quote>‘śākhayā vat‍sānapākaroti’</quote> iti
vacanāntareṇa śākhā vihitā yathā, nirvāpaḥ <quote>‘caturo muṣṭīn nirvapatti’</quote> iti । tena kāryāntara-
bhūtatvācchākhāyāḥ tāṃ prati śeṣabhūtaṃ chedanaṃ, chedanasya ca śeṣabhūtatvāttanmantro'pi tāṃ prati śeṣa-
bhūtaḥ । tataśca tasyāḥ prayojanatvāt iṣetveti ca tvāśabdena śākhāyāḥ pratyavamarśanāt bhedena
prayojana<note n="(2)"> <dn>grahaṇā</dn></note> śravaṇāt vibhāgavāk‍yavat yajuṣo bhedo nyāyya iti kathaṃ pūrvapakṣaḥ । prayojanāśravaṇa-
nibandhano yaḥ pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ sa śrūyamāṇe prayojane nopapadyate । samādhātā āha&mdash;<q>satyaṃ prayojanam ।
na tu pratipādyamānatayā</q> <note n="3">G. omits<dn>kiṃtu chedyatayā</dn></note> kintu chedyatayā । tadavacchedakatayā prayojanam । <q>pratipādyena
hi prayojanena prayojanavanto mantrāḥ</q> tathāpi kimityāha&mdash;<q>tasmādadhyāhārāpekṣatvātprati-
pādyasya sarvārthamekaṃ pratipādyaṃ</q> prayojanaṃ <q>bhaviṣyatīti darśitam ।</q> yadyanena prakāreṇa﻿<pb n="r392"/>
pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ kathaṃ tarhi <q>rāddhāntavādinastvayamabhiprāyaḥ adhyāhṛtasyaikasyānekārthatayā guṇa-
pradhānārthatā dṛṣṭārthatā vā kalpanīyā taccobhayamanyāyyam tasmādyathāviniyogaṃ vāk‍yaṃ
yāvadevoccārya</q> (yāvadevārthaḥ) yatra viniyogastāvatyeva viniyogaviṣayībhūtārthadhyāhārāt
tāvadevaikaṃ vāk‍yaṃ yathā iṣe tvetyācchinatti ūrjetvetyanumārṣṭi iti । nanu ca
itiśabdenaikasyaiva padārthasyopakārakatvaṃ bodhyate । tatkathamiṣetvetyetayoriti-
śabdena viniyogaḥ ityatrāha&mdash;<q>iṣetveti padārthadvayasambandhāt śak‍yate itiśabdena
saṃbandhaḥ pratipat‍tumiti । niyogo hi vākyārthasya karaṇatāmāpādayati । padārthasyeva
vibhaktiyogaḥ ।</q> evaṃ tāvadiṣetvetyudāharaṇe rāddhāntaṃ kṛtvā k‍lṛp‍tyudāharaṇe'pyāha&mdash;<q>evaṃ
k‍lṛptīrvācayatīti bahūnāṃ</q> k‍lṛptī nāṃ <q>viniyuktatvāt tanniṣpattyarthaṃ</q> k‍lṛptibahutvaniṣpattyarthaṃ
k‍lṛptimātrasya <q>prādhānyaṃ</q> pratipādyatvaṃ <q>nādriyate । vibhāgavat ।</q> yathā vibhāge vibhāga-﻿<pb n="r393"/>
mātrasya prādhānyaṃ na tathehāpi k‍lṛptimātrasya vivakṣayā āyurādiviśeṣasya pratipādyatvaṃ nādriyate ।
kintu vivakṣitaviśeṣasyaiva । tataśca k‍lṛptibhedādarthabhede sati yajurbhedo nyāyyaḥ । etacca
viniyogānusāreṇa k‍lṛptibahutvamāśrityocyate iti yathāviniyogaṃ parimāṇajñānādekādhi&mdash;
karaṇatvam ।</p>
<p><q>anuṣaṅgaḥ । saiveyaṃ yajurgatā kathā vartate ।</q> anenāvāntarasaṅgatiruktā । <q>nanu ca
vṛtteyaṃ kathā</q> yajuṣaḥ parimāṇaviṣayā । <q>viniyogataḥ pūrvādhikaraṇe svasāmarthyataśca ।</q>
tatpūrvādhikaraṇe <q>yajuṣaḥ parimāṇamuktam ।</q> pariharati&mdash;<q>satyamuktaṃ uktaviṣaya evāyaṃ vicāraḥ।
kaḥ punarasau ?</q> uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>yatra bahūti vāk‍yāni śeṣāpekṣīṇi vāk‍yāni</q> yāte agre rajāśaye-
tyādīti । <q>ekaśca vāk‍yaśeṣaḥ</q> tanurvarṣiṣṭhetyādi । <q>sa kiṃ yasyānantaraṃ tenaiva saṃbadhyate
uta yāvadbhirākāṅkṣayate</q> tāvadbhiriti । <q>kiṃ punaratra yuktam ? pūrvapakṣavādītvevaṃ﻿<pb n="r394"/>
manyate । ākāṅkṣāsannidhiḥ yogyatā ca saṃbandhe hetuḥ ।</q> evaṃ cet yenaiva saha sannidhānaṃ
tenaiva saṃbandhaḥ । <q>sannidhiścāpekṣikaḥ tasmādanantaraṃ sannihitamucyate</q> avyavadhānapekṣya
<q>ato nānuṣaṅgo</q> vāk‍yaśeṣasya । <q>atrābhidhīyate&mdash;satyaṃ, ākāṅkṣā sannidhiḥ yogyatvaṃ ca
saṃbandhe hetuḥ । sannidhānaṃ punaḥ nāvyavadhānamātrāpekṣam kiṃ tarhi ? sajātīyāvyavadhā-
nāpekṣam ।</q> asyārthaḥ&mdash;buddhau sannidhānamucyate । sajātīyena ca buddhivicchedaḥ kriyate ।
<q>na cātra vāk‍yaśeṣaḥ sajātīyo'rtho byavadhāyako vidyate । śoṣiṇastvasajātīyatbāt na
vyavadhānaṃ kurvanti ।</q> kutaḥ ? uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>na hi yo yamapekṣate sa tasya vyavadhāyako bhavati ।</q>﻿<pb n="r395"/>
tasyāpi tena saṃbandhāt । <q>yathā bahūni nāmāni ākhyātākāṅkṣāṇi tatsaṃvandhe cānantaryamātrāt
na vyavadhānaṃ kurvate ।</q> anyathā aruṇādīnāṃ krayeṇa saha saṃbandho na syāt somapadavyavadhā-
nāt । <q>atha manyase padadharmo'yaṃ</q>, padena padāntaravyavadhānaṃ na kriyate । padasamudāyena tu
padasamudāyasya vyavadhānaṃ kriyata eva । dūṣayati&mdash;<q>na padatvāt saṃbandhaḥ । kiṃ tarhi
ākāṅkṣitatvādeva ।</q> tenākāṅkṣitatvena padasamudāyenāpi saṃbandho bhavatyeva । yena ca﻿<pb n="r396"/>
sahasaṃvandhaḥ tasya saṃbandhinā vyavadhānaṃ na kriyate । atra <q>bhāṣyakāreṇa samudāyāpekṣatayā
ānantaryamupanyastam । samudāyibhiśca saha saṃbandhoḥ darśitaḥ</q>, tadanupapannam । yena hi
yasya saṃbandhaḥ tenaiva ca tasyānantaryamupeyam । atra ca samudāyibhiḥ saha saṃbandhaḥ ānantaryaṃ ca
samudāyasyeti matvā āha&mdash;<q>yatpunaridamuktaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa samudāyāpekṣayā''nantaryamuktaṃ,
samudāyibhiśca saha saṃbandhaḥ</q> upanyastaḥ । <q>kasmāsyārthaḥ ?</q> uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>ayameva
yo'smābhirvyākhyātaḥ ।</q> kathamayamarthaḥ ityāha&mdash;<q>etaduktaṃ bhavati । padasamudāyasyaivaikapada-
saṃbandhe nānantaryaṃ viśeṣyate ।</q> yathā padasamudāyasyaikapadasaṃbandhe ānantaryaṃ na viśeṣyate ।﻿<pb n="r397"/>
pratipadaṃ ca saṃbandhaḥ ।</q> tathehāpi <q>samudāyasyāpi</q> śeṣasaṃbandhasyāvyavadhānāt pratiśeṣi saṃbandhaḥ ।
<q>evaṃ ca paurvāparyamap‍yatantram ।</q> tatra pūrbamapi vāk‍yaśeṣabhūtaṃ bhavati । tathā paramapi । tathā
madhyabhūtamapi । tadāhurvārtikakārapādamiśrāḥ&mdash;
<lg><l>anuṣaṅgi padaṃ yatsyāt ādimadhyāntavartyapi ।</l>
<l>apekṣā''sattiyogyatvaiḥ tasya sarveṇa saṅgatiḥ ।।</l></lg>
iti। <note n="1">G. <dn>kriyāsukālaḥ sannidhiḥ yogyatvaṃ ceti tritayamanvayakāraṇaṃ</dn></note> <q>yadevok‍tamasmābhiryāvadanyat sajātīyaṃ nopanipatatīti tadevedam ।</q> yadevāsmā&mdash;
bhiruk‍taṃ yāvadanyatsajātīyaṃ nopanipatatīti tāvatkālaḥ sannidhiriti tadevedam । <q>kriyāṃstu
kālassannidhiḥ</q> ityenenāpi bhāṣyeṇok‍tam । atraivaṃ pūrvapakṣasiddhāntaracanā&mdash;lokavyavahā-
rānusāreṇa śabdānāmanvitābhidhānaṃ, tatra cākāṅkṣā sannidhiryogyatā <q>ca iti tritayamanvaya-
kāraṇaṃ upalakṣaṇam । iha ca yadyapi vāk‍yaśeṣaṃ prati sarveṣāṃ ākāṃkṣāyogyatāsti</q> tathāpi
vāk‍yaśeṣasya sarvaiḥ saha sannidhānaṃ nāstiti na sarvaiḥ saha saṃbadhyate । sākāṅkṣāṇāṃ tu pūraṇa-
madhyāhārāt bhavatu । loke dṛṣṭatvāt iti । atrābhīdhiyate&mdash;satyaṃ vyavadhānena saṃbandho na﻿<pb n="r398"/>
vyanadhānaṃ tu sajātīyakṛtaṃ draṣṭavyam । bhinnakārakasya vyavahitasyāpi kriyāpadasya sarvaiḥ saṃbandha-
darśanāt devadatta gāṃ śuklāṃ daṇḍenābh‍yāja itivat । na ca śeṣiṇaḥ śeṣapadasyāsajātīyā iti
sarvaiḥ śoṣibhiḥ śeṣapadasya saṃbandha iti ।</p>
<p><q>anuṣaṅgaḥ ।। yatredānīṃ śoṣīṇi nirākāṅkṣāṇi । śeṣaśca sākāṅkṣaḥ tatra katham ?</q> anena
pūrvasmādviśeṣamāha&mdash;pūrvatra śeṣīṇyeva sākāṅkṣāṇi । atra śeṣa eveti viśeṣaḥ । <q>tatrāpi
saiva kathā । asajātīyavyavadhānāt sarvaiḥ saṃbandhaḥ ।</q> anena siddhāntaikadeśino mataṃ tāva
dupanyasyati। asajātīyā hi śeṣasya śoṣiṇaḥ tena tairvyavadhānamavyavadhānameveti sarvaiḥ saṃbandhaḥ।
dūṣayati&mdash;<q>kathaṃ tarhi punarlikhitam ।</q> pūrvatrāpi śeṣibhirevāsajātīyatvāt vyavadhānamavyavadhāna-
meveti sarvaiḥ sambandhaḥ । ihāpi tathaiveti paunaruk‍tyameveti । pariharati&mdash;<q>tadeva tu na
jñāyate kiṃ śeṣitāmātrasajātīyatvaṃ uta pradhānapadābhiprāyamiti ।</q> etaduk‍taṃ bhavati&mdash;kiṃ
śeṣī śeṣyantarasya sajātīyaḥ tena vyavadhānaṃ sajātīyavyavadhānaṃ, tadā pradhānāntarasyābhāvāt
ubhayatra sambandhaḥ siddhayati । tatra pūrveṇa nyāyena śoṃṣitāmātraṃ sajātīyamiti prāptaṃ pūrvādhi-
karaṇok‍timātreṇa śoṣitāmātramapi sajātīyatvamāśrīyate । tataśca sarvasambandho na syāditi ।
tadvayudāsāyedaṃ punarlikhitam । <q>ekākhyātasaṃbandhe satīti ।</q> yadi hi śeṣitāmātraṃ sajātī-
yatvaṃ syāt ekākhyātasaṃbandhe'pi anuṣaṅgo na syāt । yatastvekokhyātasaṃbandhe bhavatyanuṣaṅgaḥ﻿<pb n="r399"/>
tato jñāpayati pradhānapadābhiprāyaṃ sajātīyatvamiti । dūṣayati&mdash;<q>pūrvatra vā'bhinnākhyātasaṃbandhe
sati kiṃ bhavatyanuṣaṅgaḥ ?</q> pūrvatrāp‍yekamevākhyātam । ataḥ ekākhyātasaṃbandhādevobha-
yatrāp‍yanuṣaṅgaḥ । nādhikaraṇāntarāraṃbho yuk‍taḥ । ekadeśī pṛc‍chati&mdash; <q>kimidamākhyātagrahaṇamiti ।</q>
pūrvodāharaṇenākhyātapadamityarthaḥ । uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>pradhānapadapradarśanārthamevā</q>khyātagrahaṇaṃ vivakṣitam ।
pradhānapadamātrābhiprāyeṇākhyātagrahaṇam । ekaṃ ca tatra tanūriti pradhānapadam । dūṣayati eka-
granthenāha&mdash;<q>evaṃ tarhi pūrvatrāpi</q> pradhānapadabhedādevānapaṣaṅgaḥ । ekadeśimataṃ dūṣayitvopasaṃharati
&mdash;<q>tasmādanarthakaṃ punarlekhyam ।</q> idānīṃ svamatena pūrvapakṣasiddhāntādhikaraṇaṃ viracayati
atrocyate&mdash;<q>pradhānapadābhede'pi nirākāṅkṣeṣu pradhānapadeṣvekatvāt vāk‍yaśeṣasya hyekenaiva
saṃbandho yuktaḥ ।</q> tāvataiva śeṣasyākāṅkṣānivṛtteḥ । nanu sa evaiko na jñāyate kenaikena saṃbandha
iti । tataścāgṛhyamāṇaviśeṣatvāt sarvaireva saṃbandho yukta ityatrāha&mdash;<q>śak‍yate ca viśeṣo
vak‍tum, ānantaryāta</q> iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । rāddhāntamāha&mdash;<q>satyaṃ yatrārthabhedaḥ</q> tatraikena saṃbandho
jñeyaḥ । <q>yatratvartha eva na bhidyate tatra</q> tatsaṃbandhasya vāk‍yaśeṣasya <q>pūrvavadevānuṣaṅga iti ।</q>
<note n="(1)">G.<dn>vidyate</dn></note>

﻿<pb n="r400"/>
<p><q>vyavāyāt । yatra punaḥ sajātīyena vyavadhānaṃ tatra vyavadhānānnānuṣajyeta</q> ityuktam ।
anena pratyudāharaṇamātrametaditi kathitam ।</p>
<trailer>iti mahāmahopādhyāya śrīśālikanāthabhaṭṭamiśrakṛtāyāṃ
ṛjuvimalāyāṃ pañcikāyāṃ dvitīyādhyāyasya
prathamaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>﻿<pb n="r401"/>
<trailer>ṛjuvimalāpañcikā
dvitīyādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>
<p><q>śabdāntare ।</q> atredaṃ pratibhāti । yajate dadāti juhotiṃ iti śabdāntaranibandhano
yāgādikarmabhedaḥ sūtrakāreṇokta iti । taccānupapannam । yāgādīnāṃ bhedasya svataḥ
prasiddhatvāt na prasādhyatvaṃ yuktamiti । anenābhiprāyeṇa pṛcchati&mdash;<q>śabdāntare karmabheda iti
sūtre śrūyate । kaḥ punaratra śabdo'bhipretaḥ ? kimiha karmābhipretam ? uttaraṃ-<q>śāstraṃ
śabdo'bhiprataḥ । niyogārthaḥ karma ।</q> kriyata iti vyutpattyā niyogārthasya karmatvāt ।
atra codayati&mdash;<q>kathaṃ tarhi anubandhabhedāt bheda ucyate karmaṇa iti ?</q> atra hi kṛtānu&mdash;﻿<pb n="r402"/>
bandhatvāt karmabheda ityuk‍te kṛtānubandhatvena niyogabheda iti pratīyate । pariharati&mdash;<q>kimiti vā
nocyate ?</q> codayitā āha&mdash;<q>śāstrāddhi karmaṇo'nubandhaḥ pratīyate ।</q> śās‍treṇa hi niyoga-
syānubandhaḥ pratīyate śāstrāntareṇa cānubandhāntaraṃ, anubandhāntare ca niyogabhedaḥ । na ca
karbhānubandhanirapekṣaṃ śās‍traṃ śāstratayā'vagamyate । karmānubandhāpekṣaṃ śāstratvaṃ, anubandhāntarāpekṣaṃ
śāstrāntaratvam । <q>evaṃ cetaretarāśrayaṃ syāt ।</q> tasmācchāstraparimāṇaṃ tāvadanyate vaktavya-
miti । tadāha&mdash;<q>tasmācchāstraparimāṇajñānopāyastāvadanyato vaktavyaḥ ।</q> anyathā hi
parimāṇajñānācchāstrāntare karmabheda iti na śakyate bak‍tum, tatparimāṇajñānapūrvakaṃ hi
śāstrāntaratvam । <q>tasmācchāstrāntaratve yat‍naḥ kartavyaḥ । ucyate । dvayamapyatraiva prati-
pāditam । kathaṃ? śāstrāntare sati karmabheda iti vadatā śāstrādbheda ityuktam । nānu﻿<pb n="r403"/>
bandhāt ।</q> sūtrakāreṇa hi śabdāntare iti nimittasaptamīyaṃ prayuktā । tena śabdāntara-
nimittakaḥ śāstrāntarahetukaḥ karmabhedo niyogabhedaṃ iti gaditam । na punaranubandhahetukaḥ ।
tena śabdāntaratvaṃ tāvadekaṃ niyogabhedakāraṇamuktam । tathā <q>kathaṃ punaḥ śāstrāntarapari-
jñānamiti ? atrāpi kṛtānubandhatvādityuktam ।</q> kṛtānubandhatvaṃ śabdāntaratve kāraṇa-
mityuktam । <q>tadeṣa saṃkṣepārthaḥ</q> śāstrāntarāt karmabhedo'vagamyate । śāstrāntaraṃ cānubandha-
bhedādavasīyate । anubandhabhedastu abhidhānāntarādipramāṇapañcakānugṛhītācchabdādevānirdhārita-
bhedābhedādavasitaḥ śāstraṃ bhinatti । tena netaretarāśrayatvām ।</p>
<p><q>nanu karmānubadhyate, na śāstram ।</q> <note n="(1)"> <dn>pakṣadharmo vā heturbhavati tataśca kṛtānubandhamedatvāt śāstrameda iti na yuktaṃ vak‍tum।</dn></note>pakṣadharma eva tu heturbhavati । tataśca
kṛtānubandhatvāt śāstrabheda iti na yuk‍taṃ vak‍tum । pariharati&mdash;kena vok‍taṃ karmānubadhyata
iti karmaivānubadhyata iti vayamapi brūmaḥ । <q>parimāṇajñāne hi śāstrasyānubandha upakaroti ।</q>
parakīyo'pyanubandhaḥ śāstraparimāṇajñānaheturbhavati । ākṣeptā āha&mdash;yadi karmānubadhyate, na
śās‍traṃ <q>tarhi na śāstraṃ kṛtānubandhaṃ bhavati ।</q> parihartā āha&mdash;bhavati tu kṛtānubandhaṃ śāstraṃ﻿<pb n="r404"/>
pratipādakatayā</q> karmaṇa evānubandhaḥ <q>pratītiḥ kṛtā yena tat kṛtānubandhaṃ śāstram ।</q>
kṛto'nubandho yena tat kṛtānubandhanaṃ śās‍treṇa cānubandhasya idameva karaṇaṃ yat pratipādanaṃ nāma ।
<note n="(1)"> <dn>pramāṇāntaraṃ</dn></note>prakārāntaraṃ cāha&mdash;<q>yadvā kṛtānubandhatvāt karmaṇaḥ anubandhāntareṇānvayasyānabhidhānāt
anubandhāntare śāstrāntaratvaṃ, śāstrāntaratve ca śāstrārthāntaratvam ।</q> yadyanubandhāntaratvena
śāstrāntaratvaṃ <q>kathaṃ tarhi pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ?</q> uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>evamatra pūrvapakṣayanti ayuktamidamanubandha-
bhedācchāstrabheda iti ।</q> kasmāt ? uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>dṛṣṭaṃ hi anekānubandhamekaṃ śāstram darśapūrṇa-
māsābhyāṃ svargakāmo yajeteti । evaṃ yāgadānahomānubandheṣvapi mābhūdbhedaḥ । nanu ca
karaṇetikartavyatāvyavasthānāt</q> darśapūrṇamāsābhyāmityatrābhedaḥ । iha tu sarveṣāṃ yāgadāna-﻿<pb n="r405"/>
homānāṃ svāpūrveṣu karaṇatvena saṃbandhāt bhedo yuktaḥ । pūrvapakṣyāha&mdash;<q>anuvandhāntare'pi tāva-
dabheda iti pratipannam । avasthānaṃ tu viniyogabhedāvagagyam ।</q> anubandhabhedastāvat śāstra-
bhedakatve'naikāntikaḥ । yadyapi karaṇetikartavyatā'vasthānabhede'pi viniyogavaśena dvayorapi
niyogānubandhatvāt । <q>na cāyamekāntiḥ</q> karaṇetikartavyatāvyavasthānādevānubandhabhedaḥ
śāstrasyābhedaḥ anyatra tu bheda iti । yataḥ <q>kevalakaraṇatayā vyavasthitānāmapi <note n="(1)"> G. <dn>bahūnāmanubandhānāmeka</dn></note> bahūnāmeka-
śāstrāvagamyatvaṃ<note n="2"> G. <dn>gamyānubandhatvaṃ</dn></note> darśapūrṇamāsayoḥ rājasūye ca ।</q> darśapūrṇamāsayorhi yāgaṣaṭkapratipādakam ।
ekamadhikāraśāstraṃ dṛśyate । rājasūye ca pāśukasaumikaiṣṭikadārvihomikānekānubandhāvabodhakam ।
<q>utpattāvapi ca prājāpatyāniti</q> prājāpatyaprātipadikopāttadravyadevatāsaṃbandhasaptadaśake'nubandhe-
'pyekaṃ śās‍tram । <q>nanu ca prājāpatyeṣu saṃkhyayā śāstrabhadaḥ ।</q> pariharati&mdash;<q>bhavatu saṅkhyayā</q>
bhedaḥ śāstrasya । <q>anubandhabhedastāvanna bhedakaḥ ।</q> etāvatā ca dṛṣṭāntaḥ । etaccābhyapagamyavāda-
mātram । paramārthamāha&mdash;<q>asati cānuvandhabhede saṅkhyā mettrīti<note n="(1)"> G. <dn>bahūnāmanubandhānāmeka</dn></note> namobhedavidbhayaḥ ।</q> asyārthaḥ
-ye'pi śās‍trabhedavādinaḥ te'pyanubandhabhedenaiva śāstrabhedamāhuḥ । na ca saṅkhayayā'nubandhabhedaḥ । kiṃ
tarhi ? bhāvārthamātrabhedaḥ tena prājāpatyeṣu sarvasaṃmataḥ śās‍trabhedaḥ <q>tasmāt pracayāvagamyo'yamanu-﻿<pb n="r406"/>
bandhasamudāyaḥ ekaśās‍trāvagamyaḥ । ekaśās‍trāvagamye caiko niyogārthaḥ ।</q> tadeva apūrvam ।
tasmādekamapūrvam । pūrvapakṣe yuktyantaraṃ cāha&mdash;<note n="(1)"> G. <dn>yathā</dn></note><q>yadvā pratyayāvagabhyatvānniyogārthasya sānu-
bandhataiva na pratīyate padārthasyeva padārthāntareṇa । nanu padārtho'pi padārthāntarānubaddha eva ।</q>
ekagranthenāha&mdash;<q>parasparānvayitā hyanubandhaḥ ucyate ।</q> asti ca padānāṃ parasparānvayitā ।
pariharati&mdash;<q>anabhijño bhavān anubandhānvayayoḥ ।</q> pṛcchati&mdash;<q>kaḥ punaranayoṃrviśeṣaḥ ।</q>
uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>kriyākāraka<note n="(2)"> G. <dn>guṃṇasyaida</dn></note>guṇaguṇyaidamarthyasaṃvandhitā hyanvaya ucyate । niyogasya viṣayāpatti-
ranubandhaḥ ।</q> anubandhanaṃ anubandhaḥ viṣayo'vacchedakaḥ । ananyabhāvo hi viṣayārthaḥ tena﻿<pb n="r407"/>
<note n="(1)"> G. <dn>tena yatsaṃbandhassan niyogo vedyate</dn></note>yatsaṃbandhena niyogo'bhivyajyate sa viṣayaḥ anubandhaśca sa eveti । na padārthasya padārthānta&mdash;
reṇānubandho'sti, kevalamanvaya eva । kasmātpunaḥ svānubandhataiva na syāt ityatrāha&mdash;<q>na ca
śabdāntarābhidheyo yāgādirviṣayatāmāpadyate । aviniyukta<note n="(2)"> R. <dn>vinidukta</dn></note> viniyogāpekṣitve cāgṛhyamāṇa-
viśeṣatvaṃ prayājādīnāmiva</q> ekatvātpratyayasya tadarthasyaikatvāt <note n="(3)"> G. <dn>diti । na ca</dn></note><q>tena ca</q> sarveṣāṃ saṃbandhāt
sarvānubandha eko niyogaḥ । <q>tasmādanu</q>vandharūpatayā bhedābhāvāt <q>siddhamekaśāstrābhidheṣatvaṃ</q>
sarveṣāṃ yāgādīnām । etaduk‍taṃ bhavati&mdash;yadyapyanubandhabhedena bhedaḥ tathāpyatra bhedo na yuktaḥ
anubandhabhedābhāvādeva sarveṣāmekānubandhāvasthā yataḥ । yuktyantaraṃ cāha&mdash;<q>yadvā yāgadānaho-
meṣvayamaparo viśeṣaḥ । anubandhānāṃ nānātvamapi na śakyate vak‍tum, parasparānuvāda-
saṃbhavāt yadāhavanīye juhotītivat ।</q> yathā yadāhavanīye juhotīti homaviṣayaniyogānu-
vādaḥ tathehāpi । dṛṣṭāntadvayaṃ cāha&mdash;<q>evaṃ guṇakarmasu</q> avaghātādiṣu <q>guṇavidhāneṣu ca</q>
dadhnā juhoti ityādiṣu ca niyogānuvāditvaṃ draṣṭavyam । kuta ityatrāha&mdash;<q>pradhānānupraveśi-
tvāt tadvidhānasya ।</q> guṇakarmavidhānasya । pradhānavidhyanupraveśitvāt pradhānavidhyanuvāda eva﻿<pb n="r408"/>
tadgatairliṅadibhiḥ kriyate । <q>evaṃ ca sati sarvaphalānubandhaṃ sarvaguṇānubandhaṃ sarvadhātvarthānu-
bandhamekamapūrvaṃ eko niyogārtha ityarthaḥ ।</q> śāstrābhede śāstrārthābhedādekāpūrvasaṃbandhameva
sarvam ।</p>
<p>atrābhidhīyate&mdash;<q>na sarvaviṣaya eko niyogārthaḥ pratipat‍tuṃ śakyate ।</q> kasmādi-
tyāha&mdash;<q>bhāvārtha eva hi karmaśabdo viṣayamavacchinatti bhāvārthāntaranirapekṣaḥ</q> bhāvārtha
evetyasyāyamarthaḥ&mdash;yo yāvān bhāvārthaḥ tasyāpi karmaśabdo viṣayasamarpakaḥ sa
bhāvārthāntaranirapekṣa eva viṣayamavacchinatti svārthameva viṣayatvena samarthayati । yadi
nirapekṣasya viṣayatvaṃ tadā karaṇatvamapi nirapekṣasyaiva syādityatrāha&mdash;<q>karaṇāpattau</q> hi
<q>bhāvārthāntarāpekṣā</q> bhāvārthasya <q>na viṣayāpattau</q> ananugṛhītasya karaṇatvānupapatteḥ yuktaṃ
karaṇatvaṃ bhāvārthāntarāpekṣitvaṃ viṣayabhāve tvapekṣāyāṃ heturnāsti । nanu kiṃ kāraṇatvaṃ viṣayatvaṃ ca﻿<pb n="r409"/>
bhinnaṃ yena kāraṇatve'pekṣāsti viṣayatve nāstītyucyate । bāḍhaṃ, bhinnaṃ, <q>vidheyabhūtasya hi niyogārthaṃ
prati kāraṇabhāvaḥ sādhanabhāvo'vagamyate na punaḥ tatsādhanatayaiva niyogasaṃbandhaḥ ।</q> kārya-
rūpayo hi vidhyarthaḥ kāryaṃ ca kṛtyavacchinnam । kṛtiśca puruṣaprayat‍narūpā । tadavacchinnaḥ
svakāryātmā niyatamevārthāvyabhicāritvāt । tena prathamaṃ bhāvārtho'vacchedakatayaiva saṃbadhyate ।
paścāttasya kāryasya kiṃ karaṇamityapekṣāyāmevāsau kṛtivyāpyatvādviṣayabhṛtaḥ । sa etasyāṃ kṛtau
karaṇaṃ bhavati । tadvayāpyatvādviṣayībhūtasya sādhanabhāvo na sādhanatvenaiva niyogasaṃbandho bhāvārthasya ।
tacca <q>viṣayakaraṇīye</q> viviktam । <q>yathā caitadevaṃ</q> karaṇāpattau bhāvārthāntarāpekṣā bhāvārthasya
na viṣayāpattau <q>tathā ṣaṣṭhe</q> śāstrasya vyapavadhitvaṃ vadanto <q>vakṣyāmaḥ। tasmāddhātvarthabhedanni-
yogabhedaḥ niyogabhedācca siddhaṃ karmāntaram ।</q> karmāntaraniyojyatya karmāntaraniyojyatvā-
bhāvanibandhabhedo tadbhedācca śāstramapi midyate । <q>yadapyuk‍taṃ niyogārthasya pratyayavācya-
tvādagṛhyamāṇaviśeṣatvāt sarvabhāvārthābhisaṃbandha iti । tadayuktaṃ, agṛhyamāṇaviśeṣatā
hi viniyoge na viṣaye</q> viṣayatve hi sati ya eva sabandhastenaiva bheda āpādita iti na﻿<pb n="r410"/>
tatrānyasya saṃbandhaḥ । viniyogamātre tu yukta evānyasaṃvandhe'pyanyasaṃbandhaḥ । <q>taduktaṃ bhāṣya-
kāreṇa yajirapyevaṃ svoccāraṇāṃvagamyaviṣaye noccāraṇāntaramapekṣate</q> yajerviṣayo vācyo
yāgaḥ svoccāraṇamātreṇāvagamyate na dadāti juhotītyuccāraṇāntarāpekṣatā । yā <q>punarekārthatā yāga-
dānahomānāmupavarṇitā sā nopapadyate bhinnārthāvagateḥ ।</q> yathā ca bhinnārthaḥ tathā caturthe vakṣyā-
maḥ । <q>na ca vidheyārthatve saṃbhabati anuvādakatā yuktā</q> yato lakṣaṇayā samānārthatā bhavet ।
<q>yatpunaridamuktaṃ darśapūrṇamāsayorivānekānubandhaviṣayatā evāsya vidheravagamyanta iti
parihṛtamasmābhiḥ viniyojyatayā tadavasīyate na viṣayatayā</q> karaṇabhāve hi darśapūrṇamāsa-
yorbhedena(bhedona)viṣayabhāve tantrābhihitānāṃ yathābhidhānameva viṣayabhāvaḥ tenānubandhabhedo'trāpi
nāsti kevalaṃ karaṇatvamātrabhedaḥ । kathaṃ punarviṣayatvenābhede'pi karaṇatve bhedaḥ । ucyate ।
sādhakatvena karaṇatvaṃ sādhanatvaṃ cāvāntaravyāpāranibandhanam । tatrāvāntaravyāparīmṛtotpatti-﻿<pb n="r411"/>
niyogabhedena karaṇatā bhidyate । viṣayatayā tu tannirapekṣatvānna bhidyate । yata eva ca karaṇa-
tve bhedo na viṣayatve <q>ata evāgneyādayaḥ</q> utpattiniyogā adhikāraniyogena saha ekaviṣayā
eva । teṣāmekaikaviṣayatvādadhikāraniyogasya militaviṣayatvānnābhinnaniyojyānāṃ bhinnakaraṇatā ।
teṣvapi pratyekaṃ karaṇabhāvādadhikāraniyoge ca pratyekameva karaṇatvam । <q>tasmātsiddhaṃ prativiṣayaṃ
śāstrabhedaḥ tadbhedācca karmabheda iti ।</q></p>
<p><q>ekasyaivam । uktaṃ kṛtānubandhatvāt śās‍trabhedaḥ śās‍tramedāt karmabheda iti ।
yatra punaranuvandho'pi ekastatra kathaṃ</q> śās‍trabhedaḥ । ekagranthenāha&mdash;<q>bhavatu tatraikaṃ śās‍traṃ
ekaṃ ca karma</q> anubandhabhedasya śās‍trabhedakasyābhāvāt । <q>nanu cānarthakaṃ bhavati</q> punargrahaṇaṃ﻿<pb n="r412"/>
pariharati&mdash;<q>kimidamānarthakyaṃ nāma</q>, sa evāha&mdash;<q>yadi tāvannārthapratipādakatvaṃ</q> arthaśabda-
syābhidheyavacanatvāt <q>tadayuktaṃ</q> pratipādakatvāt pratyutārthāntaratve'bhyupagagyamāne'pratipādakaṃ
bhavati । <q>atha</q> prayojanavacanatvādarthaśabdasyānarthakaṃ <q>niṣprayojanamavagamyamānaṃ hi yadi
prayojanaṃ na bhavati mā bhūta</q>, nāvaśyaṃ prayojanavattayaiva bhavitavyamiti naḥ pratijñā । yasya
prayojanamavagamyate tasya bhavatu prayojanaṃ yasya tu nāvagamyate tasya mābhūt na kācitkṣatiḥ ।
<q>tasmādekaṃ karma । atrābhidhīyate । vidyata evātrāpyanubandhabhedaḥ । kutaḥ ? uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>avi-
śeṣāt ।</q> tadeva vivṛṇoti&mdash;<q>naitacchakyate vak‍tuṃ asyārthasya itthaṃ punaḥ śrutirvartata iti ।</q>
tena bhinnā evaite yāgāḥ yajiśabdābhidheyāḥ yathā darśapūrṇamāsādayaḥ । nanu bhavatu yāgabhedaḥ
tathāpyanubandhatā kathaṃ bhidyate tadbhede ca śās‍trabhedo na yāgamātrabhede । darśapūrṇamāsādhikaraṇa-
śās‍travadityāha&mdash;<q>yāgadānahomādīnāṃ arthabhedādebānubandhatāpi bhidyate taccātrāpi tulyam ।
nanu cātraiko yāgārthaḥ pratīyate ।</q> pariharati&mdash;<q>satyamevaiko yāgaḥ</q> sa yajiśabdavācyatayā
<q>na tu vidheyatayā ।</q> (sarvaṃ) sarvatra vidheyatayā'vagamyamāno yāgo vihitasya vidhānānupapatteḥ﻿<pb n="r413"/>
bhinno'vagamyate । <q>kathaṃ punaḥ ekaḥ pratīyamāno'pi vidheyatayā nānātvaṃ bhajate</q> pṛthagyajyabhi-
dheyo yāgaḥ kathaṃ nānābhūto bhavatītyarthaḥ । uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>yathā jyotiṣṭomadarśapūrṇamāsayośca</q> bahūnā-
mapi yāgānāṃ ekaśabdābhidheyatvaṃ nānupapannam । ekopādhisaṃbhavāt sarveṃṣāṃ hi devatoddeśena
dravyatyāgarūpatā na bhidyate tena tadupādhikayajiśabdābhidheyatvaṃ nānupapannam । yadyekatve'pi
vidhiśravaṇena yajiśabdasya vidheyabhṛtabhāvārtho bhinno'vagamyate tadā yāgadānahomādīnāmapi tathaiva
bhedāvagamasiddheḥ <q>ādhastyamadhikaraṇamidānīṃ kvopayujyate ? uttaraṃ-viśeṣāddhi tatrānu-
vandhabhedaḥ ।</q> asyārthaḥ&mdash;abhidhānāntaramanubandhabhedakaṃ darśayitumādhastyamadhikaraṇam । iha
ttu punaḥ śrutirapi anubandhabhediketi vak‍tumityupayogo'dhikaraṇadvayasya । yata evābhidhānāntarā-
bhāve'pi vidhipunaḥśrutimātreṇābhedaḥ <q>tata eva bhāṣyakāreṇa pūrvapakṣe sa eva śabdaḥ punaḥ
punaḥ uccāryata iti vadatā na viśeṣādṛte'nubandhanānātvaṃ siddhayatīti pradarśitam । guṇa-
vidhānaṃ punaḥ kimarthamāśaṅkitaṃ ?</q> asyārthaḥ&mdash;puna: śrutermedakaraṇatve punarjñāte samidho﻿<pb n="r414"/>
yajatītyādiṣu guṇavidhānāśakyatvānnirarthatā । na hyeva punaḥ śruterbhedahetutā nirastā bhavati ।
uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>punaḥ śruterudāharaṇaṃ durlabhamiti manvānenedamāśaṅkitam ।</q> asyārthaḥ&mdash;punaḥśrutirbhedikā
yadi k‍vacit saṃbhavet sātu k‍vacidapi na saṃbhavati । kevalasyākhyātapadamānnasyāprayogāt ।
yadā guṇapadamupapadaṃ bhavati tadā tatra guṇavidhānāta punaḥ śratiḥ na śakyate vak‍tuṃ tadāha&mdash;
<q>guṇanānātvāddhi śratyantarabheva bhavati</q> yadāpi nāma tadāpi bhedācchrutyantarameva । tadāha
&mdash;nāmānivā bhavantu samidādipadāni । <q>tathāpi śrutyantarameva</q> tena punaḥ śruterudāharaṇaṃ
durlabham । <q>parihāraṃstu</q> kevaladhātvartha<note n="(1)"> G.<dn>asti</dn></note> vidhāvasati guṇavidhānaṃ nāma vā na saṃbhavati ।
yāvaddhi kevalo dhātvartho na vidhīyate tāvad‌guṇavidhānaṃ na saṃbhavati nirāśrayasya tasyāyogāt ।
nāmāpi nāmino'saṃbhave'nupapannameva । kasmādityāha-<q>guṇo hi vidhīyamānaḥ samidho yaja-
tīti k‍va vidhīyatām ? ।</q> ekagranthenāha&mdash;<q>yadi tāvat pradhānayāge</q> tadā <q>guṇāntareṇā-</q>
gnyādinā tasya yāgasyā<q>varodhānna</q> tat <q>saṃbhavati । atha samidyāga eba guṇavidhiḥ tadā yāga-﻿<pb n="r415"/>
vidhānamamapi prāpnoti ।</q> bhavatu yāgavidhānaṃ ko doṣa ityāha&mdash;<q>yāgavidhāne ca nivṛttirguṇa-
vidhānasya śruternāmatāvagamāt ।</q> guṇavidhāne hi matvarthalakṣaṇā doṣaḥ tena guṇavidhirnāsti ।
kintu nāmatvameva । evaṃ pañcasvapi draṣṭavyam । nanvevaṃ nāmaveyatve'pi śrutyantaramevetyatrāha
&mdash;<q>nāmno'nuvādakatvāt yajiśrutireva kevalaṃ viṣayaviśeṣaṇaṃ</q> yajireva svārthe viśiṣṭaviṣayatve-
nopanayati । nāmadheyaṃ tu yajyarthamevānuvadati । <q>tasmāttānyeva punaḥ</q> śruterudāharaṇāni ।
nanvevamapi nāmnaivātra bhedaḥ na punaḥ śrutyetyāha-<q>na cātra nāma bhedakaṃ vidhānottarakālabhāvitvā-
nnāmabhāvasya ।</q> yatra vidhirvartate tatraiva nāmnā vartitavyam । tena yadā vidhibhinno yāgo
vajinā vidheyatvenopanītaḥ tadā bhinnasya nāmadheyam, yadā'bhinnastadā abhinnasyeti nāg‍no bhedakatvaṃ
nāsti । <q>abhedakameva tarhi nāma ? <note n="(1)"> <dn>sarvatrāmidhā</dn></note>sarvatravidhānottarakālabhāvitvāt ।</q> tataśca
nāmadheyaṃ nāma pramāṇāntaraṃ bhedakamucchidyeta । <q>ucyate । samidādiṣu</q> tu na bhedakaṃ<note n="(2)"> G. <dn>tu karturamedakaṃ</dn></note>﻿<pb n="r416"/>
<q>jyotiṣṭomādiṣu yathā medakaṃ tathā tatnaiva varṇayiṣyāmaḥ ।</q> yatra punaḥ nāmākhyātaśūnyaṃ śrūyate
tatra tata eva bhede'vasite paścādyajirapi śrūyamāno bhinnayāgapara eva bhavati । kevalastu yajiḥ
sahasradakṣipādiguṇamātravidhipara eva bhavatīti saṃjñādhikaraṇe vakṣyate । <note n="(1)"> G. <dn>tasmādanubandhaviśeṣādbheda.</dn></note>tasmādaviśeṣādanuvangha-
bhedaḥ <q>anubandhabhedācchās‍trabhedaḥ śās‍trabhedāt kārya bheda iti siddham ।</q></p>
<p><q>prakaraṇaṃ tu । uk‍taṃ punaḥ śruterapyanubandhānyatvamaviśeṣāt iti ।</q> anenāvāntara-
saṃgatiḥ pūrvapakṣabījaṃ copanyasyati । ya evaṃ vidvān paurṇamāsīṃ yajate ya evaṃ vidvānamāvāsyāṃ
yajate <q>ityasyāmidānīṃ punaḥ śrūtau kimanubandhabhedo vidyate neti</q> cintyate । <q>pūrvok‍tena﻿<pb n="r417"/>
viśeṣādanubandhabhedaḥ ।</q> atra bhāṣyakāreṇa śabdāntaratvādabhyāsācceti pramāṇamupanyastam, tatrā-
kṣepamāha&mdash;<q>śabdāntaratvaṃ kimityupanyastaṃ abhyāsādevāviśeṣāditi yuktirgamyate । atrābhi-
dhīyate । ubhayaprakāro'tra bhedaścintyate । karaṇetikartavyatākṛto viṣayakṛtaśca ।</q> karaṇeti-
kartavyatātmanā sādhyabhedanibandhano'nuvandhabhedanibandhanaścātra bhedaḥ pratipādyate । <q>tatrābhyāsā-
dviṣayakṛtabhedasiddhiḥ ।</q> anubandhakṛtaḥ śās‍trabhedo nābhyāsāducyate । <q>śabdāntarātkaraṇeti-
kartavyatābhedaḥ</q> karaṇetikartavyatāśās‍trabhedanibandhanaśās‍trabhedaḥ śabdāntarāducyate । karaṇasya
hi avāntarakāryaṃ sādhyaṃ itikartavyatāyāśca karaṇopakāra iti sādhyabhedaḥ tad‍bhedācca karaṇa-
śās‍trāditikartavyatāśās‍traṃ bhidyate । karaṇetikartavyatātmanā ca bhedaḥ śabdāntaratvādbhavati । yena
śabdenāgneyādityevocyate tena kāmaśabdenādhikārasaṃbandhāt āgneyādīni karaṇāni bhavantītya-
vaghātādīnyaṅgani । <q>tasmādyuk‍tamubhayamupanyastam ।</q> yata eva hetunā sādhye ayaṃ karaṇeti-
kartavyatākṛto[bhedaḥ]nāsādhi(to)[te] lakṣyate <q>ata eva samapradhānāṅgāṅgibhāvānuvādavidhā-
nāni krameṇopanyasyāni ।</q> anyathā prayojanamātratve samapradhānāṅgāṅgibhāvayoradhikaraṇāntare﻿<pb n="r418"/>
upanyāsaḥ syāt । kasmātpunarhetoḥ sādhyatetyatrāha&mdash;<q>na vidhānamātrāt samapradhānabhāvasiddhiḥ ।
nāpyanuvādamātrāt</q> guṇapradhānabhāvaḥ । <q>kiṃ tarhi śabdāntaratvādaṅgāṅgibhāvaḥ</q> śabdāntara-
śabdena śās‍trāntaraṃ mā vijñāyītyetadarthamāha&mdash;<q>abhidhānāntaratbādityarthaḥ । abhidhānaikyācca
samapradhānabhāvaḥ ।</q> yadi vidheyāvamāvāsyāpaurṇamāsīsaṃyuk‍tau yāgau bhavataḥ tathāpi yāvadabhidhā-
naikyaṃ na bhavati tāvanna samapradhānabhāvasiddhiḥ । tathā nipāta(da)tvepi yāvadabhidhānāntaratā na
syāt evaṃ nāṅgaṅgibhāvasiddhiḥ । <q>kiṃ punaraṅgapradhānatayā bhedakathane prayojanaṃ ?</q> uttaraṃ-<q>viṣayato
vā bhedakathane kiṃ prayojanam ?</q> ekagranthenāha&mdash;<q>kathaṃ māma bhedenānuṣṭhānaṃ syāt । evaṃ
cedatrāpyaṅgatayā kathamanuṣṭhānaṃ syāt ।</q> atra yadā'bhinnasyaiva viniyogādaṅgāṅgitvaṃ syāt
tadā na bhavedabhidhānāntaratvaṃ hetuḥ । tatrābhidhānāntaravaśena tvadhikāracodanā-
yāmanupraveśānanupraveśābhyāṃ aṅgāṅgitvaṃ yadadhikāracodanānupraviṣṭaṃ tatpradhānaṃ itarattatrā-
pradhānam । codayitā āha&mdash;<q>na vrūmo'bhinnasyāṅgāṅgitvamiti । kiṃtu viṣayamātra-﻿<pb n="r419"/>
bhedādbhinnasyetyucyate</q> aṅgaṅgitvam । dūṣayati&mdash;<q>viṣayamātrabheda eva yadyaṅgāṅgitve hetuḥ
kimiti pradhānānyāgneyādīni parasparamaṅgaṃ na bhavanti samidādīni vā</q> parasparaṃ kasmānnāṅgaṃ ?
teṣvapi viṣayabhedasya vispaṣṭatā । upasaṃharati&mdash;<q>tasmāt kāryacodanāto'dhikāracodanāto
bhedo vā'ṅgāṅgitve hetuḥ na viṣayacodanāto bhedaḥ । ato viṣayatvena bhinnānāmapi kārye
śabdāntarataivānuvandhahetuḥ ।</q> kaścitkaraṇānubandhaḥ kaścic‍cotikartavyatānubandha iti ।
asminnarthe bhāṣyaṃ yojayati&mdash;<q>bhāṣye bahuvacanādviṣayamedaḥ prātipadikātkāryānyatvam ।</q>
asyārthaḥ&mdash;samapradhānānīti bahuvacanaprayogāt karmabahutvamavagamyate । tatra yadyapi siddhānte'pi
bahutvamasti tathāpyubhayasamatāpekṣayā bahutvaṃ gṛhyate । tena viṣayabhedo bahuvacanena pratijñātaḥ﻿<pb n="r420"/>
tatra cābhyāsāditi hetuḥ । tathā samapradhānaprātipadikenāpi siddhānte yatkāryaṃ karaṇopalakṣaṇa-
mabhimataṃ tato'nyatvaṃ pratijñātaṃ tatra śabdāntaratvaṃ hetuḥ yādṛśenābhidhānenāṅgaṅgitvaṃ pratipādyate
kālasaṃbandhayāgaviṣayeṇādhikāragatena astinā tataḥ śabdāntaratvādyajeḥ sarvayāgaviṣayatvāt
sarvāṇi samapradhānāni । tadevaṃ saprayojanapūrvapakṣo bhāṣyakāreṇa darśita.। <q>tadidaṃ lakṣaṇā-
dābuk‍taṃ pradhānāpradhānāni parīkṣyante bhinnānyabhinnāni; pradhānānītyanena</q> bhāṣyeṇāṅgāṅgibhāvaḥ
saṃgṛhītaḥ <q>apradhānānīti viṣayaḥ</q> saṃgṛhītaḥ । etacca tatraiva vyākhyātam । atrābhi-
dhīyate&mdash;<q>prakṛtānāṃ karmaṇāmanuvaditārau paurṇamāsyamāvāsyāsaṃyuktau । kutaḥ ? viśeṣā-
vagamāt</q> ayaṃ viśeṣo'vagamyate pūrvasyāḥ śruteriyaṃ punaḥ śrutirgamyate āgneyāgnīṣomīyopāṃ-
śuyājānāṃ ya evaṃ vidvān paurṇamāsīṃ yajate iti punaḥ śrutiḥ । tathā āgneya&mdash;aindrāgna-
sānnāyyayāgānāṃ ya evaṃ vidvānamāvāsyāṃ yajate iti । <q>kasmāt ? uttaraṃ-kālasaṃbaddhā hīyaṃ
codanā ।</q> tatrāpi kimityāha-<q>yadyatna kālasaṃsparśo'rtho na gṛhyatekevasayāgamātravidhānamāsthīyate
tadā tadarthasya</q> tasyāṃ codanāyāṃ arthasya <q>grahaṇameva nāsti anyathā</q> kālāsaṃsparśino'rthasya-
<q>navagamāt yadi kālasaṃsparśo na gṛhyate tadā pūrvasyāḥ śruteḥ iyaṃ punaḥ śrutiḥ syaṣṭā ।</q>﻿<pb n="r421"/>
kuta ityāha&mdash;<q>kālayoginī hi sā śrutiḥ ।</q> na tadāgnoyāṣṭākapāla ityādirutpatttau kālaśrava-
ṇāt । yadi teṣāmivānuvaditārau tadā tatkālayogena nāmadheyatayā paurṇamāsyamāvāsyāśabdau
prayujyete । karmāntaratve tu pratipa(vṛ)tti nimittābhāvena nāmadheyatvānupapattiḥ । na ca kāla-
viśiṣṭakarmavidhiḥ dvitīyāntasya kālavidhānānanurupatvāt । saptamīśrutirhi kālavidhānādāvu-
citā । tenāgneyādiṣu kālavidhiḥ spaṣṭaḥ । na ca vācyaṃ karmāntaravidhipakṣe paurṇamāsyāṃ
paurṇamāsyāyā yajena amāvāsyāyāmamāvāsyāyā yajena iti kālavidhimāśritya nāmadheyaṃ bhaviṣyatīti
itaretarāśrayaprasaṅgāt । sati kālavidhau paurṇamāsītvaṃ paurṇamāsītve kālavidhirityutpattikālayo-
gināmevaṃbhūtakālavidhiḥ । tataśca pravṛttinimittaśūnyatā । <q>atha kasmānna viparītaṃ ?</q> paurṇa-
māsyā saṃyuk‍tau karmavidhiḥ tatrāgneyādibhiḥ kālavidhiḥ tataśca tatprasyatayā nāmatvamiti । uttaraṃ&mdash;na
bhavati viparītaṃ <q>agnyādeḥ</q> kālato <q>hyadhikasya</q> vidyamānatvāt । <q>tasmādāgne</q>yādīnāmeva
<q>punaḥ śrutiḥ ato'nuvādaḥ anuvādatvācca kārye śabdāntaratvādaṅgāṅgibhāvena bhedaḥ। atra
āgneyādīni payo'ntāni pradhānāni prayājādīnyaṅgāni iti । kiṃ punaḥ kāraṇam ? anu-
vāda eva prayājādīnyaṅgāni na punarvidhāvapi ।</q> vidhipakṣe'pi kasmāt aṅgāṅgitā na bhavati ?
samādhātā pṛcchati&mdash;<q>kathaṃ vā vidhipakṣe'ṅgāṅgitā śaṅkayate ।</q> ākṣeptottaramāha&mdash;<q>evamā-﻿<pb n="r422"/>
śaṅkayate-tayorhi paurṇamāsyāmamāvāsyāyāṃ vā vihitayoḥ karmaṇorvacanāntareṇa kālavidhānaṃ
paurṇamāsyāṃ paurṇamāsyā yajeta amāvāsyāyāmamāvāsyāyā yajeta iti। tataḥ kiṃ</q>?
bhavatvanayorapi karmaṇorvacanāntareṇa kālavidhānaṃ tathāpi kimityāha। uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>idaṃ tato
bhavati । aṣṭānāmapi yāgānāṃ darśapūrṇamāsaśabdavācyatā bhavati</q> kālayogasya vidyamānatvāt
<q>āgneyādiguṇavidhipakṣe vā dvayoryasmin</q> pakṣe āgneyādayo guṇavidhayastasmin pakṣe dvayoreva
yāgayoḥ darśapūrṇamāsaśabdavācyatā <q>ataśca tayoreva</q> dvayoryāgayoḥ <q>taṣāṃ vā</q> aṣṭānāṃ <q>phalasaṃbandhaḥ</q>
tān prati <q>prayājādīnāmaṅgataiva । tasmādanupapannamidaṃ vidhau samaprādhānyaṃ anuvāde'ṅgāṅgiteti ।</q>﻿<pb n="r423"/>
upapadavaśena yajerviseṣapravartitā vidhipakṣe'pyaviśiṣṭeti bhāvaḥ । <q>ucyate । na kālavidhirdvayoḥ
saṃbhabati ।</q> kutaḥ ityāha&mdash;<q>prayogaśeṣatā hi paurṇamāsyāṃ paurṇamāsyayā yajeteti pratīyate na
viṣayaviśeṣatā</q> sāṅgapradhānaśeṣatā kālayorna kevalapradhānaśeṣateti ekādaśe vakṣyāmaḥ । utpatti-
kālayoganimittaṃ ca darśapūrṇamāsābhyāmityupapannam । tataścānayordarśapūrṇamāsaśabdanāmābhidheyatvāt na
prādhānyam । atra codavati&mdash;<q>yadyapyanayorutpattikālayogābhāvena darśapūrṇamāsapadavācyatā
nāsti tathāpi darśapūrṇamāsābhyāmiti ghaṇṇāṃ darśapūrṇamāsaśabdavācyatā kena vāryate</q>
teṣāmutpattikālayogitvāt । tataśca ṣaṇṇāmeva phalasaṃbandhāt bhavatu prādhānyam । pariharati
&mdash;<q>anabhijño bhavān vidhyanuvādayoḥ śabdasāmarthyasya devānāṃ priyaḥ ।</q> yādṛśamanuvāde śabda-
sāmarthyaṃ tādṛśaṃ darśayati&mdash;<q>yathā'nuvādaṃ hi śakyate saṅkhayā'vagantum । tātparye ca
viśeṣataḥ ।</q> asyārthaḥ । ya evaṃ vidvān paurṇamāsīṃ yajate iti trayāṇāmanuvādaḥ । tathā ya evaṃ﻿<pb n="r424"/>
vidvānamāvāsyāṃ yajate iti ca trayāṇām । kasmātpunaḥ trayāṇāmevānuvādaḥ yāvatā rūpavatāṃ
sarvayāmānāmeva anuvādaḥ ubhayatra kimiti na bhavati ? upapadavaśeneti cet tadayuktam
yajiparatantratvānnāmabhāvasya paurṇamāsyamāvāsyāśabdābhyāmekavacanābhyāṃ yajau vartitatyaṃ tadyaji-
sāmānādhikaraṇyabalaina । yajiśca prakṛteṣu sarvayāgeṣu vartata iti tatsāmānādhikaraṇyena
ṇaurṇamāsyamāvāsyāśabdābhyāmapi teṣveva vartitavyam । daṇḍinyāyaścānusaraṇīyo vaiśvadeva-
śabdavat । na cānuvāde bhedena vṛttiḥ pramāṇābhāvāt । yadyapi bhinnānuvādau tathāpi ubhayatra
kṛtsnānuvāda eva yuktaḥ, vidhirhi bhidyamāno vidheyamapi bhindyāta, vihitasya vidhānānupapatteḥ anu-
vādaścānūditasyāpyupapadyate eva ।</p>
<p><q>atra ca prabhākaravayasaḥ pracakṣate ।</q> nārūpatayā'smābhiranuvādo'bhidhīyate dhrauvājyasya
dravyasya saṃbhavāt । <quote>‘bārtradhnī paurṇamāsyāmanūcyete’</quote> <quote>‘vṛdhanvatī amāvāsyāyāṃ’</quote> iti vihita&mdash;
mantralabdhayośca devatayorupapatteḥ rūpalābhāt । yathok‍taṃ taṃntravātiṃke&mdash;
<p><quote>‘dhrauvaṃ sādhāraṇaṃ dravyaṃ devatā māntravarṇikī’</quote></p>
iti । kintu kālasaṃbandhe yā codanā tatra yadi yāgavidhiḥ syāta tadā vidhīyamānayoryā-
gayeḥ kālasparśābhāvāt‍tu(na)hānameva syādityanuvādatve hetuḥ । kālasaṃbandhaścedanuvāde hetuḥ
yeṣāmeva kālasaṃbandhasteṣāmevānuvādaḥ tena siddhaṃ trayāṇāṃ trayāṇāṃ cānuvāda iti । taccaikena
yacchabdenānuvādātsamudāyāpatteḥ । anuvādadvayena samudāyadvayaṃ saṃbhavati । anuvāde dvayośca
paurṇamāsyamāvāsyāśabdayoḥ prasiddhakarmanāmadheyatayoradhikāravākye'nvayabhānāt yathānuvādaṃ adhi-
kārasaṃbandhaḥ । tatra ca darśapūrṇamāsābhyāmiti dvitvasaṃkhyā samudāyadvayaviṣayā śakyate'vagantum ।
viśeṣeṇa vā'nuvādasya tatparatve yathānuvādamevādhikārasaṃbandhaḥ । yasyārthādityevaṃparatve tena
saṃkhyāyogina upapadavaśādutpattiṃ upayogināmevādhikārasaṃbandha itīdṛśamanuvāde sabdasāmarthyam ।
vidhipakṣe śabdasāmarthyamāha&mdash;<q>atātparye ayathānuvāde ca na saṃkhyāyogina upapadavaśānniyamaḥ﻿<pb n="r425"/>
śakyate'vagantum rājasūyavat ।</q> vidhipakṣe hi na yathānuvādamadhikārasaṃbandhaḥ anuvādā-
bhāvāt । nāpi vidheridaṃ tātparyaṃ ya़thānūditānāmadhikārasaṃbandha iti । (satya) [dvitva]
niṣṭhatvādanuvādābhāvācca । tataścādhikāravākyagatena yajinā sarvayāgānāmevādhikārasaṃbandhāt
majisāmānādhikaraṇyena ca darśapūrṇamāsaśabdasya karmanāmadheyatvasya amunaiva kalpyamānatvāt
prakṛtānāṃ yāgānāṃ vahutvādaṅgasya (na)[ca] dvivacanānupapatteḥ militameva darśapūrṇamāsapadaṃ
dvivacanapratirūpakaṃ bahuvacanāntaṃ yajināmadheyaṃ syāt, na yajiviśeṣe'vasthāpayitumalam ।
(pravargya)[svavarga] nāmatvādvaiśvadevaśavdavata । kintu yāvadvarge vartate rājasūyaśabdavat । upa-
saṃharati&mdash;<q>tasmānna saṃkhyā nāpyupapadaṃ viśepāvagatau hetuḥ । ato dvayaṃ</q> (nā)dhātvarthānusari
<q>tatra</q> vidhipakṣe <q>bhabatīti yuktam ।</q> tatretare <q>guṇavidhaya iti yaduk‍taṃ pakṣopanyāse tadida-
mucyate । atha kasmādāgneyādīti guṇavidhānāni na bhavanti etau karmavidhī kasmānna</q>
bhavataḥ । śakyate cāsmin pakṣe saṃkhyānusāritayā dvayoḥ <q>prādhānyaṃ darśapūrṇamāsābhyāṃ
svargakāmo yajeteti ।</q></p>﻿<pb n="r426"/>
<p><q>codanā vā ।।</q> atrocyate । na guṇavidhiḥ saṃbhavati । <q>yadi tāvatpaurṇamāsyāṃ
aṣṭākapāle bhavatīti saṃbandho vivakṣitaḥ</q> paurṇamāsīyāgo'yamaṣṭākapālo bhavatīti tadā
<q>nāyamarthaḥ sattayā'bhisaṃvadhyate iti ।</q> tadeva vivṛṇoti&mdash;<q>bhavatyarthena na saṃbadhyata</q> ityarthaḥ ।
aṣṭākapāla āgneyo bhavatītyayaṃ tadā sambandho na bhavet aṣṭākapālapaurṇamāsīsambandhasya viva-
kṣitatvāt ubhayaparatve ca vākyabhedāpatteḥ । tathā ca vacanavyaktyantaraṃ dūṣayati&mdash;<q>athā''gneyaḥ
paurṇamāsyāṃ bhavatīti vivakṣyate tadāpyāgneyapuroḍāśayorasaṃbandha eva ।</q> atra codamati
<q>pūrveṇa sahāsya pakṣasya ko viśeṣaḥ ।</q> yena bhedena nirākriyate yāvatā pūrvameveti yuktaṃ ekasmin
sambandhe vidhīyamāne sambandhāntaraṃ vidhātuṃ na śakyate । uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>ayamasmin viśeṣaḥ guṇa-﻿<pb n="r427"/>
pradhānabhāvavivakṣā bhavati । bhavatu yatheṣṭamatra tathāpi parasparasaṃbandho naiva śakyate vidhātuṃ</q>
guṇabhūtā vā pradhānabhūtā vā dravyaṃ prati paurṇamāsī । bhavatu tathāpi dravyadevatayoḥ parasparasambandho
nāstīti tatra paurṇamāsyāmaṣṭākapālo bhavatīti paurṇamāsīprādhānyapakṣaḥ āgneyaḥ paurṇamāsyāmiti
guṇatvapakṣaḥ । <q>atha paurṇamāsyāmaṣṭākapālasyāgneyatā vidhīyata</q> ityekaḥ pakṣaḥ । atha
tasyāṃ paurṇamāsyāmiti guṇatvapakṣaḥ । atha <q>tasyāṃ</q> paurṇamāsyāmā<q>gneyasyāṣṭākapālatā</q> vidhīyata
ityaparaḥ pakṣaḥ <q>idamapi pakṣadvayaṃ avivakṣotsaṃkalanāya</q> paurṇamāsyāgneyatayā bhavatīti vā paurṇa-
māsyāmāgneyasyāṣṭākapālatā bhavatīti । evaṃ cāvivakṣāśritamiti avivakṣāṃ parigaṇayitumidaṃ
pakṣadvayamupanyastam na punarnirākaraṇahetubhedo vidyate ekasminnapi pakṣe nirākṛte aparo'pi pakṣo﻿<pb n="r428"/>
nirākṛto bhavati । <q>tasmādubhayatra paurṇamāsīpadasambandho duśśakaḥ ।</q> paurṇamāsyāmaṣṭākapālasyāgne-
yasya kenacidaprāptatvāt na tatsaṃbandho'nuvadituṃ śakyate । <q>atra bhāṣyaṃ</q> <quote>“atha pauṇamāsītyu-
bhābhyāṃ”</quote> iti, tadayuktamiva pratibhāti vākyāntaravihitapaurṇamāsīsaṃjñakakarmānuvādena aneka-
guṇavidhānāsaṃbhavāt vākyabhedāpatterityāśaṅkaya saṃbhāvanāyuk‍taṃ[k‍ti] balāda(na)nubhāṣate&mdash;<q>yadapi
padadvayamagniprajāpativat ṣaurṇamāsīsaṃbandhitayā vidhīyata(tamānatvami)ityupanyastamiti ।</q>
asyārthaḥ&mdash;yathā vākyāntaravihite'pi home ekavākyatābalena samāsadvandrārthamāśritya eka-
kārakabhāvenāgniprajāpatyorvidhānam tathā paurṇamāsyāṃ āgneyo'ṣṭākapālo bhavatīti yadupanyastaṃ
<q>tatrāpi saṃbhavati padadvayasya</q> kālopalakṣite karmaṇi <q>vidhānam । arūpatā tu pūrvavadeva
āgneyāṣṭākapālayoranyonyasaṃbandhābhāvāt ।</q> tadāgneyāṣṭākapālasyāha।[ghā]radravyamevo-
ditam । na devatā abhidhānābhāvāt । <q>pūrvavadarūpatā</q> ityanena <quote>“paraspareṇa dravyadeva-
tayoḥ saṃbandhaḥ syādi”</quote>ti bhāṣyaṃ vyākhyātam । aparamapi bhāṣyaṃ <quote>“atha dravyadevate paraspareṇa
viśiṣṭe satyau paurṇamāsyā saṃbaddhayeyātāmityucyate, ya āgneyo'ṣṭākapālaḥ sa paurṇamāsyāṃ bhavati”</quote>
iti । tadayuk‍tam । saṃbandhadvayavidhāne vākyabhedaprasaṅgāt । tathā hi&mdash;āgneyāṣṭākapāla-﻿<pb n="r429"/>
saṃbandho vidheyastathābhūtena ca saha paurṇamāsīsaṃbandha iti । tatra dṛṣṭāntabalenaikavākyatāṃ
darśayan bhāṣyārthamāha&mdash;<q>athāgnīṣomavatsaṃbandhayoḥ vidhānamityucyate ।</q> nirākaraṇamāha
&mdash;<q>kāryatvātsaṃbandhasya na vidhānādṛte</q> siddhiḥ <q>agnīṣomau tu prasiddhau dvandvatayā mitrā-
varuṇavallokata</q> eva prasiddhadvandvarūpatvādagnīṣomayoḥ dvandvārtho vidheyaḥ āgneyāṣṭākapālayostu saṃbandhaḥ
kārya iti spaṣṭo vākyabhedaḥ । anena <quote>‘tasyāṣyaprasiddhatvādetadapyayuk‍taṃ’</quote> iti bhāṣyaṃ vyākhyātam ।
<q>athātrāpi pūrvakṛtaḥ saṃbandhaḥ kenacitparigṛhyate ।</q> asyārthaḥ&mdash;kenacidagnaye yaḥ saṃkalpitaḥ
aṣṭākapālaḥ saḥ paurṇamāsyāṃ vidhīyate iti । <q>tathāpi saivārūpatā</q>, iha devatātvenāgnera-
