<q>vidhānāt ।</q> havirviśe, eva vihito bhavati । anena <quote>“atha kenacit agnaye saṅkalpitaḥ
paurṇamāsyāṃ vidhīyate tathāpi devatāyā avidhānādrūpābhāva eva”</quote> iti bhāṣyaṃ vyākhyātam ।
<q>athāgneya iti siddhavadvidhāya punarāgneyatvamucyate ।</q> asyārthaḥ&mdash;āgneyo'ṣṭākapālaḥ sa
paurṇamāsyāṃ bhavatīti siddhavadāgneyaṃ vidhāya punastasyaivāpyāgnaṃyatā vidhīyata ityucyate । nirā-
karoti&mdash;<q>na sakṛduccaritasyārthadvayaṃ saṃbhavati</q> sakṛduccaritasyāgneyaśabdasya siddharūpavidheyārthaḥ
yāgārthaḥ bhavati । anena <quote>“athāgnirdevatā bhaviṣyati iti kaścid‏brūyāt sa vak‍tavyaḥ mithaścā-
narthasaṃbandha iti । nahyāgneyaśabdo'nuvādo vidhiśca bhaviṣyati”</quote> iti bhāṣyaṃ vyākhyātam,﻿<pb n="r430"/>
<quote>“kalpayiṣyāmo devatāṃ”</quote> iti bhāṣyaṃ vyācaṣṭe&mdash;<q>atha rātrisatravadagnireva devatā kalpyeta ।</q>
nirākaroti&mdash;<q>na</q> kalpyate agnirdevatā <q>pramāṇābhāvāt ।</q> atha <q>rātrisatre tarhi kathaṃ</q> ārtha-
vādikapratiṣṭhākāmiviśeṣaṇaṃ kalpyata ityatrāha&mdash;<q>tatrārthavādānupapatteḥ</q> pratiṣṭhaivādhikāriviśeṣaṇaṃ
kalpyate । svarge hi kalpyamāne'rthavādasya pratiṣṭhāphalānuvādino'nupapattiḥ । tena tadānu-
guṇyena pratiṣṭhaiva kalpyate <q>iha tu dravyamātratayaivāgneyaśabdasyopapatteḥ</q> nāgnerdevatātvaṃ kalpyate ।
kathaṃ punardravyatayaivopapattirityatrāha&mdash;<q>na dravyaṃ devatāmapekṣate । devatā hi dravyāpekṣiṇī bhavati
dravyasaṃbandhitayaiva devatetyucyate ।</q> asyārthaḥ&mdash;anyatrāgnaye saṅkalpite dravye vihitapaurṇamāsyā-
mapi tasyārgnardevātātvavidhyanupapattiḥ । agnau tu devatāyāṃ vihitāyāṃ āgneyameva dravyaṃ vihitaṃ
bhavati anāgneye dravye agnerdevatābhāvānupapatteḥ । anena ca <quote>“na asati vidhāne devatābhāvāt
saṃvandhiśabdo'yaṃ devateti sa evāgniraṣṭākapālasya devatā nājyasya”</quote> iti bhāṣyārtho nibaddhaḥ ।
<q>tasmāt devatāvidhānārthaṃ dravyadevatāsaṃbandho vidhātavyaḥ sa cedvidhīyate siddhaṃ karmāntara-
tvam ।</q> karmāntarameva karmaṇo'stviti yo vadet taṃ pratyāha-<q>na caikaṃ karma karmāntarasya rūpaṃ bhavati﻿<pb n="r431"/>
iti bhāṣyaṃ vyākhyātamiti juhoteḥ <q>arūpatvāditi [siddho]hetuḥ । atha yaduk‍taṃ lakṣaṇeti</q> anena
<quote>“yaduk‍taṃ paurṇamāsyamāvāsyāśabdau lakṣaṇayā prakṛtān yāgānabhivadituṃ śak‍nuvantau nāñjasyena”</quote>
iti bhāṣyārtho darśitaḥ । <quote>“naiṣa doṣa”</quote> ityādeḥ parihārabhāṣyasyārthamāha&mdash;<q>pramāṇāntarāvagamānna-
doṣaḥ ।</q> pramāṇāntareṇa lakṣaṇāvagamānna doṣaḥ । <quote>‘vyapadeśaśca tadvat’</quote> ityanena sūtreṇa
<q>prayājādibhya āgneyādīnāṃ śabdāntaratāṃ kathayati</q> ugrāṇi hetyugraśabdaprayogādāgneyādīnāṃ
prādhānyamavagagyate । tacca prayājādibhyaḥ śabdāntaratve sati । tataḥ ugra(gṛhya)padena vyapadeśa-
pradarśanenāgneyādīnāṃ śabdāntaratvaṃ kathitaṃ <q>śabdāntaratvācca siddho guṇapradhānabhāvaḥ tadvacca
﻿<pb n="r432/">
liṅgadarśanaṃ</q> yathā samāhityā(ya) upadiṣṭaḥ tathaiva । liṅgadarśanaṃ <quote>‘caturdaśa paurṇamāsyāmāhutayo
hūyante iti । anena liṅgadarśanācceti sūtrasyārtho darśitaḥ iti । itiśabdaḥ passimāptau ।
parisamāpte'dhikaraṇe codayati&mdash;<q>kathaṃ punaḥ bahuṣvabhidheyeṣu ekavacanaṃ paurṇamāsīmiti ।</q>
anuvādatve bahūnāmanuvādo yukta ityarthaḥ । pariharati&mdash;<q>kiṃ kurmaḥ kamupālabhemahi ।</q> nityo'yaṃ
vaidikaprayogaḥ । <q>tatra tatra bahuṣvekavacanamiti jñātamasmābhiḥ ।</q> punaścodayati&mdash;<q>jñāname-
vedamamasiddham । ekavacanaśravaṇāt (yukti)yajirupapadaṃ(vat) ca ekasyaiva pratipādakamiti
yuktamabhyupagantum ।</q> pariharati&mdash;<q>satyaṃ yuk‍taṃ na tu tadiha śakyate yajyartha-
tulyatvāt paurṇamāsyarthatulyārthatvācca ।</q> arthasaṃbandhasya ca sarveṣāmāgneyādīnāṃ tulyatvāt
agṛhyamāṇaviṣayatve cāpratipattirvā syāt sarvāvagatirvā । evaṃ saṃśayaṃ kṛtvā nirasitumāha&mdash;<q>tatra
kiṃ yuk‍taṃ nāpratipattiryuktā avagamavirodhāt sarvāvagatestu</q> (anumāna) <q>svavagamānugrahaḥ</q>﻿<pb n="r433"/>
tena saiva yuktā । <q>nanu cātra</q> sarvāvagamapakṣepi <q>ekāvagamavirodhaḥ ।</q> pariharati
&mdash;<q>parihāryavirodhastvasau pracayāvagamāt ।</q> parihāryo'sau ekāvagamavirodhaḥ । ekasya
pracayasyāvagamāt tadapekṣayā ekatvenopapatteḥ । <q>apratipattau tu avagamavirodho'parihāryaḥ ।
tasmātsūktaṃ samudāyābhiprāyamekavacanamiti । atrāpi kāladvayāvacchinnapracayāvagamāt
śakyaparihāramevedaṃ dvitvam । tasmāt vidhānapakṣe'pyaṅgāṅgitaiva nyāyyā ।</q> atrābhidhīyate
&mdash;<q>saivātrānabhijñatā'parādhyate</q> yo'sau pūrvoktaḥ <quote>“anabhijño bhavān vidhyanuvādayoḥ śabda-
sāmarthyasya”</quote> iti । kathaṃ? <q>uttaraṃ-bahuṣu dhātoḥ prāptipadikasya vā prayogaḥ tantraṃ eka-
śeṣo vā ।</q> atra ca tantraikaśeṣayoḥ pṛthagupādānaṃ vādiprasiddhimātreṇa । paramārthataḥ tantrādeka-
śeṣasya na kaścidviśeṣaḥ । <q>ubhayatra</q> tantratve ekaśeṣatve vā <q>vighipakṣe darśapūrṇamāsābhyāmiti
dvitvavirodhaḥ । kathaṃ ? yadi tāvat tantratvaṃ ṣaṇṇāmeva hi pratīyate, na punaḥ trayāṇāṃ</q>
ṣaḍapyāgneyādayo yāgāḥ tantroccāritena yajinā pratipādyāḥ na punastantreṇeme traya ucyante ।
tantradvaye hi etatsyāt । na ca tantradvayamasti <q>tantradvaye hi dviruccāraṇaṃ yajeḥ syāt ।</q>﻿<pb n="r434"/>
na catadapyasti ।</q> tathāpi kimityāha&mdash;<q>ṣaṇṇāṃ ca tantratve pracayadvayāvagatau pramāṇāntaraṃ  mṛgyam</q>
nanu kāladvayayogenātra<note n="(1)"/> G. <dn>yogena nātra</dn></note>dvayāvagatirbhaviṣyatīti tatrāha&mdash;<q>ekābhidhānāddhi ekapracayāvagatiḥ ।</q>
ekāvagatyanupraveśena hi ekapracayāpattiḥ ekābhidhānena caikāvagatiḥ । na ca trayāṇāṃ trayāṇāṃ
ekābhidhānaṃ kintu ṣaṇṇāmevaikapracayaḥ । ato'pi dvivacanavirodhaḥ । anuvādapakṣe tu tadgata-
yajyabhidhānāt tenaiva samudāyopapatteḥ samudāyadvitayopapattirityuk‍tam । dvivacanena tu trayāṇāṃ
darśaśabdavācyatvāt trayāṇāṃ ca paurṇamāsīśabdavācyatvāt bhaviṣyati samudāyadvitayopapatti-
rityatrāha&mdash;<q>ākhyātānusāri ca nāmadheyamityuk‍tam ।</q> bhāvārthe niyoga iti vadatā viṣayabhūta-
bhāvārthasāmānādhikaraṇyena nāmateti । yeṣu ṣaṭsu ākhyā vartate sa teṣu darśapūrṇamāsa-
śabdo'pi samudāyataḥ ṣaṭsu vartate bhedena । <q>tasmāt kāladvayamapyasmin pakṣe pravṛtti-</q>
ni(vṛtti)<q>mittamātraupayikam nāmnaḥ</q> na punaḥ kālayoganimittenopapadena yajerviśeṣe'vasthānam ।
<q>yathā agnihotraśabde</q> juhoterviśeṣe'vasthānam <q>tadanvayi(samā)svārthābhidhānaṃ darśapūrṇamā-
sābhyāmiti yāgamātranāmatayā pratipattavyam ।</q> tulyārthatvāt pravṛttinimittasya ।
tataśca samaprādhānyaṃ sarvayāgānāmadhikārasaṃbandhāt । evaṃ tāvat tantrapakṣa uk‍taḥ । eka-
śeṣe'pyāha&mdash;<q>evamekaśeṣo'pyayaṃ ṣaṇṇāṃ na trayāṇāṃ trayāṇām । tasmāt pracayadvayāvagati-﻿<pb n="r435"/>
rdurlabhā vidhipakṣe ।</q> anuvādapakṣe punaḥ <q>trayāṇāṃ trayāṇāṃ tantraikaśeṣayoḥ pracavadvayāvagatau satyāṃ</q>
darśapūrṇamāsābhyāmiti vākye yajiśabdaḥ <q>pracayadvayasyaivāyamekaśeṣaḥ tantratvaṃ vā ।</q> pravṛtta-
nāmadheyavaśavartitvādyaceriti <q>siddho guṇapradhānabhāvaḥ ।</q></p>
<p><q>paurṇamāsīvadupāṃśuyājaḥ ।</q> nanu yadyapyanuvādāpavādatayā trīṇyapyetānyadhikaraṇāni
saṅgatāni tathāpi asyādhikaraṇasya kathamavāntarasaṅgatiḥ । na hi nānādhikaraṇārambho-
ghaṭate tatrāha&mdash;<q>uk‍taṃ caturdaśa paurṇamāsyāmāhutayo hūyante trayodaśāmāvāsyāyāmiti । tatra
yadyeka upāṃśuyājaḥ tadaitadupapadyate । atha tu trayāṇāmanuvādaḥ upāṃśuyājamantarā
yajatīti tadā caturdaśa paurṇamāsyāmiti na ghaṭate</q> ṣoḍaśatvāpatteḥ tadidaṃ﻿<pb n="r436"/>
pūrvok‍taliṅgaprasaṅgāt pūrvādhikaraṇānantaramidamadhikaraṇamāyātam । <q>kathaṃ punaratra saṃśayaḥ</q> ? uttaraṃ
&mdash;<q>atrāpi hyāgneyādayaḥ iba</q> viṣṇurupāṃśuyaṣṭavya ityevamādayaḥ <q>trayaḥ śrūyante । kiṃ teṣāmupāṃśu-
yājamantarā yajati iti samudāyānuvāda uta vidhiriti । nanu caikamidaṃ vākyaṃ</q> jāmi-
tādoṣopakramataḥ tannirharaṇaparyantam । <q>kathamatra saṃśayaḥ? । na hyekasmin vākye bahavo vidhayaḥ
saṃbhavanti bahutve vākyabhedaprasaṅgāt ।</q> uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>tadeva tvekavākyatvamākṣipyate ।</q> kathamā-
kṣipyate? uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>jāmi vā etadyajñasya kriyate ityupakramo'yaṃ viṣṇurupāṃśu yaṣṭavya ityeva-
mādīnāṃ sādhāraṇo'yamiti pūrvapakṣavādī manyate ।</q> asyārthaḥ&mdash;yadā tu rūpalābhāt viṣṇvādi-
vākyeṣu tāvadyāgo vidhīyate । na punarupāṃśuyājavākye । tadā tāvat traya evaite iti
yuk‍taṃ saṃśayābhi(dhayaḥ)dhānam । teṣāṃ sāvāraṇo'yamupakramo yajjāmi vā etadyajñasya kriyata iti ।
﻿<pb n="r437"/>
bhavati ca sādhāraṇo vākyaśeṣaḥ</q> viṣṇvādiṣu । tanūrvarṣiṣṭheti vākyaśeṣo yathā sādhāraṇaḥ tathā
'yamapītyarthaḥ । tathā etadbāhmaṇānyetāni havīṣi iti cātideśake vākye sādhāraṇa-
vākyaśeṣadarśanāt । <q>tasmāt</q> sādhāraṇyenāpi vākyaśeṣopapatteḥ <q>upapannassaṃśayaḥ । tatra
tāvat pūrvapakṣavādī manyate sādhāraṇo'yaṃ vākyaśeṣo nyāyyaḥ । kutaḥ? rūpāvacanāt</q>
upāṃśuyājamantarā yajatīti । viṣṇādivākyeṣu yāgānāṃ vidhistatraiva rūṇlābhāt । upāṃ-
śuyājamantarā yajatīti samudāyānuvādaḥ pūrvapakṣe'rūpatvāt । siddhe ca nyāyato vidhibhede
sādhāraṇyamupakramasyeti pṛrvapakṣavādī manyate । nanu <q>cāntarā yajatīti</q> antarālakṣaṇaḥ
kālo <q>rūpamasti ।</q> pariharati&mdash;<q>nedaṃ rūpaṃ karmaṇaḥ prayuk‍te syādapi</q> kālasya prayogāṅgatvāt
prayoga prati rūpatā na karmarūpaṃ prati । <q>evaṃ tarhi upāṃśuguṇaḥ śrūyate</q> sa rūpaṃ bhavatu ।
<q>nātra guṇavidhiḥ śakyate'dhvavasātuṃ yājayogāt ।</q> upāṃśu yajanamiti kṛtvā yadyupāṃ-
śuyājaśabdena yajisāmānādhikaraṇyena guṇo vidhīyate tadā yājaśabdayogo na syāt
kuta ityāha&mdash;<q>avayavārthavatve hyasya upāṃśuyāga iti rūpaṃ rūpavivido manyante</q> yajanaṃ yāga iti
ghañi cajoḥ kugdhiṇyatoriti kutvena bhavitavyam । tasmādyājaśabdayogāt avayavārthaśūnyamevedam
﻿<pb n="r438"/>
tasmādarūpatvāt ayamapyanuvādaḥ । evaṃ ca paurṇamāsyāṃ yajannityanena</q> vākyena <q>trayāṇāme-
vaitat</q> viṣṇvādivākyayāgānāṃ <q>kālatridhānam । tatraśca caturdaśa paurṇamāsyāṃ iti liṅgaṃ
duḥ stham । kiṃ punaḥ kāraṇaṃ guṇavidhipakṣe evatadrapaṃ na punaḥ nāmādheyapakṣe, uttaraṃ
-śabdāntaramapi hyupapannaṃ nāmadheyapakṣe śakyate vak‍tuṃ guṇavidhipakṣe punaḥ yajyartha eva yajiḥ ।</q>
tataśca kutvaprasaṅgaḥ । <q>nanu ca nāmadheyapakṣe'pi yajyartha evāyaṃ</q> śabdaḥ yajināmadheyatvāt ।
yadi na yajyarthaḥ śabdaḥ kastarhi yajyarthaḥ? uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>uyāṃśuyājaśabdaḥ ।</q> tathāpi kutatvaṃ na
bhavatītyāha&mdash;<q>yajyarthasya ca yajeḥ kutvaṃ smarati । na yajyarthāvayavasya</q> anaṅgasya
parataḥ kutvaṃ; yasmācca pratyayo vidhīyate tadaṅgam dhātośca paraṃ pratyaya iti । yajyarthasya ca yajeḥ kutvaṃ
yajyarthasamudāyāvayavasya adhātutvā<q>dupapadyate upāṃśuyāja iti nāmadheyam ।</q> natu guṇavidhiḥ
<q>yatra punaravayavayogāparityāganenaiva yajirnāmatvaṃ pratripadyate tatra bhavatyeva kutvam ।</q> tatra﻿<pb n="r439"/>
yajiḥ yajyartha eva vartamāno nāmadheyaṃ tatkutvaṃ prāpnotyeva । <q>tathā ca kutvāpavādaṃ smarati
bhagavān pāṇiniḥ । prayājānūyājau yajñāṅge iti ।</q> kathaṃ punaratrāpi yajiryajyarthaḥ yāvatā
prayājaśabda eva yajyartha(eva) ityatrāha&mdash;<q>nopasargā avayavāpahnavaṃ kartu samarthāḥ ānarthakyepyu-
pasargatvasya saṃbhavāt ।</q> yadi praśabdasahita eta yajiḥ yāgaṃ brūyāta tadā hyavayavāpahnavaḥ ।
yadā punaḥ yajiḥ naiva yāgārthaḥ praśabdo'narthaka eva pralaṃbata iti tattadā nāvayavārthāvagamaḥ
śakyate vak‍tum । <q>nanu ca kriyāyoge sati ānarthakyepyupasargayogyā; tatra</q> kā kriyā ?
uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>astyevāyaṃ kriyāyogaḥ yāja iti karmaṇa eva te nāmanī prayājānūyācāviti ।</q>
tena śabdo'yaṃ kriyāvācītyastyeva kriyāyogaḥ । yata evāvyutpanno'yamupāṃśuyājaśabdo jyartho
'yaṃ yajirna bhavati <q>ata evopāṃśuyāja iti nāpavādaṃ smṛtavān śabdavit । codanā
vā । atrābhidhīyate nātrānuvādaḥ saṃbhavati ।</q> kutaḥ ? uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>anṛdyamānasyāsaṃbhavāt ।</q>﻿<pb n="r440"/>
nanu ca viṣṇurupāṃśu yaṣṭavya iti yāgacodanāḥ santītyupanyastam ।</q> pariharati&mdash;<q>ayuk‍taṃ
tadupanyastam ।</q> kutaḥ ? uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>na hi vidhyantaramasmin vākye</q> saṃbhavati vākya-
śeṣasya śravaṇāt । <q>spaṣṭe hi vidhibhede vākyaśeṣasya sādhāraṇatā upapadyate na
punaḥ sādhye; vākyaśeṣasya sādhāraṇyādvidhayaḥ vidhitvena vākyaśeṣasya sādhāraṇya-
miti itaretarāśrayaṃ bhavati ।</q> nanu ca spaṣṭa evāyamatrāpi vidhibhedaḥ viṣṇvādiśravaṇa-
syārthavattānyathānupapatterityatrāha&mdash;<q>saṃbhavati ca vākyaśeṣatayā viṣṇvādīnāmarthavattā ।</q>
stutyarthenārthavattetyarthaḥ । nanu ekenaiva stuteḥ siddhatvāt itarayoḥ na kratṛpayoga ityatrāha&mdash;<q>upāṃ-
śuyājaman‍rā yajatītyanaina saṃbandhāviśeṣāt ।</q> sarveṣāmapi sabandhāviśeṣāt stutyaivārthavattā ।
nanu sākṣādvacanalābhāt dvitvādivākyeṣu spaṣṭa eva vidhibhedaḥ ityatrāha&mdash;<q>saṃbhavati caika-
vākyatve vākyabhedo vikalpārtha eva bhavati ।</q> ekavākyatvabalena viniścitaṃ rūpagrahaṇa
﻿<pb n="r441"/>
na nyāyyamiti bhāvaḥ । <q>nanu ca rūpaṃ nāsti</q> upāṃśuyājamantarā yajatītyuktam । pari-
harati&mdash;<q>vākyāntareṇāgnihotra iba maviṣyati । dṛśyante ca vākyāntarāṇi paurṇamasyāṃ
yajan । sarvasmai vā etadājyaṃ iti ।</q> tatra paurṇamāsvāṃ yajannityatra kālavidhipare'pi agnīṣo-
mau pratīyamānau rātrisatranyāyena devatātvena dṛśyete । sarvasmai vā etadājyamityājyaṃ
dravyaṃ bidhīyate । <q>kiñca na viṣṇurupāṃśu yaṣṭavya iti yāgavidhirgamyate upapada-
śravaṇāt raktapaṭavat ।</q> yathā raktaḥ paṭo bhavatīti paṭabhavanaṃ na pratipādyate kintu raktatā-
saṃbandhaḥ tathā'trāpi yāgo na vidhīyate kintu (vispaṣṭā)viṣṇvādisaṃbandhaḥ । <q>nanu copāṃśu-
yājamantarā yajatīti upapadaśravaṇamasti</q> tena tatrāpi tatsaṃbandhavidireva dṛśyate । pariharati
&mdash;<q>satyaṃ bhāvārthatā vidhiviṣayatayā'vagamyamānā na viniyogenākṣep‍tuṃ śakyate ।</q> viniyo-
gena padāntarasaṃbandhena bhāvārthatā pūrvāparībhūtasādhyārthatā'panetuṃ śakyate । yāgaḥ vidhiviṣayatayā-
'vagamyate bhavatyevāto vidhiviṣaya ityarthaḥ । yatra ha anyasya sādhyatvenāvagatistatra bhāvārtho na
sādhyatvenāvagamyate । kiṃ tarhi ? sādhanatvena, yathā vrīhīt prokṣatīti । yatra punaḥ sādhyāntaraṃ
nāsti tatra bhāvārtha eva sādhyatayā'vagamyate yatho somena yajena iti । tadiha viṣṇvādi-﻿<pb n="r442"/>
vākyeṣu karmatvena tavyapratyayaprayogāt viṣṇvādayaḥ sādhyatvenāvasīnte iti tatra bhāvārthasya
bhāvārthatā(na sādhyatā) । antarā yajatīti tu sādhyāntarābhāvāt bhāvārtha evāyaṃ sādhyaḥ । yatra
ca sādhyāvagatistatra vidhiviṣayatvaṃ <q>pradarśitam&mdash;<quote>“bhāvārthāḥ karmaśabdā iti । tacchūnye
punaḥ”</quote></q> sādhyabhūtabhāvārthe punaḥ <q>viniyogānusārī vidhirbhavatīti viśeṣaḥ ।</q> viṣṇvādi-
vākyānāṃ antarā yajatītyatra । <q>taduk‍taṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa</q> <quote>“sa tu vidhīyate upāṃśutvādisaṃba-
ndhaḥ”</quote> iti । atra kaścidāha&mdash;<q>nanu cātra bhāṣye</q> upāṃśuyājaśavdenaiva <q>upāṃśutvaguṇo vidhīyate</q>
upāṃśutvādisaṃbandho yāge vidhīyata ityabhidhānāt । pariharati&mdash;<q>na</q> pratīyate <q>ityucyate
arthavādato guṇaprāpteḥ ।</q> yadidamupāṃśusaṃbandhitvamucyate tadarthavādabale arthavāde upāṃśutva-
kīrtanāt upāṃśutvaguṇo'vagamyate, na punarupāṃśuyājaśabdenaivopāṃśutvaguṇo vidhīyate । anyataḥ
prāpteḥ <q>aguṇavidhisvarūpatvācceti</q> pratyuk‍taṃ guṇavidhānam । tenārthavādābhiprāyeṇaiva bhāṣyaṃ﻿<pb n="r443"/>
yojanīyam । <quote>‘kathaṃ’</quote> iti bhāpyaṃ ekabhāvaḥ iti pūrayitvā ākṣipati&mdash;<q>ko'bhiprāyaḥ ?</q>
uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>ayamabhiprāyaḥ ।</q> parasparāsaṃbandhādviṣṇvādīnāṃ <q>asaṃbaddhānāṃ ca parasparaṃ padāntara-
saṃbandhastantreṇaiva nyāyyo bhavati</q> ityatro<q>pādhyantaramasti</q> viśepaṇāntaramasti । <q>kiṃ tat ?</q>
uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>prādhānye satīti vaktavyam ।</q> tathā prādhānye sati parasparasaṃbaddhānāṃ padāntarasaṃbandhaḥ
tantreṇaiva bhavati na punarguṇabhūtānāṃ, yathā'ruṇādīnāṃ pratipradhāna padāntarānvaya ipyate na punaḥ
pratiguṇam । <q>iha punaḥ upāṃśuyājamantarā yajatīti pradhānaṃ tatprādhānye ca viṣṇurityeva-
mādīnāṃ aruṇādīnāmivaikavākyatā nyāyyetyuk‍taṃ</q> kathamekabākyatvamityatrākṣepe jāmivā
etadityupakramaṃ ityādinā bhāṣyeṇa । <quote>“kaḥ punaratrārthavāda”</quote> iti bhāṣyamākṣipati&mdash;<q>kenābhiprā-
yeṇāyaṃ praśnaḥ ? śrūyatām, yenābhiprāyeṇa, antarā yajatītyantarālasaṃbandhaḥ tāvat prāpta eva ।</q>
﻿<pb n="r444"/>
kiṃ punararthavādena kriyate? yadi hyarthavādādevāyamartho labhyate rātrisatrapratiṣṭhāvat tadā
yukto'rthavādaḥ । iha punaḥ antarā yajatītyevāntarālasaṃbandhāt kimarthavādeneti matvā tasya
praścaḥ</q> mandaṃ prayojanamarthavādenetyarthaḥ । <q>uttaravādī tu jāmitādoṣasaṃkīrtanāt tanni-
rharaṇaprayojanādapi bhavatyevārthavatteti pradarśitavān ।</q> anantarayoḥ puroḍāśayoḥ karaṇe
jāmitādoṣo bhavati so'ntarākriyamāṇenopāṃśuyājena nirhaṇyate ityarthavādena pradarśyata iti
prayojanamarthavādasya । <q>tasmānnānanvayāśaṅkā vidyate ।</q> <quote>“kathaṃ punaḥ viṣṇvadayo yaṣṭavyā
ityetadavagamyate”</quote> iti bhāṣyaṃ vyācaṣṭe-<q>aucitvena stutiruktā । na cāprāptānāṃ</q> viṣṇvādīnāṃ
<q>aucityamastīti manvānaḥ kathaṃ punarviṣṇvādayo yaṣṭavyā iti pṛṣṭavān । ayaṣṭavyānve-</q>
tyuttaravādī vadati । tasyārthavādamāha&mdash;<q>na stutau pramāṇāntarāpekṣetyabhiprāyaḥ uttaravādinaḥ</q>
stutau kīrtyamānatyārthasya na pramāṇāntarāpekṣetyarthaḥ । <q>nanu ca nirālambanataivaṃ prāpnoti yadi﻿<pb n="r445"/>
viṣṇvādayo na yaṣṭavyāḥ । pariharati&mdash;<q>mṛgyatāṃ stutyanantarakālamavalambanaṃ mukhyayā gauṇyā vā
vṛttyā na punarnimittāpekṣaṃ kāryaṃ</q> nimittāni padānyapekṣamāṇasyaiva kāryaṃ na kalpanīyam ।
kārye hi nimittāvagatirityuktam । stutikāryamavagamya nimittavarṇanā kārye mukhyayā gauṇyā vā
vṛttyā abhidhānavṛtterapi tātparyavṛtterbalīyastvāt iti ।</p>
<p>atra codayati&mdash;<q>bhavatu kāryāt</q> stutirupā<q>nnimittāvagatiḥ tathāpi nimittabhāvo
vaktavyaḥ ।</q> uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>so'bhidhīyate । atra kecidāhuḥ viṣṇvādayaḥ prāptā eveti । kutaḥ ?
śākhāntaravidhānāditi । sarvaśākhāpratyayamekaṃ karmeti coktam । tathāpi śākhāntare
prāptiḥ nopalabhyate । tathāpi yāgasya coditatvāt devatākāṅkṣatvācca tasya devatāviśeṣā-
pekṣāyāṃ vākyaśeṣādapyavagatiḥ bhavatyeva ।</q> asyārthaḥ&mdash;yāge codite devatāyāṃ cāśrutāyāṃ
tatsādhyatvādyāgasyetyetasyāścālaukikatvāt viśeṣāpekṣāyāṃ vākyaśeṣabalenopasthāpitā devatā
devatātvaṃ pratipadyate । yajireva tadanvitasvārthapuktetyarthaḥ <q>(yūktyartam) । kathaṃ punarvā-
﻿<pb n="r446"/>
kyaśeṣabalena devatopatiṣṭhate ?</q> uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>upāṃśuyājavākye upāṃśutvaṃ kīrtyamānaṃ tāvat
taddharmatvena svīkriyate । anyathā hi tat pākṣikaṃ syāt । nityavacca tadanūdyate । tatra yau
pramāṇāntareṇopāṃśuyāja(na)dharmāṇau viṣṇuprajāpatī tāveva buddhisthau svadharmanirdeśādbhavata
iti tayorevānvitābhidhānānupraveśa iti । nanu ca vākyaśeṣopanyāso yatkiñcitprājā-
patyamityayaṃ na yuktaḥ ।</q> asmin hi vākyaśeṣe yatprājāpatyaṃ tadupāṃś‍veva kartavyaṃ ityavagamyate
tena prājāpatyatve siddhe upāṃśutvaprāptiriti । atrocyate । sā cāyuktā । pūrvok‍tena nyāyeno&mdash;
pāṃśutvaprāpterdarśitatvāt । ākṣepāntaraṃ cāha&mdash;<q>upāṃśutvasāmānyaṃ</q> ca viṣṇuprāptihetu<q>mupanyasya
viṣṇormantropanyāsopyatiricyate ।</q> yanmantrabalena viṣṇoḥ prāptatvamucyate tadapyatirikta-

tayopanyasyate ।</q> upāṃśutvaprāpakatayā nedamupanyasyate yatkiñcitprājāpatyamiti । <q>kintu
(yadyayaṃ) tasyaiva dāḍharyārthaṃ</q> yattadupāṃśutvaṃ arthavādaprāptaṃ vipṇuprājāpatāvetanniyāmakamupanyastam ।
tasyaiva tatprāprakatve dāḍharyārthaṃ balavattvasiddhayarthaṃ yatkiñcitprājāpatyamiti bākyaśeṣopanyāso veṣṇava-
﻿<pb n="r447"/>
mantropanyāsaśceti dvayam । etadeva darśayati&mdash;<q>viṣṇormantraviśeṣāmnānaṃ prajāpateśca vākyā-
ntare</q> upāṃśuyāje viṣṇuprajāpatī devate itītye<q>vamupapadyate ।</q> nānyathā । tena tayoratra
devatātvam । <q>ag‍nīṣomayostu vidhāyakaṃ udāhriyata eva <quote>‘tāvabrūtāmagnīṣomāvājyasyaiva
nāvupāṃśu paurṇamāsyāṃ yajan</q> iti bhāṣyamākṣipati&mdash;<q>kimidamagnīṣomayorvidhāyakaṃ iti ।</q>
ayuktametadityarthaḥ । samādhātaikadeśyāha&mdash;<q>kiṃ jātaṃ ?</q> yadi vidhāyakayiti । ākṣe-
tā''ha&mdash;<q>idameva jātaṃ viṣṇvāderaprāptiḥ ।</q> uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>aprāptaviśeṣaṃ hi vākyamarthavādādviśeṣaṃ
labhate rātrisatravat । vihitaviśeṣaṃ punaḥ nirākāṃkṣatvānna saṃvadhyate</q> arthavādāmihitena darśa-
pūrṇamāsayorivārthavādārthena balena । paramasamādhātā āha&mdash;<q>evaṃ tarhi agnīṣomayostu kathaṃ</q>
prāptiriti śaṅkāyāmuttaraṃ&mdash;<q>yasmādvidhāyake vākye udāhriyete</q> evāgnīṣomau iti prāptiḥ ।
<q>kasya vidhāyake ?</q> uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>paurṇamāsyāṃ yajanniti kālasya</q> va़idhāyake । bhāṣye ca
﻿<pb n="r448"/>
vidhāyakaśabdo na prathamāntaḥ । kintu sa saptamyanta iti । atra bhāṣyaṃ <quote>“yasyāyaṃ guṇa upabaddhaḥ
upāṃśupaurṇamāsyāṃ yajan”</quote> iti tadapyayuktaṃ kālo hyanena guṇa upabadhyate । na ca tarhi akarma-
rūpatvamastītyāśaṅkayāha&mdash;<q>yaduk‍taṃ arūpatvāditi parihṛtaṃ vacanāntaravihitatvāt rūpasyeti ।
tadidaṃ</q> vacanāntaraṃ <q>bhāṣyakāreṇa pradarśyate upāṃśu paurṇamāsyāṃ yajannityevamādinā ।</q>
tenāyaṃ bhāṣyārthaḥ yasyāyaṃ guṇa upabadhyate paurṇamāsyādiḥ upāṃśu paurṇamāsyāṃ yajannityevamādi-
bhirvākyauḥ yathā cārthadevatāsamarpakatvaṃ tathok‍tam । atra bhāṣyaṃ <quote>“yathā'gryaprāye likhitaṃ”</quote> ityeva
mādi tadākṣipati&mdash;<q>kimidamagrayaprāya iti ।</q> uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>idamidaṃ pradhānaprāye darśanaṃ upāṃ-
śuyājasyetyarthaḥ ।</q> punarākṣipati&mdash;<q>nanu cānuvādapakṣe'pi prādhānyaṃ kena vāryate</q> <quote>“paurṇamāsyāṃ
yajam”</quote> iti kālayogāt । yadyapi viṣṇvādiguṇakānāṃ yāgānāmupāṃśuyājamantarā yajatītyanu-
vādaḥ tathāpi kālayogārthaḥ, evaṃ vidvānityanuvādāt । anūditānāṃ cāghikāraṇogāt﻿<pb n="r449"/>
prādhānyaṃ kena vāryate । parataraṃ vā'grayaprāye darśanam । <q>athāyamabhiprāyaḥ tāvavrūtāmag‍nī-
ṣomāvityarthavādadarśanāt</q> (eka)[ta]syaiva kālayoga iti । tenāgnīṣomīyasyaiva prādhānyam
netareṣām । etadapyayuktam । <q>agṛhyamāṇaviṣayaviśeṣatvāt kālayogasya upāṃśuyāja-
mantarā yajanniti</q> sarvathā anuvādā<q>rthavādasya ca daṇḍinyāyenāpyupapatteḥ ।</q> tenāgnīṣo-
mādayo rūpaṃ ājyasyaiva na ityarthavādasyārthaḥ । yuktyantaraṃ cāha&mdash;<q>agrayaśabdasya caikenāpyupapa-
nnatvāt ।</q> pradhānabhṛtenāgnīṣomīyarūpeṇopāṃśuyājenāpi agryaprāyadarśanamupapadyata eveti na
siddhāntasiddhau liṅgam । samādhatte&mdash;yasyāt ayaṃ tvayā doṣa uktaḥ <q>tasmādayamabhiprāyo</q>
bhāṣyakārasya viṣṇurupāṃśu yapṭavya ityetasmin <q>vidhāne</q> hyabhyupagamyamāne <q>guṇavidhibhūtasya
yajervidhiḥ ।</q> tasya pratyayayogena guṇakarmāvagateḥ । <q>tataśca nādhikārayogyatā karmaṇaḥ</q>
yasmāduktaṃ <q>na saṃskārāḥ adhikāramarhanti</q> iti । <q>ataścāgrayaprāye darśanaṃ nopapadyate iti ।
antarā yajatīti punarbhāvārthasya prādhānyāvagateradhikārayogyaprāyadarśanamupapannaṃ bhavati ।
tasmānnānuvādo'yaṃ</q> <quote>“upāṃśuyājamantarāyajan”</quote> iti । <q>kiṃ tarhi? vidhiriti । evaṃ caikatvā-
dupāṃśuyājasya caturdaśapaurṇamāsyāmāhutayo hayanta iti sustham ।</q></p>
﻿<pb n="r450"/>
<p><q>āghārāgnihotram ।</q> pūrvapakṣāmāha&mdash;<q>uktaṃ bhāvārthāḥ karmaśabdā niyogasya viṣayatāṃ
pratipadyanta iti । yatredānīṃ guṇavidhayaḥ tatra kathaṃ bhāvārthatvaṃ</q> vidhitsitayordravyaguṇaśabdayoḥ
abhāvārthatvāt । ekagranthenāha&mdash;<q>tasmātsarvatrākhyātārthavidhānaṃ prāptaṃ dadhnā</q> juhotītyeva-
<q>mādiṣu । yadyevaṃ</q> sarvatrākhyātārthavidhānaṃ <q>kathaṃ tarhi agnihotraṃ juhotīti samudāyānuvāda-
śaṅkā ।</q> yāvatā <q>sarvatraiva dhātvarthavidhānaṃ aviśeṣācca karmabhedhaḥ ।</q> atrocyate ।
﻿<pb n="r451"/>
<q>dadhnā juhotīti guṇavati śabdo bartate</q> kriyākārakasaṃbandhāta dadhnā juhotītyatra guṇavān
bhāvārthaḥ pratīyate । <q>tataḥ kiṃ ? uttaram&mdash;idaṃ tato bhavati guṇavadvidhānaṃ dadhnā juhotītye-
vamādiṣu ।</q> nanu guṇadvidhāne kathaṃ bhāvārthaviṣayatvaṃ vidheḥ ityatrāha&mdash;<q>guṇavadvidhāne'parityakta-
bhāvārya evavidhiḥ । evaṃ ca sati śakyate'gnihotraṃ juhoti iti punaḥ śrutiḥ vak‍tuṃ dadhnā
juhotītyevamādīnāṃ, nirguṇatvādagnihotrapadārthasya</q> nirguṇāt‍tu guṇavataḥ punaḥ śrutiḥ śakyate
vak‍tum । natu saguṇānnirguṇasya punaḥ śrutirupapadyate guṇasaṃbandhasyānyathānavakalpanāt ।</p>
<p><q>nanu ca guṇavacanatā vidyate'gnihotrapadasya । satyaṃ vidyate । na juhotītyasya
sakalenāgnihotra(sya) padenāyaṃ tadvān pratīyate ।</q> tathāpi kimityāha&mdash;<q>matvarthaścā-
gnihotrapadārthaḥ । ato na matvarthena tadvān pratipat‍tuṃ śakyate</q> kevalena guṇena tadvattā
bhavati । na punaḥ guṇavattā(yatta eva ca na)[pan‍nena]matvarthena tadvattā bhavati । <q>ata eva ca
śabdavidbhiruditaṃ na matubantānmatubutpadyata iti । tasmānnaṣṭāvayabamapyavacchedakāvayavavat</q>﻿<pb n="r452"/>
daṇḍinyāyena sarvajuhotīnāṃ nāmaivaitat <q>vaiśvadevaśabdavat ।</q> ataḥ <q>samudāyānuvādo'yaṃ
agnihotraṃ juhotīti । nanu guṇavān vihitaḥ na guṇaḥ abhāvārthatvād‌guṇasya ।</q> tataśca
guṇopādānāsaṃbhavāt anarthako guṇaśabdaḥ । pariharati&mdash;<q>mābhūd‌guṇavidhānaṃ, tadviśiṣṭatā tu
nāpaṃhnotuṃ śakyate viśiṣṭasaṃpattyarthamabhāvārthānāmapyupādānaṃ na viruddhayate ।</q> nanvevaṃ tarhi
agnihotraṃ juhotīti karmavidhirastu । dadhnā juhotītyevamādibhiścāsyaiva karmaṇo guṇasaṃbandhaḥ
pratyāyyatāmityāha&mdash;<q>yasya punaragnihotraṃ juhotīti karmavidhiḥ tasya</q> vādino mate <q>dadhnājuho-
tīti vihitasyaiva guṇavattā pratīyate । tataśca</q> vihitasya karmaṇo vidhānānupapatteḥ <q>guṇa-
mātrāvaśeṣāt</q> guṇamātrasyāpi vihitasya śravaṇāt । tasya ca vihitatvasya ca śravaṇāt
tasya ca vidhiviṣayatvānupapatteḥ <q>avidhāyakānyetāni bhavanti । guṇavataśca kevalasya vihita-
tvāt upādānamapi guṇānāṃ na siddhayati । guṇavattvapratītirhi vidhiśūnyaiva tadāpyastu ।
atha guṇavidhānamapyāśrīyate</q> vihite karmaṇi tadvidhānāsaṃbhavāt guṇa eva kevalo vidhīyate ।
dūṣayati&mdash;<q>bhāvārthebhyaḥ kriyā pratīyata iti viruddhaṃ</q> bhāvārthādapi guṇāt kevalāt kriyā
pratīyata ityabhyupagamāt । yadā dravyaguṇebhyopi kriyā pratīyate tadā <q>nāmanāmivyavahāro&mdash;
cachedaśca bhavati । bhavatviti cet ।</q> bhavatu abhāvārthādapi vidhiḥ bhavatu ca nāma-
﻿<pb n="r453"/>
nāmivyavahāroccheda iti cet । dūṣayati&mdash;<q>nākarmaṇi guṇe niyogaḥ śakyate</q> sādhya-
viṣayābhiprāyasvarūpā kṛtiḥ tadāyattaḥ kāryātmā niyoga iti <q>viṣayakaraṇīye</q> darśitam ।
<q>tasmān‍nyāyyaṃ vacanaṃ bhāvārthebhyaḥ kriyā pratīyata iti । nyāyyaṃ cābhyupagamena na śakyate
bādhitum । ato dadhnā juhotītyeva vidhānamabhyupagantuṃ yuktam । upādānenāpi tāva-
d‌guṇaśruterarthavattā bhavatvityevamarthaṃvihiteṣu ca guṇavatsu nirguṇā punaḥ śrutiḥ ।</q> sā
nirguṇā teṣāmeva punaḥ śrutiḥ । <q>kathaṃ punarguṇavatsu nirguṇā punaḥ śrutiḥ</q> yadi hi sā
viguṇā syāt tadā bhaved‌guṇavataḥ punaḥ śrutiḥ aguṇā ca na tu guṇavataḥ punaḥ śrutiḥ saṃbhavati ।
uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>bhāvārthamātraparyavasāyī vidhirityuktam ।</q> yatrāpi guṇavadvidhānaṃ tatrāpi bhāvārtha-
mātraparyavasāyyeva vidhiḥ nirguṇaṃ spṛśatyapi । <q>tasmādvidheyatvena punaḥ śrutiḥ</q> nanu yadyapi
bhāvārthamātra eva vidhiḥ abhidhānaṃ tu guṇa eva kathamanuvāda ityatrāha&mdash;<q>vidhyapekṣaścāyamanu-
vādaḥ nābhidhānāpekṣaḥ ।</q> nanu ca nāviniyuk‍taṃ <q>punarupādīyate ।</q> asyārthaḥ&mdash;tārtīya-
viniyogapūrvako hi cāturthaḥ udgātrādīnāṃ vyāpāraḥ viniyogaśca vidhivyāpāraḥ । avidheyaśced‌guṇaḥ
nūnamaviniyuktaḥ aviniyuktaścet kathamupādīyata iti । pariharati&mdash;<q>kena cok‍taṃ avini-
yukta iti ।</q> viniyogaḥ parasparaṃ saṃbandhaḥ sa guṇasyāpi vidyata iti viniyukta eva guṇaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="r454"/>
punaścodayati&mdash;<q>anabhiprāyajño bhavān । etaduk‍taṃ bhavati-nāviniyuktaṃ vidhīyate nāvihita-
mupādīyate ।</q> asyārthaḥyatsabaddhamavagamyate tadvidhīyate yacca vidhīyate tannāgrimaviniyogena
viniyujyate । tadeva copādīyate । kasmātpunaḥ vihitameva viniyujyate ityatrāha&mdash;<q>vidhyartha
eva</q> hi <q>viniyogo na viśeṣaṇamarthaḥ</q> vidhirūpo'rtho viniyoga ityarthaḥ । viśeṣaṇarūpastvartho
viniyogo na bhavati । nanu vināṣi vidhitvaṃ tadvattaiva viniyogamāpādayatāṃ ityatrāha&mdash;<q>tadvattā ca
viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyatāmāpādayati naidamarthyam ।</q> aidamarthyalakṣaṇaśca saṃvandho viniyogaḥ
sa vidhivyāpāramantareṇa na bhavati tadvattāmātreṇa ।</p>
<p><q>nanu gomāniti gavāṃ gomadarthatā pratīyate</q> tena ntadvattāpyaidamarthyamāpādayatyeva ।
pariharati&mdash;<q>śarāvatyādiṣu</q> satyapi tadvattve <q>aidamarthyasyādarśanāt ।</q> yatastadvattā aidamarthyaṃ
nāvagamayati <q>tasmādgomati pramāṇāntaratastāvadaidamarthyaṃ mṛgyam । ṣaṣṭhayā tādarthyamiti cet</q>
śarāvatyāṃ saptamyarthe matup tena mābhūt tatra tādarthyaṃ ṣaṣṭhayā tu matupi tādarthyaṃ bhaviṣyatīti cet
dūṣayati&mdash;<q>mātṛmān pitṛmān ityanaikāntyāt ।</q> ṣaṣṭhayarthotpanno matum pitṛmānityatra । tā-
darthyādarśanāt ekāntaḥ ṣaṣṭhayāpi tādarthyāvagame'pi nāsti । <q>ucyate&mdash;aviniyuktasyāpi
śeṣatā nāsti asti śeṣatve aidamarthya mābhūta ।</q> tadvināpi vidhivyāpāraḥ śeṣatāyāmasatvāt
﻿<pb n="r455"/>
aidamarthyaṃ dadhyādermābhūt <q>upādānaṃ punaḥ viśeṣaṇatvāvagamapūrvakameva yathā paś‍vekatvasya paśu-
nā yajeteti</q> aviniyuk‍tasyāpi viśeṣaṇatvāvagamamātreṇopādānam tathā'trāpi ।
<q>nanu paś‍vekatvaṃ viniyuk‍tapaśuviśeṣaṇaṃ ata upādīyate viniyuktasyopādeyatvāt
dadhyādestu kathamupādānaṃ ?</q> pariharati&mdash;<q>dadhyādyapi viniyuktaviśeṣaṇameva । karmaṇo vini-
yuktatvāt phale na</q> svaviṣayatvāt । yadi paś‍vekatvatulyaṃ dadhyādi <q>evaṃ tarhyupādānaśeṣaṃ
dadhyādi ।</q> ṣariharati&mdash;<q>bhabatu na kaściddoṣaḥ । yathaiva hi dravyaliṅgasaṅkhyāśūnyaṃ vini-
yuktamapi nopādātuṃ śakyate ityekatvādaya upādīyante evaṃ karmāpi na kārakaviśeṣaśūnya-
mastīti dadhyādyupādānasiddhiḥ ।</q> yadi viśeṣaṇamātrameva dadhyādi <q>kimiti tarhi anyopādāne
vaiguṇyaśaṅkā ।</q> uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>upādānaśeṣamapi śeṣamevetyadoṣaḥ । nanu cāsminnapi pakṣe paśvā-
dīnāmapi naiva vidhānaṃ</q> tat kathamekatvasya viniyuktaviśeṣaṇatvam ? pariharati&mdash;<q>omityucyate
﻿<pb n="r456"/>
nāstveva paśvādīnāmapi vidhānam । yadi nāsti <q>kathaṃ tarhi paś‍vekatvamiveti pradarśitam ?</q> pari-
harati&mdash;<q>abhyupagamya</q> guṇavidhi<q>metatpradarśitam । yathā satyapi guṇavidhau</q> (hetva) siddhāntitaṃ
bhavanmate <q>aviniyuk‍tasyaiva paś‍vekatvasyopādānam tadvad‍dadhyāderiti ।</q> eva paś‍vekatvamiveti
pradarśitam । atra codayati&mdash;<q>tadevedamāpatitam</q> yattulyamatakathāsu śrūyate <q>ghoṭārūḍhasya
vismṛto ghoṭa iti</q> karmakartari rūpaṃ vismṛtaścittādapakrāntaḥ । etadeva darśayati&mdash;<q>vighe-
ścāviṣayā guṇā</q> guṇavidhinopādīyanta iti vidhinopādīyamānatvāt vidhiviṣayatvame yukta-
miti bhāvaḥ । pariharati&mdash;<q>atrābhidhīyate mugdhaḥ khalvasi kāryopādānaviśeṣajñāne ।</q>
niyogaḥ kāryaśabdenocyate । upādānaśabdena copādīyata ityupādānamiti kṛtyalyuṭo bahula-
miti liṭ vidheyamupādeyaṃ ca vivinakti । <q>yatra niyuṅk‍te</q> tatkāryavattayā vidhiḥ bodhayati
tadvidheyam । <q>tatsiddhaye yadupādīyate tadupādānaṃ</q> tadupādeyamityarthaḥ । <q>viniyoge cā-
viṣayatā nāmārthasyoktā । na punarviṣayaṃ pratyakārakatāpi</q> tena tatsidhyarthaṃ yuktaṃ tasyaivo-
pādānaṃ vyaktam । <q>nanu copādānamapi vidhervyāpāra eva vidhervyāpāratvāccopādānasya</q>
tatsaṃbandhāt <q>kimiti niyogaviṣayatāṃ</q> dadhyādi na <q>pratipadyate</q> eva । arthānubandhāva-
﻿<pb n="r457"/>
cchinno vidhiḥ nāmārthaviṣayo bhavati <q>anyathā</q> hi yadi viṣayāntarāvacchinno niyogo viṣayānta-
raviṣayaḥ <q>syāt tadā śāptrabhedāmedau durbhaṇau syātām ।</q> viṣayabhedena śās‍trabheda iti pratijñā ।
anyatra bhāvena ca viypayasyānavacchedakatve bhāvārthasya vidhiviṣayatvāyogāt । <q>tasmādviśeṣā-
vagatireva viśeṣasyopādānamākṣipati । na punaḥ (vi) niyogastamāskandati dravyopādāna
miva ।</q> na viniyu'jyante dravyādayaḥ kintūpādīyante kevalaṃ yathā ekatvādayo(vratayatayo) na
katau viniyujyante kintu kratusidhyarthamupādīyante । <q>tadidameva nyāyyaṃ dadhnā juhotīti viṣayaḥ ।
agnihotraṃ juhotīti samudāyānuvāda iti । saṃjñopabandhāditi kimabhyadhikamucyate ।</q> samādhatte-
uttaraṃ-<q>idamabhyadhikam ।</q> ākṣepamāśaṅkaya pariharati&mdash;paribhāṣā codīyata ityarthaḥ । kaḥ punaḥ ākṣepa
ityatrāha-<q>prakṛtebhyaḥ saṃjñāto'nyatvaṃ pratīyata ityabhaprāyaḥ । saṃjñāhi śrūyamāṇaiva prakṛtebhyo-
'nyatvamāpādayatyeva&mdash;athaiṣa jyotirityevamādiṣu</q> saṃjñāto'nyatvadarśanāt । tenāgnihotra-
ghārasaṃjñāśravaṇāt prakṛtebhyo dadhihomādibhyo'nyatvamavagamyate kathaṃ samudāyānubāda iti ।
parihāramāha&mdash;<q>satyamevaṃ</q> saṃjñāto'nyatvamiti kintu <q>viśeṣāvagatau satyāṃ jyotirādiṣu tu
sahasradakṣiṇādiviśiṣṭā viśeṣā avagamyante । na tatheha viśeṣāvagatiḥ teya</q> saṃjñāto-
'nyatvaṃ nāsti । <q>nanu vijñāyata evātrājyāghārahomau kriyāntarebhyo viśiṣṭau ।</q> tena﻿<pb n="r458"/>
viśeṣaniṣṭhā saṃjñā ghaṭate'nyatve'pi । pariharati&mdash;<q>yadyevaṃ lokata eva tarhi vijñātau</q> homāghārau
<q>kimatna vidhiḥ kariṣyati</q> homamātrasya cāghāramātrasya ca prāptatvānna vidheyatvam । yadi-
homamātrasya cāghāramātrasya ca saṃjñā syāt tadā sā <q>guṇaphalopabandheṣu saṃjñā niṣprayojanaiva</q>
juhotyāghārayati dvābhyāmapi guṇaphalopabandhasiddheḥ । <q>atha viśiṣṭasya</q> homasyāghārasya cā-
gnihotrāghārasaṃjñā <q>vācikā</q> tena guṇaphalopabandhanenārthavattvenetyucyate dūṣayati&mdash;<q>uktaṃ</q> taharyatra
samudāyātuvādakatvaṃ <q>prakṛtebhyo na viśeṣāntaramavagabhyata iti</q> hetoḥ । api cāgnihotraṃ
juhoti ādhāramāghārayatīti <q>kriyāvidhānapakṣe guṇakarmavidhānaṃ prāp‍noti dvitīyāntatvānnāmnaḥ ।</q>
agnihotrādiprātipadikasya pradhānasamarpakatvāvagateḥ । <q>tataśca nāmadheyānupapattiḥ ।। (atra pāta):</q>
﻿<pb n="r459"/>
﻿<pb n="r460"/>
﻿<pb n="r461"/>
yathaiva hi viniyojyasthatvādaviniyojyamupādeyaṃ</q> bhavati <q>evameva vidheyamapi bhavati</q> yathā
dadhnā juhotītyevamādiṣu karmavidhipakṣe viniyojyasthatayāpi dadhyādeḥ śeṣatvamupādeyatvaṃ ca । tathā
vākyāntaravihitahomasya । tathāpi śeṣatvamapi bhavatviti pūrvapakṣyāha&mdash;<q>idamayuktaṃ</q> vidheyatvaṃ
viniyuktau viniyogaśepatvaṃ yuktam । kathametadityāha&mdash;<q>aidamarthyāvagatirhi na siddhasādhya-
tāmapekṣate</q> siddhatāṃ sādhyatāṃ vā nāpekṣate tena siddhasyāpi yuk‍to viniyogaḥ <q>niyogastu
kāryāvagatipūrvaka eva</q> ya eva kāryatayā'vagamyate tadviṣaya eva niyogaḥ । tena
siddhasyāvidheyatvam । yasmāt siddhasya[na]vidheyatvamasti <q>tasmādupādānamātrameva dadhyādeḥ śakyate
vak‍tuṃ na punarvidheyatāpi</q> rāddhāntaikadeśyāha&mdash;<q>nanu cāvidheyatve dadhyādeḥ sādhanāntaranirā-
karaṇaṃ na prāptotīti</q> anirākṛte ca tasmin dadhyādipadamanarthakaṃ tena vākyāntaravihitahome-
﻿<pb n="r462"/>
dadhyādi vidheyamastu । pūrvapakṣyāha&mdash;<q>kiṃ kripatāṃ yasyārtho na vidyate tasya kimanyadata
ānarthakyāt ityuktam ।</q> tataścāyaṃ pakṣastyajyatām । āśrīyatāmasmanmataṃ dadhyādivākyeṣvegha
karmavidhiḥ agnihotraṃ juhotīti samudāyānuvāda iti । nirākartā rāddhāntaikadeśyāha&mdash;kastarhi
guṇavidhidūṣaṇe <q>parihāraḥ ?</q> pūrvapakṣyāha-kimasmānū pṛcchasi । <q>sūtrakāraṃ pṛccheti yena bhāvārthebhyaḥ
kriyāvagatiruk‍tā ।</q> sūtrakāramatānusāriṇo vayamityarthaḥ । paramarāddhāntī vadati&mdash;<q>atrābhi-
dhīyate&mdash;bhāvārtha evātrāpi vidhīyate dadhnā juhotīti</q> kastasyāgnihotraṃ ityanena viśeṣaḥ ?
<q>iyāṃstu viśeṣaḥ</q> ityāha&mdash;<q>dhātvarthasya yo'nubandhaḥ kārakaṃ tadavacchinnaḥ</q> tatsaṃbandhī na viśi-
ṣṭarūpaḥ pratīyamāno vidhīyata ityarthaḥ । kathaṃ kārakasaṃbandhena svarūpaviśeṣo bhāvārthasyāvagamyata
ityatrāha&mdash;<q>kārakamapi kiyāvacchedena</q> devatāsaṃbandhānyathānupapatteḥ yāgacodanā । tathā
gṛhṇātītyapi । kathamavacchettavyamityatrāha&mdash;<q>kārakavyāpārāvacchedenaiva ।</q> kathamavacchedakamityatrāha
﻿<pb n="r463"/>
&mdash;<q>kārakavyāpārāvacchede</q> kārakavyāpāraviśeṣe <q>dhātavaḥ pravartante । avibhāgataḥ</q> śuddhena
dhātunā avibhāgataḥ । sāmānyapareva kārakavyāpāraḥ pratipādyate । <q>kārakaviśeṣaśravaṇe</q> punaḥ
<q>sa eva</q> kārakavyāpāraviśeṣo <q>vibhāgenābagamyate</q> viśiṣṭena rūpeṇāvagamyate na ca tādṛśaṃ rūpaṃ
kārakasaṃbandhenaiva vak‍tuṃ śakyane na cānyathā bhavatyevam । <q>tataḥ kiṃ</q>&mdash;uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>vibhāgaśravaṇe-
'pi hi vibhaktasyaiva vidheyatā'vagamyate na</q> vihitatvāt <q>nāvibhaktasya</q> dharmiṇo <q>dhātvarthasya</q>
vihitatvāt <q>yatra dhātvarthāvagatiḥ tatra dhātvarthe vidhānaṃ tatsannidhau tu vibhāge'vagate
vibhāgamātravidhānam ।</q> tasmāsiddhaṃ <q>tatsannidherguṇārthena punaḥ śrutiriti ।</q> dadhnā juhotītivā-
kyasya vidhimā[trā]t dadhyādīnāmapi vidhessaṃbandho'styaidamarthyalakṣaṇaḥ । homamapi prati vainiyogikaṃ
dadhyādeḥ śeṣatvamasti । <q>juhoteruccāraṇaṃ cānuvādoguṇasaṃbandhārthaḥ । yadi juhotītyanuvādaḥ ।</q>
﻿<pb n="r464"/>
kena vārthena guṇo vidhīyata iti bhāṣyamanubhāṣyākṣipati-ko'yaṃ praśnaḥ ? ekagranthenāha-<q>nanu vidhi-
dvayamapyupagatameva agnihotraṃ</q> juhotītyeko vidhiḥ <q>dadh‍nā juhotīti parastena</q> guṇavidhānārtho
vidhirastyeva । samādhātusta<q>devedaṃ</q> vidhidvayaṃ <q>nopapadyata iti abhiprāyaḥ । kathamanupapattiḥ ?</q>
uttaragranthaḥ&mdash;<q>ekaiveyaṃ kartavyatā</q> sā ca <q>kartavyatā'vibhaktā</q>(va)nubandhādeka eva vidhirna-
vidhidvayaṃ kevalaṃ (vibhak‍tā) <q>vibhaktābanubandhau ।</q> nanvevaṃ tarhi anubandhamedāt bhinno vidhīyata
ityatrāha&mdash;<q>na cānubandho dadhyādiḥ vidhiviṣayaḥ kiṃ tarhi anubandha eva ।</q> bhāvārtha eva
vidherviṣayaḥ sa caikasya paramavasthāviśeṣa eva । so'pi kārakasaṃbandhena <q>ekatvācca</q> bhāvārthasya
<q>vidhidvayasyāviṣaya eva । tasmādekamatra vākyaṃ vidhiśūnyam । tacca</q> guṇānubandhenāśritatvāt
bhāvārthamātravidheḥ । ataḥ punarapi <q>avivakṣaiva guṇānubandhasya ।</q> parihārabhāṣyaṃ vyācaṣṭe&mdash;
<q>vākyārtho yaḥ</q> taṃ vidhātumityanubandhavistārādbhāvavistāra ityu[k‍tam] <q>tasmāt viniyoga eva
﻿<pb n="r465"/>
vigherapi viṣayopapattiḥ ।</q> tathā padārthasaṃbandhāvagatiḥ sarvaviṣayā । <quote>“yaduktaṃ nāstyā-
ghārasya prakṛtaṃ dravyadevatamiti kimevaṃ sati dravyadevatena”</quote> iti bhāṣyamanubhāṣya vyācaṣṭe&mdash;
<q>vigheyatvādeva śeṣāvagatirityuk‍tam । na ca nāsti vacanāntaravihitaṃ rūpaṃ api tu
astyeveti siddhaṃ nānuvādāviti ।</q></p>
﻿<pb n="r466"/>
<p><q>dravyasaṃyogāt । kiṃ punaḥ pūrvādhikaraṇenāsya vaiṣamyaṃ ?</q> yadevamāśaṅkate nanu somena
yajeteti yāgavidhiḥ tathā'g‍nīṣomīyaṃ paśumālabheteti ca anayostu yāgayorgṛhṇātyavadyaticoda-
nābhiḥ grahaṇāvadānamātraguṇavidhirastu pūrvādhikaraṇasiddhāntavaditi kimadhikaraṇāntareṇeti । uttaraṃ&mdash;
<q>astivaiṣamyaṃ rasahadayādibhyo dravyāntaraṃ paśusomau ।</q> asyārthaḥ-rasasaṃvandhinībhiḥ grahaṇacoda-
nābhiḥ na latāsādhanake(na) yāge guṇavidhiḥ saṃbhavati । bhinnatvādrasalatayoḥ । tathā hṛdayādi-
saṃbandhābhiścāvadānacodanābhiḥ na paśudravyayāge guṇavidhisabhavaḥ paśorhṛdayādibhyo bhinnatvāt ।
yadi bhinnatvānna guṇavidhiḥ saṃbhavati <q>evaṃ tarhi pūrvapakṣa eva nāsti</q> somena yajetetyaindravā-
yavādiyāgasamudāyānuvādaḥ tathā'g‍nīṣobhīyaṃ paśumālabhetetyayamapi hṛdayasyāgre'vadyati ityevamādī-
nāmapi pūrvapakṣo nopapadyate dravyabhedenānuvā(denā)dānupapatteḥ । pariharati-<q>na ca nāsti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।</q>
api tvastyeva <q>kramasamuccayau hi pūrvapakṣahetubhūtau ।</q> yadi hi kramasamuccayadarśanena  somena
yajetetyaindravāyavādivākyena vā devatā na saṃbhavatīti niścitaṃ tathā ag‍nīṣomīyamityatra ca hṛdayā-
divākyenāvadānavidhāyakamiti tadā balādyāgavidhāne niraste'nuvādapakṣe ca vyavasthite lakṣaṇayā-
pyanuvādo ghaṭata eva । kathaṃ punaryāgavidhipakṣe paśusomavākyayoḥ kramasamuccayadarśanādupapattiri-
﻿<pb n="r467"/>
tyatrāha&mdash;<q>ekārthatvādavadānadevatā vikalpyante iti pūrvapakṣavādī manyate ।</q> ekenaivāvadānena
ekayā ca devatayā yāgopapatteḥ dek‍tānāmavadānānāṃ ca vikalpaḥ prāpnoti bandhane khadirādīnā-
miva । <q>tadāhurvārtikakāramiśrāḥ</q>&mdash;
<lg><l><quote>‘yathaikabandhanārthatvāt palāśakhadirādayaḥ ।</l>
<l>tadbandhane vikalpyante yāge'smin devatāstathā ।।</l></lg>
iti । bhinnayāgaviṣayatve tu devatānāṃ yāgānāṃ cādṛṣṭārthānāṃ yugapadekaśabdena <note n="(1)"> G. <dn>phalena vidhiniyuktatvāt</dn></note>phalavidhānā-
dupapadyate kramasamuccayadarśanam । avadānasamuccayastu daśame vakṣyate । nanu dravyabhede
kathamanubādaḥ ityatrāha&mdash;<q>na cātyantāsaṃbandhamevedaṃ hṛdayādibhyaḥ paśutvam । na ca somādrasaḥ</q>
tena sati saṃbandhe lakṣaṇayā'nuvādaḥ । somaśabdena raso lakṣyate paśuśabdena hṛdayādiḥ ।
tasmādanuvādau nyāyyau manyate । <q>kathaṃ punaraindravāyavaṃ gṛhṇāṇi hṛdayasyāgre'vadyati iti
yāgacodanā ।</q> uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>grahaṇe tāvat dravyadevatāsaṃyogānnirvapativat gṛhṇati<note n="(2)"> G. <dn>rbhavatītya</dn></note>rbhavivya-
tītyabhiprāyaḥ ।</q> yathā vakṣyamāṇanyāyena sauryaṃ caruṃ nirvayet ityatra yāgamantareṇa dravyadevatā-
saṃbandhānupapattyā yāgacodanā tathā gṛhṇātītyapi ।</p>
﻿<pb n="r468"/>
<p><q>avadyatau tu kathaṃ ?</q> yāgacodanā dravyadevatāsaṃbandhāśravaṇāt । <note n="(1)"> G. <dn><quote>‘ekadeśina uttaraṃ’</quote></dn></note>ekadeśyuttaraṃ likhati&mdash;
avadyati <q>ityatrāpi <quote>“<note n="(2)"> G. <dn>yāgavacana</dn></note>yāgagata(pada) saṃskāradarśanāt phalacamasavat karmacodanā bhaviṣyatī-
tyabhiprāyaḥ ।</q> anyārthamavadānalakṣaṇaḥ saṃskāro'yam । prakṛtau sānnāyye yāgasādhanasya
dravyasya saṃskāraḥ pratipannaḥ tatsaṃbandhāt hṛdayādīnāmapi yāgasaṃbandho'vagamyate phalacamasavat ।
yathā bhakṣaṇasaṃbandhāt yāgaśeṣatā phalacamasasyāvagamyate tathā hṛdayādīnāmapi ।</p>
<p>tadāhurvārtikakārapādāḥ-sānnāyyaṃ vā tatprabhavatvāt iti । anena nyāyenāyamapyavadyatiḥ
sārūpyāt sānnāyyāvadyatiprakṛtiḥ । sa ca darśapūrṇamāsayoḥ yāgadravyasaṃskārārthaḥ prasiddhaḥ ।
tatra yadi hṛdayādīni yāgadravyāṇi taiḥ<note n="(3)"> G. <dn>tataḥ</dn></note> tatsaṃyogabhāñji bhavanti । nānyathā । yathaiva pūtī-
kānāmabhiṣavasaṃbandho phalacamasasya bhakṣaṇasabandhe ca śrūyamāṇe tadarhatvānyathānupapattyā yāgasaṅgati-
raśrūyamāṇāpi gamyate । tathehāpi । ākṣeptā dūṣayati <note n="(4)"> G. <dn>āhaḥ</dn></note>&mdash;<q>yuktaṃ phalacamase nirjñātayāgaśe-
﻿<pb n="r469"/>
ṣasyāsau</q> saṃskāraḥ । <q>avadyatau punaḥ mṛgyo'sau ।</q> asyārthaḥ&mdash;nirjñātayāgaśeṣo yaḥ somaḥ
tasyāsau bhakṣākhyaḥ saṃskāraḥ nyagnodhastibhinībhiḥ sabandhitvena pratīyate । tasyaiva bhakṣasya
prakṛtasya pratīteḥ tena yuk‍to yāgasaṃbandhāvagamaḥ । tatrāvadānaṃ punaḥ idaṃ na prākṛtam kiṃ
tarhi <note n="(1)"> G. <dn>anyadeyatat</dn></note>anyadevedaṃ vidhīyate । kāmaṃ darśapūrṇamāsādhikārāvadānaprakṛtikamastu । tena
tatsaṃbandhānna yāgasaṃbandho hṛdayādīnāmavagamyate । <q>saṃskārāditi cet ।</q> atha manyase
avadānalakṣaṇo'yaṃ hṛdayādīnāṃ saṃskāraḥ pratīyate । saṃskāraśca yāgaśeṣasya dṛśyate , puroḍāśaṃ
paryag‍nikarotītivat । avadyateryāgasaṃbandhitvamavagamyata iti cet । dūṣayati&mdash;<q>na vatsamāla-
bhetetyanaikāntyāt ।</q> ayāgaśeṣasyāpi vatsasya saṃskāradarśanāt ।</p>
<p><q>nanu cāprayojanavataḥ saṃskāro na bhavatīti yuktaiva karmakalyanā ।</q> dūṣayati&mdash;varaṃ
<q>tṛtīyārthe ṣaṣṭhī na punaḥ punaḥ karmakalpanā ।</q> sarvasya bhāvārthasyāpūrvaviṣayatve prasak‍te'pavādo'yaṃ
saṃskārakarmalā nāma । tacca dravyacikīrṣāhetukam । tacca dravyaṃ cikīrṣitaṃ bhavati
yasya pramāṇāntareṇopayogo bhūto bhavī vā pratīyate । yasya punarasau nāvagamyate na ca taccikīrṣitam ।
tatra bhāvārtho niyogaviṣaya evetītarat tadarthamiti nyāyāt tatraiva padāntarasaṃbandhaḥ । ato'vadyatireva
﻿<pb n="r470"/>
niyogaviṣayaḥ । hṛdayādayastu tannirvartakā iti na yāgasaṃbandho hṛdayādīnām । paramapūrvapakṣa-
vādī vadati&mdash;<q>ke'yamanupāsitaguroḥ svapratibhātaḥ tṛtoyārthe ṣaṣṭhīkalpanā । bhavantu
saṃskārā abadyaticodanāḥ । agnīṣomasaṃbandhāttu yāvatsaṃskāraṃ yāgacodanāḥ saṃpadyante ।</q>
asyārthaḥ&mdash;hṛdayasyāgre'vadyatīti na yāgacodanā । kintu avadānalakṣaṇasaṃskāracodanaiṣā ।
teṣāṃ tu hṛdayādīnāṃ paśuśabdena lakṣaṇayā anuvādaṃ kṛtvā ag‍nīṣoma<q>saṃbandho vidhīyate ।</q>
<note n="(1)"> G. <dn>yāvaduddeśaśca</dn></note>yāvaduddeśaṃ ca yāvatvākyasamāptiriti । saṃskāraṃ yāgacodanā saṃpadyante । taiścārthaprāptahṛdayā-
dyālambhaḥ। <q>pracayānuvādo'yamālabhatiriti siddham ।</q> avadīyamānānāṃ hṛdayādīnāmarthādeva
sparśalakṣaṇaḥ ālaṃbhaḥ prāptaḥ । tatsamudāyānuvādo'yamālabhatiragnīpomasaṃvandhārthaḥ । kasmātpu-
narevaṃ varṇyate yāvatā dravyadevatāsaṃyogena yāgacodanaiveyamastu na devatāmātracodanetyatrāha&mdash;
<q>tathā ca kramasamuccayadarśanamupapannārtha bhavati ।</q> nanu hṛdayādīnāṃ paśuśabdenānuvāde lakṣaṇaiva
dopa ityatrāha&mdash;<q>na cā'nuvāde lakṣaṇādoṣaḥ ।</q> vijñātatātparyaṃ hyanuvāde vākyaṃ bhavatīti ।﻿<pb n="r471"/>
tatra lakṣaṇāhyupapannā । atrabhidhīyate&mdash;<q>naitacchabdādavagantuṃ śakyate anuvādo'yamiti ।</q>
kuta ityatrāha&mdash;<q>somena yajeniti</q> somalatāviśiṣṭo <q>yajirgamyate । rasadravya(devatā)kāśca
gṛhṇātayaḥ । ato rūpāntarabagamānnānuvādaḥ śakyate'vagantum ।</q> kintu yāgavidhirevāva-
sīyate । <q>anuvāde hi lakṣaṇā</q>, lakṣaṇāta<q>ścānuvāda itītaretarāśrayam ।</q> karmāntaratve punaḥ
svato'rthāntarāvagamān‍nyāyyam । guṇaścāpūrvasaṃyogevākyayoḥ samatvāt iti nyāyāt । evaṃ
<q>paśāvapi</q> nānuvādaḥ । <q>paśuśabdo hi pucchavati vartate ।</q> pucchavattvopādhikaḥ paśuśabdaḥ ।
pucchaśca vāladhirabhimataḥ । <q>hṛdayādayastu māṃsasaṃsthānabacanāḥ ।</q> tanmātradravyabhedānnānuvādaḥ
saṃbhavati । <q>kramasamuccayadarśaṃna ca grahaṇādīnāṃ karmāntaratve'</q>bhyupagamyamāne naiva viruddham ।
yadā hi aindravāyavādivākyaiḥ devatāvidhānaṃ hadayādivākyaiścāvadānavidhānaṃ tadā vikalpa-
prasaṅgaḥ । karmāntaratve tu na kaściddoṣaḥ । etacca gṛhṇātyavadyatyoryāgacodanātvamabhyupagapyo-
﻿<pb n="r472"/>
ktam । <q>kintu somena yajena paśumālabheta iti yadaite karmacodane tadā avadyatigṛhṇātyoḥ
saṃskārakarmataivāvasīyate ।</q> kasmāt ? uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>tadā hi&mdash;gṛhyamāṇapradhāno gṛhnātiḥ</q>
<note n="(1)"> G. omits <dn>na</dn></note>na gṛhyamāṇā[guṇā] śakyate kalpayitum । asyārthaḥ&mdash;somamabhiṣuṇoti somaṃ plāvayati
somamutpunāti iti saṃskārānusārāllatā tāvanna sākṣādyāgasādhanam । kintu rasadvāreṇeti

tvāt । na punaḥ pradhānakartatāṃ pratipadyate । <q>nāpi virvapativat yāgavidhānārthaṃ prāptānu-
vādaḥ śakyate vak‍tum ।</q> grahaṇasyaiva vidheyatvasaṃbhavāt । <q>nanu ca dravyadevatāsaṃbandhānna
gṛhṇātimātraparyavasāyinī codanā śakyate vak‍tuṃ saurya caruṃ nirvapeditivat । na ca
somena yajetetyatra debatā prāptā yā'nūdyeta saṃskāraṃ vidhātum ।</q> na ca yāge yā indravā-
yvādyā devatāḥ prāptāstā yathāprāptā evānūdyante <note n="(4)"> G. <dn>grahaṇādi</dn></note>grahaṇāni vidhātuṃ yadaindravāyavādikaṃ tad‌gṛhṇati
﻿<pb n="r473"/>
iti devatāyā evāprātvāt । <q>na ca saṃskāre devatā kārakabhāvaṃ pratipadyate</q> yena grahaṇe
eva devatā svayaṃ yāyāt । <q>yāgasyaiva hi kārakaṃ na gṛhṇāteḥ ataḥ aprāptadravyadevatāsaṃyo-
gāt karmāntarāṇyevaitāni na somena yajetetyatra saṃskāra iti śakyate vak‍tum ।</q> yadā ca
karmāntarāṇyevaitāni tadā somena yajeneti devatāvirahāt balāt samudāyānuvāda iti manyate
﻿<pb n="r474"/>
atrābhidhīyate&mdash;kutaścidupādānaṃ grahaṇamityucyate । upādānaṃ ca ātmārtha parārya vā
syāt । tatra devatāśravaṇāt devatārthamiti gamyate</q> tenendravāyvādyarthaṃ grahaṇamiti graheṇepi
indravāyvādīnāṃ saṃbandho na virudhyate । <q>nanu na jātitaḥ kacit devatā nāma vidyate ।
yāhi yasya haviṣaḥ saṃbandhitvena codyate sā tasya devatā, na ca somarasasya indravāyvādyā</q>
debatāḥ <q>prāptā yena tadarthamidamupādānamityavadhāryate । athātraiva rasasya devatā codyate na
tarhi grahaṇa codanā, kintu devatāvidhiparamevaitadvākyaṃ syāt tadā na kamasamuccayadarśanaṃ
nopapadyate gṛhṇātīti ca pramādapāṭhaḥ kriyānuvādo vā syāt ।</q> sarvathā na vidheyārthaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="r475"/>
tasmāt devatāviśiṣṭagrahaṇaṃ codyata iti durbhaṇamidam ।</q> atrocyate&mdash;<q>na vramo devatā
viśiṣṭaṃ grahaṇaṃ codyata iti ।</q> kiṃ tarhi ? <note n="(1)"> G. <dn>indravāyudebatā</dn></note>indravāyūddeśaviśiṣṭagrahaṇaṃ rasasya । na
devatābhāvena grahaṇe indravāyvādīnāṃ saṃbandhaḥ kintu tānuddiśya rasasya grahaṇaṃ
kartavyamityetāvanmātraṃ vidhīyate । <q>tataḥ kiṃ ?</q> uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>idaṃ tato bhavati yāgaśeṣa-
tvādrasasya indravāyvarthatvāt</q> grahaṇasya <q>gṛhyamāṇamukhaṃ ca grahaṇasya tādarthyam ।
ataḥ indravāyvartho rasa iti gamyate, nendravāyū rasārthau ।</q> asyārthaḥ&mdash;somarasastāvadyāgārthaḥ
tasya ca grahaṇaṃ tadindravāyvartham grahaṇaṃ ca gṛhyamāṇapraghānam । tasya ca yadaidamarthyaṃ tadapi
gṛhyamāṇadvāreṇa upanayanavat । tenendravāyvarthatā rasasya gamyate । <q>yāvad‍grahaṇaṃ ca tādarthyaṃ
na yābadyāgabhāvi</q> grahamātraparyantameva rasasya tādarthyena yāvadayāgakalpanāparyantaṃ sākṣācchruta-
yāgānupraveśenaiva indravāyvādīnāṃ grahaṇasya gṛhyamāṇasya ca tādarthyasaṃpatteḥ । indravāyvādīnāṃ hi
somayāgaṃ prati devatātve rasasya yāgārthatā indravāyvarthatā ca grahaṇasya nirvahati yasmānna yāga-
paryantamidamaidamarthyamasmin vākye । <q>ata eva na yāge codanā grahaṇeṣu devatātvaṃ ca yāgārtha&mdash;
rasatādarthyāt ।</q> indravāyvarthatvāt । <q>na punaścodanāto</q> devatātvaṃ yasmānnātre<q>ndravāyvādayo
﻿<pb n="r476"/>
debatātvena codyante । ata kāryataḥ tatra devatātvaṃ nopadeśataḥ</q> rasasya yāgasiddhiḥ kāryaṃ,
grahaṇasya ca grāhyopakalpanaṃ kāryaṃ, tadetat kathaṃ ghaṭate yadīndravāyvādayo devatā bhavantīti
kāryato devatātvaṃ nopadeśataḥ । (upadeśataḥ) <q>upadeśo hi grahaṇasyendrabāyvarthatāparyava-
sāyyeva । tasmādupapannā rasasaṃskāracodanāgrahaṇādayaḥ ।</q></p>
<p><q>tadbhedāt karmaṇo'bhyāsaḥ । evaṃ ca kṛtvā kramasamuccayopapattiḥ ।</q> yadīndravāyvā-
dayo yāgā evopadiśyeran tato vikalpyeran । na caiṣāmupadeśa ityuk‍taṃ, tathāpi kimityāha
&mdash;<q>uktaṃ hi yāvad‍grahaṇabhāvī indravāyusaṃbandhaḥ na yāvadyāgabhāvīti ।</q> tena kāryato devatā-﻿<pb n="r477"/>
tvam । nanu yadi kāryato devatātvaṃ tathāpi kimiti vikalpo na syāt ityatrāha&mdash;<q>yāga-
śeṣaścāsau sakalo daśamuṣṭiprabhavo rasaḥ ।</q> ataḥ upadeśenendra<q>vāyvorayāgārthatvāt sakalasya
somarasasya yāgārthatvāt yāvagad‍grahaṇabhāvitvācca saṃvandhasyendravāyvoravaśyamāvṛttyā bhavati-
vyam ।</q> anyārthaṃ sakalasya somarasasya yāgaśeṣatvena saṃskārārhatvāt tasya ca pracuratvāt devatoddeśa-
viśiṣṭāni grahaṇāni tāvat samuccetavyāni teṣāṃ ca samuccaye sati yadyaduddeśena gṛhītaṃ tattasyā eva
devatāyai utsraṣṭavyamityarthāt yāgasyāvṛttyā bhavitavyam । <q>satyāṃ cāvṛttau siddhiḥ samuccayaḥ ।
na ca sarvasyaiva somarasasya anyasyānyasya coddeśena <note n="(1)"> G. adds <dn>tatasyaidevatārye</dn></note>grahaṇaṃ bhavati</q> saṅkalpabhedāt ।
<q>tasmādavayavaśo grahaṇam । tathā ca pātraparimāṇadarśanam ।</q> anyathā kṛtsnarasagrahaṇayogyaṃ
﻿<pb n="r478"/>
mahatpātraṃ syāt । <q>na ca vibhāgena gṛhītasya</q> rasasya <q>punarekīkaraṇ ।</q> kutaḥ ityāha
&mdash;<q>na ca dṛṣṭe saṃbhabati adṛṣṭārthatā uddeśyasya saṃbhavati ।</q> yadi hi yat yaduddeśena gṛhyate
tat taduddeśenaiva tyajyate tadā grahaṇasya pṛthakkalpanasya dṛṣṭārthatā bhavati । anyathā tvekīkaraṇe
adṛṣṭārthatā । sā tu na saṃbhavati । <q>adṛṣṭārthasya vā gṛhṇāteḥ dṛṣṭārthatā</q> devatoddeśena
viśiṣṭasya gṛhṇāteḥ dṛṣṭaṃ prayojanaṃ nāsti । tasmādadṛṣṭārthadevatoddeśaṃ parityajya kevalena dṛṣṭārthatā
na yuktā śrutahāniprasaṅgāt । <q>tasmādavayavānāmeva</q> devatoddeśaviśeṣeṇa gṛhītānāṃ yathā
<q>devatoddeśena tyāgaḥ । na caitāvatā</q> punaḥ punaḥ karaṇena <q>karmabhedaḥ bhavati</q> bhedakapramāṇābhāvāt ।
kathaṃ bhede pramāṇaṃ nāstītyatrāha&mdash;<q>somena yajetetyabhinnāvagateḥ । tasmāt sa evāyaṃ punaḥ
punarāvartata iti siddham ।</q></p>
﻿<pb n="r479"/>
<p><q>saṃskārastu na bhidyeta ।। khadirādiṣu punaḥ saṃskāraṃ</q> bandhanaṃ prati <q>śeṣabhābāvaga-
māt yuk‍to vikalpaḥ ।</q> iha punaḥ yāgaṃ prati śeṣabhāvo devatānāmupadeśato nāvagamyata iti
darśito viśeṣaḥ ।</p>
<p>bhāṣyamanubhāṣato&mdash;<q>athaindravāyavādiṣu</q> prakṛteṣu <q>latā vidhīyate ityucyeta na sā
śakyā</q>  vākyena <q>aindravāyavī vijñātuṃ śratyā hi rasa aindravāyava iti ।</q> ākṣipati
﻿<pb n="r480"/>
&mdash;<q>nanu cedamayuk‍taṃ prakṛtidravyatayā hi latāvidhānamanirastaṃ syāt । rasakāryavidhānaṃ
cāsaṃbhavadeva śaṅkitam ।</q> asyārthaḥ&mdash;<quote>‘na sā śakyā vākyenaindravāyavī vijñātuṃ śrutyā hi rasa
aindravāyava’</quote> iti parihāradarśanāt rasakārya eva latāvidhānaṃ <quote>‘athaindravāyavādiṣu’</quote> ityanenā-
śaṅkitamiva pratibhāti । anyathā prakṛtidravyatayā latāvidhāne codite śrutivākyaviśeṣeṇa
parihāro nopapadyate । śrutisaṃbandhe'pi (na) puroḍāśe vākyopaneyaprakṛtidravyabhūtavrīhyādi (vidhāna)
vākyaśravaṇāt । taccedamayuktam । prakṛtidravyavidhānāśaṅkāyā anirākṛtatvāt । asaṃbha-
vinaśca rasakāryavidhānasya āśaṅkitatvāt । na hi śrutisamarpite rase haviṣi saṃbhavati vākyena
latāyāḥ haviṣṭvena vidhānaṃ yuktaṃ śaṅkitum । tasmāt vrīhirbhiryacetetivat rasaprakṛtidravyatayā
latāvidhānamupapadyata eva somena yajeteti । tadāhurvārtikakārapādāḥ&mdash;
<lg><l>yathaivāṣṭākapālādau śraute hi sati vākyataḥ ।</l>
<l>vrīhyādayo vidhīyante tathā somo vighāsyate ।।</l></lg>
virudhyamānaṃ hi dubalaṃ bādhyate । nānuguṇam । amuguṇaśca somaḥ rasasya prakṛtyapekṣiṇaḥ
tādarthyena saṃbandhāt । tadyathā <quote>‘āg‍neyo'ṣṭākapāla’</quote> iti śrutivihitepyaṣṭākapāle sati vākyena
vrīhiyavau vidhīyamānau na virudhyete । puroḍāśāpekṣitaprakṛtirūpatvānna vrīhīn gṛhṇan aṣṭāka-
pālaṃ na karoti tena nātra karmāntaratā । tathā'tra some gṛhyamāṇe na rasaṃ parityakṣyata itya&mdash;
virodhāt pūrvatraiva saṃbhavānna guṇo bhedakaḥ syāditi । samādhatte&mdash;<q>ucyate । kinnāma nā-
śaṅkyate mūḍhamatibhiḥ, puroḍāśo hyanirūpitaprakṛtidravyatayā āgneyādiṣu pratīyate
﻿<pb n="r481"/>
tenayuk‍taṃ tatra prakṛtiviśeṣavidhānam । iha punaraindrabāyābādiṣu somarasa evāvasīyate ।
kimatra prakṛtidravyavidhānaṃ kariṣyati । tasmādanāśaṅkanīya evāyaṃ pakṣaḥ ।</q> asyārthaḥ&mdash;nātra
vrīhimudrāmudritatvaṃ saṃbhavati । tatrāgneyo'ṣṭākapāla ityetasmin vākye aṣṭākapāladravyaṃ
anirūpitaprakṛtidravyakaṃ pratīyata iti yuktaṃ tatra prakṛtidravyavidhānam । iha punaraindravāyavaṃ
gṛhṇātīti nirūpitaprakṛtidravyaṃ śrutyā samarpitam । tathā hi&mdash;yadi tāvat yāvacchrutimātrameva
gṛhītvā prakṛtidravyavidhānamāśaṅkayeta tadanupapannam । vikāradravyasyāśrutatvāt kasya
prakṛtidravyabhākāṅkṣayate । atha kiṃ tadaindravāyavaṃ ? ityapekṣāyāṃ aparyavasite vākye prakṛta-
dravyasaṃbandhe sati prakṛtividhānaṃ, <q>tadapyayuktam</q> somaṃ krīṇāti somamabhiṣuṇoti somamabhi-
plāvayati somamutpunāti iti prakṛtaparyālocanayā somarasasya saṃbandhāvagamāt rasamātrasya prakṛtya-
pekṣā nāsti । na hi somarasaḥ kiṃprakṛtika ityapekṣā'vakalpate । <q>athocyeta</q> aṇvyā
dhārayā gṛhṇāti’</quote> iti grahaṇaguṇasamarpaṇapare vākye dhārāyogyadravyamātrāvagamāt prakṛtidravyatayā
somavidhānamavakalpata iti । <q>tadanupapannam ।</q> asyāpi vākyasya grāhyāpekṣitvāt yāvacca
dhārāyogyaṃ dravyaṃ gṛhṇīyāditi kalpyate tāvat prakṛtaḥ somarasa evāsti iti sa evātra grāhyatayā
saṃbadhyate । tena prakaraṇāpekṣitve ca dravyavidhānāśaṅkā nopapadyate । tannirapekṣahavirmātra-
parigraheṇa <q>havirviśeṣavidhānāśaṅkā nopapadyata iti nirastaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa ।</q> nanu caindravā-
yavādivākyabhedena havirdravyaviśeṣasamarpaṇāt yāvacca prakaraṇamapekṣate tāvadvākye sati kimiti
haviṣṭvena somavidhānaṃ nāvakalpate । ucyate । nedamupapadyate somena yajeteti vihitayāgānuvādena
dravyavidhānam । na hi sākṣācchruto yāgo'sti kintu aindravāyavādivākyagatadravyadevatā-
saṃbandhānupapattyā yāgaḥ kalppanīyaḥ । na ca tatra prakaraṇamanapekṣya dravyadevatāsaṃbandhāvagatiḥ<note n="(1)"> G. <dn>saṃbandhobhavati</dn></note>।
﻿<pb n="r482"/>
tena yāgābhivyaktyarthaṃ prakaraṇaṃ cāpekṣaṇīyaṃ vākyeneti prakaraṇād‌durbalamatra vākyam । na ca
<note n="(1)"> G. <dn>somavākyenaindravāyavādiṣu</dn></note> somākhyadravyasaṃbanvenaivendravāyvādiyāgābhivyaktiḥ itaretarāśrayatvaprasaṅgāt । tasmāt prākaraṇikaṃ
somamevāśritya taddhitaśrutiḥ aindravāyavādiṣu varṇanīyā । tataśca śrautaḥ somarasaḥ na tatra
vākyena latāvidhānamavakalpate ।</p>
<p></q>pṛthaktvaniveśitvāt । prājāpatyān iti prājāpatyaprātipadikādvibhaktaya
utpadyante ।</q> atra ca <quote>“prājāpatyā bhavanti”</quote> <quote>“prājāpatyānālabhante”</quote> <quote>“prājāpatyaiḥ kuryāt”</quote>
ityevamādaya udāharaṇamiti matvā uk‍taṃ <q>vibhaktaya iti ।</q> prājāpatyāt iti itiśabdaḥ
pradarśanārthaḥ prājāpatyānityevamādiṣvityarthaḥ । <q>yataśca</q> vibhaktaya <q>utpadyante tad‌yuk‍taṃ</q> tadī-
yārthena yuktaṃ <q>svārthamabhivadanti । taddhitāntaṃ caitatprātipadikam । tataḥ taddhitāntasyai-

﻿<pb n="r483"/>
evātra nopapadyate</q> yasmāt <q>prājāpatyāḥ saptadaśetyevāvagabhyate</q> prājāpatyānāṃ satāṃ

prajāpatisaṃbandhāt saptadaśa paśudravyaka eko yāgaḥ syāt । prājāpatyānāṃ tu satāṃ saptadaśatve

<p>samādhatte&mdash;<q>ucyate । pratyayārthagatamevātra vibhaktayaḥ svārthaṃ pratipādayituṃ kṣamāḥ na
prakṛtyarthagatam ।</q> kutaḥ ? uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>prakṛtyarthasya pratyayārthopasarjanatvāt ।</q> pratyayārthaṃ prati
prakṛtyarthaḥ upasarjanam pratyayārthaḥ pradhānam । tathāpi kimityāha&mdash;<q>pradhānaṃ hyarthāntareṇa
saṃbadhyate । nopasarjanam ।</q> tena pratyayārthabhṛtapradhānadravyamātreṇaiva bahutvasya saṃbandhaḥ ataḥ
saptadaśaprājāpatyān iti saṃbandhaḥ। tenāsti pūrvapakṣavacanavyaktiḥ । <q>nanu caivamapi</q>
siddhāntavacanavyaktyasaṃbhavāt <q>sandeho nopapadyate । upasarjanārthasya bhedānavagamāt ।</q> yadi
hi tadgataṃ bahutvaṃ syāt tadā bahutvasya bhedamantareṇāsaṃbhavāt upasarjanārtho bhidyate, na caitadasti ।
﻿<pb n="r484"/>
samādhatte&mdash;<q>satyamevametat pradhānārtha evātra kiṃ bhinnaḥ san upasarjanena yuktaḥ uta sopa-
sarjano bhinna iti । evaṃ saṃśaye sati pūrvapakṣavādī manyate । bhinnasyopasarjanena yogo
yuktaḥ prakṛtyarthasya bhedāvagame pramāṇābhāvāt ।</q> kuta ityāha&mdash;<q>bahutvāvagamapūrvikā hi
ekaśeṣakalpanā ।</q> bahutvaṃ ca pradhānasya pratyayārthasyaiva yuktam । <q>utaḥ pratyayārthasyaivaika-
śeṣo bhavatu । tadbhedāvagamāt । na punarabhinnasyāpi prakṛtyarthasya ।</q> sābhyuccayamupa-
saṃhāramāha&mdash;<q>tasmādubhayasiddhamekayāgāvadhāraṇameva yuktam । tadidaṃ</q> ubhayasiddhatvamuktaṃ
<q>yo hi bahūn kalpayati kalpayatyasāvekamiti । kathaṃ punarasmin pakṣe'nekasmādekādaśā-
vadānasiddhiḥ ?</q> asyārthaḥ&mdash;yadaiko yāgāḥ tadaikaṃ karaṇam ekasmiṃśca karaṇe eka eva karaṇopakāraḥ
tatsiddhayarthaṃ caikaiva padārthaprāptiḥ । ataḥ eka evāvadānagaṇaḥ । sa caikasmādeva paśorevocyate
﻿<pb n="r485"/>
itītareṣāmavadānābhāvaḥ avadānadvāreṇa[hi] yāgasādhanatvam । tena yāgasādhanatā na syāt
uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>arthādāvṛttirbhaviṣyati grahaṇabhedāt jyotiṣṭomasyeva ।</q> itareṣāmapi paśūnāṃ yāga-
sādhanatāsiddhayarthaṃ yāgasyāvṛttirbhaviṣyati grahaṇabhedājjyotiṣṭomasyeva । ekadeśī vadati
&mdash;<q>atrocyate na saptadaśapaśubhirekaṃ karmopapadyate । kutaḥ ?</q> uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>ekādaśabhirabadānaiḥ

ntaraṃ devatayā saṃbandhayituṃ śakyate</q> tadīyasyāvadānasya devatoddeśena tyāgābhāvāt । <q>ataśca
grājāpatyā<note n="(1)"> G. <dn>patyairiti</dn></note>niti bahutvānupapattiḥ ।</q> ekasyaiva prājāpatyatvāt yāgabhede tvekaikayāgasya
ekaikapaśutvāt pratiyāgaṃ ca karaṇabhāvāt pratikaraṇamitikartavyatāprāpteḥ pratipaśu avadānayo-
﻿<pb n="r486"/>
gāt prājāpatyāniti yuk‍taṃ bahutvam । <q>nanu cok‍taṃ pratipaśvavadānagaṇasyāvṛttiḥ sapta-
daśānāṃ yāgasaṃbandhārthe</q> bhaviṣyati <q>gṛhṇātīnāmiva</q> yāgasaṃbandhasiddhayarthaṃ <q>jyotiṣṭomasya</q>
āvṛttiriti । pariharati&mdash;<q>yuktam । jyotiṣṭome gṛhṇātīnāmupadeśāt । atra punaḥ

avadānagaṇaḥ prāp‍nuyāt । sa ca sakṛdeva prāpnoti ekatvādyāgasya । <q>saptadaśapaśukaścāya-
meko yāgaḥ yāga<note n="(1)"> R. & G. <dn>saṃbandhāṃrtha</dn></note>saṃbandhācca <note n="(2)"> G. <dn>bhaviṣyatyavadānam</dn></note>haviṣyavadānam । ataḥ kenātra pratipaśvavadānagaṇaprāptiḥ

nibandhanaṃ pṛthaktvaṃ</q> paśūnāṃ yena pṛthaktvaṃ paśūnāmavagamya avadānasaṃskārabhedo'vagamyate ।

havirnibandhano havissaṃskārabhedaḥ ।</q> iha punaḥ havireva na bhinnamiti saṃskārasyāpyabhedena

vyaktiniṣṭhaḥ tāneva pratipādayatīti । <q>tasmāt</q> ekadevatāsaṃbandhāddhavirdvayasya <q>guṇadvayaviśiṣṭa
mekaṃ karmeti pūrvapakṣitam । siddhāntavādī tu manyate ।</q> yadyapi <q>prakṛtavyaktyavagamo
bhavati tathāpi karmāntaramevaitat āmikṣopasarjanatayā pratīyamānatvādviśveṣāṃ devānām</q>
﻿<pb n="r500"/>
<quote>‘vaiśvadevyāmikṣā’</quote> ityatra viś‍vedevāḥ āmikṣāṃ pratyupasarjanatayā pratītāḥ । atasteṣāṃ na
vājinena saṃbandha upapadyate । kasmādityāha&mdash;<q>nahyanyopasarjanamanyasaṃbandhitayā śakyeta'vagantuṃ
rājapuruṣaṃ praśyetivat ।</q> na rājā puruṣaṃ pratyupasarjanībhūto dṛśinā saṃbadhyate । <q>tasmā-
danayorā</q>mikṣāvājinayoḥ <q>ekenāsambandhaḥ</q> ekena rūpeṇa viś‍vedevā nāmikṣāvājinābhyāṃ
sambadhyante । yadi hyekena rūpeṇa sambandhaḥ syāt tataḥ ekadevatāsambandhāt militamekahaviḥ
syāt । ekaśca yāgo bhavet । vāruṇyā niṣkāsena tuṣaiścāvabhṛthaṃ yantītivat yataḥ
āmikṣāsambandhitayā na vājinasambandhaḥ ataḥ sambanghadvayāvagamāt ekatvepi viś‍veṣāṃ devānāṃ
karmabhedaḥ tatra vājiśabdenaiva devatātve āmikṣāsambandhitayā na vājinasambandhaḥ ।
<q>ataḥ sambandhadvayāvagamādekatveti</q> viś‍veṣāṃ devānāṃ <q>karmabhedaḥ ।</q> atra ca vājiśabdenaiva
debatātvaṃ nāmikṣāsaṃbandhinā rūpeṇa viś‍vedevaśabdābhidheyena । tena vājinasaṃbandhābhāvāt
ato vājiśabdenaiva devatātvamiti devatābhāvabhedāt bhedaḥ । <q>atha kasmād‍yugapadaruṇā-
vatsaṃbandho na bhavati ।</q> yathā krayasyātrāruṇaikahāyanībhyāṃ yugapat saṃbandhaḥ tathā viś‍veṣā-
mapi devānāmāmikṣāvājinābhyāṃ bhavatīti । <q>kimevaṃ</q> bhayiṣyati ? uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>ekatvenā-
vagatirbhaviṣyati ।</q> ekatvāvagateśca na bhedāvamatiḥ sidhyati । pariharati&mdash;<q>satyamevam
<note n="(1)"> G. <dn>pramāṇābhedepi</dn></note>	﻿<pb n="r501"/>
yatraikapramāṇabagamyaḥ sambandhaḥ ।</q> yathā'ruṇaikahāyanyoriva dvayorapi vāk‍yena sambandhāt; na
tatrāp‍ya[nya]saṃbandhasyānyena sambandho yukta iti śak‍yate vak‍tum । <q>nānāpramāṇagamya tu punaḥ
<note n="1"><dn>vāk‍yena bheda iti</dn></note> bhavatyeva bhedāvagatiḥ । tasmāt karmāntaratvam । nānāpramāṇābagamyatā ca</q> saṃbandhasya
darśitā bhāṣyakāreṇa <q>śrutyā vāk‍yena ceti<note n="2">G.<dn>anivāryaiva</dn></note> vadatā ।</q> viś‍veṣāṃ devānāṃ śrutyā āmikṣā-
sambandhaḥ vāk‍yena ca vājinasambandhaḥ । tena śrutyā śīghraṃ sambandhaḥ vāk‍yena vilamvena । tenāmikṣā-
saṃbandhānāṃ satāṃ na vājinasaṃbandho yuktaḥ । <q>iha tarhi kathaṃ pramāṇabhedepi dadh‍nā</q> juhoti payasā
<q>juhotītyekatvaṃ karmaṇaḥ ।</q> bhinnavāk‍yasamarpitatvāt dadhnaḥ payasaśca nirapekṣasambandhāt ekatvaṃ
karmaṇo na yuktam । uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>anupasarvanāvagateḥ</q> agnihotraṃ juhoti iti dravyāntarasambandho home
nāvagamyate । tena sarveṣāṃ guṇavidhīnāṃ sambandho yuktaḥ । <q>anupasarjanāvagateḥ ।</q> etadeva darśayati
&mdash;<q>nātra anyopasarjano homo'nyena <note n="2">G.<dn>anivāryaiva</dn></note>sam‍badhyate ।</q> dadhiviśiṣṭahomaḥ payasā na sambadhyate kintu
dravyāntaraviśiṣṭa eveti <q>aviruddhā prakṛtāvagatiḥ । ato'nyonyabhinnāmapi  dadh‍yādiśāstrāṇāṃ
abhinnamekaṃ kāryaṃ</q> agnihotrahomaniṣ‍pattilakṣaṇamiti vaiṣamyam । <q>atra bhāṣyakāreṇoktam <quote>“aprakṛte﻿<pb n="r502"/>
na devatāntareṇa vājinasya sambandha iti ।</q> tadayuktam&mdash;prakṛtaviś‍vedevaparasambandhāt
vājinasyāpi ityāśaṅkyāha&mdash;<q>aprakṛtagrahaṇaṃ devatāntaragrahaṇaṃ ca devatāntarasambandhābhi&mdash;
prāyam । na padārthābhiprāyam ।</q> kasmādityāha&mdash;<q>padārthābhedepi</q> sambandhitayā <q>bhedāvaga-
mādityuktam ।</q> nanu padārthabhedo'pi kimiti na bhavatītyatrāha&mdash;<q>na padārthabhedaḥ śak‍yate'va-
gantum । annayogādviś‍veṣāṃ devānām ।</q> vājiśabdena teṣāmevābhidhānāt । tasmāt
padārthasya<note n="(1)"> G.<dn>abheda</dn></note> <q>bhedasambandhitaiva tu bhedaheturiti siddham ।</q></p>﻿<pb n="r503"/>
<p><q>adhikaraṇāntaraṃ vā । adhikaraṇāntaraṃ veti vadetaḥ ko'bhiprāyo bhāṣyakārasya ?
nanu ca guṇārthena punaḥ śrutirityatra na caitāni karmāntarāṇītyuktam ।</q> tena pūrvapakṣā-
bhāvāt nedamadhikaraṇāntaraṃ śak‍yate vak‍tuṃ iti bhāvaḥ । <q>atra vadamāḥ&mdash;ayamabhiprāyo bhāṣya-
kārasya । atrāhi hi yasmāt dadhyupasajanaṃ</q> dadhiviśiṣṭaṃ pradhānaṃ; payasa upasarjanatayā
payoviśiṣṭatayā nāvagamyate । <q>ato'nubandhāntarasaṃbandhāt ।</q> kārakāntarasaṃbandhāt
<q>ekāvagamyamanubandhaṃ na bhavati । tasmāt pradhānasyāpi</q> homasyānyasaṃbandhasyānyena
<q>saṃbandho nopapadyate</q> upasarjanasyeva । etaduktaṃ bhavati&mdash;yadyapi vāk‍yāntareṇa dadhyādi-
sambandhaḥ <note n="(1)"> R. <dn>itarathāp‍yakarma</dn></note>tathāp‍yekakarmaniveśitvaṃ tāvatteṣāmabhimatam । tena yasyaiva dadhiviśiṣṭatvaṃ tasyaiva
payoviśiṣṭatvamapīṣyate । na ca tacchak‍yate vak‍tuṃ, anyasambaddhasyānyasambandhānupapatteḥ ।
yathā hi upasarjanībhūtamanyasambaddhamanyena na sambadhyate tathā pradhānabhūtamapi; ko viśeṣo'nya-
sabandhitve upasarjanasya pradhānasya veti । <q>rāddhāntastu satyamevaṃ yadyasaṃbaddhasya samarpakaṃ nāsti
vaiśvadevavat</q> yathā viś‍veṣāṃ devānā dravyāntarāsambaddhānāmavagatirnāsti । yadi tathehāpi homa-
sya syāt tadā bhavedeva dravyāntarāsambandhaḥ, <q>ihatvagnihotraṃ juhotīti sarvānuvandhasaṃbandhitayā
﻿<pb n="r504"/>
<p><q>asaṃba(ndha)ddhamevānubandhāntaramavagamyata iti vaiṣamyam ।</q> asyārthaḥ&mdash;agnihotraṃ
juhoti iti homastāvat dravyāntarāvaruddho na pratīyate । tatra ca guṇavidhānaṃ śak‍yata eva ।
<q>uktaṃ ca tantravārtike</q>&mdash;
<lg><l>anyenānavaruddhena guṇo yatra vidhīyate ।</l>
<l>tasmin guṇavidhiḥ śak‍ya iti karma na bhidyate ।। iti</l></lg>
yathā tasmin dadhno vidhiḥ śak‍yaḥ tathā payaso'pi । yadi dadhisambaddhe eva payo vidhīyate tadā
bhavedaśak‍yatvam । tulyapramāṇaśiṣṭāstu guṇāḥ parasparānapekṣayaiva vidhīyanta iti nātra karma-
bhedaḥ ।</p>
<p>manvevamapi ekakal‍patve'pi vikalpaḥ prāpnotīti dūṣaṇamanirastamityāha&mdash;<q>vikal‍popanyā-
sastu phalapradarśanaṃ bhedāvagamasiddhayartham । uktena nyāyena na bhedāvagatiḥ siddhayatīti
vikal‍pasiddhiḥ ।</q> asyārthaḥ&mdash;bhāṣ‍yakāreṇa yat‍sidhyarthaṃ rāddhānte vikal‍paḥ syāditi maditaṃ nāsau
mūlayuktiḥ karmabhede sati idaṃ phalabhūtamityabhyuccayaḥ । uktena nyāyena karmaik‍ye sthite yadi
vikal‍po bhavati kiṃ kriyatāṃ pramāṇāyattatvādanuṣṭhānasya ।</p>﻿<pb n="r505"/> 
<p><q>phalaśruteḥ ।</q> atra bhāṣyakāreṇa <note n="(1)"> p. 510</note> <quote>‘yat‍karmatat phalavad dṛṣṭaṃ homo'pi karma tenāpi phala-
vatā bhavitavyaṃ’</quote> iti vadatā homa eva phalavān karmatvāt kṛṣivaditi sāmānyatodṛṣṭānumānamupanyastaṃ,
tathā vikal‍pasamādyā jātaya upanyastāḥ homo'p‍yasadṛśa iti vikal‍pasamā jātiḥ । homodapi nā-
dṛṣṭamityapakarṣasamā । vrīhireva bhavedityutkarṣasamā । tatra vikalpasamālakṣaṇaṃ&mdash;sādhanadharmayukta-
dharmāntaravikalpāt sādhye dharmāntaraṃ prasajataḥ vikal‍pasamā । udāharaṇaṃ&mdash;kriyāhetuguṇayuktaṃ kiñcid‍guru
yathāloṣṭaṃ kiñcil‍lughu yathā vāyuḥ evaṃ kriyāhetuguṇayuktaṃ kiñcitkriyāvat syāt yathā loṣṭaṃ,
kiñcidakriyaṃ yathā ātmā, viśoṣo vā vācya iti । atra hi sādhanadharmabhūtakriyāhetuguṇa-
yukte dṛṣṭānte loṣṭavāyvātmake dharmāntarasya gurulaghutvādeḥ vikal‍pāt sādhyepi siṣādhayiṣitadharma&mdash;
vikal‍paṃ prasajato dūṣaṇavādino vikal‍pasamā । evamatrāpi karmatve satyapi kiñcillāṅgalādisādhyaṃ
kiñcinna eva kiñcitphalavat kiñciccāphalaṃ syāt । dṛṣṭāntadharmaṃ sādhye samāsajataḥ ut‍karṣasamā ।
udāharaṇaṃ&mdash;yadi kriyāhetuguṇayogādātmā kriyāvān vāyuloṣṭavat, evaṃ sparśavānapi syāt ।
evamatrāpi yadi kriyātvāt kṛṣivat phalavān homaḥ tarhi dṛṣṭaphalaḥ tadvatsyāditi । sādhye
dharmābhāvaṃ dṛṣṭāntātprasajataḥ apakarṣasamā । loṣṭaṃ khalu kriyāvat na vibhu(tvāt) dṛṣṭaṃ 
kāmamātmāpi kriyāvānna vibhurastviti । atrāpi kṛṣivadeva homādapi nādṛṣṭaṃ phalaṃ syāditi ।
aparā api cātrajātayaḥ śak‍yante yojayituṃ kintu aśikṣitākṣapādamatānāmāyāso bhavatī-
tyuparamyate । tathā asiddhaviruddhānaikāntikābhidhānaṃ ca bhāṣyakāreṇa kṛtam । tatra lāṅgalādi-
sādhyatvādityasiddhatoktā । dravyaguṇāvapi phalavantau dṛṣṭau dravyaguṇatvāt avayavadravyavat
avayavasaṃyogavacceti sapratisādhanatayā anaikāntikatvamuktam । sapratisādhanau cānaikāntikāveva
saṃśayahetutvāt । ekānto hi niścaya ucyate sa prayojanaṃ yasya saḥ aikāntikaḥ aikāntiko na
bhavatītyanaikāntikaḥ niścayaviparītasaṃśayakāritvādanaikāntikaḥ dharmaviruddha ivādharmaḥ । ayaṃ
coparate karmaṇītyāderbhāṣyasyārthaḥ asya cetthamupapādanā । avayavadravyairavayavyārabhyate । teṣāṃ
cārabhamāṇānāṃ parasparasaṃyogā asamavāyikāraṇabhūtāḥ, asamyuktānāmanārambhakatvāt । ato
dravyaguṇāvapi phalavantau । nanu cātrāpi karmavyatirekeṇa saṃyogānāmanutpatteḥ avaś‍yamava-
yavānāṃ āśrayaṇīyaṃ karma । tataśca tata evāvayavyutpattirastviti nāsti sapratisādhanatā ।
atrocyate&mdash;uparate karmaṇi avayavaistatsaṃyogaiścāvayavyārabhyate । sarvatraiva hi saṃyogāduparatiḥ﻿<pb n="r506"/> 
karmaṇo'pi nāśahetoḥ bhāvāt । taduk‍taṃ <q>kāś‍yapena</q> <quote>‘kāryavirodhi karma’</quote> iti । karmaṇo
hi saṃyogavibhāgau vegākhyaśca saṃskāraḥ kāryeṇa । tatra saṃyogākhyena kāryeṇa karmaṇo virodhaḥ ।
tena saṃyogāduparate karmaṇi saṃyogottarakālaṃ dravyamutpadyamānaṃ na karmakāraṇakam । etacca prapañci-
tameva <q>padārthavidbhiḥ</q> <quote>“viruddhatā ceṣṭavighātakāritvalakṣaṇā sā coktā vrīhireva bhaveta”</quote> iti ।
vrīhibhavane hi guṇakarmatā syāt । guṇaḥ karma ca na niyogasya viṣayaḥ । aviṣayācca na
phalamityuktam । yasya ca śabdasyārthena phalaṃ sādhyate tenāpūrvaṃ kṛtvā netara-
syākṣepa iti<note n="1">R.<dn>nānyatheti</dn></note>। tasmādiṣṭāṃ phalasādhanatāmeva vihantīti iṣṭavighātakāritvalakṣaṇā viruddhatā ca ।
tadidaṃ sarvamākṣipati&mdash;<q>atha kimarthamidaṃ</q><note n="(2)"> R.<dn>kimidaṃ</dn></note> sāmānyato <q>dṛṣṭamanumānamupanyastamiti । punaśca
vikal‍pasamādyā jātayaḥ</q> kimarthamupanyastāḥ । <q>asiddhānaikāntikaviruddhābhidhānasya cāna-
vasara eva ।</q> śāstrabhedābhedasiddhayarthamanubandha<q>bhedābhedaparīkṣaṇaṃ hyatra pāde prakṛtam । tacca</q>
anubandhasya bhinnatvaṃ <q>śabdāntarādisamadhigamyam । kimatrānumānena</q> pūrvapakṣavādino'nubandhasya
bhinnatvaṃ sādhayataḥ upanyastena kriyate । tad‍dūṣaṇena kiṃ rāddhāntavādinaḥ । tasya hyetadeva﻿<pb n="r507"/>
vak‍tuṃ yuk‍tam nāyamanumānasya viṣaya iti ।<q> tasmādasaṃbaddhamevedaṃ granthakhaṇḍalakaṃ <note n="(1)"> G. <dn>bhedavido</dn></note>bhedā-
bhedavido manyante । ato yadeva vāk‍yabhedabhayāt karmāntaratvamuk‍taṃ tadeva vak‍tavyaṃ pūrvapakṣe</q>
guṇāddhi karmabhedaḥ tasmin pakṣe bhavati <note n="2"> G.<dn>prakaraṇādvā</dn></note>prakaraṇāntarādvā bhavati <q>na punaḥ pramāṇāntaramupanya-
sanīyam । atrocyate&mdash;nanu na śrutaṃ bhabatā śāstrabhedapratipattiranena lakṣaṇena kriyata iti ।</q>
tathāpi kimityāha&mdash;<q>na hi śāstrācchāstrabhodo'vagamyate । kiṃ tarhi ? anubandhānyatvāva-
gamya eva । tasya cānyatvaṃ pramāṇāntarāvagamyameva । taccedaṃ dadhnā'nubaddhaṃ karma na śās‍traṃ
bhinattītyuktam</q> āghārāgnihotrādhikaraṇe । <q>karmavattayā cākarmaṇi</q> guṇe <q>vidhānamityuk‍taṃ﻿<pb n="r508"/> 
tatraiva । ekagranthenāha&mdash;<q>evaṃ cetphalānubandhe'pi karmāpannameva guṇarūpaṃ</q> vidheyaṃ <q>na svataḥ
phalena saṃbandhayituṃ śak‍yate ।</q> <note n="1">R. <dn>guṇarūpaṃ phalepi</dn></note>guṇasvarūpaphalepi karmaiva guṇānubaddhaṃ vidheyaṃ, na punaḥ
kevalaṃ guṇarūpam । <q>ataḥ karmaṇā phalasaṃbandhāt karmāntaramidaṃ phalāntarānubandhāditi
pūrvapakṣī manyate ।</q></p>
<p>atra hi dadhisādhyo homa eva phalaṃ prati vidhīyate । evaṃ cedviśiṣṭasyaiva karmaṇo vidhīya&mdash;
mānatvāt karmāntaratvam । nanu vājapeyavadvāk‍yabhedaḥ prāpnoti । na prāp‍noti । viśiṣṭa&mdash;
vidhau paraṃ matvarthalakṣaṇā na punaraprasiddhalakṣaṇā<note n="(2)"> G.<dn>kal‍panā</dn></note>। dadhipadasya hi vājapeyavat karmanāmatayā
anyato'prasiddhakal‍panā sā cāyuk‍tā । lokikī hi lakṣaṇā । haṭho'prasiddhakalpanā । vājapeye
tu surāgrahavidhānāt peyabhūtavājasaṃbandhāt pravṛttinimittasaṃbandhena yuk‍taṃ nāmadheyatvam । yadi
punaratra prakṛtameva karma phalaṃ prati vidhīyate guṇasaṃbandho'vivakṣitaḥ syāt । atha guṇaphala-﻿<pb n="r509"/>
saṃbandho'pi vivakṣyate tadā phalasaṃbandhāt karmāntaratvameva, anyathā hi phalapadamanarthakaṃ syāt ।
atha dadhisādhyatayā prakṛtameva karma phalaṃ prati vidhīyate tadā phalārthatayā dadh‍no vidhānaṃ na syāt ।
avihite ca tasmin phalārthitayā dadhnā homaṃ na kuryāt; tatra punarapi dadhipadānarthakyameva । 
tasmāt tadviśiṣṭaṃ karmāntaraṃ vidhīyata iti siddham ।</p>
<p><q>evamap‍yanumānabhāṣyaṃ katham ?</q>  uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>itthamidaṃ idamanumānabhāṣyam ।
kiṃ kāryataḥ karmāpattiṃ dravyāṇāṃ manyate bhavān ।</q> rāddhāntyeva pūrvapakṣiṇaṃ pṛcchati
<q>yadi kāryata</q> iti । indriyādeḥ phalāya karmāpattiṃ karmarūpānupraveśitāṃ bhavān manyate ।
ekagranthenāha&mdash;<q>yadi kāryataḥ karmāpattiḥ syāt tadā bhavati phalāntarānubandhāt karmāntaram
akarmabhūtasya</q> karmānanupraviṣṭasya dravyasya <q>kāryayogo na vidyata iti</q> hetoḥ । <q>atha tu niyoga-
vaśāt tadāpattiravasīyate tadā yāvanniyogaviṣayaiva sā bhavitumarhati ।</q> guṇānuraktakarma-
viṣayatvenāṣi niyogasyāvirodhāt । guṇānurāgādeva <q>phalaṃ syāt na karmaṇāḥ ।</q> tataśca[na]karmā-
ntaratvasiddhiḥ । tena tvayā kāryata eva karmāpattirāśrayaṇīyā । sā cāyuk‍teti gūḍho'bhiprāyaḥ ।
pūrvapakṣī tu viditābhiprāya āha&mdash;<q>na hi kāryataḥ sā</q> karmāpattiḥ <q>śak‍yā'vagantum ।</q> kasmādi&mdash;﻿<pb n="r510"/>
tyāha&mdash;<q>śeṣavadanumānagamyo hi kāryakāraṇabhāvaḥ ।</q> śeṣaḥ kāryaṃ tadvati kāraṇe yadanumānaṃ
taccheṣavadanumānaṃ tena kāryakāraṇabhāvo'vagamyate । kāryāddhi yadanumāna kāraṇaviṣayaṃ pravartate
tena yadavagamyate tadeva tasya kāraṇamiti kalpyate । yadi hi tat tasya
kāraṇaṃ na syāt tadā kathaṃ tadanumīyate । tathāpi kimityāha&mdash;<q>tena ca
kāraṇamātrāvagatireva na punarviśeṣasyaiva</q> karmaṇa eva <q>kāraṇatāvagatiḥ</q> dravyaguṇayorapi
kāraṇatvāvirodhāt । nanu ca <q>sāmānyato dṛṣṭaṃ karmaṇa eva phalaṃ prati kāraṇatāmavagamayati
kṛṣ‍yādiṣu darśanāt</q> homākhyaṃ karmaiva phalavat karmatvāt kṛṣivaditi । etadapi sāmānyato
dṛṣṭaṃ dūṣayati&mdash;<q>tadidānīṃ sāmānyaṃ kimiti na vidmaḥ</q> homasya ca kṛṣeśca kiṃ sāmānyamiti na
vidmaḥ yaddaśanāt kṛṣau dṛṣṭaṃ phalasādhanatvaṃ homo'p‍yanumīyeta । nanu mābhṛt sāmānyaṃ sādṛśyaṃ tu
bhaviṣyatītyatrāha&mdash;<q>sādṛśyaṃ tu susadṛśena vyavadhīyate ।</q> asyārthaḥ&mdash;na homaḥ kṛṣeḥ sadṛśaḥ
śak‍yate vak‍tum anyasya susadṛśasya dṛṣṭārthasya[darśanāt] । [phala]kāraṇahomasya ca kṛṣeśca
kiṃ tat sāmānyamiti na vidmaḥ bhidyamānatvāt । susadṛśe hi pratīte mandasādṛśyayuktasya
sādṛśyamapaiti । etacca sādṛśyasya gamakatvamaṅgīkṛtyok‍tam । paramārthatastu na sādṛśyaṃ﻿<pb n="r511"/>
gamakaṃ; <q>atha viśeṣamātraṃ</q>, kṛṣihomayornāstyeva sāmānyamiti । dūṣayati&mdash;<q>homo'pi kṛṣ‍yantara-
meva prāpnoti ।</q> na ca homaḥ kṛṣiviśeṣatayā loke pratīyate । <q>atha sādhanādyanubandhakṛtaṃ</q>
sāmānyaṃ, sādhanaṃ sādhyaṃ ca tena sāmānyamastīti । dūṣayati&mdash;<q>tatrāpi dvayamāpatati sādhana-
viśeṣo vā anubandhatayā vā'tra parigṛhyate, sādhanamātraṃ vā</q> vāk‍yasya <q>viśeṣagrahaṇe na</q>
sāmānyāvagatiḥ <q>phaladevatayoḥ</q> kṛṣisādhanāllāṅgalādeḥ tatsādhyavrīhyāderanyatvāt । <q>atha
sāmānyaṃ</q> sādhanaṃ, etaduktaṃ bhavati&mdash;kārakasādhyatvamiti । dūṣayati&mdash;<q>na kriyātvamātrameva
tatrāvaśiṣyate ।</q> kārakasādhyatvaṃ hi kriyātvameva । <q>tasmiṃśca sāmānye'naikāntikatvaṃ
viruddhatā ca ।</q> dravyaguṇayorapi dravyaguṇau kāryau dṛśyete । dravyaṃ hi dravyasya guṇasya ca
samavāyikāraṇam । tathā guṇo'pi dravyasya guṇasya cāsamavāyikāraṇam । guṇānāṃ tu
guṇavattā'samavāyikāraṇatvaṃ pracurameva । saṃyogākhyo hi guṇaḥ dravyasyāsamavāyikāraṇaṃ
rūpādayaḥ kāryadravye rūpādikamārabhante । agnisaṃyogācca[pākajarūpādayaḥ] ityādi vak‍tumati-
bahutvādaśak‍yam । tena sapratisādhanatālakṣaṇānaikāntikatā । sā cādāvuktā ।﻿<pb n="r512"/> 
viruddhatā ca sarvatra guṇakarmāvagateḥ ।</q> etacca prāgeva kṛtavivaraṇam ।  <q>tasmānna kāryataḥ
karmāpattirdravyāṇāṃ śak‍yate'vagantumiti</q> pūrvapakṣavādyupasaṃhāraḥ । vādinopasaṃhṛte rāddhāntī
pṛcchati&mdash;<q>kiṃ tarhi ?</q> karmāpattiḥ । uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>niyogata eva bhāvāpattiranugamanīyā</q> niyoga-
svabhāva evāyaṃ yena bhāvārtha eva tasya viṣayo bhavati nānya iti niyogasvabhāvaparyālocanayaiva
bhāvānupraveśitā dravyāṇāmabhidhātavyā । nānyathā । kathaṃ tarhi karmānyatvamityāha&mdash;<q>sa
cāyaṃ niyogaḥ homameva dadhisādhanaṃ phalasaṃbandhitayā'vagamayatīti</q> tasyaiva viṣayatvamiti
<q>karmabhedaḥ ।</q> anyathā hi yadi karmabhedo na syāt <q>homāsaṃbandhānna dadhnaḥ</q> karmāpattiḥ <q>prāpnoti ।</q>
asyārthaḥ&mdash;yadi prakṛtamidaṃ karma bhavet tadā tasya phalasaṃbandhaparamidaṃ vāk‍yaṃ bhavet । tataśca
dadh‍neti padaṃ homenāsaṃbadhyamānaṃ pṛthag‍vāk‍yaṃ syāt । tatastatrāpi na kevalasya phalasaṃbandha iti
karmāpattiranusaraṇīyā । na cāsāvavagamyate । <q>anavagamyamānā ca phale, na saṃbadh‍yata
ityuktam ।</q> atha prakṛtameva karma laukikakriyākārakasaṃbandhāśrayaṇena dadhnā kārakabhūtena﻿<pb n="r513"/> 
viśiṣṭaṃ phale vidhīyate tatrāha&mdash;<q>kimiti vā dadh‍nāhomo nirvartyate yadi na homārthaṃ dadhi
syāt ।</q> na kriyākārakasaṃbandhamātrāvagamenaidamarthyam । na cedamarthavyatirekeṇa dadh‍na
upādānaṃ anaṅgatvāt । aṅge hi karmataḥ vyāpanne vaiguṇyamaidamarthyaṃ ca vidhigamyam । yadi
homasya prakṛtasya phalasaṃbandhaḥ tasya ca homasya dadhisaṃbandha ityāśrīyate tato vāk‍yabhedaḥ
<q>tasmāt padadvayānvita evāyamarthaḥ phalena saṃbadhyata iti karmāntaram । anyathā hyāśri-
tatvāt prayogasyeti ।</q> yeyaṃ bhāvārthānāṃ niyogaviṣayatve yuktiḥ sā ayuktiḥ syāt । <q>yadi
kevalasyāpi</q> dravyasya <q>phalena saṃvandhaḥ syāt । ato viśiṣṭabhāvānupraveśitaiva</q> dravyasya
<q>phalasaṃbandhe hetuḥ ।</q> nanu kambalanirṇejanabdugayārthatāśaṅkā na yuktā, yasmācchabdaikasamādhi-
gamyametat । na cobhayaṃ śabdo'vagamayitumalam ityatrāha&mdash;<q>kambalanirṇejanopanyāsastu na
kāryataḥ karmāpattiriti prakaṭayati ।</q> kāryataḥ karmāpattirnāsti, kintu niyogata iti
yaduk‍taṃ tadevānena codyapurassaraṃ spaṣṭīkṛtam ।</p>﻿<pb n="r514"/> 
<p><q>atulyatvāt । atrābhidhīyate । satyam । karmatāmāpannasya guṇasya vidhānaṃ
na punaḥ karmārthatayaiveti ।</q> asyārthaḥ&mdash;dadhisādhyo homa eva phale vidhīyate <note n="(1)">G.<dn>na ca homaḥ</dn></note>sa ca homaḥ
prakṛta eva । na ca vāk‍yabhedaḥ dadhno vidhānābhāvāt । laukikena hi kriyākārakasaṃbandhena
dadhihomau parasparasaṃbaddhau, naidamarthyena । yadyapi ca homaṃ prati na dadhno vidhānaṃ tathāpi
phalārthinā dadh‍nā homaḥ kartavyaḥ । dadhyanurāgasya homagatasya anyathā saṃpattyabhāvāt ।
tasmānna karmārthatayā dadhno vidhānam । avidhāne vā kathaṃ karmāpattiḥ ? uttaram&mdash;<q>kriyākāraka-﻿<pb n="r515"/>
lakṣaṇaṃ hi saṃbandhamāśritya dravyāṇāṃ tadāpattiḥ</q> karmaṇi saṃbandhaḥ  <q>na punaḥ tādarthyamāśritya ।</q>
yadi hi tathā syāt  tadā<note n="(1)">G. <dn>karmaṇaḥ</dn></note>akarmaṇaḥ kriyānupraveśo na syāt । tasya kriyāṃ prati tādarthyā-
bhāvāt । tadanupraveśābhāve cākārakatvaprasaṅgāt tadāha&mdash;<q>akarmaṇo'kārakatvaprasaṅgāt 
iti । ato</q> homārthatvena vidhānābhāvāt <q>phalārthataiva</q> home <q>kārakabhūtasya dadh‍naḥ pratīyate</q>
nanu syāt phalārthatā, homārthatvamap‍yaparaṃ bhavatu ityatrāha&mdash;<q>homārthatvepi vākyabhedastvayai-
vok‍taḥ । viśiṣṭavidhānaṃ kimiti nāśrīyate ?</q> uttaram&mdash;viśiṣṭavidhānaṃ nāśrīyate agnihotraṃ
<q>juhotīti homāvacchinnasya karmaṇaḥ</q> puruṣaprayat‍nasya <q>prāptatvāt । anubandhasya cāprāptatvāt
tāvatā cendriyakāmādhikāranirvṛttau na śak‍yate prāptirbādhitum । nanu cāpṛthagavagamādanu-
bandhadvayasya na pṛthak‍tvenāvacchedaḥ śak‍yate'vagantum ।</q> homasya dadh‍naśca parasparasabandhānna﻿<pb n="r516"/> 
śak‍yaḥ pṛthak‍tvenāvacchedaḥ pratyetum । pṛthak‍tvena cānavagame kathametaddadhimātraṃ vidhīyate
homaśca prāptatvānna vidhīyata iti । <q>ucyate । kimatra pṛthak‍tvenāvacchedaḥ kariṣyati
yāvadaprāptaṃ hi niyogasya viṣaya ityuk‍tam ।</q> nanvevamapi dadh‍yevāprāptamiti tadeva viṣayo
niyogasyetyāpatitam । tatrāha&mdash;<q>karmāpatteśca juhotirviṣayaḥ</q> prāptāprāptavivekena dadh‍no
niyogaviṣayatvaṃ, avagatidaśāyāṃ tu homasyaiva । <q>tasmāj‍juhotyavacchinnavyāpārāśrito
dadhivyāpāraḥ phalāya codyate ।</q> nanu dadhivyāpāro dadh‍yevāśritaḥ ataḥ kathaṃ homāśrita﻿<pb n="r517"/> 
ityucyate ityāśayenāha&mdash;<q>kimidamāśrita iti kārakatāmāpanna ityarthaḥ ।</q> kārakakoṭi&mdash;
niviṣṭatvāt kārakatāmāpanna ityuk‍tam । <q>tasmāddhome kārakaṃ phalāya codyate । kena punaḥ
phale dadh‍yādi viniyuk‍tam</q> yena phalāya codyata ityucyate । uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>karmavāk‍yena ।</q>
ayamāśayaḥ&mdash;yena karma viniyujyate tena dadh‍yādyapīti । <q>adhikārānupapattyeti cet ।</q>
kāmino'dhikāraḥ phalasiddhiṃ vinā'nupapadyamānaḥ phalasiddhimavahamayatīti cet । dūṣayati
&mdash;<q>tulyamatrāpi । <quote>“ata evocevṛttikāreṇa”</quote></q> iti bhāṣyamākṣipati&mdash;<q>vṛttikāravacanaṃ kiṃparaṃ
bhāṣyakārasya ?</q>  samādhatte&mdash;<q>idaṃparam । kārakāpattirāśrayaśabdenocyate nārthāntaramiti</q>
pradarśayituṃ vṛttikāravacane āśritaśabdaṃ vyākhyātuṃ etaduk‍tam । anyathā kaścid‍vṛtti&mdash;
kāramatena virodhamāśaṅketa iti । idaṃ ca vāk‍yaṃ liṅgenāpakṛṣya vyutkrameṇa vyākhyātam ।
yata eva kārakatāpattirāśritaśabdārthaḥ <q>ata eva āśritatvātprayogasyetyatrāp‍yayamevārthaḥ ।</q>
bhāvārthānāṃ prayogaḥ dravyaguṇābhyāmāśritaḥ tatra dravyaguṇau kārakatāmāpannau iti yāvat ।</p>﻿<pb n="r518"/> 
<p>atra bhāṣyaṃ <note n="(1)"> P. 515</note> <quote>“ye bhavadīyaṃ pakṣamāśrīyeran te śrutimapabādheraṃstarām”</quote> iti । <q>kaḥ punaratra
tarabarthaḥ ?</q> ekagranthenāha&mdash;<q>ekatra home vidhīyate । anyatra dadh‍yarthaḥ na kaścidatiśayaḥ
pakṣadvaye'pi dṛśyate । ucyate; ayamasti viśeṣaḥ dadhipade hi bādh‍yamāne homapadamapi bādhitaṃ
bhavati । atastatsaṃbandhena hi tadvidheyamityuk‍tam&mdash;āśritatvātprayogasyeti ।</q> yasya
hi mate dadhneti bādhitaṃ tasya mate juhotītyapi bādhitameva homamātrasya prāptatvenāvidheyatvāt
