dadhyanubandhasya cāprāptatvāt tadanurakta eva homo vidhīyate । yadi homaḥ prāptaḥ dadhivā
aprāptaṃ tadeva kimiti na vidhīyata ityatrāha&mdash;<q>āśritatvātprayogasyeti । tasmāt saṃbandhibādhe
saṃbandhyantarabādhaḥ so'yamatiśayaḥ tarabarthaḥ । homamātrabādhe tu na kiñcidbādhitam ।
kevalasyānavagamāt ।</q> homamātraśabdena dadh‍yanavacchinno homo'bhimataḥ tasmin bādhite'pi na
kaścidbādhitaḥ <q>kevalasyānavagamāt ।</q> avagatatyāgo hi bādhaḥ । na ca kevalāvagatiḥ tena
kevalatyāge na kiñcittyaktam । kathaṃ tarhi kevalo'vagamyata ityatrāha&mdash;<q>prāptimātratayā</q> hi
<q>kevalāvagatiḥ</q> na vidheyatayā । prāpticintāyāṃ kevalaṃ prāptamityucyate vidheyastu dadh‍yunu-
bandha eva । <q>kathamiti anayā agnihotretikartavyatayeti</q> bhāṣyamanubhāṣitam ।</p>﻿<pb n="r519"/>
<p>ākṣipati&mdash;<q>nanu coparitanaṣaṭa‍kacinteyam kimityatropanyasyate ।</q> astyatro-
<q>panyāsakāraṇam । kiṃ tat ?</q>  idaṃ tat । guṇaphalasambandhe hi itikartavyatāsaṃbandho na śak‍yate-
'vadhārayitum । mā'vadhāri tathāpi kimityāha&mdash;<q>na cetikartavyatāśūnyo'dhikāravidhiḥ ।
<q>kuta etat ?</q>  uttaram&mdash;<q>adhikāraniṣṭho hi vidhiḥ niyogārthasādh‍yatayā'vagamyate ।</q> niyo-
gārthaḥ sādhyo yasminnasau niyogārthasādhyaḥ tasya bhāvaḥ tattā tayā'vagamyate । itthaṃbhūtalakṣaṇe
tṛtīyā । <q>na ca sādh‍yamanitikartavyatākamasti । ananuguhītasya karaṇatānupapatteḥ ।
sarvadā hi karaṇaṃ karaṇaṃ syāt</q> yadyananugṛhītamapi karaṇaṃ karaṇaṃ bhavet । <q>katha punariti&mdash;
kartavyatā'vadhārayituṃ na śak‍yate ।</q> uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>upadeśatastāvan‍na saṃbhavati nityānitya&mdash;
saṃyogavirodhāditi</q> darśitam tṛtīye । <q>atideśatastarhi bhavatu ।</q> pariharati&mdash;<q>so'pi
naivo'papadyate ityabhiprāyaḥ । kathaṃ nopapadyate ?</q>  it‍thaṃ nopapadyate, <q>dhātvarthasyānyaprayuk‍tatvāt ।</q>﻿<pb n="r520"/> 
tatprayogāśritatvācca guṇaphalasaṃbandhasya ।</q> dadh‍nendriyakāmasya juhuyāditi yo'yaṃ
homarūpo dhātvarthaḥ sa svādhikāraprayuktaḥ tatprayuk‍timāśritya guṇena phalaṃ kriyate । tathāpi
kimityāha&mdash;<q>anyaprayogaprayuk‍tasya</q> ca dharmajātasyānyena <q>saṃbandho nopapadyata</q> (yadātithyā-
yā ityatra) yannāma dharmajātaṃ anyadīvayāgaprayuk‍tyā tatprayuk‍taṃ tasyānyena saṃbandho nopapadyate ।
&mdash;<q>uktametat yadātithyāyā ityatra ।</q> ātithyāprayuk‍tasya barhiṣo nopasadbhiḥ agnīṣomīyeṇa
vā saṃbandho ghaṭate । tena sādhāraṇopadeśa iti । idaṃ ca dharmajātaṃ nityādhikāraprayuk‍taṃ na
sādhāraṇaṃ nityānityasaṃyogavirodhaprasaṅgāt । ato na guṇaphalādhikāreṇa saṃbadhyate ।
nanu upadeśena mā saṃbadhyatām, atideśena saṃbadhyatāṃ ityatrāha&mdash;<q>atideśo'pi naivāprayo-
jakasya ।</q> asyārthaḥ&mdash;iha hi dharmajātaṃ  prati prakṛtivikāraniyogasyaiva prayojakatvaṃ tatraiva
viniyogāt na guṇaphalādhikārasya yaścāprayojakaḥ na tasyātideśo yuktaḥ anyasaṃbandhasya
anyasaṃbandhapratītivirodhāt yadātithyāyāmiva । <q>tasmāditi</q>kartavyatāśūnyatayā <q>durbhaṇaiveyaṃ guṇa-
phalādhikāracodanā ।</q> nanu anyaprayuk‍taivetikartavyatā prasaṅgenopakārikā syāt ityatrāha
&mdash;<q>nātra prasaṅgaḥ śak‍yate vak‍tum prāp‍tyabhāvāt । prāptasya dharmajātasya</q> yatkāryaṃ tasyānya&mdash;
<q>dīyena dharmajātena siddhiḥ prasaṅgaḥ na cātra prāptirastīti pradarśitaṃ upadeśātideśayora-﻿<pb n="r521"/> 
saṃbhavāt । ataḥ kimatrā</q>gnihotretikartavyatā sannidhiḥ <q>codanāliṅgaṃ vā kariṣyati</q> prāpti-
virahāt । <q>atrocyate&mdash;bhavatvatideśāt</q> kāryataḥ <q>saṃbandhaḥ</q> itikartavyatāyāḥ । <q>nanu ca
paraprayogāśrayī guṇaprayogavidhirityuktam ।</q> pariharati&mdash;<q>nāyaṃ doṣaḥ anyaprayuk‍tasyānyena
sahopadeśo nopapadyate । atideśe punaḥ kāryataḥ saṃbandhamatideśavido manyante ।</q> ati-
deśātsaṃbandhe ko viśeṣaḥ iti pṛcchati&mdash;<q>tataḥ kiṃ ?</q> uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>kāryataḥ saṃbandhe hi
viniyogāvagaterna virodhaḥ ।</q> tadvadbhāvena prāptāt karaṇopakāralakṣaṇāt kāryāt padārthānāṃ
saṃbandhe nāsti(vi)niyogaḥ prakṛtyarthasyaiva vikṛtau kāryataḥ prāptiḥ tasmādvirodho nāstītyāha
&mdash;<q>yatra hi kāraṇapurassarā kāryāvagatiḥ sa viniyogasya viṣayaḥ । yatra punaḥ kāryataḥ
kāraṇāvagatiḥ so'tideśasya ।</q> yatra kāraṇabhūtapadārthapurassarā kāryasya karaṇopakāratyā-
vagatiḥ sa viniyogasya viṣayaḥ ।</p>
<p>prakṛtau hi padārthā eva prathamamavagamyate । teṣu gṛhīteṣu paścāt karaṇopakāraḥ teṣāṃ
dvārabhūto'dhika rabidhinā kalpyate । bikṛtau tu karaṇopakārāpekṣāyāṃ prākṛte karaṇopakāre gṛhīte
punastajjanakāpekṣā  jāyate । nanu nirjñātajanakasya karaṇopakārasya janakāpekṣaiva nāsti ।
ucyate ।  syādetadevaṃ yadi karaṇopakāramātraparyavasāyino dharmā bhaveyuḥ । te tvapūrvagṛhītāḥ
pūrvaṃ paścāt teṣāṃ dvāramātratayā karaṇopakārasaṃbandhaḥ । tena prakṛtyapūrvavartinameva te upakāraṃ
te janayanti ityupadeśenāvagatam । ato'pūrvāntaram । prāpte tasmin‍nupakāre anirjñātajanake﻿<pb n="r522"/>
tasmin yuk‍taiva janakāpekṣā । tataśca tabhyopakārasyānyatra padārthaiḥ saṃbandhaḥ pratipannaḥ te ca
padārthāstadupakāraprāp‍tyā smṛtipathamupayānti । taiśca sannihitaiḥ yogyaiḥ apekṣitaiścānvito vaikṛta-
vāk‍yavartinā liṅādiśabdenaiva sbārtho'bhidhīyate । so'yaṃ padārthānāmatideśaḥ karaṇopakāralakṣaṇa-
purassarā kāraṇabhūtapadārthāvagatirucyate । <q>yeṣāṃ tu</q> nirjñātajanakatayā padārthānāṃ prākṛtānāṃ
vikṛtau karaṇopakārasidhyarthamanuṣṭhānameva kevalaṃ na punaḥ saṃbandhāntarāvagama iti mataṃ teṣāmupadeśa
eva kevalaṃ dharmāṇāṃ, vikṛtāvap‍yupadeśe cohādyabhāvaḥ iti vakṣyāmaḥ saptame bhāgitvabidhyantayo-
rviśeṣaṃ kathayantaḥ । prapañcitaścāyamarthaḥ padārthātideśe । <q>tasmādviniyogavaiṣamyāt</q> iti-
kartavyatāsambandhivighāto yadātithyāyāmitivadiha <q>nāsti । tasmāt sūktamanayā'gnihotreti-
kartavyatayā</q> kāryataḥ prāptayā setikartavyatāko guṇaphalādhikāraḥ iti sakṣepārthaḥ । <q>atha
kasmādagnihotramevetikartavyatā</q> agnihotretikartavyateti bhāṣyārthoṃ <q>na bhavati ।</q> kathamayamarthaḥ
syāditi tatrāha&mdash;<q>āśraya evānugrāhako dravyāṇām kāryaṃ sādhayatām । āśritatvāt
prayogasyeti darśitam ।</q> homamāśritya phalaṃ sādhayato dadhnaḥ homasvarūpamevānugrāhakam ।
dūṣayati&mdash;<q>bāliśabhāṣitametat । agnihotraṃ dadh‍yanuraktameva karaṇamityuktam । kevalasyā-
navagamāt ।</q> naca svāt‍maiva svānugrāhako yuktaḥ yadyagnihotrādeva phalaṃ kathaṃ tarhiguṇātphala-
miti vyapadeśaḥ tatrāha&mdash;<q>prayuktistu kevalāśrayaprāp‍tyanusāreṇa iti guṇaphalamityucyate ।</q>
kevalo homo nityādhikāraprayuktaḥ āśrayabhūto guṇasya । guṇamātraṃ tu guṇādhikāraprayuktamiti﻿<pb n="r523"/> 
guṇasyānanyaprayojanatvāt tadupanipātena ca homāt phalasiddheḥ guṇasyaiva phalaṃ prati janakatvaṃ
vyupadiśyate । <q>tasmāt ṣaṣṭhīsamāsa evāyaṃ agnihotretikartavyatayeti ।</q> nanvagnihotrasyaikatve
kathama/?/deśa ucyate । adhikārabhedādeva adhikārārthatvāddharmāṇāṃ ekatvepi ca yukto'ti-
deśaḥ jyotiṣṭomavat । yathā nityasaṃsthajyotiṣṭomasya kāmyasaṃsthe dharmātideśaḥ tathehāpi । nanu
yadi dharmāṇāṃ upadeśātideśābhyāṃ prāptibhedaḥ tadā anuṣṭhānabhedo'pi syāt ityatrāha&mdash;<q>atideśa-
prāptasya ca dharmajātasya prasaṅgāt kāryasiddhiriti siddhamanāvṛttyaivānuṣṭhānam ।</q> <quote>“atha vā
dadhiśabdasya vivakṣitārthatvāt”</quote> iti bhāṣyamanubhāṣyākṣipati&mdash;<q>kimidaṃ pakṣāntaramivopanyasyate ?</q>
pṛcchati&mdash;<q>kimiti vā na pakṣāntaram ?</q>  uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>tadeva hi dadhyanurak‍taṃ homarūpaṃ phalā-
yetyupasaṃhṛtaṃ</q> atrāpi । etacca pūrvamap‍yuktam । tasmānnedaṃ pakṣāntaram । nanu dadhihoma-
saṃbandhasya phalāya vidhānamanena bhāṣyeṇocyate na homarūpasyetyatrāha&mdash;<q>yuk‍taṃ caitat</q> homasvarūpaṃ
phalāya codyata iti <q>saṃbandhasyānurāgāvagamyatvāt ।</q> dadhyanurak‍teti home'vagate saṃbandho
nāntarīyako'vagamyate । tena paropaśliṣṭasaṃbandhaḥ phalena saṃbandhayitumeva na śak‍yate । homa
eva dadhyanuraktaḥ phalāya codyata iti yuktam । <q>atrocyate । pakṣāntaraśaṅkānirā&mdash;
karaṇāyaitat na pakṣāntarapradarśanārthaṃ bhāṣyam ।</q>  tatrāthavāśabdaḥ āśaṅkitapakṣanirā-﻿<pb n="r524"/>
karaṇāya yathā <quote>“arthavaddharmaṃ prati pratipannā”</quote> iti । <q>kā punaratra pakṣāntaraśaṅkā yā nirā-
kriyate ?</q>  ucyate । dadhnā juhotītyanena yo dadhisaṃbandho'vagataḥ sa phalāyānena codyatām । kathaṃ
homādeva phalamiti <q>kecit teṣāmidamuttaram</q>&mdash;<quote>“atha vā dadhiśabdasya vivakṣitatvāt”</quote> iti
bhāṣyaṃ kathamuttaraṃ ityāśaṅkaya  vyācaṣṭe&mdash;<q>dadhiśabdasya vivakṣitatvāt ।</q> dadhyanuraktāddhomāt
phalasaṃbandhasya vivakṣitatvāt na saṃbandhāt phalaṃ, dadhnendriyakāmasyetyatra dadhyanurak‍taṃ homarūpameva
pratīyate, na saṃbandhaḥ । tasmāddhomādeva dadhyanuraktāt phalaṃ na homasaṃbandhāt । <q>atasmiddho
guṇaphalādhikāraḥ ।</q></p>
<p><q>sameṣu karmayuktaṃ syāt । uk‍taṃ guṇānubandhāt karmaṇaḥ phalamiti । tadidānīṃ
kīdṛśo viṣaye iti nirūpaṇāyaitadadhikaraṇadvayam । nanu śāstrabhedābhedacintā  atra﻿<pb n="r525"/>
prakṛtā ।</q> tenānenāp‍yadhikaraṇadvayena śāstrabhedābhedanirūpaṇaiva kartavyā । kiṃ viṣaya&mdash;
nirūpaṇayā । pariharati&mdash;<q>saiveyaṃ</q> śāstrabhedābhedacintā <note n="(1)"> G. <dn>viṣayatayā</dn></note><q>viṣayato nirūp‍yate । nanu ca
viparītamatredam ।</q> kasmādiyāha&mdash;<q>śāstrabhedo hi guṇaphalasaṃbandhe'pi vidyata eva ।
kathamatra nannirākaraṇādbhedaḥ ।</q> asyārthaḥ&mdash;yadi pūrvapakṣasiddhāntayoḥ śāstrabhedābhede <note n="(2)"> G.<dn>virodhaḥ</dn></note>viśeṣaḥ 
syāt tadā idamadhikaraṇamatra cintayitamucitam । iha punaḥ pūrvapakṣe guṇaphalasaṃbandhepi
śāstrāntaratvamastyeva । sādh‍yabhedāt । rāddhāntepi vidyata eva sādhyabhedādanubandhabhedācca ।
athocyeta pūrvapakṣe guṇaphalasaṃbandhe karmabhedo nāsti rāddhānte karmabheda iti yuktācintā iti ।
tatrāha&mdash;<q>śāstrabhedābhedakathā ceyaṃ iti bhāṣyavidaḥ । tasmādasamañ‍jasamiṃda karmabhedābheda&mdash;
nirūpaṇam । atrocyate । satyaṃ</q> guṇe'pi phalāya codyamāne <q>śāstrabhe</q>do'styeva । aprayo-
jakastvāśrayasya guṇaphalādhikāra iti <q>na bhedena vyapadiśyate । dhātvarthānubandhabhede punaḥ﻿<pb n="r526"/> 
saha prayok‍tṛtayā śās‍traṃ bhidyata iti bhedo vyapadiśyate ।</q> anuṣṭhānaparyantaṃ hi
śāstram । tena yatrānuṣṭhānabhedaḥ tatra śāstrabhedabuddhiḥ sphuṭatarā । yatra punaranuṣṭhānabhedo
nāsti tatra sannapi śāstrabhedo'sanniva pratīyate । yata eva prayok‍tṛtvabhedābhedābhyāṃ śāstrabheda-
buddhiḥ sphuṭā sphuṭatarā <q>ata eva ca <quote>‘athāto dharmajijñāsā”</quote> ityanena</q> sūtreṇa
<q>prayok‍tṛtvābhadena</q> adhyayanaśāstrādhyāpanaśāstrayorabhedaṃ <q>manvānasyedamuktamuttaram । ato
dhātvarthānubandhabhede guṇānubandhabhede ca viśeṣo'stīti viṣayanirūpaṇam ।</q> kiṃ sphuṭatara-
midaṃ śās‍traṃ utāsphuṭataramiti cintyate । pūrvapakṣe guṇaphalasaṃbandhāt prayok‍tṛtvābhedāt
asphuṭataram । siddhānte tu dhātvarthānubandhabhedāt prayok‍tṛtvābhedācca tadbhedāt sphuṭataraṃ iti
viśeṣa iti yuk‍taṃ vak‍tuṃ viṣayanirūpaṇam । <q>kathaṃ punaḥ agniṣṭomasāma kṛtvā yajeta iti﻿<pb n="r527"/>
pūrvāparībhāvaḥ ? kathaṃ vā nāsti ?</q>  uttaram&mdash;<q>savanadvaye hyatīte agniṣṭomasāmaprayogaḥ</q> tena
yāgaḥ pūrvakālassan agniṣṭomasāmā cāparakālaḥ । nanu tṛtīyasavanagatayāgāpekṣayā bhaviṣyati pūrvā-
parībhāvaḥ ityatrāha&mdash;<q>ekaścāyaṃ yajyarthaḥ</q> savanatrayepi । tenāsau na pūrvatayā nāpi paratayā
vyapadeṣṭuṃ yukta iti bhāvaḥ । <q>tasmādanupapattiḥ</q> pūrvāparībhāvasya । etadeva codyaparihāradvāreṇa
vivarītumupakramate&mdash;<q>nanu ca grahayajāvapi sa evāyamagniṣṭutsaṃjñako yāgaḥ ityupapadyate pūrvāparī-
bhāvaḥ ।</q> yo'sau tārtīyasavaniko grahayajiḥ tatrāpi sa evāgniṣṭutsaṃjñako grahayajiḥ tato'gniṣṭu-
tsāmāpekṣaṃ paratvamupapannaṃ tasmātsa evetyāha&mdash;<q>abhyāso hi sakalasya dhātvarthasya naikadeśasya ।</q>
pariharati&mdash;<q>ata eva ca nopapadyate</q> pūrvāparībhāvaḥ । yata evābhyāsaḥ sakalasya pūrvamapi
<q>sakalasyānuṣṭhānāt ।</q> punaścodayati&mdash;<q>parastādap‍yasti</q> so'gniṣṭatsaṃjñako yāgaḥ <q>ityupapadyata</q>
iti cet । dūṣayati&mdash;<q>na ayathābhūtatvādasyārthasya ।</q> yathābhūtaḥ śabdāta pratīyate
ekāntena parastāttvena tathābhūtasvabhāvaḥ artho nāsti pūrvāparakālavartitvāt । tena śabdā-
vagatā pūrvāparatā nopapadyate । <q>yatra hi yathābhūtaḥ pratīyamāna evārthaḥ śabdāt svabhāva-
to'pi tathaiva tatrāvipratipattiḥ</q> śabdārthayorbhavati । <q>anyathābhāve tu nautpattikatvaṃ syāt ।
autpattikaśca śabdārthayossaṃbandha iti gaditam । ato nābhyāsavaśāt</q> agniṣṭomasām﻿<pb n="r528"/> 
kṛtvā yajetetyupapadyate । sābhyāsasya yajyarthasya uttarakālīnatā'vadhāryate ।</q> na ca sā vāstavī
vidyate । <q>na caitat bhāṣyakāreṇāvamṛṣṭaṃ</q> yena tadvacanādvinirṇayaḥ syāt । tasmādasaṃbaddha-
midaṃ vāk‍yaṃ kathamudāharaṇatāṃ pratipadyate । pariharati&mdash;<q>ucyate । anavamarśanīyamevaitat</q>
yataḥ kācidap‍yanupapattirnāsti ।  yata evānavamarśanīyamevedaṃ ata eva bhāṣyakāreṇānavamṛṣṭam ।
kutaḥ ? uttaram&mdash;<q>samānakartṛkatvāpekṣatvāt pūrvāparībhāvasya ।</q> samānakartṛkayoḥ pūrva&mdash;
kāla iti smaraṇāt । samānakartṛkatvāparityāgena pūrvāparībhāvo varṇanīyaḥ । tathāpi kiṃ
ityata āha&mdash;<q>sa ca pratītāvevopapadyate । nānuṣṭhāne । samānakartṛkatāvyāghātāt</q> yadya-
nuṣṭhānagataḥ pūrvāparībhāvo<note n="(1)"><dn>gṛhyate</dn></note>'vagamyate samānakartṛkatā vyāhanyena । tena pratītāvevāśrayaṇīyam ।
tena samānakartṛkayoḥ dhātvarthayormadhye yaḥ pūrvaṃ pratīyate tatra vartamānāddhātoḥ k‍tvāpratyayo bhavatīti
sūtrārthaḥ । tasmādanuṣṭhānagatāśrayaṇe samānakartṛkatāvyāghāta ityāha&mdash;<q>ekārthānāṃ dhātvarthā-
nāmanuparatyā(nupūrvyā)'nuṣṭhānaṃ samānakartṛkatvamucyate ।</q> samāno hi kartā ekaḥ kartoṃcyate
kriyāvacchedena hi kartṛtvam । tatra yadi kriyābhedaḥ āśrīyeta tadā kartṛbhedaḥ syāt ।
nānābhūtānāṃ ca dhātvarthānāmekaprayojanavaśīkāranibandhanamekatvaṃ, ata ekaprayojanāvacchinnānāṃ
dhātvarthānāṃ ekayā pravṛttyā anuparatyā'nuṣṭhoyamānānāṃ samānakartṛkatvam । <q>tatra pūrvamidaṃ kṛtvā
paścāt kartavyamiti na śak‍yate vak‍tuṃ vyavacchedaprasaṅgāt ।</q> bhedaprasaṅgādityarthaḥ bheda-
﻿<pb n="r529"/> 
nibandhano hi pūrvāparībhāvaḥ naikasminnevaupapadyate । tenānuṣṭhāne paurvāparyāsaṃbhavāt pratītāveva
paurvāparyamāśrayaṇīyam । taccātrāpi saṃbhavati ।</p>
<p>yadyekārthānāṃ samānakartṛkāṇāṃ paurvāparyaṃ <q>kathaṃ tarhi darśapūrṇamāsābhyāmiṣṭ‍vā somena
yajeteti ।</q> tatraikārthatā nāsti । na ca samānakartṛkataiva nāstīti vācyam । <note n="(1)"> G. <dn>pratyayāntarābhāva</dn></note>k‍vāpratya-
pratyayābhāvaprasaṅgāt । uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>adhikāramātraṃ taditi vakṣyāmaḥ ।</q> nātra samānakartṛkatā
vivakṣitā । kintu pūrvakālatā, prayogasiddheyaṃ pūrvakālatā'nuṣṭhānep‍yāśrīyate । sā cādhikāra-
vaśena bhavati tena kṛtadarśapūrṇamāsaḥ some adhikārī ityetāvanmātramatra vivakṣitam । kvāpratyayastu
tāvanmātraparatvenāyathārtha eva prayuktaḥ । <q>tasmādatrāvagatau pūrvakālatā mukhaṃ vyādāya svapiti
itivatprayogasiddheḥ ।</q> yathā ceyaṃ pratītigatā pūrvakālatā anuṣṭhāne'p‍yāśrīyate tathā pañcame
vakṣyāmaḥ । pūrvapakṣamākṣipati&mdash;<q>kathamatra guṇaphalāśaṅkā । guṇāśravaṇāt vāravantīyaṃ sāma
kṛtveti sannidhānācca karmaṇaḥ । sannihite ca karmaṇi guṇaśrutiḥ tadanubandhaparatāṃ vidheḥ
jñāpayati</q> na karmasvarūpaparatāṃ iti gaditam । <q>ato dadh‍nendriyakāmavat guṇānubandhāt</q>
bhāvārthādvihitāt phalaṃ na kevalaṃ dhātvarthānubandhāt । <q>evaṃ ca etasyaiveti mukhyārthaṃ pada-
manvayi bhavati ।</q> anyathā dharmalakṣaṇayā varṇanīyaṃ syāt । <q>nanu vāravantīyaṃ revatīṣu﻿<pb n="r530"/> 
kṛtvetyaprāptā revatyo vidhātavyāḥ vāravantīyasaṃbandhitā ca ।</q> prakṛtaṃ hi karma vāyavyānu-
bandhaṃ, na raivatam । revatyanubandhastāvadvidhātavyaḥ tāsāṃ ca vāravantīyasaṃbandha iti vāk‍yabhedaḥ
tena karmāntaravidhireva yuk‍taḥ । uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>viśiṣṭayāgavādino'p‍yayaṃ tulyo doṣaḥ</q> aneka-
vidhilakṣaṇaḥ । <q>ataḥ saṃbandhavidhānākṣepāt<note n="(1)"> R. <dn>vidhānādākṣepāt</dn></note> revatīvidhānasiddhiḥ ।</q> revatyādhāre vāravantīye
vihite ākṣepeṇa revatyo vihitā bhavanti । ato na bhaviṣyati vāk‍yabhedaḥ viśvajit
sarvapṛṣṭho bhavatītivat । rāddhāntamupakramate&mdash;<q>atrābhidhīyate । nānyaprayuvatāt bhābārthāt
śāstrāntaramidam ।</q> anyaprayuk‍taṃ bhāvārthamāśritya na śāstrāntaramidam । <q>kiṃ tarhi ?
tathaiva sahaiva prayuk‍tyā śāstraṃ bhidyate ।</q> prayuktirapi bhinnā । śāstramapi bhinnam । na
punaḥ śāstrameva bhinnam prayuktirna bhidyata iti । <q>etaduk‍taṃ bhavati । karmaṇaḥ sakāśāt phala-
miti kutaḥ ? uttaraṃ&mdash;aprāptatvādrevatīnāṃ na guṇāt phalamiti śak‍yate vak‍tum । nanu
cok‍taṃ <note n="(2)"> R. <dn>vidhānādākṣepāt</dn></note>saṃbandhavidhānākṣepāt revatīvidhānasiddhiriti ।</q>  pariharati&mdash;<q>satyaṃ siddhayati
revatīvidhānaṃ na tu yāgānubandhatayā ।</q> tathāpi kimityāha&mdash;<q>guṇānubandhāt bhāvārthāt
phalaṃ guṇāt phalamityucyate na kevalāt guṇāt ।</q> phalanāmatvāt guṇaphalānāṃ <q>bhāvārtha-﻿<pb n="r531"/> 
viṣayatvācca niyogasya</q>, niyogaviṣayatvācca phalasiddheḥ । tena badyapi revatīnāmākṣepaḥ
tathāpi guṇāt phalaṃ na śak‍yate vak‍tuṃ yāmānubandhatvenāmavagamāt । bhāvārthāt phalaṃ na
guṇāt ।</p>
<p><quote>“athocyeta asya apūrvā revatīrupādāya tāsu ca vāravantīyaṃ kṛtvā tena yajetetyanuvāda”</quote>
iti bhāṣyamākṣipati&mdash;<q>anena pūrvasmāt ko viśeṣa upanyastaḥ ?</q> pūrvasmāt revatīnā-
mākṣepavidhānāt ko viśeṣa upanyastaḥ ? codyāntaramāha&mdash;<q>aprāptā revatyaḥ kathamupādīyante</q>
pariharati&mdash;<q>ayamabhiprāyaḥ&mdash;revatīviśiṣṭaṃ vārabantīyaṃ yāgānubandhatayā pratīyamānaṃ revatīḥ
ekatvavat upādānaśeṣīkaroti ।</q> tena yāgānubandhatā revatyādhārasya phalārthasya vāravantīyasya
bhaviṣyati revatīnāṃ cākṣepataḥ prāpterupādānasiddhiḥ । rāddhāntī vadati&mdash;<q>satyametat tathāp‍yagniṣṭoma
sāmeti nāvakal‍pate ।</q> kasmādityāha&mdash;<q>yāgānubandhatayā hi vāravantīyaṃ vidhīyamānaṃ
stotraviśeṣasaṃbandhitayā avagantuṃ śak‍yate ।</q> tenāgniṣṭomasāmeti na saṃbadhyate ।﻿<pb n="r532"/> 
<quote>“athāgniṣṭomasāmnaḥ kārye bhavatītyucyate”</quote> iti bhāṣyamākṣipati&mdash;<q>kimidaṃ agniṣṭomasāmnaḥ
kārye bhavatītyucyate</q> yāvatā yāgānubandhatayā pratīyamānasya stotraviśeṣasaṃbandho nopapadyate
ityuktam । pariharati&mdash;<q>yāgādyanubandhatayā hi revatīviśiṣṭaṃ vāravantīyasāma pratīyamānaṃ na
kāryaśūnyamanubandhī</q>bhavitumarhati dravyadevatādivaditi । <q>kāryaviśeṣāpekṣāyāṃ cāgniṣṭomasāma-
śabdaḥ kāryaviśeṣasamarpako bhavatīti na vāk‍yabhedaḥ</q> rāddhāntabhāṣyaṃ <quote>“etasyaivetyavivakṣitaṃ
syāt”</quote> iti tadākṣipati&mdash;<q>kimityavivakṣitaṃ ? yadyayaṃ</q> prakṛtayāgasambandhalakṣaṇo'rthaḥ
<q>śabdalabhyaḥ</q> syāt tadā vāk‍yabhedaprasaṅgo na syāt etasyetyavivakṣitam । <q>atra punaḥ
prakṛta ebāyamagniṣ‍ṭut pratīyate tasyāyaṃ etasyetyanubādaḥ ।</q> yataścāyaṃ prakṛtatayaiva saṃbandhaḥ
<q>ataścāyamavivakṣāyāmap‍yadoṣaḥ । tasmāt karmāntarayopasaṃhāro na ghaṭate revatyādhāravāra-
vantīyānubandhatayā hi na prakṛtayāgaḥ śak‍yate'vagantum ।</q> kasmādityāha&mdash;ṛgantarā-﻿<pb n="r533"/> 
dhāratayā'vagateḥ ।</q> prakṛtasya karmaṇo vāyavyādhāratvenāvagatatvāt । <q>nanupha lārthatve guṇasya</q>
nāyaṃ doṣaḥ <q>godohanavat</q> bhinnaviṣayatvena virodho nāsti । kratvarthā vāyavyāḥ phalārthā revatyaḥ
godohanavat । <q>tatra camasānubandhaṃ praṇayanaṃ pratīyamānamapi godohanānubandhatayā phalārthatve
guṇānubandhasya aviruddham । evamatrāpi ko virodhaḥ । vaktavyo vā</q> godohanena
viśeṣaḥ । <q>ayamabhidhīyate viśeṣaḥ । ap‍praṇayanārthakāryatayā godohanasya kevalapraṇaya-
nābhinirvṛttyā na virodhaḥ śak‍yate vak‍tum ।</q> godohanena paśukāmasya praṇayediti godohana-
sādhyāt praṇayanāt phalamavasīyate godohanasyāpi praṇayanarūpo'rthaḥ kāryatayā'vagamyate tena tatra
kevalapraṇayanābhinirvṛtyā na virodhaḥ śak‍yate vak‍tum । <q>iha punaryāgānubandhatayā</q> vāravantīyaṃ
<q>pratīyate</q> paśukāmo hyetena yajeteti । yāgasaṃbandhitayā phalaśravaṇāt yāgānubandhitā
vāravantīyasyāśrayaṇīyā । <q>ayāgārthaṃ ca stotramabhinirvartayatīti na prakṛtānubandhitayā﻿<pb n="r534"/> 
śak‍yate'vagantum ।</q> revatyādhāraṃ vāravantīyaṃ <q>prakṛtaṃ hyagniṣṭomasāma vāyavyānubandham ।</q> asyārthaḥ
&mdash;yataḥ phalaṃ śrūyate tadanubandhitayā vidhīyamānaṃ puruṣārtha bhavati । tataśca kratvarthena saha bhinnaviṣa-
yatvānna virudhyata iti yuktaḥ prakṛtasaṃbandhaḥ revatyādhāraṃ tu vāravantīyaṃ purupārthabhūtayāgānubandhitayā
na pratīyate yāgaṃ pratyasādhakatvāditi puruṣārthatvābhāvāt । kratvarthatve sati samānaviṣayatayā
virodhaḥ । prakṛta hyagniṣṭomasāmakāryaṃ vāyavyānubandhaṃ tadrevatyādhāravāravantīyānubandhaṃ bhavati ।
ato na prakṛtānuvandhitayā śak‍yate'vagantuṃ iti karmabhedamāpādayati । <q>yasmāt prakṛtaṃ
hyagniṣṭomasāma kāryaṃ vāyavyānubandhaṃ tasmāt kāryānubandhayorvirodhaḥ</q> vāravantīyasya yat‍kāryaṃ
prakṛtayāgasaṃbandhi vāvavyānubandhigniṣṭomasāmakāryaṃ yāścānubandhabhūtā revatyaḥ tayorvirodhaḥ na hi
revatyādhāraṃ vāravantīyaṃ vāyavyānubandhāgniṣṭomakāryakaṃ bhavati । nanu kratvarthapuruṣārthatayā bhinna-
viṣayatayā na virodho'stītyāha&mdash;<q>akāryānubandhatvāt vāravantīyasya</q> revatyādhāraṃ vāravantīyaṃ
yat‍kāryaṃ yāgaṃ pratyanubandhatvena vak‍tavyaṃ, na ca tadvak‍tuṃ śak‍yaṃ akārakatvāt akārakaṃ ca na
kriyānubandhi bhavati na cānanubandhasya puruṣārthatā iti nāsti bhinnaviṣayatvam । <q>tasmāt</q>
prakṛtayāgasaṃbandhābhāvāde<q>tasyetyavivakṣitamityuktam । anuvādānupapatteḥ । karmāntaratve﻿<pb n="r535"/> 
punaḥ saha prayuk‍tyā śāstrabhedānnāyaṃ doṣobhaviṣyati iti</q> tadīyasyāgniṣṭomasāmakāryasya
aupadeśikarevatyādhāravāravantīyānubandhasādhyatvāvirodhāt । iti śabdaḥ parisamāptau । saṃprati
bhāṣyaṃ vyākhyātumupakramate । <quote>“ubhayasmin vivakṣyamāṇe”</quote> iti bhāṣyaṃ vyācaṣṭe&mdash;<q>ubhayānuvandhitayā
vivakṣ‍yamāṇe ityarthaḥ ।</q> yāde stotre cānubandhitayā vivakṣyamāṇa ityarthaḥ । prakṛtasyāgniṣṭomasāmnaḥ
kārye stotrokhye revatyādhāravāravantīyasyānubandhatvaṃ stotranirvṛttidvāreṇa yāgānubandhiteti ।
<q>na caiko viniyogaḥ ubhayānubandhitāmāpādayituṃ kṣamaḥ ।</q> yadyeko viniyogo'nekānu&mdash;
bandhitāṃ nāṣādayati <q>kathaṃ tarhi sādhāraṇaguṇānāṃ</q> prayājādīnāṃ <q>vidhānam ।</q> uttaram
&mdash;<q>aikarūp‍ye hi tat</q> sarvāṇyāgneyādīni karmāṇ‍yekarūpāṇi na guṇapradhānabhūtāni tatra tattreṇa
saṃbandho yuktaḥ । <q>kathaṃ tarhi aṅgapradhānārthatā barhirādīnāmaika</q> <note n="(1)"> G. <dn>ekatvābhāvepi</dn></note>rūp‍yābhāve'pi । uttaram 
<q>kevalaprayogaśeṣatayā nāvacchedānubandhatayā</q>। prayogaśeṣataiva kevalā teṣām । tena
yuk‍tamaṅgapradhānārthatvam । yathā ca barhirādīnāṃ prayogaśoṣatā tathā'nantaraṃ vakṣyāmaḥ ।
avacchedo  yenāpūrvabhāvanā'vacchidyate tadanubandhatayā teṣāṃ nāṅgapradhānārthatā । <q>iha
cānubandhāvacchedānubandhatve virodha uktaḥ ।</q> anubandhaḥ stotraṃ avacchedo yāgaḥ tadanu-﻿<pb n="r536"/> 
bandhatve virodha uktaḥ । <q>kathaṃ punaratrāpi prayogānubandhatayaiva vāravantīyaṃ na parigṛhyate ।</q>
uttaraṃ&mdash;na parigṛhyate vāk‍yena yāgāvacchinvāvagateḥ । yāgenāvacchinnasya viśiṣṭasya yāga-
saṃbandhasyāvagateriti yāvat । <q>prakaraṇagamyā hi prayogānubandhatā ।</q> yau hi dravyaguṇau
prakaraṇe paṭhyete kevalaṃ kāryaṃ ca tayorviśiṣṭaṃ na  nirdiśyate tayoraṅgapradhānārthatā agṛhyamāṇa-
viśeṣatayā yathā pūrvapakṣe āruṇ‍yādīnāmag‍nyādīnāṃ ca । <q>anupādeyagamyā vā, vāk‍yādi-
bhirapi ।</q> anupādeyaṃ uddiś‍ya<note n="(1)"> G. <dn>uddeś‍yaṃ</dn></note> tadnambāpi prayogaśeṣatā vāk‍yādibhirapi bhavati । yathā 
barhirādīnāṃ <quote>‘barhiṣi havīṃṣ‍yāsādayati’</quote> iti haviśśabdena uddhiś‍yamānānāṃ aṅgapradhānahaviṣāmapi
barhirādisaṃbandhaḥ । <q>sāmarthyāvagamyā vā</q> prayogaśeṣatā <q>pradhānasaṃbandho</q> vāk‍yena dakṣiṇādiṣu
<quote>‘dīkṣāḥ somasya’</quote> <quote>‘dakṣiṇāḥ somasya’</quote> iti vāk‍yena pradhānamātrasaṃbandho dakṣiṇayāḥ । dakṣiṇā-
sāmarthyena <note n="(2)"> <dn>yāgaśeṣatā</dn></note>prayogaśeṣatā, dakṣiṇāyāḥ kartrānatikāritvāt kartuśca sāṅgapradhānārthatvāt ।
<q>iha punarvāk‍vena yāgānubandhataiva</q> na stotrānubandhateti <q>etasyetyavibakṣāprakāraḥ ।</q> yadi-﻿<pb n="r537"/> 
hi stotrānubandhatā <note n="(2)"> <dn>puruṣārthatayā</dn></note>puruṣārthatāpi syāt tadā kratvarthapuruṣārthayoḥ bhinnaviṣayatvenāvirodhāt yujyeta
prakṛtasaṃbandha iti etasyeti vivakṣitaṃ syāt । yāgānubandhatve hīṣ‍yamāṇe yāgaṃ pratyakāraka-
tvāt puruṣārthatbe asati virodhāt prakṛtasaṃbandhābhāva eva etasyetyavivakṣitaṃ syāt <quote>“atha karmā-
ntare kathamavāk‍yabheda”</quote> iti bhāṣyamākṣipati&mdash;<q>viśiṣṭavidhānasiddheḥ praś‍no nopapadyate tad‍gu-</q>
ṇādhikaraṇe hi viśiṣṭavidhānaṃ vyutpannam । ucyate । <q>avāntarasttotrasaṃbandha ṛk‍sā-
mayornopapadyate ityabhiprāyaḥ ।</q> ekaiva hi kriyā anekaviśeṣaṇaviśiṣṭā vidhīyata iti vyutpa-
n‍nam, iha tu kriyāntaraniveśinoḥ ṛk‏sāmayoḥ saṃbandho'pi vidhātumiṣyate na sa labhyata iti ।  
yadyeṣa pūrvapakṣavādino'bhiprāyaḥ <q>rāddhāntavādinastarhi ko'bhiprāyaḥ ।</q> uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>ayamabhiprāyaḥ
revatīvāravantīyayoḥ saṃbandhaḥ stotre na syāt । yadyekabhāvaviśeṣaṇaṃ ṛk dravyaṃ sāma-
vā syāt</q>  yadi yāgaviśeṣaṇe ṛkasāme syātāmityarthaḥ । <q>atra punaḥ revatī
vāravantīyasaṃbandhābhinirvṛtto bhāvaḥ</q> stotrākhyo <q>bhāvāntarasya</q> viśeṣaṇam । revatīṣu
hi vāravantīyasambandhe stotraṃ saṃpadyeta tenocyate revatīvāravantīyasambandhābhinirvṛtto
bhāva iti । <q>sa ca stotrākhyabhāvaviśiṣṭo bhāvaḥ</q> k‍tvāpratyayasāmarthyenākṣip‍to
<q>vidhīyamāno</q> yajinā viśeṣ‍yata ityabhiprāyo rāddhāntinaḥ । atra bhāṣyaṃ <quote>“dvāvap‍yetau arthau
﻿<pb n="r538"/> 
kṛtvetyeṣa śabdaḥ śak‍notyeva vadituṃ abhinirbṛttiṃ pūrvakālatāñca”</quote> iti tadākṣipati&mdash;<q>yuk‍taṃ tāvat
abhinirvṛttiṃ vadatīti । pūrvakālatāṃ cetyayuk‍tam ।</q> ekagranthenāha&mdash;<q>na revatīvāravantīya&mdash;
saṃbandhottarakālatā yajeḥ । ucyate । pratipattāveva</q> pūrvakālatvamityuktamasmābhiḥ । kathaṃ puna-
ratra bhāvadvayasya saṃbandhaḥ yena viśiṣṭavidhiḥ ityatrāha&mdash;<q>samānakartṛkatvaṃ tu ekaprayogatāmāpāda-
yatīti siddhaṃ viśiṣṭavidhānam ।</q> revatīvāravantīyasaṃbandhābhinirvṛttibhāvasamānakartṛka<note n="(1)"> G. R. <dn>yāgābhidhānāt</dn></note> yāgavidhā- 
nāt <note n="(2)"> G. <dn>viśiṣṭavidhānasiddhiḥ</dn></note>viśiṣṭavidhiḥ । <quote>“artha iti prayojanamabhidhīyata”</quote> iti bhāṣyam । tadvayācaṣṭe&mdash;<q>niyo-
<q>gārthābhiprāyametat</q> na yāgābhiprāyam niyoga eva hi pradhānabhūtaḥ sarvapadānāṃ prayojanam । <q>kathaṃ punaḥ
ekaniyogasaṃbandha iti taddarśayati&mdash;revatīṣu bāravantīyamiti । nādyāpi parisamāptiḥ﻿<pb n="b539"/> 
kriyāpekṣiṇ‍yo</q> hi dvitīyādyā vibhaktayaḥ <note n="(1)"> G. <dn>tena kriyāvidhānānna parisamāptiḥ</dn></note>kriyāṃ vinā na parisamāp‍yante ataḥ kṛt‍veti kriyā- 
saṃbandhaḥ । ayamapi ca karotiḥ kṛtveti k‍tvāntaḥ san naiva svakārakasaṃbandhaparyavasāyī । kiṃ
tarhi ? bhāvārthāntarāpekṣaḥ tatkārakaiḥ saṃbandhamanubhavati ।</q> samānakartṛkatve k‍tvāpratyayasyotpatteḥ
bhāvāntaravyatirekeṇa ca samānakartṛkatvāsaṃbhavāt । <q>bhāvārthāntaraṃ</q> ca k‍tvāpratyayenākṣiptaṃ
yattat <q>yajyarthaviśiṣṭaṃ pratīyata ityupapattyā ekaprayojanasaṃbandhaḥ iti na vāk‍yabhedaḥ
guṇaphalasaṃbandhe punarviparītametat ।</q> tatra yāga eva prakṛta: san na vidhīyate । yattu
tadāśritaṃ revatīvāravantīyasaṃbandhamabhinirvṛttaṃ bhāvāntaraṃ tadapi cāg‍niṣṭomastotrātmakaṃ prāptamiti na
vidhīyate । kintu tatra revatyo vāravantīyaṃ ca vidheyam । tataśca vāk‍yabhedaḥ । <q>atha puna-
retasyeti prakṛtavacanasya śrutyanu rodhāt revatīvāravantīyaviśiṣṭo yāgaḥ prakṛtāgniṣṭudaṅga-
tayaiva codyate ko doṣaḥ ?</q></p>﻿<pb n="r540"/> 
<p>uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>na khalukaścinmahāpātakādidoṣaḥ</q> adhikārāntarānarthak‍yaṃ tu bhavati ।
<quote>‘paśukāmo hyetena yajeta’</quote> iti । tasmin hi sārthake aṅgatvameva nopapadyate ।
<quote>“athaivamucyeta revatīṣu kṛtena vāravantīyena paśukāmo yajeta”</quote> iti bhāṣyamā-
kṣipati&mdash;<q>kimidamarthāntaramupanyastam ?</q> uttaraṃ&mdash;idaṃ arthāntaramanenopanyastam । <q>bhāva&mdash;
evāyaṃ bhāvā</q>ntaramāśritaḥ <q>kasmānna phalaṃ sādhayatīti ।</q> ekagranthenāha&mdash;<q>yathaiva hi revatīvāra-
vantīyaviśiṣṭaḥ karotyartho yajateḥ</q> siddhāntapakṣe <q>viśeṣaṇaṃ evaṃ phalārthaḥ kimiti na bhavati
rāddhāntavādī tu vadati vatanādṛte na godohanavat praṇayanasyāvihitaṃ</q> sādhanaṃ <q>sādhanaṃ bhavi-﻿<pb n="r541"/> 
tumarhati yathā godohanamavihitaṃ praṇayanasādhanaṃ bhavati na tathā yāgasya revatīvāravantīyaviśiṣṭaḥ
karotyarthaḥ । ataḥ so'pi vidhātavyaḥ । vidhīyamāne ca vāk‍yabhedaḥ । <q>kutaḥ ?</q>  uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>revatīsthavā-
ravantīyasya <note n="(1)"> <dn>kāryāntaraśravaṇāt</dn></note>kāryāntarāśrayaṇāt iti prāgap‍yuktam । yadi revatīsthavāravantīyasya yāga eva
kāryaṃ syāt taddā godohananyāyo bhavet tasya tu stotraṃ kāryaṃ; na ca yāgasya stotrasya ca
saṃbandho vihito labhyate । tadidamuktaṃ <q>ṛgantara<note n="(2)"> <dn>śravaṇāt</dn></note>pragāṇāt stotrasādhanaviśeṣahānaṃ  syāt
ataśca kratorvaiguṇ‍yaṃ syāt ।</q> ayaṃ cārtho <q>ayaṃ cārtho yāvatprakaraṇādaṅgabhāva ityetena 
bhāṣ‍yeṇa darśitaḥ । prakaraṇaṃ hi vāk‍yenāviniyuktasyaidamarthyāyālaṃ bhavati ।</q> vāk‍yena ca
revatīvāravantīyaviśiṣṭaḥ karotyarthaḥ phalārthatayā codita iti na yāgaṃ prati prakaraṇenāṅgaṃ syāt ।
tataśca yāgasaṃbandhāvagamo bādhyeta । <q>tasmānna godohanavat karmasādhanasya sataḥ phalārthatā
uyapadyate kṛtvetibhāvasya ।</q></p>﻿<pb n="r542"/> 
<p>adhikaraṇārthamupasaṃharati&mdash;<q>ataḥ prayok‍tṛśās‍trasya bhedaḥ ।</q> <quote>“yāgaguṇakaṃ vāravantīyaṃ
tad‍guṇako vā yāgaḥ”</quote> iti bhāṣyaṃ vyācaṣṭe&mdash;<q>bhāvadvayasyāsya</q> syotrayāgātmakasya <q>ekakartṛkatā-
lakṣaṇaḥ saṃbandhaḥ । aṅgaṅgibhāvastvanyato mṛgya iti darśayati ।</q> samānakartṛkatvena eka-
prayogābagamo varaṃ na punaridamaṅgaṃ ida maṅgīti viśeṣāvagamaḥ ato'sau anyato mṛgyaḥ । <q>kuto'nyataḥ ?</q>
uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>pratyayasannikarṣāditi darśitaṃ bhāṣye ।</q> yajeḥ sannikṛṣṭaḥ pratyaya iti sa eva niyogaviṣayaḥ
sa ca karaṇaṅgabhūtaṃ stotram । <quote>“atha punarviśiṣṭe yāge vidhīyamāne tatra revatīṣu vāravantīyaṃ katha-﻿<pb n="r543"/> 
magniṣṭomasāma bhavati”</quote> iti bhāṣyaṃ vyācaṣṭe&mdash;<q>yāge hi viśiṣṭe agniṣṭomasāmaviśe<note n="(1)"><dn>viśeṣaṇaṃ</dn></note> ṣaṇat‍vaṃ no-
papadyate ityarthaḥ । kāryasamarpaṇādagniṣṭomasām‍no na doṣa iti parihāro</q> bhāṣyakārīyaḥ ।
<q>athedānīṃ etasyeti kā kathā ।</q>  yadā karmāntaraṃ vidhīyata ityuktaṃ tadā kathametasyeti vacanī-
yam<note n="(2)"> G. <dn>varṇanīyam</dn></note> ? uttaraṃ&mdash;it‍tham । spaṣṭe hi <q>śās‍trabhede etaddharmakasyeti mantavyam ।</q> etacchabdo'yaṃ
tāvat āñjasyena prakṛtavartī । tatra yadā karmāntaratvaṃ niścitaṃ tadā dharmalakṣaṇārtho bhavati yatra puna-
rdharmalakṣaṇārthoṃ na bhaviṣyati avyaktatvena saumikavidhyantaprāpteḥ tatra vakṣyamāṇābhiprāyeṇa varṇyate athaiṣa
jyotirityādau । iha tu agniṣ‍ṭuto dharmā anyathā na labhyanta iti dharmalakṣaṇārtha evāyaṃ etacchabdaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>saubhare । ukto guṇādhikārasaṃbandhaḥ । yadāśrito guṇaḥ tatsaṃbandhinyadhikāre yathā</q>
<quote>‘dadh‍nendriyakāmasya juhuyāt’</quote> iti <q>guṇādhikāra iti siddham । anyāśrite guṇe﻿<pb n="r544"/> 
anyasya cādhikārasaṃbandhe bhāvādeva phalamityapi sthitam ।</q> tathā stotrāśrite guṇe(yāgāśrita)
yāgasya cādhikārasaṃbandhe yāgādeva phalam yathā etasyaiva revatīṣu ityatra । idānīṃ yadṛāśrito guṇaḥ
tatraivādhikāraḥ nidhanāśritaṃ hīṣādi tatraiva cādhikāraḥ <quote>‘hīṣiti vṛṣṭikāmasya nidhanaṃ kuryāt’</quote> iti ।
<note n="(1)"> <dn>tasmāt</dn></note><q>kasmādadhikārāntaramiti manyate ? <note n="(2)"> <dn>viśeṣaṇa</dn></note>viśeṣamapaśyan</q> yathā yo vṛṣṭikāmo yo'nnādyakāmoyaḥ
svargakāmaḥ sa saubhareṇa stuvīteti saubharādhikāraḥ tathā nidhanādap‍yadhikārāntaramiti pūrvapakṣavādī
manyate viśeṣamapaś‍yan sarvasya । <q>satyamevaṃ yadāśrito guṇastada</q> dhikāra (rāntara) saṃbandhe guṇādhikāraḥ﻿<pb n="r545"/> 
kiṃ <q>tu satyāṃ aprāptau</q> yatra prakṛto'dhikāro na prāptaḥ । <q>prāptau punaḥ abhidheye pratyabhijñānaṃ
nādhikārāntarāvagatiḥ ।</q></p>
<p>asyārthaḥ- hīṣiti vṛṣṭikāmasya nidhanaṃ kuryāt iti vṛṣṭikāmaśabdena saubharasaṃbandhyeva vṛṣṭi-
kāmaḥ pratyabhijñāyate tasyaiva hīṣiti vidhīyate sa ca nidhanatvenaiva prāptaḥ । atra nidhanamap‍yanuvāda-
eva । nanu bhāṣyakāro lakṣaṇetyāha । tatra cāyamarthaḥ pratīyate vṛṣṭikāmādiśabdena saubharameva
lakṣyata iti । na ca yathok‍tena prakāreṇa saubharaṃ lakṣyate kathametadbhāṣyamityāha﻿<pb n="r546"/> 
lakṣaṇāśabdena cāsminnadhikaraṇe abhidheyapratyabhijñānamevocyate । na padārthāntarasamarpaṇaṃ
gaṅgāyāṃ</q> ghoṣa ityādivat ।</p>
<p>ayamarthaḥ yadā vṛṣṭikāmaśabdena prakṛto vṛṣṭikāmo'bhidhīyate tadā tasya hīṣiti nidhane
vidhīyamāne tadīyasaubharasaṃbandhaḥ tasya bhavatīti puruṣeṇa saubharaṃ lakṣyate pratipādyata ityarthaḥ । na
punarvṛṣṭikāmaśabdena svapadārthaṃ parityajya saubharaṃ samarp‍yate । prakṛtād‍vṛṣṭikāmāt vṛṣṭikāmāntarā-
nava<note n="(1)"> G. <dn>rāvagatau</dn></note>gatau dṛṣṭāntamāha&mdash;<q>karmāntarānavagatiriva dadhnā juhotīti ।</q> yadi prakṛta evāyaṃ vṛṣṭikāmaḥ
<q>kimarthastarhi punaḥ śrutiḥ ।</q> uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>nidhānārtheti būmaḥ</q> nidhanībhūtahīṣ‍vidhānārthetyarthaḥ ।</p>﻿<pb n="r547"/> 
<p><q>nanvadhikāraśrutiriva nidhanaśrutirapi prakṛtābhidhāyinyeva ।</q> hīṣādayo'pi prakṛtā
eva tena te'pi prāptā eva na vidheyāḥ । uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>satyaṃ</q> nidhanaśrutirapi prakṛtābhidhāyinyeva bhavet
<q>yadyaikanidhanameva saubharaṃ syāt</q> vṛṣṭikāmanidhane <q>ayugapat‍prayoj‍yanekanidhanaṃ tu tat । ataḥ</q>
pakṣe aprāptatvāt apratyabhijñānāt siddhaṃ nidhanārthā punaḥ śrutiriti ।</p>
<trailer>।। iti pañcikāyāṃ dvitīyasya
dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ ।।</trailer>﻿<pb n="r548"/> 
<head>dvitīyādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ</head>
<p><q>guṇastu । kiṃ punaratrāpratyabhijñākāraṇaṃ</q> ityanena pūrvapakṣamākṣipati । uttaraṃ-<q>kratvabhidhānam ।</q>
rathantarasāmaśabdena kraturabhidhīyate yasya ca rathantameva sāma sa rathantarasāmā । j‍yotiṣṭomasya
ca na rathantarameva sāma, anyāni ca, anekasāmaguṇayogitvāt tadāha&mdash;<q>ratharantarasāmākhyaḥ
kraturnāsti prakṛtaḥ ।</q> yadiśrutyā hi rathantarasāmaśabdena pṛṣṭhamevocyeta tadā bhavedavayava-
prayogāpekṣayā prakṛtābhidhāyino<note n="(1)"> R. <dn>bhidhāyitā</dn></note> rathantarasāmaśabdasya prakṛtagāmitā । pṛṣṭhasya vikal‍pitasāma-
sādhanatvāt kratvabhidhāyitvaṃ tena saṃbhavati । kratvabhidhānaścāyaṃ somaśabdasāmānādhikaraṇyāt ।
somena somayāgo'tra lakṣyate yadi rathantarasāmaśabdaḥ prakṛte kratau nopapadyate <q>kathaṃ tarhi saṃśayo</q>
rāddhāntasyāsaṃbhavāt ।</p>﻿<pb n="r549"/> 
<p>uttaraṃ-<q>yadiśabdaśravaṇāt ।</q> yadiśabdo hi <q>prasiddhārthatāṃ</q> rathantarasāmaśabdasyāpādayati ।
yacca prasiddhaṃ tanna vidheyam । ato bhavati saṃśayaḥ । <q>kiṃ yadiśabdaśravaṇāt upasarjanapara-
midaṃ abhidhānaṃ</q> rathantarasya sām‍no nimittatvenābhidhānāt uta <q>svakriyābhidhānasāmarthyat﻿<pb n="r550"/> 
kratvantarābhidhānamastviti ।</q> kiṃ yuk‍tamāsmin saṃśaye । uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>abhidhānasāma-
rthyamantaraṅgaṃ</q> (na) bahiraṅgabhūto yadiśabdaḥ । <q>antaraṅgaṃ ca bahiraṅgāt balīyaḥ ।</q> kuto'ntaraṅgami-
tyatra āha&mdash;<q>paripūrṇaṃ hi padaṃ padāntaramākāṅkṣati ।</q> yuk‍tyantaraṃ cāha&mdash;<q>anvayānurodhī ca﻿<pb n="r551"/> 
<q>yadiśabdārthaḥ na svatantraḥ</q> <note n="(1)"> G.<dn>prat‍yayānāṃ</dn></note>avyayānāmanvayānuvāditvāt । <q>tasmāt</q> padāntarānvayalabhyaṃ  
<q>yathā katvabhidhānamupapadyate tathā tasyārtho varṇanīyaḥ । pradarśitāśca prakārāḥ</q> yadiśabdārtha-
varṇanopāyabhūtāḥ ।</p>
<lg><l>yadiśabdaparityāgaḥ, rucyadhyāhārakalpanā ।</l>
<l>vyavadhānena saṃbandhaḥ, hetuhetumatośca liṅ ।।</l></lg>
<p>iti pakṣavikal‍pasaṃgrahaś‍lokaśca tantravārtike ।</p>﻿<pb n="r552"/> ﻿<pb n="r553"/> 
<p><q>ekasya tu liṅgabhedāt । atrocyate&mdash;yadyabhidhānavirodhaḥ syāt</q> syādetadevaṃ yadi-
śabdārtho <q>na vivakṣ‍yeta</q> yathā kathaṃcidvarṇyeta (kal‍pyeta) yadiśabdaḥ <q>na tvatrābhidhānavirodha
upapadyate upasarjanārthe hi nimittatayā parigṛhyamāṇe kratorevābhidhānam ।</q> rathantarasāma-
śabdena yadiśabde vivakṣite'pi upasarjanārtho nimittatayā samarp‍yate tatrāpi tu kratorevābhidhānam ।<noten="(1)"> G. <dn>abhidhānameva</dn></note> 
yadi paraṃ prakṛtaṃ kraturucyate prakṛtatvādeva yadiśabdasya ca prasiddhārthāpādakatvāt । <q>nanu sāmā-
ntarasaṃbandhe sati j‍yotiṣṭomasya kratorabhidhānaṃ na prāpnoti ।</q> pariharati-<q>maivaṃ maṃsthāḥ; viro-
dhāpekṣaṃ hi sāmarthyam ।</q> asyārthaḥ&mdash;rathantaraṃ sāma yasyeti vigrahe rathantarasya viśeṣaṇatve
viśeṣaṇaṃ ca vyavacchedakatayā bhavati । sarvatra ca virodhino'rthasya vyavacchedo nāvirodhinaḥ
iha tāvat virodhi<q>bṛhatā ca rathantarasya kratusaṃbandhe virodhaḥ</q> ekakāryatvāt <q>na sāmamātreṇa ।</q>
tena rathantareṇa tadeva vyavacchite । tarhyavacchedamātreṇaiva ghaṭate viśeṣaṇatvamiti prakṛtābhidhāne-﻿<pb n="r554"/> 
'p‍yavirodhaḥ । <q>tasmādanityaḥ śabda itivadupapannamabhidhānam</q> yathā anityaśabdena nityataiva kevalaṃ
vyavacchidyate na <note n="(1)"> G.<dn>na punaḥ kṛtakatvādikamapi</dn></note>punarakriyātvādikamapi tathā rathantareṇāpi bṛhadeva vyavacchidyate na sāmāntaram ।
<q>tadyogācca</q> rathantarayogācca <q>kratoreva ca nimittatvaṃ</q> tena rūpeṇa kādācitkatvāt । yadi kratoreva
nimittatvaṃ, <q>kathaṃ tarhi upasarjanārtho nimittamityucyate ।</q> uttaraṃ&mdash;<note n="(2)"> G. <dn>tadanubandha</dn></note> <q>bṛhadrathantarānubandhānusā-
riṇī hi bhedāvagatiḥ kratoḥ tena rathantarādinānubandhena tadbhedāvagatiḥ <q>kratoḥ <note n="(3)"> G.<dn>taramānna</dn></note>tas‍māttannimitta-
mityucyate guṇaphalopabandhavat ।</q> yathā guṇaphalopabandhe guṇasya phalasādhakatvamityucyate tadvaśena﻿<pb n="r555"/> 
kratorbheda iti tathehāpi । etaduk‍taṃ bhavati । nimittabhūtasyāpi kratoḥ yannimittaṃ nimittatvaṃ
bhavati tadanubandhavaśenāvasthābhedādanubandhasya nimittatocyate । kasmādevaṃ varṇyate ityatrāha&mdash;
<q>kratoreva hi nimittatvaṃ na tadanubandhasya</q> <quote>‘yadi rathantarasāmā somaḥ syāt’</quote> iti kratoreva
nimittatvena śravaṇāt ।</p>
<p><q>aviṣṭau yajñasaṃyogāt ।</q> rājasūyādhikārādadhikārāntamannādyādikamaveṣṭernāstīti kṛtvā-
cinteyam । yadyadhikārāntaraṃ syāt tadā nimittārthataiva brāhmaṇāditvaśravaṇānāṃ syāt । <q>atra vrāhya-
ṇādiśravaṇaṃ yadyarthayogaśca saṃśayahetuḥ ।</q> rājasūye brāhmaṇavaiś‍yayoḥ asaṃbandhāt । kṣatriyasya ca nimi-
ttatvāt nimittārthatā tāvannāstīti prāpakatā pratibhāti । yadiśabdaśravaṇācca nimittārthateti saṃśayaḥ﻿<pb n="r556"/> 
yadi rājasūye brāhmaṇādīnāṃ prāptiḥ tadā pūrvādhikaraṇavat abhidhānāvirodhānnimittārthāni
śravaṇāni । atha tu na prāptiḥ tadā karmāntaravidhānaṃ</q> pūrvavat । <q>tadanurodhena ca yadyartho vyā-</q>
khyeyaḥ pūrvādhikaraṇapūrvapakṣavat । <q>kathaṃ punaḥ prāp‍tyaprāptī</q> brāhmaṇādīnāṃ trayāṇāṃ rājasūye
'vagamyete । uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>rājaśabdasyābhidheyanirūpaṇāt । yadi hi rājaśabdaḥ karmayogāt</q>
rāj‍yarakṣaṇajanapadapuruṣaparipālanakarmayogāt <q>kartari bartate tadā</q> trayāṇāmapi karmayogāt brāhmaṇādīnāṃ﻿<pb n="r557"/> 
prāptiḥ । atha <q>kartṛyogāt karma janapada</q>paripālanādi rāj‍yaśabdenā<q>bhidhīyate tadā</q> pūrvasiddho
rājā'nveṣaṇīyaḥ । śak‍yate ca nirṇetuṃ kṣatriyo'ndhrāṣāṃ prasiddhaḥ iti na prāptiḥ
brāhmaṇādīnāṃ rājakartṛke rājasūye । <q>tadā pikanemasatatāmarasādiśabdānāmiva mleccha-
vyavahārādivadeva abhidhānā</q>bhidheyāvagatiḥ । <q>kaḥ punaratra nirṇayahetuḥ ।</q> tatra pūrvapakṣa-
māha-<q>pūrvapakṣavādī tāvanmanyate karmayogāt kartaryabhidhānaṃ āryavyavahārāt ।</q> āryā hi jana-
padapālanādikartari brāhmaṇādāvapi rājaśabdaṃ prayuñjate । nanu karmānapekṣaṃ kṣatriyamātre m‍lecchānāṃ<note n="(1)"> <dn>an‍dhrāṇāṃ</dn></note> 
prayogo'stīti kathaṃ karmanimittatvanirṇayaḥ ityatrāha&mdash;<q>m‍lecchānāṃ punaḥ āryavyahāravirodhe</q> hyukta-
<q>maprāmāṇ‍yaṃ yavavarāhādiṣu</q> tena tadvayavahāro durbalaḥ āryavyavahāro balīyān । <q>nanvāryāṇāṃ mūrdhā-
bhiṣik‍tāḥ śabdavidaḥ kartṛyogāt karmaśabdaṃ smaranti</q> rājñaḥ karma rāj‍yamiti smaraṇāt । pariharati﻿<pb n="r558"/> 
&mdash;<q>satyaṃ vyavahāramūlatvāttu smṛteḥ prakṛtiprat‍yayavibhāgārthametat bhaviṣ‍yati</q>-asyārthaḥ । vyava-
hāramūlikā vyākaraṇasmṛtiḥ vyavahāraścāryāṇāṃ balīyān m‍lecchānāṃ durbala iti sthitam । tena
m‍lecchaprayogastāvanna mūlaṃ smṛteḥ । āryaprayogastu karmayogāt kartari tena tanmūlaiveyaṃ smṛtiḥ
tanmūlā cettadānuguṇ‍yena <note n="(1)"> <dn>rājñasūyānuśāsanaparā lakṣ‍yate</dn></note>rāj‍yaśabdānusāreṇa varṇanīyā <quote>‘rājñaḥ karma rāj‍yamityuk‍te jñāyata evaitat
yo rāj‍yaṃ karoti sa rājeti । nanu yadyapi rājasūye brāhmaṇādīnāṃ saṃbhavaḥ tathāpi kathaṃ nimittārthate-
t‍yatrāha&mdash;<q>prakaraṇānugrahāt yadiśabdopabandhācca nimittārthāni śravaṇāni ।</q> rājaśabdasya rāj‍ya-
nimittatve yuk‍tyantaraṃ cāha&mdash;<q>kiñca m‍lecchairapi karmayogāt kartari prayuj‍yaca evā</q>kṣatriye rāja-
śabdaḥ । <q>tataḥ kiṃ ?</q>  uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>avipratipattiḥ</q> sarvalokānāṃ karmanimittake rājaśabde, jāti-
nimittake tu vipratipannā āryā eva vipratipadyante । tena <q>tatpratipakṣatāṃ kartṛpūrvakaḥ prayogo
na bhajata ityabhiprāyaḥ ।</q></p>﻿<pb n="r559"/>
<p><q>atrābhidhīyate । prāpakāṇ‍yevaitāni</q> bacanāni । <q>kutaḥ ? smṛteḥ ।</q> kathaṃ s‍mṛteḥ prāpa-
katāvagama ityatrāha&mdash;<q>vipratipattau hi prayogasya s‍mṛtiḥ pramāṇaṃ gavādiṣ‍viva ।</q> m‍lecchaprayo-
gāryaprayogayorvipratipattau yaḥ prayogaḥ smṛt‍yā'nugṛhyate so'nādiḥ yathā gogāvyādīnāṃ vipratipattau
smaraṇam । smṛtiśca <q>kartṛyogāt karmaśabdaṃ smarati iti</q> smṛt‍yā m‍lecchaprayogo'nugṛhyate ।
ataḥ sa eva balīyān iti kṣatriyamātravacano rājaśabdaḥ । <q>nanu cāpratipakṣaḥ sārvabhaumaprayoga
(pradhāna) ityuktam । saci ca pratipakṣe s‍mṛtito nirṇayaḥ</q> tenāyaṃ s‍mṛterviṣaya eva na bhavati ।﻿<pb n="r560"/>
yuk‍tyantaraṃ cāha&mdash;āryaprayogavirodhena m‍lecchaprayoge niraste <q>āryaprayogamūlatvācca vyākaraṇa-
s‍mṛteḥ prayogādapi virodhaḥ । ataśca<quote>‘virodhe t‍vanapekṣaṃ’</quote></q>ityanena nyāyena <q>bādha eva nyāy‍yaḥ</q>
smṛteḥ । <q>prātipadikārthavibhāgena</q> prātipadikārthavivaraṇena s‍mṛtirupapadyata ityuktam ।  <q>ucyate ।
na s‍mṛtiravabādhituṃ śak‍yate ।</q> mūlābhāvāddhi s‍mṛterbādhaḥ । asti cedaṃ mūlaṃ mantrāṇāṃ prayogaḥ
s‍mṛtiḥ [teḥ] <q>nanu sārvabhaumaprayogaḥ āryavyavahāraśca virudhyate । na virudhyate ।</q> kasmādi-
tyāha&mdash;<q>andhraprayogamūlāyāmapi s‍mṛtāvupapadyata evāryavyavahāraḥ sārvabhaumat‍vaṃ ca</q> gauṇ‍yā﻿<pb n="r561"/>
vṛttyā । karmayoganimittakaḥ śabdo ghaṭata eveti bhāvaḥ । <q>tasmādvirodhe tvanapekṣamit‍yayuk‍taṃ</q>
m‍lecchaprayogamūlatvāt‍s‍mṛteḥ tena ca saha vigedhābhāvāt । nanu sārvabhaumaprayogavirodhāt m‍leccha-
prayoga evātmanaṃ na labhate kathamasau mūlamūc‍yate । s‍mṛtyanugṛhītatvāt m‍lecchaprayoga evānādiḥ
ādimānāryaprayogaḥ । na ca anāderādimān pratipakṣo bhavati svayamavidyamānatvāt tadāha&mdash;<q>aprati-
pakṣatā ca siddhaiva</q> m‍lecchaprayogasya । etadeva darśayati&mdash;<q>naivaṃ sati sārvabhaumasya pratipakṣatā
upapadyate । kāryakaratvāt prayogopapatteḥ</q> gauṇatvādityarthaḥ । mukhyapūrvakaśca gauṇa iti na mukhya-﻿<pb n="r562"/>
pratipakṣatā । <q>yaduk‍taṃ prātipadikārthavibhāgārthā s‍mṛtiriti, na mūle saṃbhavati anyārthatā
sūtrasya śak‍yate vak‍tum ।</p>
<p>adhikaraṇārthamupasaṃharati&mdash;<q>ataḥ prāpakāṇ‍yetāni</q> kṣatriyābhidheyatvādrājaśabdasya kṣatriya
evābhidheyo yasya saḥ kṣatriyābhidheyaḥ tasya bhāvastattvam । tasmādrājasūye kṣatriyasyaivādhikārāt
brāhmaṇavaiś‍yayorasaṃbhavāt kṣatriyasyāvyabhicārānna nimittārthāni śravaṇāni kintu prāpakāṇīti ।</p>﻿<pb n="r563"/>﻿<pb n="r564"/>
<p><q>ādhāne ।</q> nanu śās‍trabhedalakṣaṇamadh‍yāye'sminnārab‍dham । na cātra śās‍trabhedo vidyate
niyogaśūnyatvādādhānasya । kutastacchunyatā ? guṇakarmaṇāṃ niyogaviṣayatvāsaṃbhavāt । sādh‍ya-
dvayasyaikavāk‍yasamavāyavirodhāt agnayaḥ sādh‍yāḥ niyogaśca ityanupapan‍nam । kathaṃ tarhi niyo-
ge'pi sādh‍ye sbargādeḥ sādh‍yatvopagamaḥ ? yathā tat tathā śrūyatām । niyoganuguṇatayaiva adhi-
kāriviśeṣaṇabhūtasvargaḥ sādh‍yo'bhyupagamyate । śābdo hi svargasyādhikāriviśeṣaṇatayaivānvayaḥ
arthāttu sādh‍yatā । ihāpi tathaiveti cet । na । tathā phalasya kām‍yamānatayā adhikāriviśeṣaṇa-
tvānupapatteḥ । yadeva hi niyogasādh‍yaṃ phalaṃ tatkāmanāviśiṣṭa eva niyoge niyoj‍yatayā saṃbadh‍yate
nānyasādh‍yaphalakāmanāviśiṣṭaḥ । na cāniyogasādhyaḥ karmatvena śravaṇa[śrūyamāṇa] kriyāsaṃbandha-
nibandhanatvācca karmabhāvasya । etacca tṛtīye nipuṇataramupapādayiṣ‍yāmaḥ । yatra ca niyogo nāsti
tatra tāvadanubandhabhedena śās‍trabhedo na śak‍yate vak‍tum anubandhābhāvāt । niyogaviṣayo hi
anubandhaśabdenocyate । sādh‍yabhedādapi śās‍trabhedo na śak‍yate vak‍tuṃ āhavanīyādīnāmeva
sarvādhāne sādh‍yatvāt ।</p>
<p>anenāśayena pṛcchati&mdash;<q>kimatra cin‍tyata iti ।</q> uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>ādhānagato bhedaścin‍tyate</q>
asyārthaḥ&mdash;śās‍trabhede'pi cin‍tyamāne taddhetutayā anubandhībhūtabhānārthabhedo'p‍yatra cin‍tanīyaḥ ।
tatprasaṅgena bhāvārthamātragato'pi bhedo'tra cin‍tyate <quote>‘prājāpatyānālabhate’</quote> itivat । ādhānagata-
﻿<pb n="r565"/>
bhedacin‍tāmevāha&mdash;<q>kiṃ bhinnamādhānamutaikamiti । nanu ṣaṣṭhe'pi adhikārārthatayā bheda-
eva cintitaḥ ।</q> nacobhayatrāpi pūrvapakṣe hetubhedaḥ yena tannirākāraṇāyādhikaraṇadvayamārabhyate ।
tadāha&mdash;<q>ya evaṃ vidvānagnimādhatte itīdameva bhedapratipakṣatayā upanyastam । arthākṣepaśca</q>
ubhayatra । ya evaṃ vidvān iti sāmānyeba sarveṣāmādhānaṃ vihitam । tadevānusṛtya nimittārthā-
nyetāni śravaṇāni । vasante brāhmaṇo'gninādadhīteti । brāhmaṇa ādadhāno vasanta ādadhīta
iti । tenādhānasyāvidheyatvāt brāhmaṇādyanubhedepi na bhedaḥ । tathā kāmaśrutayo hyāha-
vanīyādisādh‍yāḥ । āhavanīyādibhirvinā'nupapannāḥ ādhānamātraikasādh‍yatvādāhavanīyādīnāṃ
ādhānamākṣipantīti tatraivāyaṃ brāhmaṇādīnāṃ vasantādiniyama iti । <q>tasmāt</q> vyut‍pādyabhedābhā-
vāt tat ṣāṣṭhikamidamadhikaraṇaṃ <q>vā nārabdhavyam । ekasyaiva nyāyasya phaladvayamidam ।</q>
yasmāt eko nyāyaḥ siddhānte ya evaṃ vidvānagnimādhatte iti saṃbhāraśeṣabhūtaḥ ato nādhānavidhāyaka-
miti । tathā alaukikatvādāhavanīyādiśabdavāc‍yasyārthasya tatsādhanatvenādhānasyāparijñānāt
nārthādākṣepaḥ kramate iti tasyaiva nyāyasya phaladvayametat yadādhānasya bhinnatvaṃ śadrādīnāṃ cānadhi-
kāraḥ&mdash;<q>atrocyate । bhede hyādhānasyānubandhabhedo hetuḥ</q> bhāvārthasyāpi yo bhedaḥ atrāpi kārakānu-﻿<pb n="r566"/>
bandhabheda eva hetuḥ । <q>ato brāhmaṇādyanubandhabhedaḥ abhede na yuk‍taḥ ।</q> vidhīyamānabhevādhānaṃ
yadā brāhmaṇādyanubandhaṃ bidhayate tadā bhinnaṃ bhavati । tena vidhīyamāna ādhāne brāhmaṇādīnāṃ anu-
bandhasādhanatvādādhānasya bhedaḥ sādh‍yate । <q>tatra punaradhikṛtasya agnayaḥ uta sāgnikasyādhikāraḥ
ityanyaiva cintā ।</q> yadā adhikṛtānāṃ satāṃ agnayaḥ tadā prāpakeṣ‍vagniśravaṇeṣu yeṣāmadhikṛtā-
nāmag‍nayaḥ saṃbhabanti teṣāmāhavanīyādiṣu karmāṇi bhaviṣ‍yanti । anyeṣāṃ tu tairapi vinā'dhikāra-
balena karmaṇi bhaviṣ‍yanti । yadā tu sāgnikasyādhikāraḥ tadā brāhmaṇādīnāmevāg‍neradhikārasya
vidyamānatvātteṣāmevādhikāro bhaviṣyati nānyeṣāmityeṣā ṣāṣṭhī cintā । <q>sa cāyaṃ viśeṣaḥ tatraiva
nipuṇataraṃ varṇyate । iha tu kevalavidhānābhāvāt brāhmaṇādyanubandhabhedādbheda ityuk‍tam ।</q>
kevalasya brāhmaṇānubandharahitasyādhānasya vidhānābhāvāt brāhmaṇādyanubandhasyaiva vidhānāt ādhāna-
syaiva bheda ityuktam ।</p>
<p><q>kaḥ punaratra bhedābhedayoḥ karmaṇi viśeṣaḥ ?</q> uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>ayameva viśeṣaḥ yasya hi yasmin</q>
kāle ādhānaṃ vihitaṃ tasya varṇasya tadaivādhānam । brāhmaṇasya vasante ādhānaṃ vihitamiti
brāhmaṇa eva vasante ādhatte । nānyaḥ, tathā abrāhmaṇaḥ avasanta eva nānyasmin iti ।
nimittārthāyāṃ tu śrutau brāhmaṇādayo vasantādiṣ‍veva ityaniyamāt vasantādiṣ‍vanyo'p‍yādadhīta ।
vidhānapakṣe tu vasantakālikaṃ brāhmaṇādikartṛkaṃ cādhānamāhavanīyādīnāmutpattyādikamiti yat‍kāle
yasya vihitaṃ tat‍kālameva sa ādhātumarhati ।</p>﻿<pb n="r567"/>
<p>punaścodayati&mdash;<q>nimittārthāyāmapi śrutau tulyametat ubhayaniyamāt</q> agṛhyamāṇaviśeṣa-
tayobhayaṃ niyamyata iti bhābaḥ । <q>evaṃ tarhi nakṣatrādyādhāna</q>māhavanīyādīnāṃ etatkālīnameva
trayāṇāmapi <q>varṇānāṃ kathaṃ syāditi viśeṣaḥ</q> kṛttikāsvagnimādadhīta amāvāsyāyāmagnimādadhīta
ityevamādi yannakṣatrādyādhānaṃ tatkālīnameva (tat) trayāṇāmapi varṇānāṃ saṃbhavāditi vasantādi-
kālīnameva yathā syāt bhāvārthāśritatvāt guṇavidheḥ vasantādikālīnaśca bhāvārtha iti tatraiva
nakṣatrādiniyamaḥ nimittārthapakṣe tu aniyamaḥ animittatvādasya । <q>adhikāre ca punarbiśeṣaṃ
darśayiṣyāmaḥ ।</q> yadā hi nimittārthāḥ śrutayaḥ tadā'niyatakālaṃ śṛdrādīnāmapi ādhānaṃ syāt
iti agnimattayā ca teṣāmap‍yadhikāraḥ syāt iti । anyathā tu brāhmaṇādīnāmevādhikāraḥ ।
atra <q>bhāṣ‍yakāreṇok‍taṃ</q><note n="(1)"> P. 569.</note> <quote>“yadā ādhānaṃ vidhīyate  tadā āt‍manepadārtho vivakṣitaḥ tataścātmārtha-
mevāhitāgniyaḥ āhavanīyādayo bhavanti tataśca kṛtrimādinivṛttiḥ”</quote> iti । tadākṣipati
&mdash;<q>nanvātmanepadopanyāso'dhikāra evopayuj‍yate kṛtrimādinivṛttyarthaṃ na punarbhedacintāyā-﻿<pb n="r568"/>
mupayuj‍yate । pārārthyepi hi ādhānasya anubandhabhedāt sidh‍yatyeva bhedaḥ । tanni-
mittatvāt</q> anubandhabhedanimittatvāt ādhānabhedasya । yadyap‍yāt‍manepadārtho na vivakṣita&mdash;
stathāpi vidheyatve sati sidh‍yatyeva bhedaḥ āt‍manepadārthe tu vivakṣite'dhikāra eva
viśeṣaḥ kṛtrimādīnāmanāhavanīyatvāt āhitāgnināmadhikārāvadhāraṇāt anāhitāgnīnāmadhi-
kārābhāvāt tenātmanepadārthopanyāsa ihāsaṅgata ityarthaḥ । <q>ucyate । evañcādhikāra-
virodho na bhaviṣ‍yatītyabhyuccayo draṣṭavyaḥ ।</q> yadā vidheyamādhānaṃ tadā āt‍manepadārthasya vivakṣi-
tatvāt āhitāgnīnāmevādhikāra iti yaducyate tadasmatpakṣa evopapannaṃ bhavatītyabhyuccayo'yaṃ bhāṣya-
kāreṇok‍taḥ ।</p>﻿<pb n="r569"/>﻿<pb n="r570"/>﻿<pb n="r571"/>
<p><q>ayaneṣu । saṃjñā cotpattisaṃyogādityanena nyāyena dākṣāyaṇasaṃjñā darśapūrṇamāsākhyāt
karmaṇo bhet‍trītipūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।</q></p>﻿<pb n="r572"/>
<p><q>vikārovā । uc‍yate&mdash;satyaṃ saṃjñābhet‍trī yatra prakṛte karmaṇi guṇāntaraviśiṣṭe
guṇāntaraviśiṣṭāḥ sādhikārāḥ codanāḥ śrūyanta﻿<pb n="r573"/>
tatra saṃjñānyatvataḥ karmānyatvaṃ ākhyātasāmānādhikaraṇ‍yaṃ pradarśayadbhiḥ pradarśitamasmābhiḥ ।</q>
asyārthaḥ&mdash;saṃjñā hi bhinnopalabhyamānā bhinnaṃ saṃjñinamupasthāpayati । saṃjñivācinā ca tasyāḥ sāmā-
nādhikaraṇ‍yamiti saṃjñino'pi bhedo bhavati । anena ca prakāreṇa tasya saṃjñāyāḥ karmabhedā-
pādakatvaṃ yatra prakṛtaṃ guṇāntarayuk‍taṃ yathā j‍yotiṣṭomo dvādaśaśatadakṣiṇānvitaḥ । guṇāntara-
yuktāścodanāḥ śrūyante etena sahasradakṣiṇena yajeteti । tatra ca saṃjñopakal‍pitabheda-
nirvāhakaguṇāntaramasti tathā yadyavādhikāro'pi na śrūyate adhikārakal‍panābhayāt prakṛta eva
guṇāntaramapi vidhīyeta । sādhikāratve tu evanna saṃbhavati । iha ca dākṣāyaṇādisaṃjñā yadyapi
bhedamāpādayati tathāpi bhedanirvāhakaṃ guṇāntaraṃ nāsti । tena prakṛtasyaiva karmaṇo nāmadheya-
bhidamapīti niścayaḥ ।</p>﻿<pb n="r574"/>
<p><q>yacca samāptaṃ ca phale vākyamiti</q> tasyāyamarthaḥ&mdash; <q>na phalacodanā karmāntaratva-
māpādacituṃ kṣamā <note n="(1)"> G. <dn>anuba</dn></note>ananubandhatvāt phalānāṃ</q>, akārakabhūtāni phalāni na kriyā&mdash;
bhedamāpādayitu kṣamāṇītyarthaḥ । yadi phalaṃ karmabhedāpādakaṃ na bhavati kathaṃ tarhi <quote>“phalaṃ
cākarmasannidhau”</quote> iti bhedakāraṇamupanyastam । pariharati&mdash;<q>asannidhānameva tatra kāraṇa-
mupanyastaṃ na phalam ।</q> kathaṃ tarhi asannidhānaṃ bhedakāraṇaṃ ityatrāha&mdash;<q>na hyasannihitaṃ karma
yajinā viśeṣataḥ pratipādayituṃ śakyate ।</q> yajeryāgamātravacanatvāt । yato vihitaṃ pratya-﻿<pb n="r575"/>
bhijñātumaśak‍yaṃ <q>tasmādvidhāna eva viśeṣo'vagantavyaḥ ।</q> vidhānabaśena cāpūrvayāgaviśeṣo
vidhīyata iti niścīyate । kimarthaṃ tarhi tatra phalaṃ ceti phalagrahaṇam । ucyate ।
dṛrasthamapi karma tatra dravyadevatāviśeṣāvagamena pratyabhijñāsyate iti yo manyate taṃ prati phalaṃ
cetyuktam । <q>phalaśravaṇe <note n="(2)"> G. <dn>punarākṣepo hi</dn></note>hi karmaṇo vidheyatvaṃ tatra ca dravyaṃ devatā ca na śak‍nutaḥ
pratyabhijñāmāpādayituṃ dūrasthatvāditi । iha punaḥ sannihitaṃ karmāstīti na phalaṃ bhedaka-
mucyate <q>saṃjñāntaropabandhasya ca prayojanaṃ kathaṃ nāma tatpravṛttinimittaguṇayuktasya vidhāna-
miti</q> dākṣāyaṇaśabdasyāvṛttilakṣaṇaguṇayogo nimittam । tatra phalaṃ prajādikaṃ prakṛtādadhikaṃ
yathā syādityevamarthaṃ saṃjñāntaropādānam ।</p>﻿<pb n="r576"/>
<p><q>saṃskāraścāprakaraṇe ।</q> nanu ekaśās‍tratve'vagamyamāne kathamatra pūrvapakṣitamityāśaṅkyāha&mdash;
<q><quote>‘vāyavyaṃ ś‍vetamālabheta’</quote> ityasmin vāk‍ye parasparānanvitameva padārthajātaṃ lakṣyate</q>
tena yuktā pūrvapakṣāśaṅkā । kathamananvitam ? uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>ayamālabhatirna drabdevatānvayi ।</q>
dravyadevatayorālabhatau saṃbandhābhāvāt । tasmāt parasparānvayo na ghaṭate । <q>tasmādālabhate-
rvidhānaṃ dravyadevatāsaṃbandhanirapekṣasya । anuvādo vā ।</q> tatra prathama<q>pūrvapakṣavādī
anuvādaṃ manyate ś‍vetapadānvayalābhāt । ato yadālameta tat ś‍vetaṃ iti vāk‍yārthaḥ ।</q></p>﻿<pb n="r577"/>
tenaiṣā ālambheḥ ś‍vetākhyaguṇavidhiḥ । <q>vāyavyabrahmavarcasakāmapadayoḥ kā vārtā ?</q> brahmavarcasa-
kāmapadaṃ kāmipadopalakṣaṇārthaṃ tena bhūtikāmo draṣṭavyaḥ । uttaraṃ&mdash;ālabhatinā saha <q>parasparā-
saṅgateḥ vāk‍yāntaramiti manyate pūrvapakṣavādī ।</q> <quote>‘ś‍vetamālabheta’</quote> ityekaṃ vāk‍yaṃ
<quote>‘vāyavyaṃ kuryāt bhūtikāma’</quote> ityaparam, <q>aruṇāvat</q> yathā aruṇādhikaraṇapūrvapakṣe aruṇayeti
vāk‍yāntaraṃ tathā'trāpītyarthaḥ । yāvaduktaṃ <q>veti brahmavarcasakāmapadānvayo'pi labhyate</q> ityane-
nābhiprāyeṇa aparaḥ pakṣaḥ । <q>ś‍vetamālabheta brahmavarcasakāma iti</q> vāk‍yārthaḥ । <q>paraṃ vāyavya-
padasyaikasyaivoddhāraḥ</q> yāvatsaṃbhavaṃ ekavākyatā'nugrahītuṃ nyāyyetyarthaḥ । yuk‍tyantaraṃ cāha&mdash;
<q>etadeva ca yuktaṃ īṣālambhasyāprakṛtatvāt ।</q> tatra guṇavidhānāsaṃbhavāt । sannihite hi
bhāvārthe guṇānurāgamātre vidhervyāpāro vijñāyate । asannihite punaḥ (guṇa) bhāvārthavidheranyatra<note n="(1)"> G. <dn>vidhānāt</dn></note>
ko vidhiṃ vyāpārayituṃ kṣamaḥ । <q>atha liṅartho vihitopalakṣaṇārthaḥ parigṛhyate</q> tena vihite
dūrasthepi īṣālambhe guṇavidhiriti । dūṣayati&mdash;guṇasyāpi <q>vidhānaṃ na prāp‍noti । vidherupala-</q>
kṣaṇaparatvāt ।</p>﻿<pb n="r578"/>﻿<pb n="r579"/>
<p><q>yajatistu । ucyate&mdash;syādetadevaṃ yadi samastapadānvayo na saṃbhavati saṃbhavati
t‍vasau ।</q> uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>vāyavyaṃ ś‍vetamālabheta bhūtikāma iti ।</q> vāyudevatyaś‍vetaguṇadravvakayāgaṃ
kuryād‏bhūtikāma iti ālabhetetyanayā liṅā vidhīyate । yadyevaṃ vidhīyate <q>kathaṃ tarhyālabhatira-
nvayī</q> bhaviṣyati uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>anuvādo'yamālabhatiḥ anyataḥ prāpterālambhasya ।</q> nanvevamapi avidhīya-
mānatvādvidhāvananvitamevetyatrāha&mdash;<q>aprāptasya hyanvayo na saṃbhavati na punaravidhīyamāna-
syāpi ।</q> aprāptasyahyanvayamātramapi na saṃbhavati na punaḥ prāptasya, prāptamavidhīyamānamapi
vidhinānvitameva svargakāmapadavat । ato dravyadevatāsaṃbandhavidhānāt tasya  ca yāgamanta&mdash;
reṇānupapatteḥ yāgākṣepāt yajimān ālabhatiriti aikāśāstryam । na ca  saṃbhavatyanvaye śāstra-
bhedo bhavati <quote>“praviśa piṇḍī”</quote> itivat <quote>‘praviśagṛhaṃ’</quote> ityekaṃ śās‍traṃ,  praviśya ca <quote>‘bhakṣaya piṇḍīṃ’</quote>
iti dvitīyam । iha tu pūrvoktayā nīt‍yā saṃbhavati parasparasaṃbandha<note n="(1)"> <dn>parasparānvaya</dn></note> iti na śāstrabheda iti﻿<pb n="r580"/>
śāstrabhedāpādakatayā ca pūrvapakṣe lakṣaṇasaṅgatiḥ । atra bhāṣyakāra evamāha <note n="(1)"> p. 578</note> <quote>“ālambhanirvāpau 
prākṛtau lakṣayitvā ś‍veto guṇo vighātavyaḥ caruśca । tau cālambhanirvāpau bhūtikāmasya brahma-
varcasakāmasya ca । tatra vāk‍yaṃ bhidyeta”</quote> iti । tadākṣipati&mdash;<q>nanu ca guṇavidhipakṣadūṣaṇe
anekaguṇavidhānaṃ darśayati</q> bhāṣyakāraḥ <q>uktaṃ ca bhavadbhiḥ na vāyavyabrahmavarcasakāmau
saṃbadhyete</q> iti । tena kimityasadadhyāropeṇa bhāṣyakāro vāk‍yabhedamāpadayati&mdash;<q>ucyate ।
nāyamabhiprāyo bhāṣyākārasya īṣālaṃbhe padadvayavidhānamiti ।</q> asyārthaḥ&mdash;īṣālambhe padadvaya-
saṃbandhaḥ pūrvapakṣe'bhimata ityanenābhiprāyeṇa na bhāṣyakāreṇaitaduktam । <q>kathaṃ tarhyetaduk‍taṃ ?</q>
uttaraṃ&mdash;<note n="(2)"> G. <dn>aprāp‍tyeda</dn></note>āpādyedamuktam । <q>yadi prāptānuvādena īṣālambhe ś‍veto guṇo vidhīyeta [kiṃ na] 
prākṛte'pi । atha kasmādālambho vāyavye kvāpi sthite aprakṛtepi</q> na vidhīyate <q>brahmavacasa-
﻿<pb n="r581"/>
kāme vā ? ko nu khalu nirṇayaḥ ? īṣālambhe ś‍vetaguṇavidhānamityatra</q> yāvatā nāstyeva
nirṇayaḥ । nanvālambhaḥ prāptaḥ tenāsau na vidhīyata ityatrāha&mdash;<q>na cālambhaprāptau pramāṇamasti ।</q>
asannihitatvāttasyetyuk‍tam । <q>idaṃ cāparam । kathaṃ</q> ś‍vetaṃ vāyavyaṃ kuryāt bhūtikāma iti
vidhāvāśrīyamāṇe <q>ālabhaterananvayamāśaṅkaya</q> bhāṣyakāreṇoktam&mdash;<q>tañcālabhatyarthaviśiṣṭa-
miti ।</q> tadayuktam । yāvatā ālabhatyartho'rthaprāpto'nūdyata ityuktam । na punastadviśiṣṭasya﻿<pb n="r582"/>
vidhānamuktam । uttaram&mdash;<q>idaṃ taduk‍taṃ nāyamekasya vāk‍yasyātibhāraḥ yaduta kriyādvaya-
saṃvandhinamarthaṃ vidhirvidadhātīti ।</q> ekā yāgakriyā tābhyāmanvitamap‍yarthaṃ śaknotyekamapi
vāk‍yaṃ bodhayitum । <q>aṅgāṅgibhāvasyānyataḥ siddheḥ</q> arthādevālambho'ṅgatayā prāptaḥ sannanudyate ।
<q>tasmādālabhatyarthaviśiṣṭamityanvayābhiprāyametat</q> bhāṣyakārīyaṃ vacanaṃ arthaprāptālabhatyarthā-
nvito vidhīyata ityarthaḥ । anūdyamānasya bhavatyevānvaya iti niravadyam ।</p>﻿<pb n="r583"/>
<p><q>viśaye prāyadarśanāt ।</q> <quote>“kimidaṃ viśaye prāyadarśanaṃ”</quote> ityanena bhāṣyeṇa <q>sūtrasyā-
nākṣiptaviṣayatāṃ darśayati</q> bhāṣyakāraḥ । nedaṃ sūtraṃ viṣayamākṣep‍tuṃ samartham । <quote>“āgamagamyo'tra﻿<pb n="r584"/>
viṣayaḥ ।</q> āptopadeśagamyo'tra <q>viṣayaḥ na sūtragamya</q> ityartho bhāṣyasya । <q>tathā</q> cāgama-
gamyatvameva <q>pradarśitaṃ vṛttikāravacanāt viṣayamavagacchāmaḥ upapadyate cetyanena । kaḥ puna-
ratna pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ</q> yāvatā dravyadevatāsaṃbandhāśravaṇāt yāvaduk‍tacodanaiva nyāyyā । uttaraṃ﻿<pb n="r585"/>
&mdash;<q>ālabhatisāmānyāt</q> ālabhatiḥ prāṇidravyasaṃyuk‍to yajimān dṛṣṭaḥ eṣo'pi tathāvidhaḥ ।
tenānenāpi <q>yajimataiva bhavitavyamiti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ dravyadevatāsaṃbandhāśravaṇāt na yajimāniti
rāddhāntaḥ ।</q> yajimattve devatāsaṃbandha eva prayojakaḥ prāṇidravyasaṃyogaścāprayojakaḥ anyathāpi 
ghaṭamānatvāt iti yāvaduktacodanaiveti rāddhāntaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>saṃyuktastu । kimityadhikaraṇāntaramidamiti ।</q> yāvatā'trāpi dravyadevatāsaṃbandhā-
śravaṇācca (ālambha)<q>mātramevedaṃ na yajimatī</q> codaneti । uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>arthavādāt devāta-
saṃbandhāśaṅkānirākaraṇārthaṃ</q> bṛhaspatervā etadanna yannīvārāḥ ityarthavāde devatāsaṃbandho nīvā-﻿<pb n="r586"/>
rāṇāmavagamyate । tasyātiparokṣāvṛttiḥ mābhūditi rātrisatranyāyena yajimatyeveyaṃ codanā
āśrīyate । imāmāśaṅkāṃ nirākartumidamadhikaraṇam । kathaṃ punarasyā nirākaraṇamitya-
trāha&mdash;<q>viśeṣākāṅkṣayāṃ hi arthavādānnirṇayaḥ iha tu upadhāne viniyuktatvāt dravyastuti-
paraiva devatāśrutiḥ ।</q> yadi hi yāgamātramatra coditaṃ syāt tatra devatākāṅkṣayāṃ arthavādā-
nnirṇayaḥ syāt yathā rātrisatre'dhikāriviśeṣaṇākāṅkṣāyām । iha tu carorupadhāne viniyuktatvāt
prayojanākāṅkṣā nāsti । tasyāṃ cāsatyāṃ arthavādānuguṇyena na śakyate yāmaḥ prayojanatayā
kalpayitum । upadhānaṃ codāsīnabhūtasya sthāpanamātramucyate । na punaḥ kāryāntaropayogitayā﻿<pb n="r587"/>
samīpasthāpanam । yadi hi tathā syāt  syādapi prayojanākāṅkṣā । ato devatāśrutirārthavādikī
dravyastutiparaiva iti hetoḥ idamap‍yudāharaṇaṃ <q>pūrveṇa tulyam ।</q> atrāpi yāvaduktacodanaiva ।</p>
<p><q>pātnīvate tu pūrvavatvādavacchedaḥ । uk‍taṃ dravyadevatāsaṃyuk‍taṃ saṃskāra <note n="(1)"> G. <dn>karmavācakaṃ</dn></note> karmavadvāk‍yaṃ 
yāgasya codakamiti ।</q> ihedānīṃ saṃśayyate । <q>prakṛte yāge</q> sati kiṃ dravyadevatā
saṃyuk‍taṃ <q>saṃskārakarmavadvāk‍yaṃ saṃskāramātrasyaiva vidhāyakaṃ<note n="(2)"> G. <dn>prakṛte punaḥ pātnīvataṃ paryagnikṛtamutsujati iti paryagnikaraṇalakṣaṇasaṃskārayuk‍taṃ vāk‍yaṃ śrūyamāṇaṃ kiṃ prakṛte yāge saṃskāramātrasyaiva vidhāya kamastu atha vā</dn></note> uta idamapi yāgasyaiva vidhā-
yakamiti tvāṣṭre pātnīvate yāge atha vā yāgāntarameva vidadhyāditi sandehaḥ । <q>kathaṃ punaḥ spaṣṭe
prakṛtayāgavacanatve saṃśayaḥ</q> pātnīvataśabdasya spaṣṭaṃ prakṛtayāgavacanatvaṃ prakṛtasyāpi pat‍nī-
﻿<pb n="r588"/>
vaddevatākatvāditi kathaṃ saṃśayaḥ ? uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>saguṇanirguṇaśravaṇāt ।</q> pūrvatra saguṇā devatā 
tvāṣṭra pāt‍nīvatamiti śravaṇāt । uttaratra nirguṇaṃ śravaṇaṃ pāt‍nīvataṃ paryagnikṛtaṃ ityetāvanmātram ।
ato na prakṛtābhidhānaṃ spaṣṭam । etadeva vivṛṇoti&mdash;<q>saguṇaṃ hi prakṛtaṃ nirguṇaṃ ceha śrūyate-
pāt‍nīvatamiti । tasmādapratya</q>bhijñānāt <q>karmāntarametat । utsṛjatiparyagnikṛtaśabdau ca</q>
kāryataḥ prāptāvanūdyete utsṛjatiparyagnikṛtaśabdau bayorutsargaparyagnikaraṇayostau kāryataḥ prāptā-
vanūdyete utsargastyāgaḥ sa devatāsaṃbandhānyathānupapattyā prāptaḥ paryagnikaraṇamapi codakaprāptam ।
<q>kimidamuk‍taṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa&mdash;api ca tvāṣṭre vidhīyamāne paryagnikṛtasyeti viśeṣaṇaṃ nāva-
kalpata iti ।</q> uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>viśiṣṭānuvādalakṣaṇo vāk‍yabheda iti ।</q> paryagnikṛtaṃ tvāṣṭra-
mutsṛjatīti vidhīyamāne viśiṣṭānuvādalakṣaṇo vāk‍yabhedaḥ । tena paryagnikṛtamiti viśeṣaṇaṃ
nāvakalpyata iti । ākṣeptā āha&mdash;<q>nanu prakṛtaḥ paryagnikṛta eva ।</q> tena nedaṃ viśeṣaṇaṃ,﻿<pb n="r589"/>
kevalaṃ nit‍yānuvādo'yaṃ, <q>kastatra vāk‍yabhedaḥ ।</q> samādhā āha&mdash;<q>prakṛtatvena hyavivakṣitānva-
yo labhyate na punarvivakṣāpyutsarge ।</q> yadi paryagnikṛtasya sataḥ utsargo vidhīyate tadā paryagni-
kṛtaviśeṣaṇaṃ vivakṣitavyam । tacca prakṛtatvena [na]labhyate । avivakṣitasyānvayamātraṃ
prakṛtatvena labhyate tenāsti vāk‍yabhedaḥ । <q>idamaparaṃ kiṃ</q> bhāṣyakāreṇok‍taṃ <quote>“paryagnikṛtasya
pāt‍nīvatatā vidhīyata”</quote> iti yāvatā <q>pāt‍nīvatameva kevalaṃ vidhīyate</q> pāt‍nīyataṃ kuryāditi
tatra vāk‍yāntaragataḥ paśuśabdo'nuṣaṅgeṇa saṃbadhyate । tasya ca paśoḥ pat‍nīvaddevatākasya
<q>paryagnikṛtatā prāptavānūdyate ।</q> uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>saiveyaṃ</q> paryagnikṛtatā prāptā <q>anena prakāreṇa darśitā
bhāṣyakāreṇa</q> yasya paśoḥ pāt‍nīvatatā vidhīyate tasya paryagnikaraṇena bhavitavyamiti matvok‍taṃ
paryagnikṛtasya pāt‍nīvatatā vidhīyata iti ।</p>﻿<pb n="r590"/>
<p><q>atrocyate&mdash;paryagnikṛtasyāyamutsargaścodyate prakṛtasya ।</q> asyārthaḥ&mdash;paryagnikṛtaśabda
evoddeśyaptamarpakaḥ sa ca yaugikatvāt prakṛtagāmī । tena prakṛtasyauvotsargavidhiḥ । <q>nanu ca tvāṣṭraṃ
pāt‍nīvatamiti</q> pūrvatra <q>śravaṇāt na pāt‍nīvataśabdena prakṛtābhidhānamupapadyate ।</q> tena yadyapi
paryagnikṛtaśabdaḥ prakṛte vartituṃ kṣamaḥ tathāpi pāt‍nīvataśabdānvayānna prakṛtābhidhānamupapadyate । <q>ucyate
na nopapadyate</q> prakṛtābhidhānaṃ api tūpapadyata eva । kasmādityatrāha&mdash;<q>yatra hi samāse-
nābhidhānaṃ tatra vyastasyābhidhānānupapattiḥ aindrāg‍ne āg‍neyavat । yatra punaḥ vyastayora-
bhidhānaṃ</q> prakṛtepi <q>prasiddhaṃ na tatrārthāntare<note n="(1)"> R. <dn>vṛttiḥ</dn></note>buddhirupapadyate <q>tasmāt saṃskāravidhāna-
mevedam ।</q> nanūtsargaparyagnikaraṇayoḥ prāptatvāt na bidhānamarthavadityatrāha&mdash;<q>avacchedaphalaṃ</q>
apūrvopadeśo'yaṃ iti navame vakṣyāmaḥ । <q>nanu paryagnikṛtavivakṣā utsarge nopapadyate ityuk‍taṃ﻿<pb n="r591"/>
vāk‍yabhedaprasaṅgāditi । atrocyate&mdash;<q>sat‍yaṃ nopapadyate padi pāt‍nīvataśabdo vivakṣyeta sa
tu prakṛtābhidhānāt prāptānvayavacana evetyadoṣaḥ ।</q> uktametat paryagnikṛtaśabda evoddeśya-
samarpakaḥ sa ca prakṛtaparaḥ yaścāsau prakṛtaḥ tasya pāt‍nīvatatā nit‍yaprāptaivānūdyata iti vāk‍ya&mdash;
bhedalakṣaṇādoṣaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>adravyat‍vāt । sa evāyaṃ vicāro'nuvartata iti  ।</q> kiṃ <q>yajimat saṃskārakarma
uta kevalasaṃskārakarmavidhānamiti ।</q> anenāvāntarasaṅgatimāha । <q>tadidaṃ cintyate&mdash;kiṃ﻿<pb n="r592"/>
<note n="(1)"> G. <dn>grahaṇavatī atra</dn></note>grahaṇamātracodane ete uta yajimatī iti । ki yuktam ? aprayojanavataḥ saṃskārā- 
bhāvāt yāgaśabdaśravaṇācca<note n="(2)"> G. <dn>sā nayuktā</dn></note> somayuktāt yajimatī codane</q> prayojanaśūnyasya saṃskārānupapatteḥ 
prayojanākāṅkṣayāṃ <quote>‘yo'dābhyaṃ gṛhītvā somāya  yajate’</quote> iti somayuktayāgaśravaṇāt yāgārtha- 
somākhyadravyasaṃskāratvamevāvasīyate । tena yajimatī codane iti । codanaiva codanamiti draṣṭavyam ।
<q>gṛhṇātiścālabhativat prāpta evānūdyate sasomaśabdaḥ ।</q> avyaktatvena saumikavidhyanta-
prāpteḥ । <q>nanu ca aṃśau somayukto yajirna śrūyate ।</q> pariharati&mdash;<q>uk‍taṃ niṣprayojanasya saṃskārā-
bhāvāt adābhyasāhacaryācca tadvadbhaviṣyatīti । nanu jyotiṣṭomasyaivāyaṃ yajiranuvādaḥ﻿<pb n="r593"/>
kasmānna bhaviṣyati yena karmāntaraṃ vidhatte । uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>aprakṛtatvāt । prakṛte hi viśeṣe
sāmānyavacano viśeṣavacanaḥ śabdo</q> bhaviṣyati <q>nāprakṛte । tasmādyajimatī ete codane
ucyate । saṃskāramātracodane ete । kasmāt ? ।</q> uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>tābanmātraśravaṇāt</q> grahaṇākhya-
saṃskāravidhirevāyaṃ na yāgavidhiḥ । <q>nanu ca somavān yajiratra śrūyata ityuktam ।</q> pari-
harati&mdash;<q>sat‍yaṃ śrūyate anyaparastu saḥ ।</q> eṣa ha vai haviṣā haviryajate yo'dābhyaṃ gṛhītvā somāya
yajate ityarthavādārtho yajiḥ na vidheyārthaḥ tena grahaṇamātrameva vidhīyate । <q>nanu ca kevala-
saṃskāracodane anarthake bhavataḥ prayojanavato'śravaṇāt sannidhānābhāvācca ।</q> tena
<note n="(1)"> <dn>prayojanavat‍saṃskāryadravyapareṇa arthavaśena tāvat jātisomaśabdavatsomayāgadravyabhūtaṃ saṃskāryaṃ ।<dn> G.</note>prayojanavatsaṃskārāryāpekṣāyāṃ arthavādagato yajatiḥ sasomakaḥ somaṃ yāgadravyabhūtaṃ saṃskāryaṃ
samarpayiṣyati । tena yajaticodane ete saṃpat‍syete iti । <q>atrābhidhīyate&mdash;somayukto﻿<pb n="r594"/>
yajiḥ nānyārthatāṃ pratipattuṃ śak‍noti yadi na jyotiṣṭomamanuvadati ।</q> asyārthaḥ&mdash;soma-
śabdayuktastāvadyajiḥ anuvādabhūto'rthavāde pratīyate । yadi jyotiṣṭomaparastadā'nuvādo'va-
kal‍pate । anyathā gi vidheyārthaḥ syāt । nanu somavantamapi yāgamanuvadati kimiti
j‍yotiṣṭomamevānuvadati yāvatā vikṛtayo'pi somavatya eveti tatrāha&mdash;<q>sa hyupadeśāt somavān ।</q>
tena sa eva pratīyate nirapekṣatvāt somasaṃbandhasya । tasmāt tasya jyotiṣṭomasya saṃskāra
evāyam । tat‍sāhacaryāccāṃśāvarpātyuk‍taṃ grahaṇamātracodanā ।</p>
<p><q>agnistu । <quote>‘ya evaṃ vidvānagniṃ cinuta’</quote> iti kimiyaṃ saṃskāracodanā uta yaji-
mat‍karmeti</q> saṃśayaḥ । anenāvāntarasaṅgatimāha&mdash;<q>yajimat‍karmeti brūmaḥ ।</q> kuta ityāha﻿<pb n="r595"/>
yajisāmānādhikaraṇ‍yādagniśabdasya <quote>“athāto'gnimagniṣṭomenānuyajanti”</quote> ityagniśabdo yajisamānādhi-
karaṇaḥ anyathā dvitīyādvayānupapatteḥ । na cāgniṃ cayanena saṃskṛtyetyayamasyārthaḥ adhyāhāraprasaṅgāt ।
yāgavacanatve tu <quote>‘upāṃśuyājamantarā yajati’</quote> itivat upapannaiva dvitīyā । tasyāpi bhāvanākarmatvāt
<q>tenāyamarthaḥ ।</q> agniṃ anuyajati agnisaṃjñakaṃ yāgaṃ karotītyarthaḥ । agniṣṭomākhyastotra-
guṇavidhiścāyaṃ, agniṃ cinuta iti yāgasyotpatteḥ anuśabdaśca jyotiṣṭomāpekṣaḥ tadvikārāṇāṃ
taduttarakālabhāvitvāt । yadyayaṃ agniṃcinuta iti yāgavidhiḥ <q>cinetiridānīṃ kimarthaḥ ।
ālabhativadbhaviṣyati ।</q> arthaprāptānuvāda <q>iti cet ।</q> dūṣayati&mdash;<q>tannopapadyate । tatra hi
kāryataḥ prāptirālabhateḥ । iha punaḥ na cinoteḥ anyataḥ kāryāvagatiḥ</q> anuṣṭhānāvagatiḥ ।﻿<pb n="r596"/>
<q>upadeśāt</q> kāryāvagatiścinote<q>riti cet, na, vāk‍yabhedaprasaṅgāt</q>, yāgaśca vidheyaḥ
cayanaṃ ca । nanu cayanaviśiṣṭo yāgo vidhāsyate । na, viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāvasyānyato'siddheḥ ।
prakaraṇādbhaviṣyatīti cet । <q>prakaraṇamapi hi vāk‍yabhedasavyapekṣameva</q> utpannasya prakaraṇena
viniyogāt । tena cayanotpattyartha pṛthag‍vāk‍yamaṅgīkaraṇīyam । pariharati&mdash;<q>evaṃ tarhi yaṃ
kañcitsaṅgātaṃ kāryataḥ prāptamaṅgīkṛtyānuvādo bhaviṣyati ।</q> grahaṇasaṅghātaṃ vā anuvadatī-
tyarthaḥ । <q>atha vā <quote>‘iṣṭakābhiragniṃ cinute’</quote> iti prāptasya ayamanuvādo</q> bhaviṣyati ।
<q>tathā ca liṅgadarśanam ।</q> <quote>‘agneḥ stotraṃ’</quote> <quote>‘agneḥ śas‍traṃ’</quote> iti ।</p> 
<p><q>dravyaṃ vā syāccodanāyāḥ ।</q> atrocyate&mdash;<q>saṃskāracodanaivaiṣā । kutaḥ ? saṃskāra-
śabdaśravaṇāt agniśabdasya ca j‍valane rūḍhatvāt ।</q> tena jvalanasaṃskāro'yaṃ pratīyate ।﻿<pb n="r597"/>
kathaṃ tarhi agnimanuyajatīti ?</q>  pariharati&mdash;<q>cayanasaṃskṛte'gnau<note n="(1)"> G. <dn>cayanasaṃskārāhite</dn></note>sati paścādyajatī&mdash;
tyarthaḥ ।</q> etadeva sphuṭayati&mdash;<q>cayanamabhinirvṛtyeti yāvat ।</q> etaduk‍taṃ bhavati&mdash;rūḍhayā
agniśabdaśravaṇe sati agniṃcitvetyadhyāhāro'pi nyāyya eva, na punaḥ k‍lṛptaśaktiparityāgena
śak‍tyantarāśrayaṇamiti । <q>atha yalliṅgamuk‍taṃ taccayanasaṃskṛtāgniyuk‍te yāge draṣṭavyam ।</q>
gat‍yantarābhāvāt । tatra lakṣaṇayā'gniśabdena yāgo'vagamyate । <q>tāsveva codanāsu</q>
nānyāsu pramāṇābhāvāt ।</p>﻿<pb n="r598"/>
<p><q>prakaraṇāntare । māsamagnihotraṃ juhotīti śrūyate tatra śāstrāntaramidamagnihotraśāstrā-
duta neti cintyate ।</q> anenādhyāyasaṅgatiruktā । <q>nanu ca māsavidhāne'pi śāstrānta-
ramevaitat ।</q> ataḥ pakṣadvayepi śāstrabhedānnedamadhikaraṇamārabdhavyamasmin lakṣaṇe । pariharati
&mdash;<q>vāk‍yāntaramevedaṃ na śāstrāntaram ।</q> anubandhabhedābhāvāt tadanapekṣasādhyāntarābhāvācca ।
<q>tulyakāryaguṇāntaravidhānāpekṣaṃ tu bhavati śāstrāntaram na kevalabhāvavidhānāpekṣam ।</q>
guṇābhidhānapakṣe'pi guṇāntaravidhānāpekṣayā bhavati śāstrāntaraṃ anyonyanirapekṣatulyasādhyāntara-
yogāt । etaccādye prapañcitam । tena guṇavidhipakṣe agnihotraśās‍treṇābhedaḥ karmavidhi-
pakṣe tvanubandhabhedādbheda iti yuktā cintā ।</p>﻿<pb n="r599"/>
<p><q>kiṃ yuktam ? uttaraṃ-na śāstrāntaramidaṃ naiyamika evāyaṃ guṇavidhiḥ । kutaḥ ?
agnihotraśabdābhidhānena pratyabhijñānāt ।</q> asyārthaḥ&mdash;agnihotraśabdābhidhānaṃ tāvat
pratyabhijñāyate । abhidhānābhede ca nābhidheyasya bhedo yuktaḥ । tena naiyamika evāyaṃ guṇa-
vidhiḥ । nanūpasadbhiścaritveti guṇāntaramaṣi śrūyate । kathaṃ tatra guṇaghidhiḥ, vāk‍yabheda-
prasaṅgāt । ucyate । bhavatu vāk‍yabhedaḥ na punarābhidhānikī pratyabhijñā bādhituṃ śak‍yate ।
tenātra vāk‍yabhedalakṣaṇayoḥ kasya balīyastvamiti cintyate । tatra pūrvapakṣī śrautavṛttibalena
vāk‍yabhedameva nyāyyaṃ manyate । śrutasidhyarthamaśrutasyāpi vāk‍yabhedāderāśrayaṇīyatvāt ।﻿<pb n="r600"/>
atrocyate&mdash;prakaraṇāntare prayojanānyatvam । kimidaṃ prakaraṇāntara iti ।</q> uttaraṃ
&mdash;<q>aprakṛtābhidhāna iti ।</q> nāyaṃ juhotīti prakṛtābhidhāyī tena karmāntaraṃ tadāha&mdash;<q>nātra
prakṛtasyābhidhāyako juhotīti śabdaḥ dadhnā juhotitivat ।</q> vaidharmyadṛṣṭānto'yam ।
<q>nanu cāgnihotraśabdābhidhānānnaiyamika evāvagamyate ।</q> pariharati&mdash;<q>na juhoteranyārthā&mdash;
vagateḥ । kathaṃ punaranyārthāvagatiḥ ? upasadbhiścaritveti śravaṇāt ।</q> prāptakriyānuvādenā-
nekaguṇavidhānānupapatteḥ vāk‍yabhedaprasaṅgāt । bhavatu vāk‍yabheda iti cet । na parasparānva-
yāvagateḥ । yāvanti padāni parasparānvayaṃ pratipat‍tumalaṃ tāvadekaṃ vāk‍yamiti loke vyutpattiḥ
tena laukikavyutpattyanusāreṇa ekavāk‍yatvāddhomāntaravidhirevāyaṃ gamyate । <q>juhotyarthānusārya-
yamagnihotraśabdaḥ na viparītaḥ ।</q> homāntara evāyaṃ dharmalakṣaṇayā agnihotraśabdaḥ na tu
naiyamika eva juhotirvartate । tasmāt siddhaṃ prakaraṇāntaratvam । <q>prakaraṇāntare ca</q>
prayojanāntaratvāt <q>śāstrāntaratvam ।</q> anekaguṇaśravaṇaṃ cāprakṛtābhidhānasidhyarthaṃ na punastata
eva bheda iti । tena na guṇādbhedaḥ ।</p>﻿<pb n="r601"/>
<p><q>phalaṃ ca । kimidamanyadeva bhedakāraṇaṃ</q> phalamiti<note n="(1)"> G. <dn>phalarūpaṃ bhedakāntaraṃ</dn></note>। anena pratijñāvirodhamāśaṅkate ।
abhidhānāntarādayo hi ṣaḍeva bhāvārthasya bhedakāraṇatvena pratijñātāḥ na phalam । <q>nedaṃ bheda-
kāntaramiti vrūmaḥ । atrāpi<note n="(2)"> G. <dn>adhikṛtābhi</dn></note>aprakṛtābhidhānataiva pratipādyate । kathaṃ ? tena prakāreṇa</q>
kaḥ pūrvapakṣaḥ kaścottara ityarthaḥ । tatra pūrvapakṣamāha&mdash;<q>pūrvatra upasadbhiścaritveti guṇāntara-
śravaṇādaprakṛtābhidhānatoktā ।</q> idānīṃ <q>punaḥ phalasaṃbandhenāprakṛtābhidhānaṃ pratīyata iti
pūrvapakṣavādino'bhiprāyaḥ</q> karmaṇo <q>vidheyatvāt ।</q> asyārthaḥ&mdash;dravyadevatābhyāṃ karma prakṛta-
meva pratyabhijñāyate । tacca vihitamiti tanna vidheyam kintu tatra phalameva vidhoyatām aprāptāṃśa-﻿<pb n="r602"/>
sya vidheyatvāt tena nāprakṛtābhidhānam । <q>rāddhāntī tu manyate । anyārthe bhavatyapi
<note n="(1)"> G. <dn>prakṛtābhidhānam</dn></note></q> yathā somāya yajata iti । <q>svārthe prakṛte punaḥ na prakṛtābhidhānaṃ pratī-
yate ।</q> vidheye bhāvārthe na dravyadevate prakṛtābhidhānamāpādayituṃ śak‍nutaḥ vidheyasya bhinna-
tvāt । <q>phalasaṃbandhe ca svārtho bhāvaśabdaḥ ।</q> kasmādityāha&mdash;<q>na hyabhāvārthasya
vidhānaṃ saṃbhavatītyuk‍tam ।</q> yatrāpi guṇavidhānaṃ tatrāpi bhāva eva tadanurakto vighīyate ।
nanu ca phalānurakto bhāvārtho vidhātuṃ śakyate ityatrāha&mdash;<q>na ca dadhyādivat bhāvānupraveśi-
tā'dhikārapadasya saṃbhavatīti vakṣyāmaḥ</q> ṣaṣṭhādye । tena na tadanurakto bhāvārtho vidhīyate
tena bhāvārthasaṃbandhābhāvāt niyogamātrasaṃbandhitvānniyojyasya । ato'trāpi karmaiva phalaṃ prati
vidheyam । vidhīyamānatve <q>cāprakṛtābhidhānamiti siddham ।</q></p>﻿<pb n="r603"/>
<p><q>sannidhau । uktaṃ phalaṃ cākarmasannidhau iti । tasyaivedaṃ pratyudāharaṇam ।</q>
etadeva darśayati&mdash;<q>karmasannidhau phalayogo na śāstrabhedamāpādayati</q> śāstrasādhyabhedābhāvāt
utpattyadhikārayogeko<note n="(1)"> G. <dn>eka eva</dn></note>'dhikāravidhiḥ sādhyo yataḥ । <q>nanu ca vigheyaparatvāt bhāvārthasya kiṃ
sannidhiḥ kariṣyati ।</q> asyārthaḥ । yadyapi bhāvārthaḥ sannihito'sti tathāpi<note n="(2)"> <dn>phalaṃ pratividheyatvāt</dn></note>
phalasyāvidheyatvāt bhāvārthasya vidheyatvādanyatvaṃ yuktam । pariharati&mdash;<q>satyaṃ vidheyo
bhāvārthaḥ na punaḥ sannidhānamatikrāmati</q> sannihita eva vartata ityarthaḥ । <q>nanu atatpara-
tvādabhidhānasya kiṃ sannidhiḥ kariṣyati ।</q> [sannihitasya] vidhānānupapatteḥ na prakṛtaparo
bhāvārthaśabda iti nāsti sannidhānasyopayogaḥ । pariharati&mdash;<q>idaṃ kariṣyati</q> sannidhiḥ
﻿<pb n="r604"/>
<q>anyapare'bhighāne anyato buddhiṃ niruṇaddhi ।</q> tadetat prakṛtayāgasvarūpaṃ phale vighīyate
tasyaiva prakṛtatvena yajinā'bhidhānāt । etadeva darśayati&mdash;<q>upadeśaparamapyabhidhānaṃ
sannidhau sati na viśeṣāntaraṃ ākṣep‍tuṃ kṣamaḥ ।</q> adhikāreṇa utpattirākṣeptavyā । tatra
sannihitāyām‌tpattau saiva sannihite sambadhyate tasminneva yāge yajirvartata ityarthaḥ । <q>tasmāt
sannidhau tvavibhāgāditi yuktam ।</q></p>
<p><q>āg‍neyastu । aviśeṣāt karmāntaramityāśaṅkitaṃ pūrvapakṣavādinā āg‍neyamātra
śravaṇāt ।</q> samivo yajati tanṛnapātaṃ yajati itivadavibhāgāt ।</p>﻿<pb n="r605"/>
<p><q>atrocyate&mdash;rāddhāntavādī tu paurṇamāsīyuk‍taṃ vidhāyakaṃ manyate apratipakṣatvāt ।</q>
amāvāsyāmātrayoginā vākyena vidhānaṃ ubhayakālayoginā cānuvāda iti na śakyate vak‍tuṃ paurṇa-
māsīsabanvasyāprāptatvāt ubhayasaṃbandhinaḥ tāvadvidhānaṃ kevalāmāvāsyāsaṃbandino'nuvādakatopapadyate ।
tena gṛhyamāṇaviśeṣatvāt paurṇamāsīyuk‍taṃ tāvadvidhāyakam । vihitasya ca punarvacanaṃ na śakyate-
'rthāntaratayā pratipat‍tum । nanu abhyāsādhikaraṇepyevameva kasmānna bhavatītyāśaṅkayāha&mdash;<q>abhyā-
﻿<pb n="r606"/>
sādhikaraṇe punaḥ vidhānāviśeṣāt</q> sarveṣāṃ vidhānamityuk‍taṃ iha tu gṛhyate viśeṣa ityuktam ।
<q>nanu ca niṣprayojanaṃ punarvacanamityuk‍taṃ</q> tena vidhānameva bhavatu nānuvādaḥ । pariharati
&mdash;<q>na prayojanavaśādarthāntarapratipattiḥ । avagama eva hi tatvānyatve hetuḥ ।</q> atra
cānyatve heturna śakyate'vagantum । kintu tattvameva tenāprayojanatvepi nānuvādanivāraṇam ।
evaṃ tāvadānarthakyamaṅgīkṛtyoktam । saṃpratyānarthakyaṃ nāstītyāha&mdash;<q>na cānarthakyaṃ aindrāgna-
vidhānaṃ prayojanamityuk‍taṃ</q> bhāṣye । aindrāgnavidhānārtho'yamartha iti ।</p>
<trailer>iti ṛjuvimalāyāṃ pañcikāyāṃ dvitīyādhyāyasya
tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>﻿<pb n="r607"/>
<head>atha dvitīyādhyāyasya</head>
<head>caturthaḥ pādaḥ</head>
<p><q>yāvaj‍jīviko'bhyāsaḥ । yāvaj‍jīvamagnihotraṃ juhotītyatra cintyate । kiṃ
kāmyācchāstrāntaramutaikaṃ śāstramiti ।</q> anenādhyāyasaṅgatimāha । kālavidhau na
śāstrāntaram pṛthagadhikāre tu kāryabhedācchāstrāntaram । kiṃ prāptam ? <q>karmaṇaḥ prāptatvāt</q>
upapadārthasya kālasyāprāptatvāt । <q>guṇavidhiḥ tataśca ekaṃ śāstram । kaḥ punaratra guṇo
vidhīyate ।</q> ekagranthenāha&mdash;<q>jīvanaṃ tāvat ।</q> ajīvato homāsaṃbhavāt nityaprāptaṃ na
<q>vidheyam ।</q> yadi jīvanasya śrautasya vidhānaṃ na saṃbhavati <q>evaṃ tarhi</q> tallakṣito <q>jīvana-
﻿<pb n="r608"/>
lakṣitaḥ kālo vidhīyatām । <q>nanu cāsāvapi jīvanakālo nityaprāpta eva</q> jīvanayuga-
pad‍bhūto'pi kālo nityaprāpta eva । sarve hi jīvanakāla eva juhvati । pariharati&mdash;na nityaprāptaḥ
<q>yāvadanubandhatayā'prāpteḥ ।</q> yāvaj‍jīvanakālaḥ tāvati hotavyamityarthaḥ । sa ca kālo homenāna-
bhyastena na śakyate'vāp‍tumityarthāt abhyāsaḥ kāryaḥ । <q>atha ko'yaṃ kālo nāma yadi</q> tāvedvaiśe-
ṣikābhimataḥ sa nitya ekarūpaḥ prāpta eva । uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>yaḥ kālavidbhiruktaḥ</q> sa kālo vighīyate
<q>ke kālavidaḥ ?</q> kiṃ vaiśeṣikā iti bhāvaḥ । uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>jyotirvidaḥ</q> kālavidaḥ । ādi-
tyādigati<note n="(1)"> G. <dn>prameya</dn></note>pracaya eva kāla iti jyotirvidaḥ । sa vidhīyate <q>tathā ca liṅgadarśanam ।</q>
﻿<pb n="r609"/>
karturvā । atrocyate-adhikāracodanaiṣā na kālavidhiḥ ।</q> ataśca kāmyācchāstrāntaram । kiṃ
punaḥ kāraṇaṃ adikāracodanaiṣā na kālavidhiḥ ? uttaraṃ&mdash;<q>kālavidhau hi padadvayamapi lakṣaṇa-
﻿<pb n="r610"/>
yā'nvayi bhavati ।</q> jīvanena kālo lakṣaṇīyaḥ । juhotītyanena homābhyāsaḥ na hi
tallakṣaṇayā vinā yāvaj‍jīvanakālena sahānvayaḥ saṃbhavati । <q>adhikāropadeśe punaḥ śrutyā</q>
padadvayamanvayi bhavati ।</p>
<p>yāvaj‍jīvamiti homena jīvanasya vyāptiḥ pratīyate । kathaṃ ca homena jīvanaṃ
vyāpyate yadi jīvanamadhikāriviśeṣaṇaṃ bhavati । etacca ṣaṣṭhe vakṣyāmaḥ । <q>na ca saṃbhavantyāṃ
﻿<pb n="r611"/>
śrutau lakṣaṇāśrayaṇe kāraṇamasti । tasmādadhikāracodanaiṣā ।</q> adhikāracodanāyāṃ
﻿<pb n="r612"/>
ca prayogāntarasiddhiḥ । <q>evaṃ ca kṛtvāliṅgadaśenāni ghaṭante ।</q> api vā eṣa svargāllokā-
cchidyate ityevamādīni । jarāmaraṇaṃ ca yatpūrvapakṣiṇā satratulyadarśanamupanyastaṃ tat satravat
santatabhāvādapyupapadyate ityuktam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="r613"/>
<p><q>nāmarūpa । atra medapramāṇābhāsāni pūrvapakṣe upanyasya rāddhānte</q> kecit grantha-
sambandhitayā <q>kecit svādhyāyadharmatayā kecit vikalpāśrayaṇena kecit kratvantarā-
śrayaṇena kecidyadeti kālayogāt ityevamādibhiḥ parihāraiḥ parihṛtāni ।</q> atra bheda-﻿<pb n="r614"/>
pramāṇābhāsāni pūrvapakṣe upanyasyetyādi bhāṣyoditaiḥ parihāraiḥ parihṛtāni nirākṛtāni । ataḥ
kvacit parihāragranthasaṃbandhitayā kāṭhakaṃ kālāpakaṃ iti samākhyābhedena yaḥ karmabheda uktaḥ saḥ
kāṭhakādisamākhyānāṃ granthasabandhitayā parihṛtaḥ । tathā kecitparihārāḥ svādhyāyasaṃbandhitayā
bhūmaumojanādidharmabhedena yaḥ karmabhedaḥ āśaṅkitaḥ sa bhūmau bhojanādīnāṃ svādhyāyādhyayanamātra-
saṃbandhitayā parihṛtaḥ । tathā kecitparihārāḥ vikalpāśrayaṇena yaḥ kapālabhedādinā karmabheda
āśaṅkitaḥ sa vikalpāśrayaṇena parihṛtaḥ । ekasmin karmaṇi vikalpena nānāsaṃkhyāsaṃbandhopapatteḥ ।
kecitparihārāḥ kratvantarāśrayaṇena dīkṣitatvamadīkṣitatvaṃ ca । yaduk‍taṃ puroḍāśināṃ sānnāyināṃ
ca sārasvate darśanaṃ bhedakāraṇatayā, tadyadā puroḍāśino yāga na sānnāyinaḥ iti kālabhedayogena
parihṛtam । (yadvādaśāhadarśanaṃ bhedasādhanāyopanyastaṃ na dvādaśāhāśrayaṇena parihṛtam) tathā
kecitparihārāḥ yadetikālayogāt । atra hi etadvaktavyam yathā samidādīnāṃ abhyāsādbhedo
bhavati tathā'trāpi kimita na bhavati । ucyate । ekasyāṃ śākhāyāṃ vidhibhedena vidheyabhedo na
yuktaḥ । ato'jñātajñāpanaṃ apravṛttapravartanaṃ ca vidhivyāpāraḥ yadyekameva karma syāt tadidaṃ dvayamapi
nopapadyate śākhāntareṣu tu bhinneṣu pramātṛṣu tadbhedenaiva ajñātajñāpanaṃ apravṛttapravartanaṃ ca
vidherupapannamiti na śak‍noti bhedamāpādayitum ।</p>
<trailer>iti mahāmahopādhyāyaśālikanāthamiśrakṛtāyāṃ ṛjuvimalāyāṃ pañacikāyāṃ
dvitīyasyādhyāyasya
caturthaḥ pādaḥ
samāptaścādhyāyaḥ<trailer>
